Chapter_Header: 1
Verse_Ch: 1:1 不从恶人的计谋，不站罪人的道路，不坐亵慢人的座位； ###EN### Blessed is the man Who does not walk In the counsel of the wicked, Nor stand on the path of sinners, Nor sit in the seat of mockers;
Verse_Ch: 1:2 惟喜爱耶和华的律法，昼夜默想，这人便为有福。 ###EN### Rather his delight is in the law of Jehovah, And in His law he meditates by day and by night.
Verse_Ch: 1:3 他要像一棵树栽在溪水旁，按时令结果子，叶子也不枯干；凡他所作的，尽都顺利。 ###EN### And he will be like a tree Transplanted beside streams of water, Which yields its fruit in its season, And whose foliage does not wither; And everything he does prospers.
Verse_Ch: 1:4 恶人并不是这样，乃像糠秕被风吹散。 ###EN### The wicked are not so, But are like chaff, Which the wind drives away.
Verse_Ch: 1:5 因此当审判的时候，恶人必站立不住；罪人在义人的会中，也是如此。 ###EN### Therefore the wicked will not stand in the judgment; Nor the sinners, in the assembly of the righteous.
Verse_Ch: 1:6 因为耶和华知道义人的道路；恶人的道路，却必灭亡。 ###EN### For Jehovah knows the way of the righteous, But the way of the wicked will perish.
Chapter_Header: 2
Verse_Ch: 2:1 外邦为什么吼闹，万民为什么谋算虚妄的事？ ###EN### Why are the nations in an uproar, And why do the peoples contemplate a vain thing?
Verse_Ch: 2:2 地上的君王一齐起来，臣宰一同商议，要抵挡耶和华并祂的受膏者， ###EN### The kings of the earth take their stand, And the rulers sit in counsel together, Against Jehovah and against His Anointed:
Verse_Ch: 2:3 说，我们要挣开他们的捆绑，摆脱他们的绳索。 ###EN### Let us break apart their bonds And cast their ropes away from us.
Verse_Ch: 2:4 那坐在诸天之上的必发笑；主必嗤笑他们。 ###EN### He who sits in the heavens laughs; The Lord has them in derision.
Verse_Ch: 2:5 那时祂要在怒中对他们说话，在烈怒中惊吓他们， ###EN### Then He will speak to them in His anger, And in His burning wrath He will terrify them:
Verse_Ch: 2:6 说，我已经立我的王在锡安我的圣山上了。 ###EN### But I have installed My King Upon Zion, My holy mountain.
Verse_Ch: 2:7 受膏者说，我要传述耶和华的命令；祂曾对我说，你是我的儿子，我今日生了你。 ###EN### I will recount the decree of Jehovah; He said to Me: You are My Son; Today I have begotten You.
Verse_Ch: 2:8 你求我，我就将列国赐你为基业，将地极赐你为产业。 ###EN### Ask of Me, And I will give the nations as Your inheritance And the limits of the earth as Your possession.
Verse_Ch: 2:9 你必用铁杖打破他们；你必将他们如同窑匠的瓦器摔碎。 ###EN### You will break them with an iron rod; You will shatter them like a potter's vessel.
Verse_Ch: 2:10 现在你们君王应当留意；你们地上的审判官该受警戒。 ###EN### Now therefore, O kings, be prudent; Take the admonition, O judges of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 2:11 当存畏惧事奉耶和华，又当存战兢而欢乐。 ###EN### Serve Jehovah with fear, And rejoice with trembling.
Verse_Ch: 2:12 当以嘴亲子，恐怕祂发怒，你们便在路中灭亡，因为祂的怒气快要发作。凡投奔于祂的，都是有福的。 ###EN### Kiss the Son Lest He be angry and you perish from the way; For His anger may suddenly be kindled. Blessed are all those who take refuge in Him.
Chapter_Header: 3
Verse_Ch: 3:1 耶和华阿，我的敌人何其多！有许多人起来攻击我！ ###EN### Jehovah, how many are my adversaries! Many are those who rise up against me!
Verse_Ch: 3:2 有许多人论到我说，他得不着神的拯救！ 细拉 ###EN### Many are those who say of my soul, There is no salvation for him in God!
Verse_Ch: 3:3 但你耶和华是我四围的盾牌，是我的荣耀，又是叫我抬起头来的。 ###EN### But You, O Jehovah, are a shield around me, My glory and the One who lifts up my head.
Verse_Ch: 3:4 我用我的声音呼求耶和华，祂就从祂的圣山上应允我。 细拉 ###EN### With my voice I call out to Jehovah, And He answers me from His holy mountain.
Verse_Ch: 3:5 我躺下睡觉，我醒过来，因为有耶和华扶持我。 ###EN### I lay down and slept; I awoke, for Jehovah sustains me.
Verse_Ch: 3:6 虽有成万的民周围攻击我，我也不怕。 ###EN### I will not fear the myriads of the people Who have set themselves against me all around.
Verse_Ch: 3:7 耶和华阿，求你起来；我的神阿，求你救我！愿你击打我一切仇敌的腮骨，敲碎恶人的牙齿。 ###EN### Arise, O Jehovah; Save me, O my God! Oh that you would strike all my enemies on the cheek; And break the teeth of the wicked.
Verse_Ch: 3:8 拯救属于耶和华；愿你赐福给你的民。 细拉 ###EN### Salvation is of Jehovah: Your blessing be upon Your people.
Chapter_Header: 4
Verse_Ch: 4:1 显我为义的神阿，我呼求的时候，求你应允我；我在窘困中，求你使我宽广；求你恩待我，听我的祷告。 ###EN### When I call out, answer me, O God of my righteousness; Make room for me when I am in straits; Be gracious to me and hear my prayer.
Verse_Ch: 4:2 人哪，你们将我的荣耀变为羞辱，要到几时呢？你们喜爱虚妄，寻求虚谎，要到几时呢？ 细拉 ###EN### O sons of men, how long will my glory be made a reproach? How long will you love vanity, will you seek a lie?
Verse_Ch: 4:3 你们要知道，耶和华已经分别虔诚人归祂自己；我呼求耶和华，祂必听我。 ###EN### But know that Jehovah sets apart the faithful man for Himself. Jehovah hears when I call out to Him.
Verse_Ch: 4:4 你们生气，却不要犯罪；在床上的时候，要心里思想，并要肃静。 细拉 ###EN### Be angry, yet do not sin; Consider in your heart upon your bed, And be silent.
Verse_Ch: 4:5 当献上公义的祭，又当信靠耶和华。 ###EN### Offer sacrifices of righteousness, And trust in Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 4:6 有许多人说，谁能指示我们什么好处？耶和华阿，求你仰起脸来，光照我们。 ###EN### Many are those who say, Who will show us any good? Lift up upon us the light of Your countenance, O Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 4:7 你使我心里快乐，胜过人丰收五谷新酒时的快乐。 ###EN### You have put joy in my heart, More than when the grain and new wine of others abound.
Verse_Ch: 4:8 我必安然躺下睡觉，因为独有你耶和华使我安然居住。 ###EN### In peace I will both lie down and sleep, For You alone, O Jehovah, cause me to dwell in safety.
Chapter_Header: 5
Verse_Ch: 5:1 耶和华阿，求你侧耳听我的言语，顾念我的呻吟。 ###EN### To my words give ear, O Jehovah; Consider my moaning.
Verse_Ch: 5:2 我的王我的神阿，求你垂听我呼求的声音；因为我向你祷告。 ###EN### Give heed to the sound of my cry, My King and my God; For to You do I pray.
Verse_Ch: 5:3 耶和华阿，早晨你必听我的声音；早晨我必向你陈明我的心意，并要守望。 ###EN### O Jehovah, in the morning You will hear my voice; In the morning I will set forth my words in order to You, And I will watch.
Verse_Ch: 5:4 因为你不是喜悦邪恶的神；恶人不能与你同居。 ###EN### For You are not a God who delights in wickedness; Evil will not sojourn with You.
Verse_Ch: 5:5 夸口的人不能站在你眼前；凡作孽的，都是你所恨恶的。 ###EN### Those who boast will not stand Before Your eyes; You hate all workers of iniquity.
Verse_Ch: 5:6 说谎言的，你必灭绝；好流人血弄诡诈的人，为耶和华所憎恶。 ###EN### You will destroy those who speak lies. Jehovah abhors a man of bloodshed and deceit.
Verse_Ch: 5:7 至于我，我必凭你丰盛的慈爱进入你的居所；我必存敬畏你的心向你的圣殿下拜。 ###EN### But as for me, in the abundance of Your lovingkindness I will come into Your house; I will bow down toward Your holy temple In fear of You.
Verse_Ch: 5:8 耶和华阿，求你因那埋伏等候我的人，凭你的公义引领我；使你的道路在我面前平直。 ###EN### O Jehovah, lead me in Your righteousness On account of those who lie in wait for me; Make Your way straight before me.
Verse_Ch: 5:9 因为他们口中没有诚实；他们内里尽是败坏；他们的喉咙是敞开的坟墓；他们用舌头谄媚人。 ###EN### For there is no truth in their mouth; Their inward part is corruption itself; Their throat is an open grave; They flatter with their tongue.
Verse_Ch: 5:10 神阿，求你定他们有罪；愿他们因自己的计谋跌倒；愿你因他们许多的过犯，把他们赶逐出去，因为他们背叛了你。 ###EN### Hold them guilty, O God; Let them fall by their own counsels; Because of the multitude of their transgressions thrust them out, For they have rebelled against You.
Verse_Ch: 5:11 凡投奔于你的，愿他们喜乐，永远欢呼；愿你覆庇他们；又愿那爱你名的人，都因你欢欣。 ###EN### But let all who take refuge in You rejoice; Let them shout for joy forever; And may You spread a cover over them; And those who love Your name Will exult in You.
Verse_Ch: 5:12 因为耶和华阿，你必赐福与义人；你必用恩惠如同盾牌环绕他。 ###EN### For You will bless the righteous man, O Jehovah; You will surround him with favor as with a shield.
Chapter_Header: 6
Verse_Ch: 6:1 耶和华阿，求你不要在怒中责备我，也不要在烈怒中惩治我。 ###EN### O Jehovah, do not rebuke me in Your anger, Nor chasten me in Your burning wrath.
Verse_Ch: 6:2 耶和华阿，求你恩待我，因为我衰弱；耶和华阿，求你医治我，因为我的骨头发颤， ###EN### Be gracious to me, O Jehovah, for I am languishing; Heal me, O Jehovah, for my bones are shaken,
Verse_Ch: 6:3 我的魂也大大的惊惶。耶和华阿，你要到几时才救我呢？ ###EN### And my soul is greatly shaken. But as for You, O Jehovah, how long?
Verse_Ch: 6:4 耶和华阿，求你转回，搭救我的魂；因你慈爱的缘故，求你拯救我。 ###EN### Return, O Jehovah; deliver my soul; Save me for Your lovingkindness' sake.
Verse_Ch: 6:5 因为在死地无人记念你；在阴间有谁称谢你？ ###EN### For in death there is no remembrance of You; In Sheol who can give thanks to You?
Verse_Ch: 6:6 我因唉哼而困乏；我每夜流泪，把床榻漂起，把褥子湿透。 ###EN### I am weary with my groaning; Every night I cause my bed to swim; With my tears I dissolve my couch.
Verse_Ch: 6:7 我因忧愁眼睛干瘪；又因我一切敌人的缘故，眼睛昏花。 ###EN### My eye is wasted because of grief; It has aged because of all those who vex me.
Verse_Ch: 6:8 你们一切作孽的人，离开我罢，因为耶和华听了我哭泣的声音。 ###EN### Depart from me, all you workers of iniquity, For Jehovah has heard the sound of my weeping.
Verse_Ch: 6:9 耶和华听了我的恳求；耶和华收纳我的祷告。 ###EN### Jehovah has heard my supplication; Jehovah receives my prayer.
Verse_Ch: 6:10 我的一切仇敌都必羞愧，大大惊惶；他们必要退后，忽然羞愧。 ###EN### All my enemies will be ashamed and greatly dismayed; They will turn back; they will be put to shame suddenly.
Chapter_Header: 7
Verse_Ch: 7:1 耶和华我的神阿，我投奔于你；求你救我脱离一切追赶我的人，将我救拔出来； ###EN### O Jehovah my God, in You do I take refuge. Save me from all who pursue me, and deliver me;
Verse_Ch: 7:2 恐怕他们像狮子撕裂我，甚至撕碎，无人搭救。 ###EN### Lest he tear my soul like a lion, Tearing it apart without anyone to deliver it.
Verse_Ch: 7:3 耶和华我的神阿，我若行了这事，我的手中若有不义， ###EN### O Jehovah my God, if I have done this, If there is unrighteousness in my hands,
Verse_Ch: 7:4 我若以恶报那与我和好的人，(那无故与我为敌的人，我倒拯救了他，) ###EN### If I have recompensed with evil him who was at peace with me (Rather, I have delivered him who vexed me without cause);
Verse_Ch: 7:5 就任凭仇敌追赶我，并且追上；将我的性命践踏在地上，使我的荣耀归于尘土。 细拉 ###EN### Let the enemy pursue my soul and overtake me, And let him trample my life to the ground And lay my glory down in the dust.
Verse_Ch: 7:6 耶和华阿，求你在怒中起来，挺身抵挡我敌人的暴怒；求你为我醒起；你已经下令施行审判。 ###EN### Arise, O Jehovah, in Your anger; Lift Yourself up against the overflowing wrath of those who vex me, And awake for me: You have commanded judgment.
Verse_Ch: 7:7 愿众民的会环绕你；愿你从其上归回高处。 ###EN### And let the assembly of the peoples surround You, And over it return on high.
Verse_Ch: 7:8 耶和华要向众民施行审判；耶和华阿，求你按我的公义，并按我里面的纯全，判断我。 ###EN### Jehovah will execute judgment on the peoples; Judge me, O Jehovah, according to my righteousness And according to my integrity that is with me.
Verse_Ch: 7:9 愿恶人的恶断绝；愿你坚立义人；因为公义的神察验人的心肠肺腑。 ###EN### Oh, let the evil of the wicked come to an end, But establish the righteous man. For the righteous God Tries the hearts and the inward parts.
Verse_Ch: 7:10 我的盾牌是在于神，祂拯救心里正直的人。 ###EN### My shield is with God, Who saves the upright in heart.
Verse_Ch: 7:11 神是公义的审判者，又是天天向恶人发怒的神。 ###EN### God is a righteous Judge And a God who has indignation every day.
Verse_Ch: 7:12 若有人不回头，祂必磨快祂的刀，拉紧祂的弓，预备妥当。 ###EN### If one does not turn, He will whet His sword. He bends His bow and makes it ready.
Verse_Ch: 7:13 祂也预备了杀人的器械攻击那人；祂使所射的箭燃烧。 ###EN### And He prepares instruments of death against him; He has made His arrows fiery shafts.
Verse_Ch: 7:14 看哪，恶人受生产罪孽之苦；所怀的是毒害，所生的是虚假。 ###EN### Behold, the evil man travails with iniquity; He conceives mischief and brings forth falsehood.
Verse_Ch: 7:15 他掘了坑，又挖深了，竟掉在自己所挖的陷阱里。 ###EN### He digs a pit and hollows it out, Then he falls into the hole that he has made.
Verse_Ch: 7:16 他的毒害必回到自己头上；他的强暴必落在自己头顶上。 ###EN### His mischief returns upon his own head, And upon the crown of his own head his violence comes down.
Verse_Ch: 7:17 我要照着耶和华的公义称谢祂，歌颂耶和华至高者的名。 ###EN### I will give thanks to Jehovah according to His righteousness, And I will sing psalms to the name of Jehovah the Most High.
Chapter_Header: 8
Verse_Ch: 8:1 耶和华我们的主阿，你的名在全地何其尊大；你将你的荣美彰显于天！ ###EN### O Jehovah our Lord, How excellent is Your name In all the earth, You who have set Your glory over the heavens!
Verse_Ch: 8:2 你因敌人的缘故，从婴孩和吃奶的口中，建立了能力，使仇敌和报仇的，闭口无言。 ###EN### Out of the mouths of babes and sucklings You have established strength Because of Your adversaries, To stop the enemy and the avenger.
Verse_Ch: 8:3 我观看你指头所造的天，并你所陈设的月亮星宿， ###EN### When I see Your heavens, the works of Your fingers, The moon and the stars, which You have ordained,
Verse_Ch: 8:4 便说，人算什么，你竟顾念他？世人算什么，你竟眷顾他？ ###EN### What is mortal man, that You remember him, And the son of man, that You visit him?
Verse_Ch: 8:5 你使他比天使微小一点，并赐他荣耀尊贵为冠冕。 ###EN### You have made him a little lower than angels And have crowned him with glory and honor.
Verse_Ch: 8:6 你派他管理你手所造的，使万物， ###EN### For You have caused him to rule over the works of Your hands; You have put all things under his feet:
Verse_Ch: 8:7 就是一切的牛羊并田野的兽， ###EN### All sheep and oxen, As well as the beasts of the field,
Verse_Ch: 8:8 空中的鸟，海里的鱼，凡经行海道的，都服在他的脚下。 ###EN### The birds of heaven and the fish of the sea, Whatever passes through the paths of the seas.
Verse_Ch: 8:9 耶和华我们的主阿，你的名在全地何其尊大！ ###EN### O Jehovah our Lord, How excellent is Your name In all the earth!
Chapter_Header: 9
Verse_Ch: 9:1 耶和华阿，我要全心称谢你；我要述说你一切奇妙的作为。 ###EN### I will give thanks to You, O Jehovah, with all my heart; I will tell out all Your wonders.
Verse_Ch: 9:2 我要因你喜乐欢欣；至高者阿，我要歌颂你的名。 ###EN### I will rejoice and exult in You; I will sing psalms to Your name, O Most High.
Verse_Ch: 9:3 我的仇敌转身退去的时候，他们一见你的面，就跌倒灭亡。 ###EN### When my enemies turn back, They stumble and perish at Your presence.
Verse_Ch: 9:4 因你已经为我伸冤，为我辨屈；你坐在宝座上，按公义审判。 ###EN### For You have upheld my right and my cause; You sit on the throne, judging righteously.
Verse_Ch: 9:5 你曾斥责外邦，灭绝恶人；你涂抹了他们的名，直到永永远远。 ###EN### You have rebuked the nations; You have destroyed the wicked; You have blotted out their name forever and ever.
Verse_Ch: 9:6 仇敌到了尽头；他们被毁坏，直到永远；你拆毁了他们的城邑；连他们的名号，都归于无有。 ###EN### The enemies are finished; they are in perpetual ruins; And You have uprooted their cities; the very memory of them has perished.
Verse_Ch: 9:7 惟耶和华坐着为王，直到永远；祂已经为审判立定祂的宝座。 ###EN### But Jehovah sits enthroned forever; He has established His throne for judgment.
Verse_Ch: 9:8 祂要按公义审判世界，按公正判断众民。 ###EN### And it is He who judges the world with righteousness; He executes judgment on the peoples with equity.
Verse_Ch: 9:9 耶和华要给受欺压的人作高台，在急难的时候作高台。 ###EN### And Jehovah is a high retreat for the oppressed, A high retreat in times of distress.
Verse_Ch: 9:10 耶和华阿，认识你名的人要信靠你，因你没有离弃寻求你的人。 ###EN### And those who know Your name put their trust in You, For You have not forsaken those who seek You, O Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 9:11 应当歌颂住在锡安的耶和华，将祂所行的传扬在众民中； ###EN### Sing psalms to Jehovah, the Inhabitant of Zion; Declare His deeds among the peoples,
Verse_Ch: 9:12 因为祂追讨流人血的罪，记念被杀的人，不忘记困苦人的哀求。 ###EN### For He who avenges bloodshed remembers those who were slain; He does not forget the cry of the afflicted.
Verse_Ch: 9:13 耶和华阿，你是从死门把我提拔起来的；求你恩待我，看那恨我的人所加给我的苦难， ###EN### Be gracious to me, O Jehovah; look on my affliction from those who hate me, You who raise me from the gates of death,
Verse_Ch: 9:14 好叫我述说你一切可赞美的事，并在锡安城的门，因你的救恩欢乐。 ###EN### That I may tell out all Your praises And, in the gates of the daughter of Zion, exult in Your salvation.
Verse_Ch: 9:15 外邦人陷在自己所掘的坑中；他们的脚在自己暗设的网罗里缠住了。 ###EN### The nations have sunk in the pit that they have made; In the net that they hid, their own foot is caught.
Verse_Ch: 9:16 耶和华已将自己显明了，祂已施行公理；恶人被自己手所作的缠住了。希该昂细拉 ###EN### Jehovah has made Himself known; He has executed justice; The wicked have been snared in the work of their hands.
Verse_Ch: 9:17 恶人，就是忘记神的外邦人，都必归到阴间。 ###EN### The wicked will be turned back to Sheol, All the nations who forget God.
Verse_Ch: 9:18 穷乏人必不永久被忘，困苦人的指望，必不永远落空。 ###EN### For not always will the needy be forgotten, Nor will the hope of the afflicted perish forever.
Verse_Ch: 9:19 耶和华阿，求你起来！不要让人得胜；愿外邦人在你面前受审判。 ###EN### Arise, O Jehovah! Let not mortal man prevail; Let the nations be judged in Your sight.
Verse_Ch: 9:20 耶和华阿，求你使他们恐惧；愿外邦人知道自己不过是人。 细拉 ###EN### Put them in fear, O Jehovah; Let the nations know that they are mortal men.
Chapter_Header: 10
Verse_Ch: 10:1 耶和华阿，你为什么站在远处？在急难的时候，为什么隐藏？ ###EN### Why, O Jehovah, do You stand far off? Why do You hide Yourself in times of distress?
Verse_Ch: 10:2 恶人在骄横中，把穷苦人追得火急；愿他们陷入自己所设的计谋里！ ###EN### Arrogantly the wicked hotly pursue the poor-May they be caught in the plots that they devise!
Verse_Ch: 10:3 因为恶人夸耀自己魂里的欲望；贪婪的人咒诅耶和华，并且轻慢祂。 ###EN### For the wicked man boasts of the desire of his soul, And the rapacious man curses, even despises, Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 10:4 恶人面带高傲，说，耶和华必不追究；他一切所想的，都以为没有神。 ###EN### The wicked man, according to the haughtiness of his countenance, Says, He will not require it; All his thoughts are this: There is no God!
Verse_Ch: 10:5 他的道路总是亨通；你的审判高高在上，超过他的眼界；至于他一切的敌人，他都向他们喷气。 ###EN### His ways succeed at all times; Your judgments are on high, out of his sight; As for all his adversaries, he snorts at them.
Verse_Ch: 10:6 他心里说，我必不动摇，世世代代不遭灾难。 ###EN### He has said in his heart, I will not be shaken; I will be in no trouble forever.
Verse_Ch: 10:7 他满口是咒诅、诡诈、欺压；他的舌底是毒害、罪孽。 ###EN### His mouth is full of curses and of deceit and oppression; Under his tongue are mischief and iniquity.
Verse_Ch: 10:8 他在村庄埋伏等候；他在隐密处杀害无辜的人；他的眼睛窥探不幸的人。 ###EN### He sits in the ambushes of the open villages; In hidden places he murders the innocent; His eyes secretly watch for the unfortunate.
Verse_Ch: 10:9 他埋伏在隐密处，如狮子蹲在洞中；他埋伏，要掠取穷苦人；他拉网，就把穷苦人掠去。 ###EN### He lurks in secret like a lion in its covert; He lurks ready to seize the poor; He seizes the poor, drawing them up in his net.
Verse_Ch: 10:10 他屈身蹲伏，不幸的人就倒在他强劲的爪下。 ###EN### He stoops, he crouches, And the unfortunate fall by his mighty claws.
Verse_Ch: 10:11 他心里说，神已经忘记了；祂掩面，绝不看这事。 ###EN### He has said in his heart, God has forgotten; He has hidden His face; He will never see this.
Verse_Ch: 10:12 耶和华阿，求你起来；神阿，求你举手；不要忘记穷苦人。 ###EN### Arise, O Jehovah; O God, lift up Your hand. Do not forget the poor.
Verse_Ch: 10:13 恶人为何轻慢神，心里说，你必不追究？ ###EN### Why does the wicked man despise God And say in his heart, You will not require it?
Verse_Ch: 10:14 其实你已经看见；因为毒害和苦恼，你都察看，为要亲手施行报应。不幸的人把自己交托你；你向来是帮助孤儿的。 ###EN### You do see! For You observe mischief and vexation, To requite it with Your own hand. To You the unfortunate one commits his cause; You have been the help of the orphan.
Verse_Ch: 10:15 愿你打断恶人和坏人的膀臂；愿你追究他的恶，直到无可察觉。 ###EN### Break the arm of the wicked man and the evil doer; Seek out his wickedness until You find no more.
Verse_Ch: 10:16 耶和华永永远远为王；外邦人从祂的地已经灭绝了。 ###EN### Jehovah is King forever and ever; The nations have perished from His land.
Verse_Ch: 10:17 耶和华阿，卑微人的愿望，你已经听见；你必坚固他们的心；你必亲耳垂听他们的祈求， ###EN### You have heard the desire of the lowly, O Jehovah; You will establish their heart; You will cause Your ears to listen,
Verse_Ch: 10:18 为要给孤儿和受欺压的人伸冤，使地上的人不再威吓他们。 ###EN### In order to execute justice for the orphan and the oppressed one, That the mortal man of the earth may terrorize no longer.
Chapter_Header: 11
Verse_Ch: 11:1 我投奔于耶和华；你们怎么对我说，你当像鸟逃往山上去？ ###EN### In Jehovah have I taken refuge. How can you say to my soul, Flee to the mountains like a bird?
Verse_Ch: 11:2 恶人弯弓，把箭搭在弦上，要在黑暗中射那心里正直的人。 ###EN### For behold, the wicked bend the bow; They ready their arrow on the string To shoot in the dark at the upright in heart.
Verse_Ch: 11:3 根基若毁坏，义人还能作什么呢？ ###EN### When the foundations are destroyed, What will the righteous man do?
Verse_Ch: 11:4 耶和华在祂的圣殿里；耶和华的宝座在天上。祂的眼目察看；祂的目光察验世人。 ###EN### Jehovah is in His holy temple; Jehovah-His throne is in heaven. His eyes behold; His eyelids try the sons of men.
Verse_Ch: 11:5 耶和华试炼义人；惟有恶人和喜爱强暴的人，祂心里恨恶。 ###EN### Jehovah tries the righteous man; But the wicked man and him who loves violence, His soul hates.
Verse_Ch: 11:6 祂要向恶人密布网罗；有烈火、硫磺、热风，作他们杯中的分。 ###EN### He will rain down snares upon the wicked; Fire and brimstone and a scorching wind will be the portion of their cup.
Verse_Ch: 11:7 因为耶和华是公义的；祂爱公义的行为。正直人必得见祂的面。 ###EN### For Jehovah is righteous; He loves righteous deeds. The upright man will behold His face.
Chapter_Header: 12
Verse_Ch: 12:1 耶和华阿，求你拯救，因虔诚人断绝了，忠信人已经从世人中间消失了。 ###EN### Save, O Jehovah; for the faithful man is no more, For the trustworthy have vanished from among the sons of men.
Verse_Ch: 12:2 人人向邻舍说虚谎的话；他们说话，是嘴唇油滑，心口不一。 ###EN### Each man speaks falsehood with his neighbor; With flattering lips and a double heart they speak.
Verse_Ch: 12:3 凡油滑的嘴唇，说夸大话的舌头，愿耶和华剪除； ###EN### May Jehovah cut off all the flattering lips, The tongue speaking great things,
Verse_Ch: 12:4 他们曾说，我们必能以舌头得胜；我们的嘴唇是我们自己的；谁能作我们的主呢？ ###EN### Those who said, With our tongue we will prevail; Our lips are our own: Who is our lord?
Verse_Ch: 12:5 耶和华说，因为困苦人所受的蹂躏，因为穷乏人的叹息，我现在要起来，把他安置在他所切慕的稳妥之地。 ###EN### Because of the devastation of the poor, because of the sighing of the needy, I will now arise, says Jehovah; I will set him in the safety that he longs for.
Verse_Ch: 12:6 耶和华的言语，是纯净的言语，如同地上炉中炼过的银子，精炼过七次。 ###EN### The words of Jehovah are pure words, Silver refined in a furnace on the earth, Purified seven times.
Verse_Ch: 12:7 耶和华阿，你必保守他们；你必护卫他们永远脱离这世代的人。 ###EN### You, O Jehovah, will keep them; You will guard them from this generation forever.
Verse_Ch: 12:8 卑贱的事在世人中被高举，恶人就到处游行。 ###EN### The wicked go about all around, While vileness is exalted among the sons of men.
Chapter_Header: 13
Verse_Ch: 13:1 耶和华阿，你忘记我要到几时呢？要到永远么？你掩面不顾我要到几时呢？ ###EN### How long, O Jehovah? Will You forget me continually? How long will You hide Your face from me?
Verse_Ch: 13:2 我魂里筹算，心里终日愁苦，要到几时呢？我的仇敌高居我上，要到几时呢？ ###EN### How long will I bear concern in my soul And sorrow in my heart day after day? How long will my enemy be exalted over me?
Verse_Ch: 13:3 耶和华我的神阿，求你看顾我，应允我；求你使我眼目光明，免得我沉睡至死； ###EN### Consider and answer me, O Jehovah my God; Enlighten my eyes lest I sleep the sleep of death,
Verse_Ch: 13:4 免得我的仇敌说，我胜过了他；免得我的敌人在我摇动的时候欢乐。 ###EN### Lest my enemy say, I have prevailed against him, And my adversaries exult when I am shaken.
Verse_Ch: 13:5 但我信靠你的慈爱；我的心要因你的救恩欢乐； ###EN### But I trust in Your lovingkindness; My heart will exult in Your salvation;
Verse_Ch: 13:6 我要向耶和华歌唱，因祂用厚恩待我。 ###EN### I will sing to Jehovah, For He has dealt bountifully with me.
Chapter_Header: 14
Verse_Ch: 14:1 愚顽人心里说，没有神。他们都是败坏，行了可憎恶的事；没有一个人行善。 ###EN### The fool has said in his heart, There is no God. They are corrupt; they commit abominable deeds; There is none who does good.
Verse_Ch: 14:2 耶和华从天上垂看世人，要看有明白的没有，有寻求神的没有。 ###EN### Jehovah looked down from heaven Upon the sons of men To see if there was anyone who had insight, Who seeks after God.
Verse_Ch: 14:3 他们都是偏离正路，一同变为败坏；没有行善的，连一个也没有。 ###EN### They have all turned aside; They are together perverse. There is none who does good; There is not even one.
Verse_Ch: 14:4 作孽的都没有知识么？他们吞吃我的百姓，如同吃饭一样，并不呼求耶和华。 ###EN### Have they no knowledge, all the workers of iniquity, Who eat up my people as they would eat up bread And do not call upon Jehovah?
Verse_Ch: 14:5 他们在那里大大的害怕，因为神是在义人的族类中。 ###EN### There they were in great fear, For God is among the generation of the righteous.
Verse_Ch: 14:6 你们叫困苦人的谋算变为羞辱，然而耶和华是他们的避难所。 ###EN### You put the counsel of the afflicted to shame, But Jehovah is their refuge.
Verse_Ch: 14:7 但愿以色列的救恩从锡安而出！耶和华使祂被掳的子民归回，那时雅各要欢腾，以色列要喜乐。 ###EN### O that the salvation of Israel might come forth from Zion! When Jehovah turns the captivity of His people, Jacob will exult, Israel will rejoice.
Chapter_Header: 15
Verse_Ch: 15:1 耶和华阿，谁能寄居你的帐幕？谁能住在你的圣山？ ###EN### O Jehovah, who may sojourn in Your tent? Who may dwell on Your holy mountain?
Verse_Ch: 15:2 就是行为纯全，作事公义，从心里说实话的人。 ###EN### He who walks in integrity And does righteousness And speaks truth from his heart.
Verse_Ch: 15:3 他不以舌头谗谤人，不恶待朋友，也不随伙辱骂邻里。 ###EN### He does not slander with his tongue; He does not do evil to his friend, Nor does he take up a reproach against his neighbor.
Verse_Ch: 15:4 他眼中藐视可弃绝的人，却尊重敬畏耶和华的人。他发了誓，虽然自己吃亏，也不更改。 ###EN### In his eyes a reprobate is despised, But he honors those who fear Jehovah. Should he swear to his harm, He does not change.
Verse_Ch: 15:5 他不放债取利，也不受贿赂以害无辜。行这些事的人，必永不动摇。 ###EN### He does not lend his money on interest, Nor accept a bribe against the innocent. He who does these things will not be shaken forever.
Chapter_Header: 16
Verse_Ch: 16:1 神阿，求你保守我，因为我投奔于你。 ###EN### Preserve me, O God, for I take refuge in You.
Verse_Ch: 16:2 我对耶和华说，你是我的主；我的好处不在你以外。 ###EN### I say to Jehovah, You are my Lord; No good have I beyond You;
Verse_Ch: 16:3 论到地上的圣民，他们是尊高的人，是我所最喜悦的。 ###EN### As for the saints who are on the earth, they are the excellent; All my delight is in them.
Verse_Ch: 16:4 以别神代替耶和华的，他们的愁苦必加增；他们所浇奠的血我不献上，我嘴唇也不题别神的名号。 ###EN### The sorrows of them who bartered for some other god will be multiplied; Their drink offerings of blood I will not offer, Nor will I take up their names upon my lips.
Verse_Ch: 16:5 耶和华是我的产业，是我杯中的分；我所得的分你为我持守。 ###EN### Jehovah is the portion of my inheritance and of my cup; You maintain my lot.
Verse_Ch: 16:6 用绳量给我的地界，坐落在佳美之处；我的产业实在美好。 ###EN### The measuring lines have fallen on pleasant places for me; Indeed the inheritance is beautiful to me.
Verse_Ch: 16:7 我必颂赞那指教我的耶和华；我的心肠在夜间也警戒我。 ###EN### I will bless Jehovah, who counsels me; Indeed in the nights my inward parts instruct me.
Verse_Ch: 16:8 我将耶和华常摆在我面前；因祂在我右边，我便不至摇动。 ###EN### I have set Jehovah before me continually; Because He is at my right hand, I shall not be shaken.
Verse_Ch: 16:9 因此我的心快乐，我的灵欢腾；我的肉身也安然居住。 ###EN### Therefore my heart rejoices and my glory exults; Even my flesh dwells securely.
Verse_Ch: 16:10 因为你必不将我的魂撇在阴间，也不叫你的圣者见朽坏。 ###EN### For You will not abandon my soul to Sheol, Nor let Your Holy One see the pit.
Verse_Ch: 16:11 你必将生命的道路指示我；在你面前有满足的喜乐；在你右手中有永远的福乐。 ###EN### You will make known to me the path of life; In Your presence is fullness of joy; At Your right hand there are pleasures forever.
Chapter_Header: 17
Verse_Ch: 17:1 耶和华阿，求你听闻公义，垂听我的呼吁；求你侧耳听我这不出于诡诈嘴唇的祷告。 ###EN### Hear, O Jehovah, what is righteous; Give heed to my cry; Give ear to my prayer, Which is not made with lips of deceit.
Verse_Ch: 17:2 愿你对我的判语，从你面前发出；愿你的眼睛察看公正。 ###EN### May a judgment for me come forth from Your presence; May Your eyes regard equity.
Verse_Ch: 17:3 你已经试验我的心；你在夜间鉴察我；你熬炼我，却找不着什么。我立志使我口中没有过犯。 ###EN### You have examined my heart; You have visited me by night; You have tried me: You have found nothing. I have resolved that my mouth will not transgress.
Verse_Ch: 17:4 论到人的行为，我借着你嘴唇的言语，保守自己不行强暴人的道路。 ###EN### Regarding the works of man, by the word of Your lips, I have kept myself from the paths of the violent man.
Verse_Ch: 17:5 我的步伐稳踏在你的路径上，我的脚步未曾滑跌。 ###EN### My steps have held fast to Your tracks; My footsteps have not slipped.
Verse_Ch: 17:6 神阿，我呼求你，因为你必应允我；求你向我侧耳，听我的言语。 ###EN### I call on You, for You will answer me, O God; Incline Your ear to me; hear my speaking.
Verse_Ch: 17:7 求你奇妙的显示你的慈爱；你用右手拯救投靠你的，脱离起来攻击他们的人。 ###EN### Wondrously display Your lovingkindness, You who save by Your right hand Those who take refuge in You from them who rise up against them.
Verse_Ch: 17:8 求你保护我，如同保护你眼中的瞳人；将我隐藏在你翅膀的荫下， ###EN### Guard me like the pupil of Your eye; In the shadow of Your wings hide me
Verse_Ch: 17:9 使我脱离欺压我的恶人，就是围困我，要害我命的仇敌。 ###EN### From the presence of the wicked who oppress me, From my deadly enemies, who close in upon me.
Verse_Ch: 17:10 他们关闭了他们被脂油包裹的心，用口说狂妄的话。 ###EN### They have shut up their fat hearts; With their mouths they speak arrogantly.
Verse_Ch: 17:11 现在他们围困了我们的脚步；他们瞪着眼，要把我们推倒在地。 ###EN### Now they have surrounded us in our steps; They have fixed their eyes on casting us down to the ground.
Verse_Ch: 17:12 他像狮子急要抓食，又像少壮狮子蹲伏在隐密处。 ###EN### He is like a lion that is eager to tear, And like a young lion lurking in hidden places.
Verse_Ch: 17:13 耶和华阿，求你起来，迎面抵挡他，将他打倒。求你用你的刀救护我的性命脱离恶人； ###EN### Arise, O Jehovah, confront him; bring him down. With Your sword rescue my soul from the wicked man,
Verse_Ch: 17:14 耶和华阿，求你用手救护我脱离世人，脱离那些只在今生有业分的世人；你把你的财宝充满他们的肚腹；他们因有儿女就心满意足，将他们的富余 留给他们的婴孩。 ###EN### From mortal men with Your hand, O Jehovah, From mortal men of the world, whose portion is in this life, And whose belly You fill with Your treasure; They are satisfied with children, And they leave their abundance for their little ones.
Verse_Ch: 17:15 至于我，我必在义中见你的面；我醒了的时候，必因见你的形像而心满意足。 ###EN### As for me, in righteousness I will behold Your face; When I awake, I will be satisfied with Your likeness.
Chapter_Header: 18
Verse_Ch: 18:1 耶和华我的力量阿，我爱你。 ###EN### I love You, O Jehovah, my strength.
Verse_Ch: 18:2 耶和华是我的岩石，我的山寨，我的解救者；是我的神，我的磐石，我所投靠的；是我的盾牌，拯救我的角，我的高台。 ###EN### Jehovah is my crag and my fortress and my Deliverer; My God, my rock, in whom I take refuge; My shield and the horn of my salvation, my high retreat.
Verse_Ch: 18:3 我呼求当受赞美的耶和华，就蒙拯救脱离仇敌。 ###EN### I called upon Jehovah, who is worthy of praise, And from my enemies I was saved.
Verse_Ch: 18:4 曾有死亡的绳索围绕我；毁灭的急流使我惊惧。 ###EN### The cords of death encompassed me; And the torrents of destruction assailed me.
Verse_Ch: 18:5 阴间的绳索缠绕我；死亡的网罗临到我。 ###EN### The cords of Sheol surrounded me; The snares of death confronted me.
Verse_Ch: 18:6 我在急难中呼求耶和华，向我的神呼救。祂从殿中听了我的声音，我在祂面前的呼救入了祂的耳中。 ###EN### In my distress I called upon Jehovah And cried out to my God. He heard my voice from His temple, And my cry before Him came to His ears.
Verse_Ch: 18:7 那时因祂发怒，地就摇撼战抖，山的根基也震动摇撼。 ###EN### Then the earth shook and quaked, And the foundations of the mountains trembled and shook about, For He was furious.
Verse_Ch: 18:8 从祂鼻孔冒烟上腾，从祂口中发火焚烧；连炭也烧着了。 ###EN### Smoke went up from His nostrils, And fire from His mouth devoured; Coals blazed forth from Him.
Verse_Ch: 18:9 祂使天下垂，亲自降临；有幽暗在祂脚下。 ###EN### He bowed the heavens and descended, And deep darkness was under His feet.
Verse_Ch: 18:10 祂乘坐基路伯飞行；祂驾御风的翅膀快飞。 ###EN### He rode upon a cherub and did fly; He darted upon the wings of the wind.
Verse_Ch: 18:11 祂以黑暗为藏身之处，以乌黑的水云、天空的厚云为祂四围的帷幕。 ###EN### He made darkness His hiding place, His pavilion around Him: Dark waterclouds, thick clouds of the skies.
Verse_Ch: 18:12 有冰雹和火炭，透过祂的厚云，从祂面前的光辉中发出。 ###EN### Out of the brightness before Him there broke through His clouds Hail and fiery coals.
Verse_Ch: 18:13 耶和华也在天上打雷，至高者发出声音。 ###EN### Then Jehovah thundered in heaven, And the Most High uttered His voice.
Verse_Ch: 18:14 祂射出箭来，使我的仇敌四散；祂发出闪电，使他们溃乱。 ###EN### And He sent forth His arrows and scattered my enemies; And He shot forth lightning bolts and discomfited them.
Verse_Ch: 18:15 耶和华阿，你的斥责一发，你鼻孔的气一出，海底就出现，居人之地的根基也显露。 ###EN### The channels of the sea were seen, And the foundations of the habitable land were laid bare At Your rebuke, O Jehovah, At the blast of the breath of Your nostrils.
Verse_Ch: 18:16 祂从高天伸手抓住我，把我从大水中拉上来。 ###EN### He reached forth from on high; He took me; He drew me out of great waters.
Verse_Ch: 18:17 祂救我脱离我的劲敌，和那些恨我的人，因为他们比我强盛。 ###EN### He delivered me from my strong enemy And from those who hate me, for they were too mighty for me.
Verse_Ch: 18:18 我遭遇灾难的日子，他们迎面攻击我，但耶和华成了我的扶持。 ###EN### They confronted me in the day of my calamity, But Jehovah became my support.
Verse_Ch: 18:19 祂领我到宽阔之处；祂救拔我，因祂喜悦我。 ###EN### He brought me forth to a place broad and free; He rescued me, for He took delight in me.
Verse_Ch: 18:20 耶和华按着我的公义报答我，按着我手中的清洁回报我。 ###EN### Jehovah has recompensed me according to my righteousness; According to the cleanness of my hands He has repaid me.
Verse_Ch: 18:21 因为我谨守了耶和华的道路，未曾作恶离开我的神。 ###EN### For I have kept the ways of Jehovah And have not acted wickedly by turning away from my God.
Verse_Ch: 18:22 祂的一切典章常在我面前；祂的律例，我也未曾离弃。 ###EN### For all His judgments were before me, And I did not turn His statutes away from me.
Verse_Ch: 18:23 我向祂作了完全人，我也保守自己远离我的罪孽。 ###EN### I was perfect toward Him, And I kept myself from my iniquity.
Verse_Ch: 18:24 所以耶和华按我的公义，按我在祂眼前手中的清洁回报我。 ###EN### Therefore Jehovah recompensed me according to my righteousness, According to the cleanness of my hands in His sight.
Verse_Ch: 18:25 慈爱的人，你以慈爱待他；完全的人，你以完全待他。 ###EN### With the faithful You show Yourself faithful, With a perfect man You show Yourself perfect,
Verse_Ch: 18:26 纯洁的人，你以纯洁待他；乖僻的人，你以弯曲待他。 ###EN### With the pure You show Yourself pure, And with the perverse You show Yourself contrary.
Verse_Ch: 18:27 因为你必拯救困苦的百姓，却使高傲的眼目降卑； ###EN### For it is You who save the afflicted people, But the haughty eyes You bring down;
Verse_Ch: 18:28 你必点亮我的灯；耶和华我的神必照明我的黑暗。 ###EN### For it is You who light my lamp; Jehovah my God lights up my darkness;
Verse_Ch: 18:29 我借着你冲入敌军，借着我的神跳过墙垣。 ###EN### For by You I can run up against a troop; Indeed by my God I can leap over a wall.
Verse_Ch: 18:30 至于神，祂的道路是完全的；耶和华的话是炼净的。凡投靠祂的，祂便作他们的盾牌。 ###EN### As for God-His way is perfect ; The word of Jehovah is tried. He is a shield to all who take refuge in Him.
Verse_Ch: 18:31 除了耶和华，谁是神呢？除了我们的神，谁是磐石呢？ ###EN### For who is God other than Jehovah, And who is a rock but our God?
Verse_Ch: 18:32 惟有那以力量束我的腰，使我道路完全的，祂是神； ###EN### The God who girds me with strength And makes my way perfect,
Verse_Ch: 18:33 祂使我的脚快如母鹿的蹄，又使我在高处站稳； ###EN### Who makes my feet like hinds' feet And sets me on my high places,
Verse_Ch: 18:34 祂教导我的手能以争战，使我的膀臂能开铜弓。 ###EN### Who teaches my hands to wage war So that my arms may bend a bronze bow.
Verse_Ch: 18:35 你把你救恩的盾牌赐给了我，你的右手扶持我；你的温和俯就使我为大。 ###EN### And You have given me the shield of Your salvation, And Your right hand supports me; And Your condescending gentleness has made me great.
Verse_Ch: 18:36 你使我脚下的地步宽阔，我的脚未曾滑跌。 ###EN### You have broadened the places of my steps under me, And my feet have not slipped.
Verse_Ch: 18:37 我追赶我的仇敌，并且追上他们；不将他们灭绝，我总不转回。 ###EN### I pursued my enemies and overtook them, And I did not turn back until they were consumed.
Verse_Ch: 18:38 我击溃他们，使他们不能起来；他们都倒在我的脚下。 ###EN### I shattered them, so that they were not able to rise up; They fell under my feet.
Verse_Ch: 18:39 你以力量束我的腰，使我能争战；你也使那起来攻击我的，都服在我以下。 ###EN### And You girded me with strength for war; You brought down under me those who rose up against me.
Verse_Ch: 18:40 你又使我的仇敌在我面前转背逃跑，我就歼灭那恨我的人。 ###EN### You also made my enemies turn their back to me, And I annihilated those who hated me.
Verse_Ch: 18:41 他们呼求，却无人拯救；就是呼求耶和华，祂也不应允。 ###EN### They cried out, but there was no one to save them; They cried out to Jehovah, but He did not answer them.
Verse_Ch: 18:42 我捣碎他们，如同风前的灰尘；我践踏他们，如同街上的泥土。 ###EN### Then I beat them like dust before the wind; Like the mud of the streets I pounded them.
Verse_Ch: 18:43 你救我脱离百姓的争竞，立我作列国的元首；我素不认识的民必事奉我。 ###EN### You rescued me from the strivings of the people; You have made me the head of the nations; A people whom I had not known serves me.
Verse_Ch: 18:44 他们一听见我的名声，就必顺从我；外邦人要归顺我。 ###EN### At the mere hearing of a report, they obey me; Foreigners come cringing to me;
Verse_Ch: 18:45 外邦人要沮丧，战战兢兢的出他们的营寨。 ###EN### Foreigners are discouraged And come quaking out of their fortresses.
Verse_Ch: 18:46 耶和华是活神；愿我的磐石受颂赞；愿拯救我的神被高举； ###EN### Jehovah lives; and blessed be my rock, And exalted be the God of my salvation,
Verse_Ch: 18:47 这位神就是那为我伸冤，使众民服在我以下， ###EN### The God who executes vengeance for me And subdues peoples under me,
Verse_Ch: 18:48 又使我脱离仇敌的。你还把我举起，高过那些起来攻击我的；你救我脱离强暴的人。 ###EN### Who rescues me from my enemies. Indeed You exalted me above those who rise up against me; From the violent man You delivered me.
Verse_Ch: 18:49 耶和华阿，因此我要在列国中称谢你，歌颂你的名。 ###EN### Therefore I give thanks to You among the nations, O Jehovah; And I will sing psalms to Your name.
Verse_Ch: 18:50 耶和华向祂所立的王显极大的救恩，施慈爱给祂的受膏者，就是给大卫和他的后裔，直到永远。 ###EN### It is He who magnifies salvation to His king And executes lovingkindness to His anointed, To David and to his seed forever.
Chapter_Header: 19
Verse_Ch: 19:1 诸天述说神的荣耀，穹苍传扬祂手的作为。 ###EN### The heavens declare the glory of God, And the firmament proclaims the work of His hands.
Verse_Ch: 19:2 这日到那日发出言语；这夜到那夜传出知识。 ###EN### Day to day pours forth speech, And night to night tells out knowledge.
Verse_Ch: 19:3 无言无语，也无声音可听。 ###EN### There is no speech and there are no words; Their voice is not heard.
Verse_Ch: 19:4 它们的准绳通遍全地，它们的言语达到地极。神在诸天为太阳安设帐幕； ###EN### In all the earth their line has gone forth, And their words to the end of the world. In the heavens He has made a tent for the sun,
Verse_Ch: 19:5 太阳如同新郎出洞房，又如勇士欢然奔路。 ###EN### And he, like a bridegroom, goes forth from his canopy; He rejoices like a mighty man running the course.
Verse_Ch: 19:6 它从天这边出来，绕到天那边；没有一物被隐藏不得它的热气。 ###EN### His going forth is from the end of the heavens, And his circuit is unto their ends; And there is nothing hidden from his heat.
Verse_Ch: 19:7 耶和华的律法完全，能苏醒人的魂；耶和华的法度可靠，能使愚蒙人有智慧； ###EN### The law of Jehovah is perfect, Restoring the soul; The testimony of Jehovah is faithful, Making the simple wise;
Verse_Ch: 19:8 耶和华的训辞正直，能快活人心；耶和华的命令清明，能明亮人眼； ###EN### The precepts of Jehovah are right, Making the heart joyous; The commandment of Jehovah is clear, Enlightening the eyes;
Verse_Ch: 19:9 耶和华的教训洁净，存到永远；耶和华的典章真实，全然公义。 ###EN### The fear of Jehovah is pure, Enduring forever; The judgments of Jehovah are truth And altogether righteous.
Verse_Ch: 19:10 都比金子可羡慕，且比极多的精金可羡慕；比蜜甘甜，且比蜂房下滴的蜜甘甜。 ###EN### More to be desired are they than gold, Even much refined gold; Sweeter also than honey And the drippings of the honeycomb.
Verse_Ch: 19:11 况且你的仆人藉此受警戒，谨守这些便有大赏赐。 ###EN### Moreover by them Your servant is warned; In keeping them there is much reward.
Verse_Ch: 19:12 谁能察知自己的错失呢？愿你不定罪我隐而未现的过错。 ###EN### Who can discern his errors? Clear me of my secret faults.
Verse_Ch: 19:13 还求你拦阻仆人，不犯任意妄为的罪；不容这罪辖制我；我便可以完全，免犯大过。 ###EN### Also keep back Your servant from presumptuous sins; Do not let them have dominion over me; Then I will be blameless and cleared Of great transgression.
Verse_Ch: 19:14 耶和华我的磐石，我的救赎主阿，愿我口中的言语，心里的意念，在你面前蒙悦纳。 ###EN### May the words of my mouth and the meditation of my heart Be acceptable before You, O Jehovah, my rock and my Redeemer.
Chapter_Header: 20
Verse_Ch: 20:1 愿耶和华在你遭难的日子应允你；愿雅各神的名将你安置在高处； ###EN### May Jehovah answer you in the day of trouble; May the name of the God of Jacob set you on high.
Verse_Ch: 20:2 愿祂从圣所差来帮助，从锡安扶持你。 ###EN### May He send you help from the sanctuary And support you from Zion.
Verse_Ch: 20:3 愿祂记念你的一切素祭，悦纳你的燔祭。 细拉 ###EN### May He remember all your meal offerings And accept your burnt offering.
Verse_Ch: 20:4 愿祂照你心所愿的赐给你，成就你的一切筹算。 ###EN### May He give you according to your heart's desire And fulfill all your intention.
Verse_Ch: 20:5 我们要因你的救恩得胜欢呼，在我们神的名里竖立旌旗。愿耶和华成就你一切所求的。 ###EN### May we shout victoriously in Your salvation And raise the banner in the name of our God. May Jehovah fulfill all your petitions.
Verse_Ch: 20:6 现在我知道耶和华拯救祂的受膏者，必从祂的圣天上应允他，用祂右手的大能拯救他。 ###EN### Now I know That Jehovah saves His anointed; He will answer him from His holy heaven With mighty acts of salvation from His right hand.
Verse_Ch: 20:7 有人夸车，有人夸马，但我们要夸耶和华我们神的名。 ###EN### Some boast in chariots, and some in horses; But we boast in the name of Jehovah our God.
Verse_Ch: 20:8 他们都屈身仆倒，我们却起来，立得正直。 ###EN### They are humbled and fallen, But we have risen and stand upright.
Verse_Ch: 20:9 耶和华阿，求你拯救！我们呼求的时候，愿王应允我们。 ###EN### Save, O Jehovah! May the king answer us when we call.
Chapter_Header: 21
Verse_Ch: 21:1 耶和华阿，王因你的能力喜乐；他因你的救恩，何其欢腾。 ###EN### O Jehovah, in Your strength the king rejoices, And in Your salvation how greatly does he exult.
Verse_Ch: 21:2 他心里所愿的，你已经赐给他；他嘴唇所求的，你未尝不应允。 细拉 ###EN### You have given him his heart's desire And have not withheld the request of his lips.
Verse_Ch: 21:3 你以美福迎接他，把精金的冠冕戴在他头上。 ###EN### For You meet him with blessings of goodness; You have set a crown of refined gold on his head.
Verse_Ch: 21:4 他向你求寿，你便赐给他，就是日子长久，直到永远。 ###EN### He asked life of You; You granted it to him: Length of days forever and ever.
Verse_Ch: 21:5 他因你的救恩大有荣耀；你将尊荣威严加在他身上； ###EN### His glory is great in Your salvation; You have laid majesty and splendor upon him;
Verse_Ch: 21:6 你使他有洪福，直到永远；又使他在你面前欢喜快乐。 ###EN### For You have made him to be blessings forever; You have made him glad with rejoicing in Your presence.
Verse_Ch: 21:7 王信靠耶和华；因至高者的慈爱，他必不摇动。 ###EN### For the king trusts in Jehovah; And because of the lovingkindness of the Most High, he is not shaken.
Verse_Ch: 21:8 你的手要搜出你的一切仇敌；你的右手要搜出那些恨你的人。 ###EN### Your hand finds all Your enemies; Your right hand finds those who hate You.
Verse_Ch: 21:9 你面光显现的时候，要使他们如在炎热的火炉中；耶和华要在祂的怒中吞灭他们，火要把他们烧尽了。 ###EN### You make them like a furnace of fire When Your presence appears. Jehovah swallows them in His anger, And fire devours them.
Verse_Ch: 21:10 你必从地上灭绝他们的子孙，从世人中间灭绝他们的后裔。 ###EN### You destroy their fruit from the earth, And their seed from among the sons of men.
Verse_Ch: 21:11 因为他们有意加害于你；他们想出计谋，却不能成功。 ###EN### Although they intend evil against You, And they think up a scheme, they will not prevail.
Verse_Ch: 21:12 你必使他们转背逃跑；你对准他们的脸，搭箭在弦。 ###EN### For You make them turn their back; You aim with Your bowstrings at their faces.
Verse_Ch: 21:13 耶和华阿，愿你因自己的能力得高举；我们就唱诗，歌颂你的大能。 ###EN### Be exalted, O Jehovah, in Your strength; We will sing and psalm Your might.
Chapter_Header: 22
Verse_Ch: 22:1 我的神，我的神，你为什么弃绝我？为什么远离不救我，不听我唉哼的言语？ ###EN### My God, my God, why have You forsaken me? Why are You so far from saving me, From the words of my groaning?
Verse_Ch: 22:2 我的神阿，我白日呼求，你不应允；夜间呼求，也得不着安宁。 ###EN### O my God, I call out in the day, but You do not answer; And in the night, but there is no rest for me.
Verse_Ch: 22:3 但你是圣别的，是用以色列的赞美为宝座的。 ###EN### But You are holy, You who sit enthroned Upon the praises of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 22:4 我们的祖宗信靠你；他们信靠你，你便解救他们。 ###EN### In You our fathers trusted; They trusted and You rescued them.
Verse_Ch: 22:5 他们哀求你，便蒙解救；他们信靠你，就不羞愧。 ###EN### To You they cried out and were delivered; In You they trusted and were not put to shame.
Verse_Ch: 22:6 但我是虫，不是人，是众人所羞辱，百姓所藐视的。 ###EN### But I am a worm and not a man, A reproach of men and one despised by the people.
Verse_Ch: 22:7 凡看见我的都嗤笑我；他们撇嘴摇头，说， ###EN### All who see me deride me; They sneer at me; they shake their heads, saying,
Verse_Ch: 22:8 他把自己交托耶和华，耶和华可以救护他罢；耶和华既喜悦他，可以搭救他罢。 ###EN### He committed himself to Jehovah; let Him rescue him; Let Him deliver him since He takes pleasure in him.
Verse_Ch: 22:9 但你是叫我出母腹的；我在母怀里，你就使我有倚靠的心。 ###EN### But You are the One who drew me forth from the womb, Who made me trust while at my mother's breasts.
Verse_Ch: 22:10 我从母胎里就被交托给你；从我母腹中，你就是我的神。 ###EN### I was cast upon You from birth; From my mother's womb You have been my God.
Verse_Ch: 22:11 求你不要远离我，因为患难临近了，没有人帮助我。 ###EN### Do not be far from me, For trouble is near, For there is none to help me.
Verse_Ch: 22:12 有许多公牛围绕我；巴珊大力的公牛包围我。 ###EN### Many bulls surround me; The mighty bulls of Bashan encompass me.
Verse_Ch: 22:13 他们向我张口，好像抓撕吼叫的狮子。 ###EN### They open their mouth at me, Like a ravening and roaring lion.
Verse_Ch: 22:14 我如水被倒出来，我的骨头都脱了节。我的心如蜡，在我里面融化。 ###EN### I am poured out like water, And all my bones are out of joint. My heart is like wax; It is melted within me.
Verse_Ch: 22:15 我的精力枯干，如同瓦片，我的舌头贴在牙床上；你将我安置在死地的尘土中。 ###EN### My strength is dried up like a shard, And my tongue is stuck to my jaws; You have put me in the dust of death.
Verse_Ch: 22:16 犬类围着我；恶党环绕我；他们扎了我的手，我的脚。 ###EN### For dogs surround me; A company of evildoers encloses me; They pierce my hands and feet.
Verse_Ch: 22:17 我的骨头，我都能数算；他们瞪着眼看我。 ###EN### I count all my bones; They look, they stare at me.
Verse_Ch: 22:18 他们分了我的外衣，又为我的衣服拈阄。 ###EN### They divide my garments to themselves, And for my clothing they cast lots.
Verse_Ch: 22:19 耶和华阿，求你不要远离我；我的帮助阿，求你快来援助我。 ###EN### But You, O Jehovah, be not far off; O my help, hasten to aid me.
Verse_Ch: 22:20 求你救我的魂脱离刀剑，救我宝贵的生命脱离犬类的爪； ###EN### Deliver my soul from the sword, My precious life from the power of the dog;
Verse_Ch: 22:21 救我脱离狮子的口；求你应允我，使我脱离野牛的角。 ###EN### Save me from the mouth of the lion; Indeed while I am in the horns of wild oxen, answer me.
Verse_Ch: 22:22 我要向我的弟兄宣告你的名；在会中我要赞美你。 ###EN### I will declare Your name to my brothers; In the midst of the assembly I will praise You.
Verse_Ch: 22:23 你们敬畏耶和华的人，要赞美祂！你们雅各的后裔，都要荣耀祂！你们以色列的后裔，都要畏惧祂！ ###EN### You who fear Jehovah, praise Him! All you seed of Jacob, glorify Him! And stand in awe of Him, all you seed of Israel!
Verse_Ch: 22:24 因为祂没有轻看、厌恶受苦之人的苦难；也没有向他掩面；那受苦之人向祂呼求的时候，祂就垂听。 ###EN### For He has not despised nor detested The affliction of him who is afflicted; And He has not hidden His face from him; But when he cried out to Him, He heard.
Verse_Ch: 22:25 我在大会中赞美你的话，是从你而来的；我要在敬畏耶和华的人面前还我的愿。 ###EN### From You comes my praise in the great assembly; My vows will I pay before those who fear Him.
Verse_Ch: 22:26 卑微的人必吃得饱足；寻求耶和华的人必赞美祂－愿你们的心永远活着！ ###EN### The lowly will eat and be satisfied; Those who seek after Jehovah will praise Him-May your hearts live forever!
Verse_Ch: 22:27 地的四极都要想念耶和华，并且归向祂；列国的万族，都要在你面前敬拜。 ###EN### All the ends of the earth Will remember and return to Jehovah, And all families of the nations Will worship before You;
Verse_Ch: 22:28 因为国度是耶和华的，祂在列国中掌权。 ###EN### For the kingdom is Jehovah's, And He rules among the nations.
Verse_Ch: 22:29 地上一切丰肥的人，必吃喝而敬拜。凡下到尘土中不能存活自己性命的人，都要在祂面前下拜。 ###EN### All the flourishing of the earth Will eat and worship. All who go down into the dust will bow down before Him, Even he who does not keep his soul alive.
Verse_Ch: 22:30 必有后裔事奉祂；主的事必传述与后代。 ###EN### A seed will serve Him; That which concerns the Lord will be told to a coming generation.
Verse_Ch: 22:31 他们必来把祂的公义传给将要生的民，言明这是祂所行的。 ###EN### They will come and declare His righteousness To a people yet to be born, that He has done this.
Chapter_Header: 23
Verse_Ch: 23:1 耶和华是我的牧者；我必不至缺乏。 ###EN### Jehovah is my Shepherd; I will lack nothing.
Verse_Ch: 23:2 祂使我躺卧在青草地上，领我在可安歇的水边。 ###EN### He makes me lie down in green pastures; He leads me beside waters of rest.
Verse_Ch: 23:3 祂使我的魂苏醒，为自己的名引导我走义路。 ###EN### He restores my soul; He guides me on the paths of righteousness For His name's sake.
Verse_Ch: 23:4 我虽然行过死荫的幽谷，也不怕遭害，因为你与我同在；你的杖，你的竿，都安慰我。 ###EN### Even though I walk Through the valley of the shadow of death, I do not fear evil, For You are with me; Your rod and Your staff, They comfort me.
Verse_Ch: 23:5 在我敌人面前，你为我摆设筵席；你用油膏了我的头，使我的福杯满溢。 ###EN### You spread a table before me In the presence of my adversaries; You anoint my head with oil; My cup runs over.
Verse_Ch: 23:6 我一生一世必有恩惠慈爱随着我，我且要住在耶和华的殿中，直到永远。 ###EN### Surely goodness and lovingkindness will follow me All the days of my life, And I will dwell in the house of Jehovah For the length of my days.
Chapter_Header: 24
Verse_Ch: 24:1 地和其中所充满的，世界和住在其间的，都属耶和华。 ###EN### The earth is Jehovah's, and its fullness, The habitable land and those who dwell in it.
Verse_Ch: 24:2 祂把地奠定在海上，坚立在江河之上。 ###EN### For it is He who founded it upon the seas And established it upon the streams.
Verse_Ch: 24:3 谁能登耶和华的山，谁能站在祂的圣所？ ###EN### Who may ascend the mountain of Jehovah, And who may stand in His holy place?
Verse_Ch: 24:4 就是手洁心清，魂不仰慕虚妄，不诡诈起誓的人。 ###EN### He who has clean hands and a pure heart, Who has not lifted up his soul to falsehood Or sworn deceitfully.
Verse_Ch: 24:5 他必从耶和华得着祝福，又从救他的神得着公义。 ###EN### He will receive blessing from Jehovah, And righteousness from the God of his salvation.
Verse_Ch: 24:6 这是寻求耶和华的族类，是寻求你面的雅各。 细拉 ###EN### This is the generation of those who seek Him, Those who seek Your face, even Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 24:7 众城门哪，你们要抬起头来；永久的门户阿，你们要被举起；荣耀的王将要进来。 ###EN### Lift up your heads, O gates; And be lifted up, O long enduring doors; And the King of glory will come in.
Verse_Ch: 24:8 那荣耀的王是谁呢？就是刚强大能的耶和华，在争战中有大能的耶和华！ ###EN### Who is the King of glory? Jehovah strong and mighty! Jehovah mighty in battle!
Verse_Ch: 24:9 众城门哪，你们要抬起头来；永久的门户阿，你们要把头抬起；荣耀的王将要进来。 ###EN### Lift up your heads, O gates; And lift up, O long enduring doors; And the King of glory will come in.
Verse_Ch: 24:10 那荣耀的王是谁呢？万军之耶和华－祂是荣耀的王！ 细拉 ###EN### Who is this King of glory? Jehovah of hosts-He is the King of glory!
Chapter_Header: 25
Verse_Ch: 25:1 耶和华阿，我的魂仰望你。 ###EN### To You, O Jehovah, I lift up my soul.
Verse_Ch: 25:2 我的神阿，我素来信靠你；求你不要叫我羞愧；不要叫我的仇敌向我夸胜。 ###EN### O my God, I trust in You; Do not let me be ashamed; Do not let my enemies exult over me.
Verse_Ch: 25:3 凡等候你的必不羞愧；惟有那无故行奸诈的，必要羞愧。 ###EN### Indeed may all who wait on You not be ashamed; May those who deal treacherously without cause be ashamed.
Verse_Ch: 25:4 耶和华阿，求你将你的道路指示我，将你的路径教训我。 ###EN### Make Your ways known to me, O Jehovah; Teach me Your paths.
Verse_Ch: 25:5 求你以你的真理引导我，教训我；因为你是救我的神；我终日等候你。 ###EN### Guide me in Your truth, and teach me; For You are the God of my salvation; I wait on You all the day long.
Verse_Ch: 25:6 耶和华阿，求你记念你的怜恤和慈爱，因为这是亘古以来所常有的。 ###EN### Remember Your compassions, O Jehovah, And Your acts of kindness, for they are from of old.
Verse_Ch: 25:7 求你不要记念我幼年的罪行，和我的过犯；耶和华阿，求你因你的良善，按你的慈爱记念我。 ###EN### The sins of my youth and my transgressions, do not remember; According to Your lovingkindness, remember me, For the sake of Your goodness, O Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 25:8 耶和华是良善正直的；所以祂必指示罪人当行的路。 ###EN### Jehovah is good and upright; Therefore He instructs sinners concerning the way.
Verse_Ch: 25:9 祂必按公理引领卑微的人，将祂的道路教训他们。 ###EN### He guides the lowly in justice And teaches the lowly His way.
Verse_Ch: 25:10 对遵守祂的约和祂法度的人，耶和华所行的都是慈爱和真实。 ###EN### All the paths of Jehovah are lovingkindness and truth To those who observe His covenant and His testimonies.
Verse_Ch: 25:11 耶和华阿，求你因你的名赦免我的罪孽，因为我的罪孽重大。 ###EN### For the sake of Your name, O Jehovah, Pardon my iniquity, for it is great.
Verse_Ch: 25:12 谁是敬畏耶和华的人？耶和华必指示他当选择的道路。 ###EN### Who then is the man who fears Jehovah? Him will He instruct concerning the way that he should choose.
Verse_Ch: 25:13 他的魂必居住在福乐中；他的后裔必承受地土。 ###EN### His soul will dwell in prosperity, And his seed will possess the land.
Verse_Ch: 25:14 耶和华亲密的指教敬畏祂的人；祂必使他们得知祂的约。 ###EN### The intimate counsel of Jehovah is to those who fear Him, And His covenant will He make known to them.
Verse_Ch: 25:15 我的眼目时常仰望耶和华，因为祂必将我的脚从网里拉出来。 ###EN### My eyes are continually turned to Jehovah, For He will bring my feet out of the net.
Verse_Ch: 25:16 求你转向我，恩待我，因为我孤独困苦。 ###EN### Turn toward me, and be gracious to me, For I am alone and afflicted.
Verse_Ch: 25:17 求你解除我心里的愁苦，救我脱离我的祸患。 ###EN### Relieve the troubles of my heart, And bring me out of my distresses.
Verse_Ch: 25:18 求你看顾我的困苦和我的患难，赦免我一切的罪。 ###EN### Look on my affliction and my suffering, And forgive all my sins.
Verse_Ch: 25:19 求你察看我的仇敌，因为他们人多；并且他们凶暴的痛恨我。 ###EN### Look on my enemies, for they are many; Indeed they hate me with a violent hatred.
Verse_Ch: 25:20 求你保守我的性命，搭救我；不要让我羞愧，因为我投奔于你。 ###EN### Keep my soul, and deliver me; Do not let me be put to shame, For I take refuge in You.
Verse_Ch: 25:21 愿纯全正直保守我，因为我等候你。 ###EN### May integrity and uprightness preserve me, For I wait on You.
Verse_Ch: 25:22 神阿，求你救赎以色列脱离他一切的愁苦。 ###EN### Redeem Israel, O God, Out of all his troubles.
Chapter_Header: 26
Verse_Ch: 26:1 耶和华阿，求你为我伸冤，因我向来行事纯全，并且信靠耶和华；我必不摇动。 ###EN### Judge me, O Jehovah; For I have walked in my integrity, And in Jehovah I have trusted; I will not waver.
Verse_Ch: 26:2 耶和华阿，求你察看我，试验我，熬炼我的肺腑心肠。 ###EN### Examine me, O Jehovah, and try me; Test my inward parts and my heart.
Verse_Ch: 26:3 因为你的慈爱常在我眼前，我也按你的真理而行。 ###EN### For Your lovingkindness is before my eyes, And I have walked in Your truth.
Verse_Ch: 26:4 我没有和虚谎人同坐，也不与假冒为善的人往来。 ###EN### I do not sit with men of falsehood, Nor will I associate with hypocrites.
Verse_Ch: 26:5 我恨恶作恶之人的会，必不与恶人同坐。 ###EN### I hate the assembly of evildoers, Nor will I sit with the wicked.
Verse_Ch: 26:6 耶和华阿，我要洗手表明无辜，好环绕你的祭坛， ###EN### I wash my hands in innocence And go around Your altar, O Jehovah,
Verse_Ch: 26:7 发出称谢的声音，并述说你一切奇妙的作为。 ###EN### Making myself heard with the voice of thanksgiving And telling out all Your wonderful deeds.
Verse_Ch: 26:8 耶和华阿，我爱你所住的殿，和你的荣耀所居之处。 ###EN### O Jehovah, I love the habitation of Your house, And the place where Your glory abides.
Verse_Ch: 26:9 不要把我的魂和罪人一同除掉，也不要把我的性命和流人血的一同除掉。 ###EN### Do not gather my soul with sinners, Nor my life with men of bloodshed,
Verse_Ch: 26:10 他们的手中有恶计，右手满有贿赂。 ###EN### In whose hand is a wicked scheme, And whose right hand is full of bribes.
Verse_Ch: 26:11 至于我，我行事纯全；求你救赎我，恩待我。 ###EN### But as for me, I walk in my integrity; Redeem me and be gracious to me.
Verse_Ch: 26:12 我的脚站在平坦地方；在众会中我要颂赞耶和华。 ###EN### My foot stands on level ground; In the assemblies I will bless Jehovah.
Chapter_Header: 27
Verse_Ch: 27:1 耶和华是我的亮光，是我的拯救；我还怕谁呢？耶和华是我生命的力量；我还惧怕谁呢？ ###EN### Jehovah is my light and my salvation; Whom shall I fear? Jehovah is the strength of my life; Whom shall I dread?
Verse_Ch: 27:2 那作恶的，就是我的敌人，我的仇敌，他们前来吃我肉的时候，就绊跌仆倒。 ###EN### When evildoers come near me To devour my flesh, It is they, my adversaries and my enemies, Who stumble and fall.
Verse_Ch: 27:3 虽有军兵安营攻击我，我的心也不害怕；虽有争战兴起攻击我，我仍是安然。 ###EN### If an army camps against me, My heart does not fear; If a battle arises against me, In spite of this I am confident.
Verse_Ch: 27:4 有一件事，我曾求耶和华，我仍要寻求；就是一生一世住在耶和华的殿中，瞻仰祂的荣美，在祂的殿里求问。 ###EN### One thing I have asked from Jehovah; That do I seek: To dwell in the house of Jehovah All the days of my life, To behold the beauty of Jehovah, And to inquire in His temple.
Verse_Ch: 27:5 因为在我遭难的日子，祂必将我隐藏在祂的遮蔽处；祂必把我藏匿在祂帐幕的隐密处，将我高举在磐石上。 ###EN### For He will conceal me in His shelter In the day of trouble; He will hide me in the hiding place of His tent; He will raise me up upon a rock.
Verse_Ch: 27:6 现在我得以昂首，高过四围的仇敌。我要在祂的帐幕里献欢呼的祭；我要唱诗，歌颂耶和华。 ###EN### And now my head is lifted up Above my enemies who surround me. And I will offer in His tent Sacrifices of shouts of joy: I will sing and psalm to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 27:7 耶和华阿，我用声音呼吁的时候，求你垂听，并求你恩待我，应允我。 ###EN### Hear, O Jehovah, when I call with my voice, And be gracious to me and answer me.
Verse_Ch: 27:8 你说，你们当寻求我的面；那时我的心向你说，耶和华阿，你的面我正要寻求。 ###EN### When You say, Seek My face, To You my heart says, Your face, O Jehovah, will I seek.
Verse_Ch: 27:9 不要向我掩面；不要在怒中赶逐仆人；你向来是我的帮助。救我的神阿，不要丢弃我，也不要离弃我。 ###EN### Do not hide Your face from me; Do not turn Your servant away in Your anger; You have been my help. Do not abandon me or forsake me, O God of my salvation.
Verse_Ch: 27:10 我父母离弃我，耶和华必收留我。 ###EN### If my father and my mother forsake me, Jehovah will take me up.
Verse_Ch: 27:11 耶和华阿，求你将你的道路指教我，因那埋伏等候我者的缘故，引导我走平坦的途径。 ###EN### Teach me, O Jehovah, Your way, And lead me on a level path Because of those who lie in wait for me.
Verse_Ch: 27:12 求你不要把我交给敌人，遂其所愿；因为作假见证的，和口吐凶恶的，起来攻击我。 ###EN### Do not give me over To the desire of my adversaries; For false witnesses have risen up against me, And those who breathe out threats.
Verse_Ch: 27:13 我信我必在活人之地得见耶和华的美善。 ###EN### I have believed That I would see the goodness of Jehovah In the land of the living.
Verse_Ch: 27:14 要等候耶和华；当壮胆，坚固你的心；要等候耶和华。 ###EN### Wait for Jehovah; Be strong, and let your heart be encouraged. Yes, wait for Jehovah.
Chapter_Header: 28
Verse_Ch: 28:1 耶和华阿，我向你呼求；我的磐石阿，不要不听我；恐怕你向我闭口，我就如下到坑中的人一样。 ###EN### To You, O Jehovah, do I call out; My rock, do not be deaf to me, Lest, if You are silent to me, I become like those who go down into the pit.
Verse_Ch: 28:2 我呼求你，向你至圣所举手的时候，求你垂听我恳求的声音。 ###EN### Hear the voice of my supplications When I cry out to You, When I lift up my hands Unto Your innermost sanctuary.
Verse_Ch: 28:3 不要把我和恶人，并作孽的，一同拖去除掉；他们与邻舍说和平话，心里却是奸恶。 ###EN### Do not drag me away with the wicked And with the workers of iniquity, Who speak peace to their neighbors While evil is in their heart.
Verse_Ch: 28:4 愿你按着他们所作的，并他们所行的恶报应他们；愿你照着他们手所作的报应他们；愿你将他们所应得的报应加给他们。 ###EN### Repay them according to what they have done And according to the evil of their deeds; According to the work of their hands repay them; Return to them their due.
Verse_Ch: 28:5 他们既然不留心耶和华所行的，和祂手所作的，祂就必拆毁他们，不建立他们。 ###EN### For they do not regard the acts of Jehovah Or the work of His hands; He will tear them down And not rebuild them.
Verse_Ch: 28:6 耶和华是当受颂赞的，因为祂听了我恳求的声音。 ###EN### Blessed be Jehovah, For He has heard the voice of my supplications.
Verse_Ch: 28:7 耶和华是我的力量，是我的盾牌；我的心信靠祂，我就得帮助；所以我的心欢乐；我必用诗歌称谢祂。 ###EN### Jehovah is my strength and my shield; My heart trusts in Him, and I am helped; Therefore my heart exults; And with my song do I give thanks to Him.
Verse_Ch: 28:8 耶和华是祂百姓的力量，又是祂受膏者得救的保障。 ###EN### Jehovah is their strength; And He is a stronghold of salvation to His anointed.
Verse_Ch: 28:9 求你拯救你的百姓，赐福给你的产业，牧养他们，怀抱他们，直到永远。 ###EN### Save Your people, And bless Your inheritance; And shepherd them and carry them forever.
Chapter_Header: 29
Verse_Ch: 29:1 神的众子阿，你们要将荣耀能力归给耶和华，都归给耶和华； ###EN### Ascribe to Jehovah, O sons of the Mighty, Ascribe to Jehovah glory and strength;
Verse_Ch: 29:2 要将耶和华的名所当得的荣耀归给祂；当以圣别的妆饰敬拜耶和华。 ###EN### Ascribe to Jehovah the glory of His name; Worship Jehovah in holy splendor.
Verse_Ch: 29:3 耶和华的声音在众水之上；荣耀的神打雷，耶和华打雷在大水之上。 ###EN### The voice of Jehovah is over the waters; The God of glory thunders, Jehovah over the great waters.
Verse_Ch: 29:4 耶和华的声音大有能力；耶和华的声音满有威严。 ###EN### The voice of Jehovah is powerful; The voice of Jehovah is full of majesty.
Verse_Ch: 29:5 耶和华的声音震破香柏树；耶和华震碎利巴嫩的香柏树。 ###EN### The voice of Jehovah breaks the cedars; Indeed Jehovah breaks the cedars of Lebanon in pieces;
Verse_Ch: 29:6 祂使利巴嫩跳跃如牛犊，使西连跳跃如野牛犊。 ###EN### And He makes Lebanon skip like a calf, And Sirion like a young wild ox.
Verse_Ch: 29:7 耶和华的声音使火焰分岔。 ###EN### The voice of Jehovah cleaves out flames of fire.
Verse_Ch: 29:8 耶和华的声音震动旷野；耶和华震动加低斯的旷野。 ###EN### The voice of Jehovah shakes the wilderness; Jehovah shakes the wilderness of Kadesh.
Verse_Ch: 29:9 耶和华的声音使母鹿落胎，使林木落叶光秃；凡在祂殿中的都说，荣耀！ ###EN### The voice of Jehovah causes the hinds to calve And strips the forests bare; And in His temple all say, Glory!
Verse_Ch: 29:10 洪水泛滥之时，耶和华坐在宝座上；耶和华坐着为王，直到永远。 ###EN### Jehovah sat enthroned at the Flood, And Jehovah sits as King forever.
Verse_Ch: 29:11 愿耶和华赐力量给祂的百姓。愿耶和华赐平安的福给祂的百姓。 ###EN### May Jehovah give strength to His people. May Jehovah bless His people with peace.
Chapter_Header: 30
Verse_Ch: 30:1 耶和华阿，我要尊崇你，因为你曾救拔我，不让仇敌向我夸耀。 ###EN### I extol You, O Jehovah, for You have drawn me up And have not let my enemies rejoice over me.
Verse_Ch: 30:2 耶和华我的神阿，我曾呼求你，你医治了我。 ###EN### O Jehovah my God, I cried out to You, And You healed me.
Verse_Ch: 30:3 耶和华阿，你曾把我的魂从阴间提上来，使我存活，不至于下到坑中。 ###EN### O Jehovah, You have brought up my soul from Sheol; You have preserved me alive that I would not go down into the pit.
Verse_Ch: 30:4 耶和华的圣民哪，你们要歌颂祂，赞美祂可记念的圣名。 ###EN### Sing psalms to Jehovah, you who are His faithful ones; And praise His holy memorial.
Verse_Ch: 30:5 因为祂的怒气不过是转眼之间，祂的恩惠乃是一生之久；一宿虽然有哭泣，早晨便必欢呼。 ###EN### For His anger lasts but a moment, His favor, a lifetime; Weeping may linger in the evening, But a ringing shout goes up in the morning.
Verse_Ch: 30:6 至于我，我在平顺时曾说，我永不动摇。 ###EN### As for me, I said in my prosperity, I will never be shaken.
Verse_Ch: 30:7 耶和华阿，你曾施恩惠，叫我的山坚立。你掩了面，我就惊惶。 ###EN### O Jehovah, by Your favor You had made my mountain stand strong. You hid Your face; I was troubled.
Verse_Ch: 30:8 耶和华阿，我曾呼求你；我向耶和华恳求，说， ###EN### To You, O Jehovah, I called out; And to Jehovah I made my supplication.
Verse_Ch: 30:9 我被害流血，下到坑中，有什么益处呢？尘土岂能赞美你，传说你的信实么？ ###EN### What profit is there in my blood if I go down into the pit? Will the dust praise You? Will it declare Your faithfulness?
Verse_Ch: 30:10 耶和华阿，求你应允我，恩待我。耶和华阿，求你帮助我。 ###EN### Hear, O Jehovah, and be gracious to me. O Jehovah, be my help.
Verse_Ch: 30:11 你已将我的哀哭变为跳舞；你已将我的麻衣解下，用喜乐给我束腰， ###EN### You have turned for me my mourning into dancing; You have loosened my sackcloth And girded me with rejoicing,
Verse_Ch: 30:12 好叫我的灵歌颂你，并不住声。耶和华我的神阿，我要赞美你，直到永远。 ###EN### That my glory might sing psalms to You and not be silent. O Jehovah my God, I will praise You forever.
Chapter_Header: 31
Verse_Ch: 31:1 耶和华阿，我投靠你；求你使我永不羞愧。求你凭你的公义搭救我。 ###EN### In You, O Jehovah, do I take refuge; Never let me be put to shame. Rescue me in Your righteousness.
Verse_Ch: 31:2 求你向我侧耳，快快救我。求你作护卫我的磐石，作拯救我的山寨。 ###EN### Incline Your ear to me; Deliver me speedily. Be to me a rock of protection, A fortress, to save me.
Verse_Ch: 31:3 因为你是我的岩石，我的山寨；所以求你为你名的缘故，引导我，引领我。 ###EN### For You are my crag and my fortress; Therefore for Your name's sake Lead me and guide me.
Verse_Ch: 31:4 求你救我脱离人为我暗设的网罗，因为你是我的保障。 ###EN### Bring me out of the net That they have secretly laid for me, For You are my protection.
Verse_Ch: 31:5 我将我的灵交在你手里；耶和华真实的神阿，求你救赎我。 ###EN### Into Your hand I commit my spirit; Redeem me, O Jehovah, God of truth.
Verse_Ch: 31:6 我恨恶那尊奉虚无不实之神的人，但我信靠耶和华。 ###EN### I hate those who regard vanities of falsehood, But I trust in Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 31:7 我要因你的慈爱欢腾喜乐，因为你已经看见我的困苦，知道我魂中的艰难。 ###EN### I will exult and rejoice in Your lovingkindness, Since You have seen my affliction; You know the distress of my soul.
Verse_Ch: 31:8 你未曾把我交在仇敌手里；你使我的脚站在宽阔之处。 ###EN### And You have not delivered me into the hand of the enemy; You have made my feet stand in a place broad and free.
Verse_Ch: 31:9 耶和华阿，求你恩待我，因为我在急难之中。我的眼睛因忧愁而干瘪，连我的魂与身子，也都衰残。 ###EN### Be gracious to me, O Jehovah, for I am in distress. My eye is wasted away with grief, Indeed my soul and body.
Verse_Ch: 31:10 我的生命在愁苦中耗尽，我的年岁在叹息里旷废。我的力量因我的罪孽衰败，我的骨头也枯干。 ###EN### For my life has been consumed in sorrow, And my years, in sighing. My strength fails because of my iniquity, And my bones have wasted away.
Verse_Ch: 31:11 我因一切敌人成了凌辱的对象，在邻舍跟前更是这样；那认识我的都惧怕我；在街上看见我的都躲避我。 ###EN### Because of all my adversaries, I have become a reproach, And especially so to my neighbors, And something dreaded to my acquaintances; Those who see me on the street flee from me.
Verse_Ch: 31:12 我被忘记，如同死人，无人思念；我好像毁坏的器皿。 ###EN### I am forgotten, like a dead man out of mind; I am like a destroyed vessel.
Verse_Ch: 31:13 我听见了许多人的谗谤；四围都是惊吓。他们一同商议攻击我的时候，就图谋要害我的性命。 ###EN### For I hear the slander of many; Terror is on every side. When they take counsel together against me, They scheme to take my life.
Verse_Ch: 31:14 耶和华阿，我仍旧信靠你；我说，你是我的神。 ###EN### But I trust in You, O Jehovah; I say, You are my God.
Verse_Ch: 31:15 我一生的事在你手中；求你救我脱离仇敌的手，和那些追逼我的人。 ###EN### My times are in Your hand; Deliver me from the hand of my enemies and from those who pursue me.
Verse_Ch: 31:16 求你使你的脸光照仆人，凭你的慈爱拯救我。 ###EN### Cause Your face to shine upon Your servant; Save me in Your lovingkindness.
Verse_Ch: 31:17 耶和华阿，我呼求你的时候，求你叫我不至羞愧；求你使恶人羞愧，使他们在阴间静默无声。 ###EN### O Jehovah, do not let me be put to shame when I call out to You; Let the wicked be put to shame; let them be silent in Sheol.
Verse_Ch: 31:18 那逞骄傲轻慢，出狂妄的话攻击义人的，愿他虚妄的嘴哑而无言。 ###EN### Let the lips of falsehood be made dumb, Which speak arrogantly against the righteous With pride and contempt.
Verse_Ch: 31:19 你的美善，就是你为敬畏你的人所积存的，并你为投靠你的人，在世人面前所施行的，是何等大呢！ ###EN### How great is Your goodness, Which You have stored up for those who fear You, Which You have accomplished in the sight of the sons of men For those who take refuge in You!
Verse_Ch: 31:20 你必把他们藏在你面前的隐密处，免得遇见人的计谋；你必将他们隐藏在遮蔽处，免受口舌的争闹。 ###EN### You hide them in the hiding place of Your presence Apart from the conspiracies of men; You lay them away secretly in a shelter Apart from the contention of tongues.
Verse_Ch: 31:21 耶和华是当受颂赞的，因为祂在坚固城里，奇妙的向我施展祂的慈爱。 ###EN### Blessed be Jehovah, For He displayed His lovingkindness wondrously To me in a fortified city.
Verse_Ch: 31:22 至于我，我曾惊惶的说，我从你眼前被隔绝；然而，我呼求你的时候，你仍听我恳求的声音。 ###EN### I, on my part, had said in my alarm, I am cut off before Your eyes; But instead You heard The voice of my supplications When I cried out to You.
Verse_Ch: 31:23 耶和华的圣民哪，你们都要爱祂；耶和华护卫忠信的人，足足报应行事骄傲的人。 ###EN### Love Jehovah, all you who are His faithful ones; Jehovah guards the trustworthy, And recompenses abundantly Him who acts haughtily.
Verse_Ch: 31:24 凡仰望耶和华的人，你们都要壮胆，坚固你们的心。 ###EN### Be strong, and let your heart be encouraged, All you who hope in Jehovah.
Chapter_Header: 32
Verse_Ch: 32:1 得赦免其过，遮盖其罪的，这人是有福的。 ###EN### Blessed is he whose transgression is forgiven; Whose sin is covered.
Verse_Ch: 32:2 耶和华不算为有罪孽，灵里没有诡诈的，这人是有福的。 ###EN### Blessed is the man to whom Jehovah does not impute iniquity And in whose spirit there is no deceit.
Verse_Ch: 32:3 我闭口不认罪的时候，因终日唉哼，而骨头枯干。 ###EN### When I kept silent, my bones wasted away Through my groaning all day long.
Verse_Ch: 32:4 白日黑夜，你的手在我身上沉重；我的精液耗尽，如在夏天的干旱中。 细拉 ###EN### For day and night Your hand Was heavy upon me; My life sap was dried up As in the drought of summer.
Verse_Ch: 32:5 我向你陈明我的罪，不遮瞒我的罪孽。我说，我要向耶和华承认我的过犯；你就赦免我的罪孽。 细拉 ###EN### I acknowledged my sin to You, And I did not cover my iniquity. I said, I will confess my transgressions to Jehovah. Then You forgave the iniquity of my sin.
Verse_Ch: 32:6 为此，凡虔诚人都当趁你可寻到的时候祷告你；大水泛溢的时候，必不能临及他。 ###EN### Because of this let everyone who is faithful Pray to You at a time when You may be found; Surely when great waters overflow, They will not reach him.
Verse_Ch: 32:7 你是我藏身之处；你必保守我脱离患难，以得救的欢呼四面环绕我。 细拉 ###EN### You are my hiding place; You preserve me from trouble; You surround me with the ringing shouts of deliverance.
Verse_Ch: 32:8 我要教导你，指示你当行的路；我要劝戒你，定睛在你身上。 ###EN### I will instruct you and teach you concerning the way you should go; I will counsel you; my eye is upon you.
Verse_Ch: 32:9 你不可像那无知的骡马，必用嚼环辔头勒住；不然，就不能驯服。 ###EN### Do not be like a horse or like a mule, without understanding; Whose trappings consist of bit and bridle to restrain them, Else they do not come near you.
Verse_Ch: 32:10 恶人必多受苦楚；惟独信靠耶和华的，必有慈爱四面环绕他。 ###EN### Many are the sorrows that the wicked have; But he who trusts in Jehovah is encompassed by lovingkindness.
Verse_Ch: 32:11 你们义人应当因耶和华喜乐欢腾；你们心里正直的人，都当欢呼。 ###EN### Rejoice in Jehovah and exult, O righteous ones; And give a ringing shout, all you who are upright in heart.
Chapter_Header: 33
Verse_Ch: 33:1 义人哪，你们应当因耶和华欢呼；正直人的赞美是合宜的。 ###EN### Rejoice in Jehovah, O righteous ones. Praise is becoming to the upright.
Verse_Ch: 33:2 你们应当弹琴称谢耶和华，用十弦瑟歌颂祂。 ###EN### Give thanks to Jehovah with the lyre; With the harp of ten strings sing psalms to Him.
Verse_Ch: 33:3 应当向祂唱新歌；弹得巧妙，加上欢呼。 ###EN### Sing Him a new song; Play skillfully with a joyous shout.
Verse_Ch: 33:4 因为耶和华的言语正直；凡祂所作的，尽都信实。 ###EN### For the word of Jehovah is right, And all His work is done in faithfulness.
Verse_Ch: 33:5 祂喜爱公义和公平；遍地满了耶和华的慈爱。 ###EN### He loves righteousness and justice; The earth is full of the lovingkindness of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 33:6 诸天藉耶和华的话而造，万象藉祂口中的气而成。 ###EN### By the word of Jehovah the heavens were made, And all their host, by the breath of His mouth.
Verse_Ch: 33:7 祂聚集海水如垒，把深洋安放在库房。 ###EN### He gathers the water of the sea like a heap; He puts the deep waters into storage places.
Verse_Ch: 33:8 愿全地都敬畏耶和华；愿世上的居民都畏惧祂。 ###EN### Let all the earth fear Jehovah; Let all the inhabitants of the world stand in awe of Him.
Verse_Ch: 33:9 因为祂说有，就有；命立，就立。 ###EN### For He spoke, and it was; He commanded, and it stood.
Verse_Ch: 33:10 耶和华使列国的筹算归于无有，使众民所打算的无有功效。 ###EN### Jehovah brings the counsel of the nations to nothing; He frustrates the intentions of the peoples.
Verse_Ch: 33:11 耶和华的筹算永远立定，祂心中所打算的万代常存。 ###EN### The counsel of Jehovah stands forever; The intentions of His heart stand from generation to generation.
Verse_Ch: 33:12 以耶和华为神的，那国是有福的；祂所拣选为自己产业的，那民是有福的。 ###EN### Blessed is the nation whose God is Jehovah, The people whom He has chosen as His own possession.
Verse_Ch: 33:13 耶和华从天上观看；祂看见一切的世人。 ###EN### Jehovah looks from heaven; He sees all the sons of men.
Verse_Ch: 33:14 祂从祂的居所，察看地上一切的居民； ###EN### From the site of His habitation He gazes At all the inhabitants of the earth,
Verse_Ch: 33:15 祂是那塑造他们众人心的，洞悉他们一切作为的。 ###EN### He who fashions the hearts of them all, He who discerns all their works.
Verse_Ch: 33:16 君王不能因兵多得胜；勇士不能因力大得救。 ###EN### No king is saved by a great army; A mighty man is not delivered by great strength.
Verse_Ch: 33:17 靠马得救是枉然的；马也不能因力大救人。 ###EN### A horse is a vain thing for salvation, And it cannot deliver by its great power.
Verse_Ch: 33:18 看哪，耶和华的眼目，看顾敬畏祂的人，和仰望祂慈爱的人， ###EN### Behold, the eye of Jehovah is upon those who fear Him, Upon those who hope in His lovingkindness,
Verse_Ch: 33:19 要救他们的性命脱离死亡，并使他们在饥荒中存活。 ###EN### To deliver their soul from death And to preserve them alive in famine.
Verse_Ch: 33:20 我们的魂向来等候耶和华；祂是我们的帮助，我们的盾牌。 ###EN### Our soul waits on Jehovah; He is our help and our shield;
Verse_Ch: 33:21 我们的心必因祂喜乐，因为我们向来信靠祂的圣名。 ###EN### For in Him our heart rejoices, Because in His holy name we trust.
Verse_Ch: 33:22 耶和华阿，求你照着我们所仰望你的，向我们施慈爱。 ###EN### May Your lovingkindness, O Jehovah, be upon us, Even as we have hoped in You.
Chapter_Header: 34
Verse_Ch: 34:1 我要时时颂赞耶和华；赞美祂的话必常在我口中。 ###EN### I will bless Jehovah at all times; His praise will continually be in my mouth.
Verse_Ch: 34:2 我的魂必因耶和华夸耀；卑微的人听见，就要喜乐。 ###EN### My soul makes its boast in Jehovah; The lowly hear and they rejoice.
Verse_Ch: 34:3 你们要和我一同尊耶和华为大，一同高举祂的名。 ###EN### Magnify Jehovah with me, And let us exalt His name together.
Verse_Ch: 34:4 我曾寻求耶和华，祂就应允我，救我脱离一切使我恐惧的。 ###EN### I sought Jehovah, and He answered me; And He delivered me from all that terrified me.
Verse_Ch: 34:5 人仰望祂，便有光荣；他们的脸必不蒙羞。 ###EN### They looked to Him and were radiant; And their faces will never be abashed.
Verse_Ch: 34:6 我这穷苦人呼求，耶和华便垂听，救我脱离一切患难。 ###EN### This poor man called out, and Jehovah heard; And He saved him out of all his troubles.
Verse_Ch: 34:7 耶和华的使者，在敬畏祂的人四围安营，搭救他们。 ###EN### The angel of Jehovah encamps Around those who fear Him, and He delivers them.
Verse_Ch: 34:8 你们要尝尝，便知道耶和华是美善的；投奔于祂的人有福了。 ###EN### Taste and see that Jehovah is good; Blessed is the man who takes refuge in Him.
Verse_Ch: 34:9 耶和华的圣民哪，你们当敬畏祂，因敬畏祂的一无所缺。 ###EN### Fear Jehovah, you who are His saints; For there is no lack with those who fear Him.
Verse_Ch: 34:10 少壮狮子，还缺食忍饿；但寻求耶和华的，什么好处都不缺。 ###EN### The young lions hunger and starve, But those who seek Jehovah will not lack any good thing.
Verse_Ch: 34:11 孩子们，你们当来听我的话；我要教导你们敬畏耶和华。 ###EN### Come, children; hear me. I will teach you the fear of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 34:12 谁是那喜爱生命，爱慕长寿，要享美福的人？ ###EN### Who is the man who desires life, Who loves having days in order to see good?
Verse_Ch: 34:13 你要禁止舌头不出恶言，嘴唇不说诡诈的话。 ###EN### Guard your tongue from evil, And your lips from speaking deceit.
Verse_Ch: 34:14 要离恶行善，寻求和睦，一心追赶。 ###EN### Turn away from evil and do good; Seek peace and pursue it.
Verse_Ch: 34:15 耶和华的眼目看顾义人，祂的耳朵听他们的呼求。 ###EN### The eyes of Jehovah are set toward the righteous, And His ears, toward their cry.
Verse_Ch: 34:16 耶和华向行恶的人变脸，要从地上剪除他们的名号。 ###EN### The face of Jehovah is against those who do evil, To cut off the memory of them from the earth.
Verse_Ch: 34:17 义人呼求，耶和华听见了，便救他们脱离一切患难。 ###EN### The righteous cry out, and Jehovah hears; And He saves them out of all their troubles.
Verse_Ch: 34:18 耶和华靠近伤心的人，拯救灵里痛悔的人。 ###EN### Jehovah is near to those who are broken in heart, And He saves those who are contrite in spirit.
Verse_Ch: 34:19 义人多有患难，但耶和华救他脱离这一切； ###EN### Many are the troubles of the righteous man, But Jehovah delivers him from all of them.
Verse_Ch: 34:20 又保全他一身的骨头，连一根也不折断。 ###EN### He keeps all his bones; Not one of them is broken.
Verse_Ch: 34:21 恶必害死恶人；恨恶义人的，必被定罪。 ###EN### Evil will slay the wicked, And those who hate the righteous man will be condemned.
Verse_Ch: 34:22 耶和华救赎祂仆人的魂；凡投奔于祂的，必不至定罪。 ###EN### Jehovah redeems the soul of His servants, And none who take refuge in Him will be condemned.
Chapter_Header: 35
Verse_Ch: 35:1 耶和华阿，与我相争的，求你与他们相争；与我相战的，求你与他们相战。 ###EN### Strive, O Jehovah, with those who strive with me; Battle against those who battle against me.
Verse_Ch: 35:2 求你拿着大小的盾牌，起来帮助我； ###EN### Take hold of buckler and shield, And rise up as my help.
Verse_Ch: 35:3 抽出枪来，挡住那追赶我的；求你对我的魂说：我是你的拯救。 ###EN### Draw out also the spear, and close up the way Against those who pursue me; Say to my soul, I am your salvation.
Verse_Ch: 35:4 愿那寻索我命的，蒙羞受辱；愿那谋害我的，退后羞愧。 ###EN### Let those who seek my life Be put to shame and humiliated; Let those who devise evil for me Be turned back and confounded.
Verse_Ch: 35:5 愿他们像风前的糠秕，有耶和华的使者赶逐他们。 ###EN### Let them be like chaff before the wind, With the angel of Jehovah driving them on.
Verse_Ch: 35:6 愿他们的道路，又暗又滑，有耶和华的使者追赶他们。 ###EN### Let their way be darkness and slipperiness itself, With the angel of Jehovah pursuing them.
Verse_Ch: 35:7 因他们无故的为我暗设网罗；无故的挖坑要害我的命。 ###EN### For without cause they hid their net for me; Without cause they dug a pit for me.
Verse_Ch: 35:8 愿毁灭不知不觉间临到他身上；愿他暗设的网缠住自己；愿他落在其中灭没。 ###EN### Let destruction come upon him unawares, And let his net, which he hid, catch him; Let him fall into it, into destruction.
Verse_Ch: 35:9 我的魂就必因耶和华欢腾，因祂的救恩欢喜。 ###EN### Then my soul will exult in Jehovah; It will rejoice in His salvation.
Verse_Ch: 35:10 我的骨头都要说，耶和华阿，谁能像你救护穷苦人，脱离那比他强壮的，救护困苦穷乏人，脱离那抢夺他的？ ###EN### All my bones will say, Jehovah, who is like You, Who delivers the poor from him who is too strong for him, And the poor and needy from him who robs him?
Verse_Ch: 35:11 恶毒的见证人起来，盘问我所不知道的事。 ###EN### Malicious witnesses rise up; They ask me about things I know nothing of.
Verse_Ch: 35:12 他们向我以恶报善，使我的魂孤苦。 ###EN### They repay me evil for good; I am bereaved in soul.
Verse_Ch: 35:13 至于我，当他们有病的时候，我便穿麻衣，禁食刻苦己心；我的祷告回到自己的怀中。 ###EN### But I, when they were sick, Had sackcloth as my clothing; I afflicted my soul with fasting, And my prayer returned to my own bosom.
Verse_Ch: 35:14 我这样行，好像他是我的朋友，我的弟兄；我悲哀屈身，如同人为母亲哀痛。 ###EN### I conducted myself as if it had been my friend or my brother; Like one mourning for his mother, I bowed down gloomily.
Verse_Ch: 35:15 但我跌倒了，他们却欢喜，大家聚集；我所不认识的那些毁谤者，聚集攻击我；他们不住的把我撕裂。 ###EN### But at my stumbling they rejoice and gather together; The attackers, whom I did not know Gather together against me; They tear at me and do not cease.
Verse_Ch: 35:16 他们如同不虔敬、好讥诮的阿谀之人，向我咬牙切齿。 ###EN### As profane mocking parasites, They gnash their teeth at me.
Verse_Ch: 35:17 主阿，你看着不理，要到几时呢？求你救我的魂脱离他们的残害，救我宝贵的生命脱离少壮狮子。 ###EN### O Lord, how long will You look on? Rescue my soul from their destruction, My precious life from the lions.
Verse_Ch: 35:18 我要在大会中称谢你，在强大的民中赞美你。 ###EN### I will give You thanks in the great congregation; Among a mighty people I will praise You.
Verse_Ch: 35:19 求你不让那无理与我为仇的，向我夸耀；不让那无故恨我的，向我挤眼。 ###EN### Do not let those who are wrongly my enemies rejoice over me; Do not let those who hate me without cause narrow their eyes at me.
Verse_Ch: 35:20 因为他们不说和平话，倒设想诡诈的言语，害地上的安静人。 ###EN### For they do not speak peace, But devise words of deceit Against the quiet people of the land.
Verse_Ch: 35:21 他们大大张口攻击我，说，阿哈！阿哈！我们的眼已经看见了。 ###EN### And they open their mouth wide against me; They say, Aha! Aha! Our eyes have seen it.
Verse_Ch: 35:22 耶和华阿，你已经看见了；求你不要闭口。主阿，求你不要远离我。 ###EN### You have seen, O Jehovah; do not be silent. O Lord, do not be far from me.
Verse_Ch: 35:23 我的神我的主阿，求你奋兴醒起，判清我的事，伸明我的冤。 ###EN### Awake, and stir Yourself for my cause, For my claim, O my God and my Lord.
Verse_Ch: 35:24 耶和华我的神阿，求你按你的公义为我伸冤，不让他们向我夸耀。 ###EN### Vindicate me according to Your righteousness, O Jehovah my God; And do not let them rejoice over me.
Verse_Ch: 35:25 不让他们心里说，阿哈！遂我们的心愿了；不让他们说，我们已经把他吞了。 ###EN### Do not let them say in their heart, Aha! That is what we wanted. Do not let them say, We have swallowed him up.
Verse_Ch: 35:26 愿那喜欢我遭难的，一同抱愧蒙羞；愿那向我妄自尊大的，披惭愧，蒙羞辱。 ###EN### May those who rejoice at my trouble Be ashamed and confounded together; May those who magnify themselves against me Be clothed with shame and humiliation.
Verse_Ch: 35:27 愿那喜悦我公义得表白的，欢呼喜乐；愿他们常说，当尊耶和华为大，祂喜悦祂的仆人安好。 ###EN### May those who delight in the vindication of my righteousness Give a ringing shout and rejoice, And may they say continually, Jehovah be magnified, Who delights in the well-being of His servant.
Verse_Ch: 35:28 我的舌头要终日论说你的公义，并且赞美你。 ###EN### And my tongue will declare Your righteousness And Your praise all day long.
Chapter_Header: 36
Verse_Ch: 36:1 恶人的罪过在他心里说话；他眼中不怕神。 ###EN### Transgression speaks to the wicked Within his heart; There is no dread of God Before his eyes.
Verse_Ch: 36:2 他谄媚自己，在他看来，他的罪孽不会被查出、被恨恶。 ###EN### For he flatters himself in his own eyes, That his iniquity cannot be found out and hated.
Verse_Ch: 36:3 他口中的言语，尽是奸恶诡诈；他不再明智，不再行美善的事。 ###EN### The words of his mouth are wickedness and deceit; He has ceased being wise and doing good.
Verse_Ch: 36:4 他在床上图谋奸恶，站立在不善的道路上，不弃绝恶事。 ###EN### He plans wickedness on his bed; He sets himself on a way that is not good; He does not reject evil.
Verse_Ch: 36:5 耶和华阿，你的慈爱，及于诸天；你的信实，达到穹苍。 ###EN### O Jehovah, Your lovingkindness is in the heavens; Your faithfulness reaches unto the skies.
Verse_Ch: 36:6 你的公义，好像神的众山；你的判断，如同深渊；耶和华阿，人和牲畜，你都救护。 ###EN### Your righteousness is like the mountains of God; Your judgments are like the great deep; You preserve man and beast, O Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 36:7 神阿，你的慈爱，何其宝贵！世人投靠在你翅膀的荫下。 ###EN### How precious is Your lovingkindness, O God! Thus the sons of men take refuge in the shadow of Your wings.
Verse_Ch: 36:8 他们必因你殿里的肥甘得以饱足，你也必叫他们喝你乐河的水。 ###EN### They are saturated with the fatness of Your house, And You cause them to drink of the river of Your pleasures.
Verse_Ch: 36:9 因为在你那里，有生命的源头；在你的光中，我们必得见光。 ###EN### For with You is the fountain of life; In Your light we see light.
Verse_Ch: 36:10 愿你不断施慈爱给认识你的人，以公义待心里正直的人。 ###EN### Continue Your lovingkindness to those who know You, And Your righteousness to those who are upright in heart.
Verse_Ch: 36:11 不要让骄傲人的脚践踏我，也不要让凶恶人的手赶逐我。 ###EN### Do not let the foot of the arrogant come upon me, Nor let the hand of the wicked drive me away.
Verse_Ch: 36:12 在那里，作孽的人已经仆倒；他们被推倒，不能再起来。 ###EN### There the workers of iniquity are fallen; They are cast down and unable to rise.
Chapter_Header: 37
Verse_Ch: 37:1 不要因作恶的，忿忿不平，也不要嫉妒那行不义的。 ###EN### Do not be incensed because of evildoers; Do not be envious of wrongdoers.
Verse_Ch: 37:2 因为他们如草快要枯萎，又如青菜快要枯干。 ###EN### For they soon wither like grass And fade away like green herbage.
Verse_Ch: 37:3 你当信靠耶和华而行善；住在地上，以祂的信实为粮。 ###EN### Trust in Jehovah, and do good; Dwell in the land, and feed on His faithfulness.
Verse_Ch: 37:4 你要以耶和华为乐，祂就将你心里所求的赐给你。 ###EN### Delight yourself in Jehovah, And He will give you the requests of your heart.
Verse_Ch: 37:5 当将你的事交托耶和华，并信靠祂，祂就必成全。 ###EN### Commit your way to Jehovah, And trust in Him; and He will act.
Verse_Ch: 37:6 祂要使你的公义如光发出，使你的公平明如正午。 ###EN### And He will cause your righteousness to go forth like light, And your justness like noonday.
Verse_Ch: 37:7 你当在耶和华面前静默，耐心等候祂；不要因那道路亨通的，和那恶谋成就的，忿忿不平。 ###EN### Be still before Jehovah, and wait for Him; Do not be incensed because of him who enjoys prosperity on his way, Because of the man who performs his evil schemes.
Verse_Ch: 37:8 当止住怒气，离弃忿怒；不要忿忿不平，以致作恶。 ###EN### Cease from anger and forsake wrath; Do not be incensed; it leads only to evil.
Verse_Ch: 37:9 因为作恶的，必被剪除；惟有等候耶和华的，必承受地土。 ###EN### For the evildoers will be cut off; But those who wait on Jehovah, They will inherit the land.
Verse_Ch: 37:10 还有片时，恶人要归于无有；你就是细察他的地方，他也不在了。 ###EN### And in a little while longer there will be no wicked man; Indeed, you will look diligently for his place, and he will not be there.
Verse_Ch: 37:11 但卑微的人必承受地土，以丰盛的平安为乐。 ###EN### But the lowly will inherit the land And delight themselves in the abundance of peace.
Verse_Ch: 37:12 恶人设谋害义人，又向他咬牙。 ###EN### The wicked man makes evil schemes against the righteous man And gnashes his teeth at him.
Verse_Ch: 37:13 主要笑他，因见他受罚的日子将要来到。 ###EN### The Lord will laugh at him, For He sees that his day will come.
Verse_Ch: 37:14 恶人已经拔刀拉弓，要打倒困苦穷乏的人，要杀戮道路正直的人。 ###EN### The wicked have drawn out the sword And bent their bow, To cast the poor and the needy down, To slaughter those who are upright in their way.
Verse_Ch: 37:15 他们的刀必刺入自己的心，他们的弓必被折断。 ###EN### Their sword will enter their own heart, And their bows will be broken.
Verse_Ch: 37:16 一个义人所有的虽少，胜过许多恶人的富余。 ###EN### Better is the little that the righteous man has Than the abundance of many wicked.
Verse_Ch: 37:17 因为恶人的膀臂必被折断，但耶和华扶持义人。 ###EN### For the arms of the wicked will be broken, But Jehovah upholds the righteous.
Verse_Ch: 37:18 耶和华知道完全人的日子，他们的产业要存到永远。 ###EN### Jehovah knows the days of the perfect, And their inheritance will be forever.
Verse_Ch: 37:19 他们在患难的时候不至羞愧，在饥荒的日子必得饱足。 ###EN### They will not be put to shame in a time of evil, And in the days of famine they will be satisfied.
Verse_Ch: 37:20 恶人却要灭亡，耶和华的仇敌要像草地的华美：他们要消灭，要如烟消灭。 ###EN### But the wicked will perish, And the enemies of Jehovah will be like the glory of the pastures: They are consumed; in smoke they are consumed.
Verse_Ch: 37:21 恶人借贷而不偿还，义人却恩待人，并且施舍。 ###EN### The wicked borrow but do not repay, But the righteous is gracious and gives.
Verse_Ch: 37:22 蒙耶和华赐福的，必承受地土，被祂咒诅的，必被剪除。 ###EN### For those blessed by Him will inherit the land, But those cursed by Him will be cut off.
Verse_Ch: 37:23 义人的脚步被耶和华立定，他的道路，耶和华也喜爱。 ###EN### A man's steps are established by Jehovah, And He delights in his way.
Verse_Ch: 37:24 他虽失脚，也不至全身仆倒；因为耶和华搀扶他的手。 ###EN### If he falls, he is not utterly cast down; For Jehovah upholds him by the hand.
Verse_Ch: 37:25 我从前年幼，现在年老，却未见过义人被弃，也未见过他的后裔讨饭。 ###EN### I was once a young man; now I am old. Yet I have not seen the righteous man forsaken, Nor his seed seeking bread.
Verse_Ch: 37:26 他终日恩待人，借给人；他的后裔也蒙福。 ###EN### He is always gracious and lends, And his seed becomes a blessing.
