Verse_Ch: 37:27 你当离恶行善，就可永远安居。 ###EN### Turn away from evil and do good, And abide forever.
Verse_Ch: 37:28 因为耶和华喜爱公平，不撇弃祂的圣民；他们永蒙保守；但恶人的后裔必被剪除。 ###EN### For Jehovah loves justice And does not abandon His faithful ones; They are kept forever; But the seed of the wicked is cut off.
Verse_Ch: 37:29 义人必承受地土，永居其上。 ###EN### The righteous will inherit the land, And they will abide in it forever.
Verse_Ch: 37:30 义人的口吐露智慧，他的舌头讲说公平。 ###EN### The mouth of the righteous utters wisdom, And his tongue speaks justice.
Verse_Ch: 37:31 神的律法在他心里；他的脚步必不滑跌。 ###EN### The law of his God is in his heart; His steps do not slip.
Verse_Ch: 37:32 恶人窥探义人，想要杀他。 ###EN### The wicked man watches for the righteous man And seeks to slay him.
Verse_Ch: 37:33 耶和华必不撇他在恶人手中，当他受审判的时候，也不定他的罪。 ###EN### Jehovah does not leave him in his hand, Nor let him be condemned when he is judged.
Verse_Ch: 37:34 你当等候耶和华，谨守祂的道路，祂就抬举你，使你承受地土；恶人被剪除的时候，你必看见。 ###EN### Wait for Jehovah, And keep His way; And He will exalt you to inherit the land; When the wicked are cut off, you will see it.
Verse_Ch: 37:35 我见过恶人强横可怕，好像青翠树在本土生长茂盛。 ###EN### I have seen the wicked man terrorizing, And spreading himself like a luxuriant native tree.
Verse_Ch: 37:36 有人从那里经过，不料，他不在了；我寻找他，却寻不着。 ###EN### Then someone passes by, and behold, he is not there; I search for him, and he is not found.
Verse_Ch: 37:37 你要细察完全人，观看正直人；因为和平人有好结局。 ###EN### Observe the perfect man, and watch the upright man; For there is a future for the man of peace.
Verse_Ch: 37:38 至于有过犯的人，必全然灭绝；恶人终必被剪除。 ###EN### But the transgressors will be altogether destroyed; The future of the wicked will be cut off.
Verse_Ch: 37:39 但义人蒙拯救，是出于耶和华；祂在患难时作他们的保障。 ###EN### And the salvation of the righteous is from Jehovah; He is their stronghold in a time of distress.
Verse_Ch: 37:40 耶和华帮助他们，解救他们；祂解救他们脱离恶人，把他们救出来，因为他们投靠祂。 ###EN### And Jehovah helps them and rescues them; He rescues them from the wicked, And saves them, for they take refuge in Him.
Chapter_Header: 38
Verse_Ch: 38:1 耶和华阿，求你不要在怒中责备我，不要在烈怒中惩治我。 ###EN### O Jehovah, do not rebuke me in Your indignation, Nor chasten me in Your burning wrath.
Verse_Ch: 38:2 因为你的箭射入我身，你的手压住我。 ###EN### For Your arrows have sunk deep in me, And Your hand has come down heavy upon me.
Verse_Ch: 38:3 因你的恼怒，我的肉无一完全；因我的罪，我的骨头无一健全。 ###EN### There is no soundness in my flesh due to Your indignation; There is no wholeness in my bones due to my sin.
Verse_Ch: 38:4 我的罪孽高过我的头，如同重担叫我担当不起。 ###EN### For my iniquities have passed over my head; Like a heavy burden, they are too heavy for me.
Verse_Ch: 38:5 因我的愚昧，我的伤口发臭流脓。 ###EN### My wounds are odious and festering Due to my foolishness.
Verse_Ch: 38:6 我屈身弯腰，弯到极低，终日徘徊哀痛。 ###EN### I am bent down and bowed utterly; I go about all day long mourning.
Verse_Ch: 38:7 我满腰灼痛，我的肉无一完全。 ###EN### For my loins are filled with burning, And there is no soundness in my flesh.
Verse_Ch: 38:8 我被压伤，身体麻木；因心里叹息，我就呼喊。 ###EN### I am benumbed and crushed utterly; I cry out due to the groaning of my heart.
Verse_Ch: 38:9 主阿，我的心愿都在你面前，我的叹息不向你隐瞒。 ###EN### O Lord, all my desire is before You, And my groaning is not hidden from You.
Verse_Ch: 38:10 我心跳动，我力衰微；连我眼中的光，也没有了。 ###EN### My heart throbs; my strength fails me; And as for the light of my eyes, neither is it with me.
Verse_Ch: 38:11 我的爱友良朋，因我的灾病，都躲在旁边站着；我的亲属也远远的站立。 ###EN### Those who love me and those who are my friends stand aloof from my plague, And my relatives stand far away.
Verse_Ch: 38:12 寻索我命的，设下网罗；想要害我的，口出败坏，终日思想诡诈。 ###EN### And those who seek my soul lay traps for me, And those who pursue my misfortune speak of destruction, And they contemplate deceit all day long.
Verse_Ch: 38:13 但我如聋子不能听，像哑巴不能开口。 ###EN### But I, like a deaf man, cannot hear; And I am like a dumb man, who cannot open his mouth.
Verse_Ch: 38:14 我如不听见的人，口中没有辩驳。 ###EN### Indeed I am like a man who does not hear And in whose mouth there are no reproofs.
Verse_Ch: 38:15 耶和华阿，我仰望你；主我的神阿，你必应允我。 ###EN### For in You, O Jehovah, do I hope; You will respond, O Lord my God.
Verse_Ch: 38:16 我曾说，恐怕他们向我夸耀；免得我失脚的时候，他们向我夸大。 ###EN### For I said, May they never rejoice over me! When my foot slips, they magnify themselves over me.
Verse_Ch: 38:17 我随时会跌倒，我的痛苦常在我面前。 ###EN### For I am ready to stumble, And my pain is before me continually.
Verse_Ch: 38:18 我要陈明我的罪孽；我要因我的罪担忧。 ###EN### For I declare my iniquity; I am anxious because of my sin.
Verse_Ch: 38:19 但我的仇敌又活泼又强壮；无理恨我的人甚多。 ###EN### But my enemies are vigorous; they are strong; And those who wrongly hate me are many.
Verse_Ch: 38:20 以恶报善的作我的对头，因为我追求良善。 ###EN### Those also who repay evil for good Are my adversaries because I pursue what is good.
Verse_Ch: 38:21 耶和华阿，求你不要撇弃我；我的神阿，求你不要远离我。 ###EN### Do not abandon me, O Jehovah; O my God, do not be far away from me.
Verse_Ch: 38:22 拯救我的主阿，求你快快帮助我。 ###EN### Hasten to help me, O Lord, my salvation.
Chapter_Header: 39
Verse_Ch: 39:1 我曾说，我要谨守我的道路，免得我用舌头犯罪；恶人在我面前的时候，我要笼住我的口。 ###EN### I said, I will keep my ways, So that I do not sin with my tongue; I will keep a muzzle on my mouth When the wicked are before me.
Verse_Ch: 39:2 我默然无声，连好话也不出口；我的痛苦就发动了。 ###EN### I was dumb and silent; I held my peace, even from good; And my pain was stirred up.
Verse_Ch: 39:3 我的心在我里面发热；我默想的时候，火就烧起；我便用舌头说话： ###EN### My heart was hot within me; While I mused, the fire burned; I spoke with my tongue:
Verse_Ch: 39:4 耶和华阿，求你叫我晓得我的结局，我的寿数几何。愿我知道我的生命何其短暂。 ###EN### O Jehovah, cause me to know my end, And the measure of my days, what it is. May I know how transient I am.
Verse_Ch: 39:5 看哪，你使我的年日窄如手掌，我一生的年数，在你面前如同无有；各人站得稳妥的时候，不过尽是虚幻。 细拉 ###EN### Behold, You have made my days as mere handbreadths, And my lifetime is as nothing before You; Surely every man at his best is altogether vanity.
Verse_Ch: 39:6 世人行动实系幻影；他们忙乱，真是枉然：积蓄财宝，却不知将来有谁收取。 ###EN### Surely man goes about as a semblance; Surely they bustle about in vain: He heaps up riches yet knows not Who will gather them.
Verse_Ch: 39:7 主阿，如今我等什么呢？我的指望在乎你。 ###EN### And now what am I waiting for, O Lord? My hope-it is in You.
Verse_Ch: 39:8 求你救我脱离一切的过犯；不要使我受愚顽人的羞辱。 ###EN### Deliver me from all my transgressions; Do not make me the fool's reproach.
Verse_Ch: 39:9 因为这是你所作的，我就闭口不语。 ###EN### I was dumb; I did not open my mouth; For You have done this.
Verse_Ch: 39:10 求你把你的击打从我身上挪去；因你的手与我为敌，我便消灭。 ###EN### Remove Your plague from me; By the hostility of Your hand I am consumed.
Verse_Ch: 39:11 你因人的罪孽，就责备惩治他，叫他所喜爱的消失，如被虫蛀。众人真是虚幻。 细拉 ###EN### With rebukes You chasten a man because of iniquity, And cause what is desirous to him to disappear like a moth. Surely every man is vanity.
Verse_Ch: 39:12 耶和华阿，求你听我的祷告，侧耳听我的呼求；我流泪，求你不要静默无声。因为我在你面前是客旅，是寄居的，像我列祖一样。 ###EN### Hear my prayer, O Jehovah; And give ear to my cry; Do not hold Your peace at my tears. For I am a stranger with You, A sojourner, as all my fathers were.
Verse_Ch: 39:13 求你转眼不看我，使我在去而不返之先，可得畅快。 ###EN### Look away from me, that I may be cheerful, Before I go away and am no more.
Chapter_Header: 40
Verse_Ch: 40:1 我曾耐心等候耶和华，祂就侧耳垂听我的呼求。 ###EN### I waited patiently on Jehovah, And He inclined to me And heard my cry.
Verse_Ch: 40:2 祂从毁灭的坑里，从淤泥中，把我拉上来；祂使我的脚立在磐石上，使我脚步稳当。 ###EN### Then He brought me up out of a pit of destruction, Out of the miry clay; And He set my feet upon a rock, Establishing my steps.
Verse_Ch: 40:3 祂赐新歌在我口中，就是对我们神的赞美。许多人必看见而惧怕，并要倚靠耶和华。 ###EN### Then He put a new song in my mouth, A praise to our God. Many see it and fear, And they trust in Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 40:4 那以耶和华为倚靠，不理会狂傲和偏向虚假之辈的，这人便为有福。 ###EN### Blessed is the man Who makes Jehovah his trust And does not turn to the proud Or to those who turn aside after deception.
Verse_Ch: 40:5 耶和华我的神阿，你所行的奇事，并你向我们所怀的意念甚多，不能向你陈明。我若要宣告并讲论，其事不胜述说。 ###EN### Many, O Jehovah my God, are the wonderful deeds which You have done And Your thoughts toward us; They cannot be set in order unto You. Were I to declare and speak of them, They would be too numerous to recount.
Verse_Ch: 40:6 祭物和供物，你不喜悦；你已经开通我的耳朵；燔祭和赎罪祭，非你所要。 ###EN### You do not delight in sacrifice and offering; You have prepared ears for Me; You do not require burnt offering and sin offering.
Verse_Ch: 40:7 于是我说，看哪，我来了；我的事经卷上已经记载了。 ###EN### Then I said, Behold, I have come; In the scroll of the book It is written concerning Me.
Verse_Ch: 40:8 我的神阿，我乐意实行你的旨意；你的律法在我里面。 ###EN### I delight in doing Your will, O My God; Indeed Your law is within My inward parts.
Verse_Ch: 40:9 我在大会中宣传公义的佳音。看哪，我必不止住我的嘴唇；耶和华阿，这是你所知道的。 ###EN### I bear tidings of righteousness In the great congregation. Behold, I will not withhold My lips; O Jehovah, You know.
Verse_Ch: 40:10 我未曾把你的公义隐藏在心里；我已陈明你的信实和救恩；在大会中，我未曾隐瞒你的慈爱和真实。 ###EN### I have not hidden Your righteousness Within My heart; I have declared Your faithfulness and Your salvation; I have not concealed Your lovingkindness and Your truth from the great congregation.
Verse_Ch: 40:11 耶和华阿，求你不要向我止住你的怜恤；愿你的慈爱和真实，常常保守我。 ###EN### You, O Jehovah, do not withhold Your compassions from me; May Your lovingkindness and Your truth Preserve me continually.
Verse_Ch: 40:12 因有祸患围困我，不可胜数；我的罪孽追上了我，使我不能看见；这些罪孽比我的头发还多；我就心寒胆战。 ###EN### For evils encompass me until they cannot be counted; My iniquities have so overtaken me That I cannot see; They are more numerous than the hairs of my head; Thus my heart fails me.
Verse_Ch: 40:13 耶和华阿，求你喜悦搭救我；耶和华阿，求你快快帮助我。 ###EN### Be pleased, O Jehovah, to deliver me; O Jehovah, hasten to help me.
Verse_Ch: 40:14 愿那些寻索要灭我命的，一同抱愧蒙羞；愿那些喜悦我遭难的，退后受辱。 ###EN### May those who seek my life to destroy it Be put to shame and confounded together; May those who take delight in my misfortune Be turned back and humiliated.
Verse_Ch: 40:15 愿那些对我说，阿哈，阿哈的，因羞愧败亡。 ###EN### May those who say to me, Aha! Aha! Be desolate because of their shame.
Verse_Ch: 40:16 愿一切寻求你的，因你欢喜快乐；愿那些爱你救恩的，常说，当尊耶和华为大！ ###EN### May all those who seek You Be glad and rejoice in You; May those who love Your salvation say continually, May Jehovah be magnified!
Verse_Ch: 40:17 但我是困苦穷乏的；愿主顾念我。你是帮助我的，搭救我的；我的神阿，求你不要耽延。 ###EN### But I am poor and needy; May the Lord think about me. You are my help and my Deliverer; O my God, do not delay.
Chapter_Header: 41
Verse_Ch: 41:1 眷顾贫穷人的有福了；他遭难的日子，耶和华必搭救他。 ###EN### Blessed is he who considers the poor; In the day of evil Jehovah will deliver him.
Verse_Ch: 41:2 愿耶和华保守他，使他存活；愿他在地上蒙福；求你不要把他交给仇敌，遂其所愿。 ###EN### May Jehovah keep him and preserve him alive; May he be blessed in the land; And do not give him over to the hdesire of his enemies.
Verse_Ch: 41:3 他患病在榻，耶和华必扶持他；他在病中，你为他铺床。 ###EN### Jehovah will sustain him on his sickbed; You make all his bed in his illness.
Verse_Ch: 41:4 我曾说，耶和华阿，求你恩待我；求你医治我的魂，因为我得罪了你。 ###EN### I said, O Jehovah, be gracious to me; Heal my soul, for I have sinned against You.
Verse_Ch: 41:5 我的仇敌用恶言议论我，说，他几时死，他的名才灭没呢？ ###EN### My enemies speak evil against me: When will he die and his name perish?
Verse_Ch: 41:6 他若来看我，就说假话。他心里积存罪孽，走到外边才说出来。 ###EN### And if he comes to see me, he speaks falsehood. His heart gathers iniquity to itself; When he goes out, he speaks it.
Verse_Ch: 41:7 一切恨我的，都交头接耳的议论我；他们设计要害我。 ###EN### All who hate me whisper together against me; Against me they devise my misfortune.
Verse_Ch: 41:8 他们说，有恶病贴在他身上；他躺下，必不能再起来。 ###EN### Some evil illness, they say, has been poured out on him; And when he lies down, he will not rise again.
Verse_Ch: 41:9 连我知己的朋友，我所倚靠，吃过我饭的，也用脚踢我。 ###EN### Even my familiar friend, in whom I trusted, Who ate my bread, has lifted his heel against me.
Verse_Ch: 41:10 耶和华阿，求你恩待我，使我起来，我好报复他们。 ###EN### But You, O Jehovah, be gracious to me and raise me up That I may recompense them.
Verse_Ch: 41:11 因我的仇敌不得向我夸胜欢呼，由此我便知道你喜爱我。 ###EN### By this I know that You delight in me, That my enemy has not shouted in triumph over me.
Verse_Ch: 41:12 至于我，因我的纯全，你扶持了我，使我永远站在你的面前。 ###EN### And as for me, You uphold me in my integrity, And You set me in Your presence forever.
Verse_Ch: 41:13 耶和华以色列的神，是当受颂赞的，从永远直到永远。阿们，阿们。 ###EN### Blessed be Jehovah the God of Israel, From eternity to eternity. Amen and Amen.
Chapter_Header: 42
Verse_Ch: 42:1 神阿，我的魂切慕你，如鹿切慕溪水。 ###EN### As the hart pants After the streams of water, So my soul pants For You, O God.
Verse_Ch: 42:2 我的魂渴想神，就是活神。我几时才可以来朝见神呢？ ###EN### My soul thirsts for God, For the living God. When will I come and appear Before God?
Verse_Ch: 42:3 我昼夜以眼泪当饮食；人终日对我说，你的神在那里？ ###EN### My tears have been my food Day and night, While they say to me all day long, Where is your God?
Verse_Ch: 42:4 我从前与众人同往，用欢呼赞美的声音，领他们到神的殿里，大家守节；我追想这些事，就倒出里面的魂，极其悲伤。 ###EN### These things I remember, And I pour out my soul within me: That I passed through with the throng; I led them to the house of God With the voice of a joyous shout and praise, The festal multitude.
Verse_Ch: 42:5 我的魂哪，你为何忧闷？为何在我里面烦躁？应当仰望神；因祂的脸是我的救恩，我还要赞美祂。 ###EN### Why are you cast down, O my soul? And why are you disquieted within me? Hope in God, for I will yet praise Him For the salvation of His countenance.
Verse_Ch: 42:6 我的神阿，我的魂在我里面忧闷；所以我从约但地，从黑门岭，从米萨山，记念你。 ###EN### O my God, my soul is cast down within me; Therefore I remember You From the land of the Jordan and the Hermons, From Mount Mizar.
Verse_Ch: 42:7 你的瀑布发声，深渊就与深渊响应；你的波浪洪涛，都漫过我身。 ###EN### Deep calls unto deep At the sound of Your water spouts; All Your waves and Your billows Pass over me.
Verse_Ch: 42:8 白昼耶和华必向我施慈爱；黑夜我要歌颂祷告那作我生命的神。 ###EN### By day Jehovah commands His lovingkindness, And by night His song is with me, A prayer to the God of my life.
Verse_Ch: 42:9 我要对神我的磐石说，你为何忘记我？我为何因仇敌的欺压，徘徊哀痛呢？ ###EN### I say to God my rock, Why have You forgotten me? Why do I go mourning Because of the oppression of the enemy?
Verse_Ch: 42:10 我的敌人辱骂我，好像打碎我的骨头，他们终日对我说，你的神在那里？ ###EN### As with a shattering in my bones, My adversaries reproach me, While they say to me all day long, Where is your God?
Verse_Ch: 42:11 我的魂哪，你为何忧闷？为何在我里面烦躁？应当仰望神；因我还要赞美祂，祂是我脸上的救恩，是我的神。 ###EN### Why are you cast down, O my soul? And why are you disquieted within me? Hope in God; for I will yet praise Him, The salvation of my countenance and my God.
Chapter_Header: 43
Verse_Ch: 43:1 神阿，求你为我伸冤，向不虔诚的国，为我辨屈；求你救我脱离诡诈不义的人。 ###EN### Render judgment for me, O God; And plead my cause Before an unfaithful nation; From the deceitful and unjust man Deliver me.
Verse_Ch: 43:2 因为你是保护我的神。你为何丢弃我？我为何因仇敌的欺压，徘徊哀痛呢？ ###EN### For You are the God of my protection. Why have You rejected me? Why do I go about mourning Because of the oppression of the enemy?
Verse_Ch: 43:3 求你发出你的亮光和真实，好引导我，带我到你的圣山，到你的帐幕。 ###EN### Send forth Your light and Your truth; They will lead me; They will bring me to Your holy mountain And to Your tabernacles.
Verse_Ch: 43:4 我就到神的祭坛，到我最喜乐的神那里；神阿，我的神，我要弹琴赞美你。 ###EN### And I will go to the altar of God, To God my exceeding joy; And I will praise You with the harp, O God, my God.
Verse_Ch: 43:5 我的魂哪，你为何忧闷？为何在我里面烦躁？应当仰望神；因我还要赞美祂，祂是我脸上的救恩，是我的神。 ###EN### Why are you cast down, O my soul? And why are you disquieted within me? Hope in God, for I will yet praise Him, The salvation of my countenance and my God.
Chapter_Header: 44
Verse_Ch: 44:1 神阿，你在古时，在我们列祖的日子所行的事，我们的列祖给我们讲述过，我们亲耳听见了。 ###EN### O God, we have heard with our ears; Our fathers have recounted it to us, The work You did in their days, In the days of old.
Verse_Ch: 44:2 你曾用手赶出外邦人，却栽培了我们列祖；你苦待众民，却叫我们列祖发旺伸展。 ###EN### You, by Your hand, Have dispossessed nations, but You have planted our fathers; You afflicted peoples, but You spread our fathers forth.
Verse_Ch: 44:3 因为他们不是靠自己的刀剑得地土，也不是靠自己的膀臂得拯救；乃是靠你的右手、你的膀臂、和你脸上的亮光，因为你喜悦他们。 ###EN### For they did not possess the land by their sword, Nor did their arm save them; Rather it was Your right hand and Your arm, And the light of Your countenance; For You delighted in them.
Verse_Ch: 44:4 神阿，你是我的王；求你出令，使雅各得拯救。 ###EN### You are my King, O God; Command salvation for Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 44:5 我们藉你要推倒我们的敌人；藉你的名要践踏那起来攻击我们的人。 ###EN### Through You we thrust back our adversaries; Through Your name we trample those who rise up against us.
Verse_Ch: 44:6 因为我必不倚靠我的弓，我的刀也不能拯救我。 ###EN### For I will not trust in my bow, Nor will my sword save me.
Verse_Ch: 44:7 惟你救了我们脱离敌人，使恨我们的人羞愧。 ###EN### But You save us from our adversaries, And You put to shame those who hate us.
Verse_Ch: 44:8 我们终日因神夸耀，还要永远赞美你的名。 细拉 ###EN### In God we boast all day long, And we praise Your name forever.
Verse_Ch: 44:9 然而你丢弃了我们，使我们受辱，不和我们的军兵同去。 ###EN### Nevertheless You have rejected us and humiliated us, And You have not gone forth with our armies.
Verse_Ch: 44:10 你使我们从敌人面前转身退后；那恨我们的人任意抢夺。 ###EN### You have caused us to turn back from the adversary, And those who hate us take spoil for themselves.
Verse_Ch: 44:11 你把我们交给人，好像快要被吃的羊，把我们分散在列国中。 ###EN### You have given us over like sheep to be eaten And have scattered us among the nations.
Verse_Ch: 44:12 你以贱价卖了你的子民，所得的价值并没有使你得利。 ###EN### You have sold Your people for nothing And have not gone high on their price.
Verse_Ch: 44:13 你使我们受邻国的羞辱，被四围的人嗤笑讥刺。 ###EN### You have made us a reproach to our neighbors, A mocking and a derision to those around us.
Verse_Ch: 44:14 你使我们在列国中成了笑谈，使众民向我们摇头。 ###EN### You have made us a proverb among the nations, Something to shake the head at among the peoples.
Verse_Ch: 44:15 我的凌辱终日在我面前，我脸上的羞愧将我遮蔽； ###EN### All day long my humiliation is before me, And the shame of my face covers me,
Verse_Ch: 44:16 都因那辱骂并毁谤者的声音，又因仇敌和报仇者的嘴脸。 ###EN### Because of the voice of him who reproaches and reviles, Because of the presence of the enemy and of him who avenges himself.
Verse_Ch: 44:17 这都临到我们身上；我们却没有忘记你，也没有对你的约不忠实。 ###EN### All this has come upon us; but we have not forgotten You, Nor have we been false to Your covenant.
Verse_Ch: 44:18 我们的心没有退后，我们的脚步也没有偏离你的路； ###EN### Our heart has not turned back, Nor have our steps deviated from Your way;
Verse_Ch: 44:19 但你在野狗之处压伤我们，用死荫遮蔽我们。 ###EN### But You have crushed us in the place of jackals And have covered us with the shadow of death.
Verse_Ch: 44:20 倘若我们忘了我们神的名，或向别神伸开双手祷告， ###EN### If we have forgotten the name of our God Or spread out our hands to a strange god,
Verse_Ch: 44:21 神岂不鉴察这事么？因为祂晓得人心里的隐秘。 ###EN### Will God not search this out? For He knows the hidden things of the heart.
Verse_Ch: 44:22 但我们为你的缘故，终日被杀，人看我们如将宰的羊。 ###EN### But for Your sake we are slain all day long; We are considered as sheep for slaughter.
Verse_Ch: 44:23 主阿，求你醒起！为何尽睡呢？求你兴起！不要永远丢弃我们。 ###EN### Awake! Why are You sleeping, O Lord? Arise! Do not reject us forever.
Verse_Ch: 44:24 你为何掩面，忘了我们所遭的苦难，和所受的欺压？ ###EN### Why do You hide Your face And forget our affliction and our oppression?
Verse_Ch: 44:25 我们的性命伏于尘土；我们的肚腹紧贴地面。 ###EN### For our soul bows down to the dust; Our body clings to the earth.
Verse_Ch: 44:26 求你起来帮助我们，因你慈爱的缘故救赎我们。 ###EN### Rise up; be our help, And redeem us for Your lovingkindness' sake.
Chapter_Header: 45
Verse_Ch: 45:1 我心里涌出美辞，讲说我论到王的作品。我的舌头是快手的笔。 ###EN### My heart overflows with a good matter; I speak what I have composed concerning the King. My tongue is the pen of a ready writer.
Verse_Ch: 45:2 你比世人更美，你的嘴唇满溢恩典；所以神赐福给你，直到永远。 ###EN### You are fairer than the sons of men; Grace is poured upon Your lips; Therefore God has blessed You forever.
Verse_Ch: 45:3 大能者阿，愿你腰间佩刀，大有尊荣和威严。 ###EN### Gird Your sword upon Your thigh, O mighty One, In Your majesty and Your splendor.
Verse_Ch: 45:4 为了真理、温柔、公义，愿你在威严中坐车前往，无不得胜；愿你的右手施行可畏的事。 ###EN### And in Your splendor ride on victoriously Because of truth and meekness and righteousness; And let Your right hand teach You awesome deeds.
Verse_Ch: 45:5 你的箭锐利，射中王敌之心；众民仆倒在你以下。 ###EN### Your arrows are sharp: The peoples fall under You; The arrows are in the heart of the King's enemies.
Verse_Ch: 45:6 神阿，你的宝座是永永远远的；你国的权杖是正直的权杖。 ###EN### Your throne, O God, is forever and ever; The scepter of uprightness is the scepter of Your kingdom.
Verse_Ch: 45:7 你爱公义，恨恶邪恶；所以神，就是你的神，用欢乐的油膏你，胜过膏你的同伙。 ###EN### You have loved righteousness and hated wickedness; Therefore God, Your God, has anointed You With the oil of gladness above Your companions.
Verse_Ch: 45:8 你的衣服，都有没药、沉香、桂皮的香气；象牙宫中有丝弦乐器的声音，使你快乐。 ###EN### All Your garments smell of myrrh and aloes, of cassia; From palaces of ivory, harpstrings have made You glad.
Verse_Ch: 45:9 有君王的女儿，在你尊贵妇女之中；王后佩戴俄斐金饰，站在你右边。 ###EN### The daughters of kings are among Your most prized; The queen stands at Your right hand in the gold of Ophir.
Verse_Ch: 45:10 女子阿，你要听，要看，要侧耳而听；要忘记你的民，和你的父家； ###EN### Hear, O daughter, and see; and incline your ear; And forget your people and your father's house;
Verse_Ch: 45:11 王就羡慕你的美貌。因为祂是你的主，你当敬拜祂。 ###EN### Thus the King will desire your beauty. Because He is your Lord, Worship Him.
Verse_Ch: 45:12 推罗的女子必带着礼物而来；民中的富足人，必向你求恩。 ###EN### And the daughter of Tyre will come with a gift; The rich among the people will entreat your favor.
Verse_Ch: 45:13 王女在宫里，极其荣华；她的衣服是用金线交织成的。 ###EN### The King's daughter is all glorious within the royal abode; Her garment is a woven work inwrought with gold.
Verse_Ch: 45:14 她要穿刺绣的衣服，被引到王前；随从她的陪伴童女，也要被带到你面前。 ###EN### She will be led to the King in embroidered clothing; The virgins behind her, her companions, Will be brought to You.
Verse_Ch: 45:15 她们要喜乐欢欣的被引导；她们要进入王宫。 ###EN### They will be led with rejoicing and exultation; They will enter the King's palace.
Verse_Ch: 45:16 你的子孙要接续你的列祖；你要立他们在全地作首领。 ###EN### In the place of Your fathers will be Your sons; You will make them princes in all the earth.
Verse_Ch: 45:17 我必叫你的名被万代记念；所以众民要永永远远赞美你。 ###EN### I will cause Your name to be remembered in all generations; Therefore the peoples will praise You forever and ever.
Chapter_Header: 46
Verse_Ch: 46:1 神是我们的避难所和力量，是我们患难中随时可得的帮助。 ###EN### God is our refuge and strength; A help in distress, He is most readily found.
Verse_Ch: 46:2 所以地虽改变，山虽摇动到海心， ###EN### Therefore we will not fear, Though the earth change, And the mountains slip into the heart of the seas;
Verse_Ch: 46:3 其中的水虽匉訇翻腾，山虽因海涨而战抖，我们也不害怕。 细拉 ###EN### Though the waters of the sea roar and foam; Though the mountains shake at its swelling.
Verse_Ch: 46:4 有一道河，这河的支流，使神的城快乐；这城就是至高者支搭帐幕的圣处。 ###EN### There is a river whose streams gladden the city of God, The holy place of the tabernacles of the Most High.
Verse_Ch: 46:5 神在城中；城必不动摇；到天一亮，神必帮助这城。 ###EN### God is in the midst of her; she will not be moved; God helps her at the dawn of the morning.
Verse_Ch: 46:6 外邦喧嚷，列国动摇。神发声，地便镕化。 ###EN### The nations rage; the kingdoms are moved. He utters His voice; the earth melts.
Verse_Ch: 46:7 万军之耶和华与我们同在；雅各的神是我们的高台。 细拉 ###EN### Jehovah of hosts is with us; The God of Jacob is our high retreat.
Verse_Ch: 46:8 你们来看耶和华的作为，看祂怎样使地荒凉。 ###EN### Come, see the works of Jehovah, How He has made desolations on earth.
Verse_Ch: 46:9 祂止息刀兵，直到地极；祂折弓断枪，用火焚烧战车。 ###EN### He makes wars cease unto the end of the earth; He breaks the bow and cuts the spear to pieces; He burns the war wagons with fire.
Verse_Ch: 46:10 你们要住手，要知道我是神。我必在列国中被高举；我必在遍地上被高举。 ###EN### Be still and know that I am God. I will be exalted among the nations; I will be exalted on earth.
Verse_Ch: 46:11 万军之耶和华与我们同在；雅各的神是我们的高台。 ###EN### Jehovah of hosts is with us; The God of Jacob is our high retreat.
Chapter_Header: 47
Verse_Ch: 47:1 万民哪，你们都要拍掌；要用夸胜的声音向神欢呼。 ###EN### Clap your hands, all you peoples; Shout to God with the voice of a triumphant sound.
Verse_Ch: 47:2 因为耶和华至高者是可畏的：祂是管理全地的大君王。 ###EN### For Jehovah Most High is awesome: A great King over all the earth.
Verse_Ch: 47:3 祂叫众民服在我们以下，又叫列邦服在我们脚下。 ###EN### He subdues peoples under us, And nations under our feet.
Verse_Ch: 47:4 祂为我们选择产业，就是祂所爱之雅各的荣耀。 细拉 ###EN### He chose our inheritance for us, The excellency of Jacob, whom He loved.
Verse_Ch: 47:5 神在欢呼声中上升；耶和华在角声中上升。 ###EN### God ascends amidst shouting; Jehovah, at the sound of a trumpet.
Verse_Ch: 47:6 你们要向神歌颂，歌颂；要向我们的王歌颂，歌颂。 ###EN### Sing psalms to God, sing psalms; Sing psalms to our King, sing psalms.
Verse_Ch: 47:7 因为神是全地的王；你们要用悟性歌颂。 ###EN### For God is the King of all the earth; Sing psalms with understanding.
Verse_Ch: 47:8 神作王治理列国；神坐在祂的圣宝座上。 ###EN### God reigns over the nations; God sits upon His holy throne.
Verse_Ch: 47:9 众民的君王聚集，要作亚伯拉罕之神的民；因为地的盾牌是属神的；祂大得高举。 ###EN### The princes of the peoples have been gathered As the people of the God of Abraham; For the shields of the earth belong to God; He is greatly exalted.
Chapter_Header: 48
Verse_Ch: 48:1 耶和华为大，在我们神的城中，在祂的圣山上，该大受赞美。 ###EN### Great is Jehovah, And much to be praised In the city of our God, In His holy mountain.
Verse_Ch: 48:2 在北面的锡安山，是大君王的城，居高华美，为全地所喜悦。 ###EN### Beautiful in elevation, The joy of the whole earth, Is Mount Zion, the sides of the north, The city of the great King.
Verse_Ch: 48:3 神在城的宫中自显为高台。 ###EN### God has made Himself known In her palaces as a high retreat.
Verse_Ch: 48:4 看哪，众王会合，一同经过。 ###EN### For, behold, the kings have assembled themselves; They passed by together.
Verse_Ch: 48:5 他们见了这城，就诧异惊惶，急忙逃跑。 ###EN### They saw; therefore they were astounded. They were dismayed; they hurried off in alarm.
Verse_Ch: 48:6 战兢在那里抓住他们；他们疼痛挣扎，好像产难的妇人一样。 ###EN### Trembling seized them there; Writhing, like that of a woman in labor;
Verse_Ch: 48:7 神阿，你用东风打破他施的船只。 ###EN### With an east wind You shattered The ships of Tarshish.
Verse_Ch: 48:8 我们在万军之耶和华的城中，就是我们神的城中，所看见的，正如我们所听见的。神必坚立这城，直到永远。 细拉 ###EN### As we have heard, So we have seen In the city of Jehovah of hosts, In the city of our God. God will establish her forever.
Verse_Ch: 48:9 神阿，我们在你的殿中，想念你的慈爱。 ###EN### We consider, O God, Your lovingkindness In the midst of Your temple.
Verse_Ch: 48:10 神阿，你受的赞美，正如你的名一样，直到地极；你的右手满了公义。 ###EN### As Your name is, O God, So is Your praise Unto the ends of the earth; Your right hand is full of righteousness.
Verse_Ch: 48:11 因你的判断，锡安山应当快乐，犹大的女子应当欢腾。 ###EN### Let Mount Zion rejoice; Let the daughters of Judah exult Because of Your judgments.
Verse_Ch: 48:12 你们当周游锡安，四围旋绕，数点城楼。 ###EN### Walk about Zion, and go around her; Count her towers.
Verse_Ch: 48:13 当细看她的外郭，巡察她的宫殿，为要传述给后代。 ###EN### Consider carefully her bulwarks; Pass between her palaces; That you may recount it to the generation following.
Verse_Ch: 48:14 因为这神永永远远为我们的神；祂必引导我们，直到死时。 ###EN### For this God is our God forever and ever. He will guide us even unto death.
Chapter_Header: 49
Verse_Ch: 49:1 万民哪，你们都当听这话；世上一切的居民， ###EN### Hear this, all you peoples; Give ear, all you inhabitants of the world,
Verse_Ch: 49:2 无论上流下流，富足贫穷，都当侧耳听； ###EN### Both low and high, Rich and poor together;
Verse_Ch: 49:3 我口要说智慧的话，我心所默想的是通达的事。 ###EN### My mouth will speak wisdom, And the meditation of my heart will be that of understanding.
Verse_Ch: 49:4 我要侧耳听比喻，用琴解谜语。 ###EN### I will incline my ear to a parable; I will disclose my riddle upon the harp.
Verse_Ch: 49:5 在患难的日子，欺诈我者的罪孽四面环绕我，我何必惧怕？ ###EN### Why should I fear in the days of evil, When the iniquity of those who supplant me surrounds me,
Verse_Ch: 49:6 那些人不过是倚靠自己的财货，夸耀自己钱财的丰裕， ###EN### Those who trust in their wealth And boast in the multitude of their riches?
Verse_Ch: 49:7 他们一个也无法赎自己的弟兄，或替他将赎价给神， ###EN### None can by any means redeem his brother Or give to God a ransom for him
Verse_Ch: 49:8 (因为赎他生命的价值极贵，只可永远罢休，) ( ###EN### For the redemption of their soul is costly And must be given up forever),
Verse_Ch: 49:9 叫他仍长远活着，不见朽坏。 ###EN### That he would yet live always And not see corruption.
Verse_Ch: 49:10 他必见智慧人死亡；又见愚顽人和无知人一同灭亡，将他们的财货留给别人。 ###EN### For he will see that wise men die; The foolish one and the senseless one perish alike And leave their wealth to others.
Verse_Ch: 49:11 他们心里思想，他们的家必永存，他们的住处必留到万代；他们以自己的名，称自己的地。 ###EN### Their inward thought is that their houses will remain forever, That their habitations will remain from generation to generation; They call lands after their own names.
Verse_Ch: 49:12 但人在尊贵中不能长久，乃像要灭亡的畜类一样。 ###EN### But man in honor does not remain; He is like the beasts that perish.
Verse_Ch: 49:13 这就是信赖自己者的道路；也是在他们以后，称许他们话语者的道路。 细拉 ###EN### Such is the way of those who are self-confident, And of those after them who approve of their sayings.
Verse_Ch: 49:14 他们如同羊群派定下阴间；死亡必牧养他们。并且他们要直下到坟墓，他们的形体必被阴间所灭，以致他们无处可住。 ###EN### Like a flock, they are appointed for Sheol; Death will shepherd them. And straight to the grave they will descend, And their form will be for Sheol to consume That there be no abode for them.
Verse_Ch: 49:15 只是神必救赎我的魂，脱离阴间的能力，因祂必收纳我。 细拉 ###EN### But God will redeem my soul From the power of Sheol, For He will receive me.
Verse_Ch: 49:16 见人发财、家室增荣的时候，你不要惧怕。 ###EN### Do not fear when a man becomes rich, When the glory of his house increases.
Verse_Ch: 49:17 因为他死的时候，什么也不能带去；他的荣耀不能随他下去。 ###EN### For when he dies, he will take nothing; His glory will not descend after him.
Verse_Ch: 49:18 他活着的时候，虽然自求多福，(你若使自己得福，人必夸奖你，) ###EN### Though he blessed his soul while he lived-And men praise you when you do good for yourself -
Verse_Ch: 49:19 他必到他历代的祖宗那里去；他们永不见光。 ###EN### It will go to the generation of his fathers; They will never see light.
Verse_Ch: 49:20 人在尊贵中却没有悟性，就像要灭亡的畜类一样。 ###EN### A man in honor but without understanding Is like the beasts that perish.
Chapter_Header: 50
Verse_Ch: 50:1 大能者神耶和华，已经发言呼唤大地，从日出之地到日落之处。 ###EN### The Mighty One, God Jehovah, Speaks and summons the earth From the rising of the sun to its setting.
Verse_Ch: 50:2 从全美的锡安，神已经发光了。 ###EN### Out of Zion, the perfection of beauty, God shines forth.
Verse_Ch: 50:3 我们的神要来，绝不静默；有烈火在祂面前吞灭，有暴风在祂四围猛刮。 ###EN### Our God has come and will not be silent; Fire devours before Him, And around Him it is exceedingly tempestuous.
Verse_Ch: 50:4 祂呼唤上天下地，为要审判祂的民，说， ###EN### He calls to the heavens above, And to the earth that He may judge His people:
Verse_Ch: 50:5 招聚我的圣民到我这里来，就是那些用祭物与我立约的人。 ###EN### Gather My saints to Me, Those who have made a covenant with Me by sacrifice.
Verse_Ch: 50:6 诸天必表明祂的公义，因为神自己是审判者。 细拉 ###EN### Then the heavens declare His righteousness, For God Himself is Judge.
Verse_Ch: 50:7 我的民哪，你们当听，我要说话；以色列阿，我要警戒你：我是神，是你的神。 ###EN### Hear, O My people, and I will speak; O Israel, and I will testify against you: I am God, your God.
Verse_Ch: 50:8 我不是因你的祭物责备你，你的燔祭常在我面前。 ###EN### I will not reprove you because of your sacrifices, And your burnt offerings are before Me continually.
Verse_Ch: 50:9 我不从你家中取公牛，也不从你圈内取山羊； ###EN### I will not take a bull from your house Nor goats from your folds,
Verse_Ch: 50:10 因为树林中的百兽都是我的，千山上的牲畜也是我的。 ###EN### For every animal of the forest is Mine, The cattle upon a thousand hills.
Verse_Ch: 50:11 山中的飞鸟，我都认识；野地的走兽，我全知悉。 ###EN### I know every bird of the mountains, And I am aware of everything that moves in the field.
Verse_Ch: 50:12 我若是饥饿，我不用告诉你；因为世界和其中所充满的，都是我的。 ###EN### If I were hungry, I would not tell you; For the world is Mine and the fullness thereof.
Verse_Ch: 50:13 我岂吃公牛的肉，或喝山羊的血呢？ ###EN### Shall I eat the flesh of bulls Or drink the blood of goats?
Verse_Ch: 50:14 你要向神献上感谢祭；又要向至高者还你的愿； ###EN### Offer to God a sacrifice of thanksgiving, And repay your vows to the Most High;
Verse_Ch: 50:15 并要在患难之日呼求我：我必搭救你，你也要荣耀我。 ###EN### And call upon Me in the day of trouble: I will deliver you, and you will glorify Me.
Verse_Ch: 50:16 但神对恶人说，你有何权传述我的律例，口中提到我的约呢？ ###EN### But to the wicked God says, What right do you have to declare My statutes And take up My covenant in your mouth,
Verse_Ch: 50:17 其实你恨恶管教，将我的言语丢在背后。 ###EN### Seeing that you hate correction And cast My words behind you?
Verse_Ch: 50:18 你见了盗贼，就乐意与他在一起；你又与行奸淫的人，一同有分。 ###EN### When you see a thief, you take pleasure in him; And your portion is with adulterers.
Verse_Ch: 50:19 你口任说恶言，你舌编造诡诈。 ###EN### You let your mouth loose for evil, And your tongue frames deceit.
Verse_Ch: 50:20 你坐着毁谤你的兄弟，谗毁你母亲的儿子。 ###EN### You sit and speak against your brother; You defame the son of your mother.
Verse_Ch: 50:21 你行了这些事，我还闭口不言；你想我恰和你一样。其实我要责备你，将这些事摆在你眼前。 ###EN### These things you do, and I keep silent; You think that I am altogether like you. I will rebuke you and set forth the matter in order before your eyes.
Verse_Ch: 50:22 你们忘记神的，要思想这事，免得我把你们撕碎，无人搭救。 ###EN### Consider this then, you who forget God, Lest I tear you apart and there be none to deliver you.
Verse_Ch: 50:23 凡献上感谢祭的，便是荣耀我；那使自己道路正直的，我必使他看见神的救恩。 ###EN### Whoever offers a sacrifice of thanksgiving glorifies Me; And to him who sets his way right I will show the salvation of God.
Chapter_Header: 51
Verse_Ch: 51:1 神阿，求你按你的慈爱恩待我，按你丰盛的怜恤涂抹我的过犯。 ###EN### Be gracious to me, O God, according to Your lovingkindness; According to the greatness of Your compassions blot out my transgressions.
Verse_Ch: 51:2 求你将我的罪孽洗涤净尽，并洁净我的罪。 ###EN### Wash me thoroughly from my iniquity, And from my sin cleanse me.
Verse_Ch: 51:3 因为我知道我的过犯，我的罪常在我面前。 ###EN### For I do know my transgressions, And my sin is before me continually.
Verse_Ch: 51:4 我向你犯罪，惟独得罪了你；我在你眼前行了这恶。因此你责备的时候，显为公义；判断的时候，显为清正。 ###EN### Against You and You alone have I sinned, And I have done what is evil in Your sight. Therefore You are righteous when You speak; You are clear when You judge.
Verse_Ch: 51:5 看哪，我是在罪孽里生的，我母亲在罪中怀了我。 ###EN### Behold, I was brought forth in iniquity, And in sin did my mother conceive me.
Verse_Ch: 51:6 看哪，你所喜爱的，是内里真实；你在我隐密处，必使我认识智慧。 ###EN### Behold, You delight in truth in the inward parts; And in the hidden part You would make known wisdom to me.
Verse_Ch: 51:7 求你用牛膝草洁净我的罪，我就洁净；求你洗涤我，我就比雪更白。 ###EN### Purge my sin with hyssop, and I will be clean; Wash me, and I will be whiter than snow.
Verse_Ch: 51:8 求你使我得听欢喜快乐的声音，使你所压伤的骨头，可以踊跃。 ###EN### Let me hear gladness and joy, That the bones which You have broken may exult.
Verse_Ch: 51:9 求你掩面不看我的罪，涂抹我一切的罪孽。 ###EN### Hide Your face from my sins, And blot out all my iniquities.
Verse_Ch: 51:10 神阿，求你为我造清洁的心，使我里面重新有正直的灵。 ###EN### Create in me a clean heart, O God, And renew a steadfast spirit within me.
Verse_Ch: 51:11 不要丢弃我，使我离开你的面；不要从我取去你圣别的灵。 ###EN### Do not cast me from Your presence, And do not take the Spirit of Your holiness away from me.
Verse_Ch: 51:12 求你使我复得你救恩之乐，赐我乐意的灵扶持我。 ###EN### Restore to me the gladness of Your salvation, And sustain me with a willing spirit.
Verse_Ch: 51:13 我必将你的道路指教有过犯的人，罪人必回转归向你。 ###EN### I will teach transgressors Your ways, And sinners will turn back to You.
Verse_Ch: 51:14 神阿，拯救我的神阿，求你救我脱离流人血的罪；我的舌头就欢唱你的公义。 ###EN### Deliver me from the guilt of bloodshed, O God, O God of my salvation; And my tongue will ring forth Your righteousness.
Verse_Ch: 51:15 主阿，求你使我嘴唇张开，我的口便传扬赞美你的话。 ###EN### O Lord, open my lips, And my mouth will declare Your praise.
Verse_Ch: 51:16 你本不喜爱祭物；若喜爱，我就献上；燔祭你也不喜悦。 ###EN### For You do not delight in sacrifice; Otherwise I would offer it; You take no pleasure in burnt offerings.
Verse_Ch: 51:17 神所要的祭，就是忧伤的灵；神阿，忧伤痛悔的心，你必不轻看。 ###EN### The sacrifices of God are a broken spirit; A broken and a contrite heart, O God, You will not despise.
Verse_Ch: 51:18 求你按你的美意善待锡安，建造耶路撒冷的城墙。 ###EN### Do good in Your good pleasure unto Zion; Build the walls of Jerusalem.
Verse_Ch: 51:19 那时，你必喜爱公义的祭、燔祭、并全牲的燔祭；那时，人必将公牛献在你坛上。 ###EN### Then You will delight in the sacrifices of righteousness, In burnt offerings and whole burnt offerings; Then they will offer bulls upon Your altar.
Chapter_Header: 52
Verse_Ch: 52:1 勇士阿，你为何以作恶自夸？神的慈爱是常存的。 ###EN### Why do you boast in evil, O mighty one? God's lovingkindness endures continually.
Verse_Ch: 52:2 行诡诈的人哪，你的舌头图谋败坏的事，好像磨快的剃刀。 ###EN### Your tongue devises destruction; It is like a sharpened razor, O worker of deceit.
Verse_Ch: 52:3 你爱恶不爱善，爱说谎不爱说公义。 细拉 ###EN### You have loved evil rather than good, Falsehood rather than speaking righteousness.
Verse_Ch: 52:4 诡诈的舌头阿，你爱说一切吞吃人的话。 ###EN### You have loved all the devouring words, O deceitful tongue.
Verse_Ch: 52:5 神也要拆毁你，直到永远；祂要把你拿去，从你的帐棚中抽出，从活人之地将你连根拔除。 细拉 ###EN### God will likewise break you down forever; He will take you and pluck you up from your tent, And uproot you from the land of the living.
Verse_Ch: 52:6 义人要看见而惧怕，并要笑他，说， ###EN### And the righteous will see it and fear, And they will laugh at him, saying,
Verse_Ch: 52:7 看哪，这就是那不以神为他力量的人，只倚仗他丰盛的财富，在欲望上坚立自己。 ###EN### Behold, this is that mighty man Who did not make God his strength, But trusted in the multitude of his riches And strengthened himself in his desire.
Verse_Ch: 52:8 至于我，我像神殿中青翠的橄榄树，永永远远倚靠神的慈爱。 ###EN### But I, like a flourishing olive tree In the house of God, Trust in God's lovingkindness Forever and ever.
Verse_Ch: 52:9 我要称谢你，直到永远，因为你行了这事；我也要在你圣民面前仰望你的名，这名本为美好。 ###EN### I will give You thanks forever, For You have acted; And I will hope in Your name in the presence of Your faithful ones, For it is good.
Chapter_Header: 53
Verse_Ch: 53:1 愚顽人心里说，没有神。他们都是败坏，行了可憎恶的事；没有一个人行善。 ###EN### The fool has said in his heart, There is no God. They are corrupt and commit abominable deeds; There is none who does good.
Verse_Ch: 53:2 神从天上垂看世人，要看有明白的没有，有寻求祂的没有。 ###EN### God looked down from heaven Upon the sons of men To see if there was anyone who had insight, Who seeks after God.
Verse_Ch: 53:3 他们各人都退后，一同变为败坏；并没有行善的，连一个也没有。 ###EN### All of them have turned back; They are together perverse. There is none who does good; There is not even one.
Verse_Ch: 53:4 作孽的没有知识么？他们吞吃我的百姓如同吃饭一样，并不呼求神。 ###EN### Have they no knowledge, the workers of iniquity, Who eat up my people as they would eat up bread And do not call upon God?
Verse_Ch: 53:5 他们在无可惧怕之处，大大的害怕，因为神把那安营攻击你之人的骨头散开了。你使他们蒙羞，因为神弃绝了他们。 ###EN### There they were in great fear, Where there was no fear. For God scattered the bones Of him who encamped against you. You put them to shame Because God has rejected them.
Verse_Ch: 53:6 但愿以色列的救恩从锡安而出！神使祂被掳的子民归回，那时雅各要欢腾，以色列要喜乐。 ###EN### Oh that the salvation of Israel might come forth from Zion! When God turns the captivity of His people, Jacob will exult, Israel will rejoice.
Chapter_Header: 54
Verse_Ch: 54:1 神阿，求你以你的名救我，凭你的大能为我伸冤。 ###EN### O God, save me by Your name, And execute judgment for me by Your might.
Verse_Ch: 54:2 神阿，求你听我的祷告，侧耳听我口中的言语。 ###EN### O God, hear my prayer; Give ear to the words of my mouth.
Verse_Ch: 54:3 因为外人起来攻击我，强暴人寻索我的命；他们不把神摆在眼里。 细拉 ###EN### For strangers have risen up against me, And those who terrorize seek my life; They do not set God before them.
Verse_Ch: 54:4 看哪，神是帮助我的，主是扶持我命的。 ###EN### Behold, God is my Helper; The Lord is among those who sustain my soul.
Verse_Ch: 54:5 祂要报应那些埋伏等候我之人的恶。求你凭你的信实灭绝他们。 ###EN### He will return the evil to those who lie in wait for me. Annihilate them in Your faithfulness.
Verse_Ch: 54:6 我要把甘心祭献给你；耶和华阿，我要赞美你的名，这名本为美好。 ###EN### I will offer a freewill offering to You; I will praise Your name, O Jehovah, for it is good.
Verse_Ch: 54:7 祂从一切的急难中，把我救出来；我的眼睛也看见了我仇敌遭报。 ###EN### For He has delivered me from all distress, And my eye looks triumphantly upon my enemies.
Chapter_Header: 55
Verse_Ch: 55:1 神阿，求你侧耳听我的祷告；不要隐藏不听我的恳求。 ###EN### Give ear, O God, to my prayer; And do not hide Yourself from my supplication.
Verse_Ch: 55:2 求你垂听我，应允我。我哀叹不安，发声唉哼， ###EN### Give heed to me, and answer me. I grow restless in my complaint and moan,
Verse_Ch: 55:3 都因仇敌的声音，恶人的欺压；因为他们使祸患落在我身上，发怒气以我为敌。 ###EN### Because of the voice of the enemy, Because of the oppression of the wicked man; For they drop iniquity upon me, And in anger they make me their enemy.
Verse_Ch: 55:4 我的心在我里面绞痛，死的惊惶落在我身上。 ###EN### My heart writhes within me, And the terrors of death have fallen upon me.
Verse_Ch: 55:5 恐惧战兢临到我，惊恐漫过了我。 ###EN### Fear and trembling have come upon me, And shuddering overwhelms me.
Verse_Ch: 55:6 我说，但愿我有翅膀像鸽子，我就飞去，得以栖息。 ###EN### And I say, Oh that I had wings like a dove! Then I would fly away and be at rest.
Verse_Ch: 55:7 我必远游，宿在旷野。 细拉 ###EN### Indeed I would wander far away; I would lodge in the wilderness.
Verse_Ch: 55:8 我必速速逃走，脱离狂风暴雨。 ###EN### I would hasten my escape From the storm wind and the tempest.
Verse_Ch: 55:9 主阿，求你使他们混乱，意见分歧；因为我在城中看见了强暴和争竞的事。 ###EN### Confuse, O Lord, divide their tongue; For I have seen violence and contention in the city.
Verse_Ch: 55:10 他们在城墙上昼夜绕行；在城内有罪孽和患难。 ###EN### Day and night they go around it, Upon its walls; And iniquity and trouble are in the midst of it.
Verse_Ch: 55:11 城内也有毁坏人的事，欺压和诡诈不离其街市。 ###EN### Utter ruin is in the midst of it, And oppression and deceit Do not depart from its streets.
Verse_Ch: 55:12 原来不是仇敌辱骂我；若是仇敌，还可忍耐。也不是恨我的人向我夸大；若是恨我的人，还可躲避他。 ###EN### For it is not an enemy who reproaches me; Otherwise I could bear it. It is not he who hates me who magnifies himself against me; Otherwise I could hide myself from him.
Verse_Ch: 55:13 不料是你，你原与我平等，是我的密友，是我的知己。 ###EN### But it is you, my equal, My close friend and my acquaintance.
Verse_Ch: 55:14 我们素常甜蜜的交谈；我们与群众在神的殿中同行。 ###EN### We were in sweet counsel together; We walked with the throng in the house of God.
Verse_Ch: 55:15 愿死亡忽然临到他们；愿他们活活的下入阴间；因为在他们的住处，在他们中间，都是邪恶。 ###EN### Let death surprise them; May they go down into Sheol alive. For evil is in their dwelling, in the midst of them.
Verse_Ch: 55:16 至于我，我要呼求神，耶和华必拯救我。 ###EN### As for me, I call out to God, And Jehovah will save me.
Verse_Ch: 55:17 我要在晚上、早晨、晌午，哀怨悲叹，祂必听我的声音。 ###EN### Evening and morning and at noontime I complain and moan, And He hears my voice.
Verse_Ch: 55:18 祂救赎我命脱离攻击我的人，使我得享平安，因为与我相争的人甚多。 ###EN### He has redeemed my soul in peace From the battle against me, For many are they who strive with me.
Verse_Ch: 55:19 那从亘古坐在宝座上的神，必听见而苦待他们－细拉 因为他们没有改变，也不敬畏神。 ###EN### God hears and answers them-Even He who sits enthroned from of old-Because with them there is no change, And they do not fear God.
Verse_Ch: 55:20 他伸手攻击与他和好的人；他违犯自己的约。 ###EN### He put forth his hands against those who were at peace with him; He profaned his covenant.
Verse_Ch: 55:21 他的口如奶油光滑，他的心却怀着争战；他的话比油柔和，其实是拔出来的刀。 ###EN### Smooth were the buttery words of his mouth, But his heart was war; More soothing than oil were his words, But they were in fact drawn swords.
Verse_Ch: 55:22 你要把你的重担卸给耶和华，祂必扶持你；祂永不叫义人动摇。 ###EN### Cast your burden upon Jehovah, And He will sustain you; He will never allow the righteous to be moved.
Verse_Ch: 55:23 神阿，你必使那些人下入朽坏的坑。流人血行诡诈的人，必活不到半世；但我要信靠你。 ###EN### But You, O God, will bring them down Into the lowest pit. Men of bloodshed and deceit Will not live out half their days; But I will trust in You.
Chapter_Header: 56
Verse_Ch: 56:1 神阿，求你恩待我，因为人践踏我，终日攻击欺压我。 ###EN### Be gracious to me, O God; for man tramples me; All day long he, fighting, oppresses me.
Verse_Ch: 56:2 埋伏等候我的人，终日践踏我，因逞骄傲攻击我的人甚多。 ###EN### Those who lie in wait for me trample me all day long, For many are those who arrogantly fight against me.
Verse_Ch: 56:3 我惧怕的时候要信靠你。我信靠神，我赞美祂的话； ###EN### When I am afraid, I trust in You.
Verse_Ch: 56:4 我信靠神，必不惧怕；血肉之人能把我怎么样呢？ ###EN### In God, whose word I praise, In God do I trust, and I will not be afraid. What can flesh do to me?
Verse_Ch: 56:5 他们终日扭曲我的话；他们一切的计谋，都是要害我。 ###EN### All day long they wrest my words; All their thoughts are against me for evil.
Verse_Ch: 56:6 他们聚集，埋伏窥探我的脚踪，等候要害我的命。 ###EN### They gather themselves; they lurk; They watch my steps, As they have waited to take my life.
Verse_Ch: 56:7 他们有罪孽，还能逃脱么？神阿，求你在怒中使众民坠落灭亡。 ###EN### Will there be deliverance for them in spite of their iniquity? In anger cast down the peoples, O God.
Verse_Ch: 56:8 我几次流离，你都数算。求你把我的眼泪装在你的皮袋里。这不都记在你册子上么？ ###EN### You have counted my wanderings. Put my tears into Your bottle. Are they not in Your book?
Verse_Ch: 56:9 我呼求的日子，我的仇敌都要转身退后；神帮助我，这是我所知道的。 ###EN### Then my enemies will turn back When I call; This I know, That God is for me.
Verse_Ch: 56:10 我信靠神，我赞美祂的话；我信靠耶和华，我赞美祂的话； ###EN### In God, whose word I praise, In Jehovah, whose word I praise,
Verse_Ch: 56:11 我信靠神，必不惧怕；人能把我怎么样呢？ ###EN### In God do I trust; I will not be afraid. What can man do to me?
Verse_Ch: 56:12 神阿，我向你所许的愿在我身上；我要将感谢祭献给你。 ###EN### Your vows, O God, are on me; I will render thank offerings to You.
Verse_Ch: 56:13 因为你救了我的命脱离死亡；你确实救了我的脚不至跌倒，使我在活人的光中行在神面前。 ###EN### For You have delivered my soul from death, Indeed, my feet from stumbling, That I may walk before God In the light of the living.
Chapter_Header: 57
Verse_Ch: 57:1 神阿，求你恩待我，恩待我；因为我的心投靠你；我要投靠在你翅膀的荫下，等到灾害过去。 ###EN### Be gracious to me, O God, be gracious to me; For my soul takes refuge in You; Indeed in the shadow of Your wings I will take refuge, Until the destruction passes by.
Verse_Ch: 57:2 我要呼求至高的神，就是为我成全诸事的神。 ###EN### I call out to God the Most High, To the God who accomplishes all things for me.
Verse_Ch: 57:3 神必从天上发出慈爱和信实，并拯救我，祂斥责那践踏我的人；细拉神必向我发出祂的慈爱和信实。 ###EN### He sends forth from heaven and saves me; He reproaches him who would trample me; God sends forth His lovingkindness and His faithfulness.
Verse_Ch: 57:4 我的性命在狮子中间；我躺卧在性如烈火的世人当中，他们的牙齿是枪是箭；他们的舌头是快刀。 ###EN### My soul is among lions; I lie down among those who blaze forth, the sons of men, Whose teeth are spears and arrows, And whose tongue is a sharp sword.
Verse_Ch: 57:5 神阿，愿你被高举，过于诸天；愿你的荣耀遍及全地。 ###EN### Be exalted above the heavens, O God; Let Your glory be above all the earth.
Verse_Ch: 57:6 他们为我的脚步设下网罗，压制我的心。他们在我面前挖了坑，自己反掉在其中。 细拉 ###EN### They have prepared a net for my steps; My soul is bowed down. They have dug a pit before me; They have fallen into it themselves.
Verse_Ch: 57:7 神阿，我心坚定，我心坚定。我要唱诗，我要歌颂。 ###EN### My heart is steadfast, O God; My heart is steadfast. I will sing, indeed I will sing psalms.
Verse_Ch: 57:8 我的荣耀阿，你当醒起；琴瑟阿，你们当醒起！我要极早醒起。 ###EN### Awake, my glory; Awake, O harp and lyre! I will awaken the dawn.
Verse_Ch: 57:9 主阿，我要在众民中称谢你；我要在列邦中歌颂你。 ###EN### I will give thanks to You among the peoples, O Lord; I will sing psalms to you among the nations.
Verse_Ch: 57:10 因为你的慈爱如诸天之大；你的信实达到穹苍。 ###EN### For Your lovingkindness is as great as the heavens; And Your faithfulness reaches the sky.
Verse_Ch: 57:11 神阿，愿你被高举，过于诸天；愿你的荣耀遍及全地。 ###EN### Be exalted above the heavens, O God; Let Your glory be above all the earth.
Chapter_Header: 58
Verse_Ch: 58:1 审判者阿，你们果真讲公义么？世人哪，你们施行审判，岂按正直么？ ###EN### Do you indeed, O judges, speak righteousness? Do you judge in uprightness, O sons of men?
Verse_Ch: 58:2 不然，你们是心中谋行不义；你们在地上称出你们手所行的强暴。 ###EN### No, in heart you perform injustice; You weigh out the violence of your hands on earth.
Verse_Ch: 58:3 恶人一出母胎，就与神疏远；一离母腹，便走错路，说谎言。 ###EN### The wicked are estranged from the womb; They err from their birth, speaking lies.
Verse_Ch: 58:4 他们的毒气，好像蛇的毒气；他们好像闭耳的聋虺， ###EN### Their venom is like the venom of a serpent; They are like the deaf cobra that has shut its ear,
Verse_Ch: 58:5 不听行法术者的声音，也不听灵巧念咒者的声音。 ###EN### Which does not hear the sound of the charmers Or the wise spellbinder.
Verse_Ch: 58:6 神阿，求你敲碎他们口中的牙；耶和华阿，求你敲掉少壮狮子的大牙。 ###EN### O God, break their teeth in their mouth; Break off the fangs of the young lions, O Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 58:7 愿他们消融如水流去。他们射箭的时候，愿箭仿佛被砍断。 ###EN### Let them melt like water that runs off. When he shoots his arrows, Let them be as though they were cut off.
Verse_Ch: 58:8 愿他们像蜗牛消融逝去，又像妇人坠落未见天日的胎。 ###EN### Let them be like a snail that melts and goes away, Like a woman's miscarriage, which by no means sees the sun.
Verse_Ch: 58:9 你们用荆棘烧火，锅还不觉热，祂要把青的和烧着的一齐用旋风刮去。 ###EN### Before your pots can feel the fire of the thorns, Whether green or burning, He will sweep them away.
Verse_Ch: 58:10 义人见仇敌遭报，就欢喜；他要在恶人的血中洗脚。 ###EN### The righteous man will rejoice when he sees vengeance; He will wash his feet in the blood of the wicked.
Verse_Ch: 58:11 人必说，义人诚然有果子；在地上果有施行审判的神。 ###EN### And men will say, Indeed there is fruit for the righteous man; Indeed there is a God who judges on earth.
Chapter_Header: 59
Verse_Ch: 59:1 我的神阿，求你救我脱离仇敌，把我安置在高处，脱离那些起来攻击我的人。 ###EN### Deliver me from my enemies, O my God; Set me on high, secure from those who rise up against me.
Verse_Ch: 59:2 求你救我脱离作孽的人，救我脱离流人血的人。 ###EN### Deliver me from the workers of iniquity, And save me from men of bloodshed.
Verse_Ch: 59:3 因为看哪，他们埋伏，要害我的命；有能力的人聚集攻击我。耶和华阿，这不是为我的过犯，也不是为我的罪。 ###EN### For behold, they lie in wait for my soul; The strong gather themselves against me. Not because of any transgression of mine nor because of any sin of mine, O Jehovah,
Verse_Ch: 59:4 我虽然无过，他们还是跑来，预备好攻击我；求你醒起，前来帮助我，并且察看。 ###EN### Not for any fault of mine, they run and ready themselves; Awake to meet me, and see.
Verse_Ch: 59:5 万军之神耶和华，以色列的神阿，求你兴起，惩罚万邦；不要怜悯一切诡诈作孽的人。 细拉 ###EN### Indeed You, O Jehovah, God of hosts, God of Israel, Arise to punish all the nations; Have no mercy upon any who treacherously commit iniquity.
Verse_Ch: 59:6 他们晚上转回，叫号如狗，围城绕行。 ###EN### They return in the evening; They growl like a dog And go around the city.
Verse_Ch: 59:7 看哪，他们口中喷吐恶言，嘴里有刀；他们说，有谁听见？ ###EN### Behold, they belch forth with their mouth; Swords are in their lips; For, Who, they say, hears?
Verse_Ch: 59:8 但你耶和华必向他们发笑；你要嗤笑万邦。 ###EN### But You, O Jehovah, laugh at them; You have all the nations in derision.
Verse_Ch: 59:9 我的力量阿，我必儆醒等候你；因为神是我的高台。 ###EN### O my strength, I will watch for You; For God is my high retreat.
Verse_Ch: 59:10 我的神要以慈爱迎接我；神要叫我看见那些埋伏等候我的人遭报。 ###EN### My God in His lovingkindness will meet me; God will let me look triumphantly upon those who lie in wait for me.
Verse_Ch: 59:11 不要杀他们，恐怕我的民忘记；主阿，你是我们的盾牌，求你用你的能力使他们四散，且降为卑。 ###EN### Do not slay them, lest my people forget; Scatter them by Your power, and bring them down, O Lord our shield.
Verse_Ch: 59:12 因他们口中的罪，和嘴里的言语，并所说咒骂虚谎的话，愿他们在自己的狂傲中被缠住。 ###EN### For the sin of their mouth, For the word of their lips, Let them even be taken in their arrogance, And because of the cursing and the lying that they speak.
Verse_Ch: 59:13 求你在怒中消灭他们；消灭他们以至于无有；人必知道神在雅各中间掌权，直到地极。 细拉 ###EN### Consume them in wrath; consume them so that they are no more; And men will know that God rules in Jacob Unto the ends of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 59:14 到了晚上，他们转回；他们叫号如狗，围城绕行。 ###EN### They return in the evening; They growl like a dog And go around the city.
Verse_Ch: 59:15 他们走来走去，寻找食物；若不得饱，就流连在外。 ###EN### They wander about for food; And if they are not filled, they linger.
Verse_Ch: 59:16 但我要歌唱你的力量；早晨我要欢唱你的慈爱；因为你作过我的高台，在我急难的日子，作过我的避难所。 ###EN### But I will sing of Your strength; And I will joyfully sing of Your lovingkindness in the morning. For You have been my high retreat And a refuge in the day of my distress.
Verse_Ch: 59:17 我的力量阿，我要歌颂你，因为神是我的高台，是向我施慈爱的神。 ###EN### O my strength, unto You I will sing psalms, For God is my high retreat, My God of lovingkindness.
Chapter_Header: 60
Verse_Ch: 60:1 神阿，你丢弃了我们，使我们破败；你向我们发怒。求你使我们复兴。 ###EN### O God, You have rejected us; You have broken out upon us; You have been angry. Restore us.
Verse_Ch: 60:2 你使地震动，而且崩裂。求你将裂口医好，因为地摇动。 ###EN### You have caused the earth to quake; You have split it open. Heal the breaks in it, for it totters.
Verse_Ch: 60:3 你叫你的民遇见艰难；你叫我们喝那使人东倒西歪的酒。 ###EN### You have shown Your people hard things; You have made us drink wine to stagger us.
Verse_Ch: 60:4 你把旌旗赐给敬畏你的人，可以为真理扬起来。 细拉 ###EN### You have given a banner to those who fear You, To be displayed because of the truth.
Verse_Ch: 60:5 求你用右手拯救我们，应允我们，好叫你所亲爱的人得救。 ###EN### That Your beloved ones may be delivered, Save with Your right hand, and answer us.
Verse_Ch: 60:6 神已经在祂的圣别中说，我要欢乐；我要分开示剑，丈量疏割谷。 ###EN### God has spoken in His holiness: I will exult; I will divide Shechem And measure out the Valley of Succoth.
Verse_Ch: 60:7 基列是我的，玛拿西也是我的，以法莲是我的头盔；犹大是我的杖； ###EN### Gilead is Mine, and Manasseh is Mine, And Ephraim is the helmet for My head; Judah is My scepter.
Verse_Ch: 60:8 摩押是我的沐浴盆；我要向以东抛鞋；非利士阿，你要因我欢呼。 ###EN### Moab is My washbowl; Upon Edom I will cast My sandal; Philistia, shout aloud because of Me.
Verse_Ch: 60:9 谁能领我进被围困的城？谁能引我到以东地？ ###EN### Who will bring me into the besieged city? Who will lead me to Edom?
Verse_Ch: 60:10 神阿，你不是丢弃了我们么？神阿，你不和我们的军兵一同出战么？ ###EN### Will not You, O God, who rejected us? And will You not go forth, O God, with our armies?
Verse_Ch: 60:11 求你帮助我们脱离敌人，因为人的拯救是枉然的。 ###EN### Give us help from the adversary, For a salvation by man is vain.
Verse_Ch: 60:12 我们因神才得奋勇行事，践踏我们敌人的就是祂。 ###EN### In God we will do valiantly, And it is He who will tread down our adversaries.
Chapter_Header: 61
Verse_Ch: 61:1 神阿，求你听我的呼求，垂听我的祷告。 ###EN### Hear, O God, my cry; Give heed to my prayer.
Verse_Ch: 61:2 我心里发昏的时候，我要从地极呼求你。求你领我到那比我更高的磐石。 ###EN### From the end of the earth I will call out unto You When my heart faints; Lead me to the rock that is higher than I.
Verse_Ch: 61:3 因为你作了我的避难所，作了我在仇敌面前的坚固台。 ###EN### For You are a refuge to me, A strong tower before the enemy.
Verse_Ch: 61:4 我要永远住在你的帐幕里；我要投靠在你翅膀下的隐密处。 细拉 ###EN### Let me sojourn in Your tent forever; Let me take refuge in the covering of Your wings.
Verse_Ch: 61:5 神阿，你已听了我所许的愿；你已将敬畏你名之人的产业赐给了我。 ###EN### For You, O God, have heard my vows; You have given me the inheritance of those who fear Your name.
Verse_Ch: 61:6 你要加添王的寿数；愿他的年岁代代无穷。 ###EN### You will add days to the days of the king; May his years be like generation after generation.
Verse_Ch: 61:7 愿他永远住在神面前；愿你分派慈爱和信实保守他。 ###EN### May he dwell forever before God; Appoint lovingkindness and faithfulness, that they may preserve him.
Verse_Ch: 61:8 这样，我要歌颂你的名，直到永远，好天天还我所许的愿。 ###EN### So I will sing psalms to Your name forever, As I repay my vows day by day.
Chapter_Header: 62
Verse_Ch: 62:1 我的魂默默无声，专等候神；我的救恩是从祂而来。 ###EN### My soul waits in silence for God alone; My salvation is from Him.
Verse_Ch: 62:2 惟独祂是我的磐石和我的拯救，是我的高台；我必不很动摇。 ###EN### He alone is my rock and my salvation, My high retreat; I will not be greatly shaken.
Verse_Ch: 62:3 你们大家攻击一人，把他杀害，如同毁坏歪斜的墙，将倒的壁，要到几时呢？ ###EN### How long will you assail a man So that you may slay him, all of you, Like a leaning wall or a tottering fence?
Verse_Ch: 62:4 他们彼此商议，专要从他的尊位上把他推下；他们喜爱谎话；口虽祝福，心里却咒诅。 细拉 ###EN### They only make plans to thrust him down from his dignity; They take delight in lies; With their mouth they bless, But inwardly they curse.
Verse_Ch: 62:5 我的魂哪，你当默默无声，专等候神，因为我的盼望是从祂而来。 ###EN### My soul, wait in silence for God alone, For my expectation is from Him.
Verse_Ch: 62:6 惟独祂是我的磐石和我的拯救，是我的高台，我必不动摇。 ###EN### He alone is my rock and my salvation, My high retreat; I will not be shaken.
Verse_Ch: 62:7 我的拯救和我的荣耀，都在于神；我力量的磐石，我的避难所，是在神里面。 ###EN### On God my salvation and my glory depend; The rock of my strength, my refuge, is in God.
Verse_Ch: 62:8 百姓阿，你们当时时信靠祂，在祂面前倾心吐意；神是我们的避难所。 细拉 ###EN### Trust in Him at all times, O people; Pour out your heart before Him; God is a refuge to us.
Verse_Ch: 62:9 下流人不过是虚空，上流人不过是虚假；放在天平里就必升起；他们一共比空气还轻。 ###EN### Men of low degree are but a vapor; Men of high degree, a lie. In the balances they go up; Together they are less than a vapor.
Verse_Ch: 62:10 不要靠强暴得财，也不要妄想靠抢夺得利；若财宝加增，不要放在心上。 ###EN### Do not trust in oppression, And do not vainly hope in robbery; If wealth increases, Do not set your heart on it.
Verse_Ch: 62:11 神说了一次、两次，我都听见，就是能力属于神。 ###EN### Once has God spoken; Twice have I heard this, That strength belongs to God.
Verse_Ch: 62:12 主阿，慈爱也是属于你，因为你照着各人所行的报应他。 ###EN### To You also, O Lord, belongs lovingkindness; For You repay every man according to his work.
Chapter_Header: 63
Verse_Ch: 63:1 神阿，你是我的神，我切切的寻求你。在干旱疲乏无水之地，我的魂渴想你，我的身切慕你。 ###EN### O God, You are my God; I seek You diligently. My soul thirsts for You, My flesh faints in longing for You, In a dry and weary land without water.
Verse_Ch: 63:2 我在圣所中曾如此瞻仰你，为要见你的能力和你的荣耀。 ###EN### So I have looked upon You in the sanctuary, Seeing Your power and Your glory.
Verse_Ch: 63:3 因你的慈爱比生命更好，我的嘴唇要称颂你。 ###EN### Because Your lovingkindness is better than life, My lips praise You.
Verse_Ch: 63:4 我还活的时候要这样颂赞你；我要在你的名里举手。 ###EN### Thus I bless You while I live; I lift up my hands in Your name.
Verse_Ch: 63:5 我在床上记念你，在夜更的时候默想你，我的魂就像饱足了脂膏肥油，我要以欢呼的嘴唇赞美你。 ###EN### My soul is satisfied as with the rich fatness, And my mouth praises You with lips of joyous shouting,
Verse_Ch: 63:6  ###EN### When I remember You while on my bed, When I consider You in the night watches.
Verse_Ch: 63:7 因为你曾帮助我，我要在你翅膀的荫下欢呼。 ###EN### For You have been my help, And in the shadow of Your wings I will shout for joy.
Verse_Ch: 63:8 我魂紧紧的跟随你；你的右手扶持我。 ###EN### My soul pursues after You; Your right hand upholds me.
Verse_Ch: 63:9 但那些寻索要灭我命的人，必往地的低下之处去； ###EN### But those who seek my life to destroy it Will go into the lower parts of the earth;
Verse_Ch: 63:10 他们必交在刀剑的权势下，成为狐狸的食物。 ###EN### They will be given over to the power of the sword; They will be the portion of foxes.
Verse_Ch: 63:11 但王必因神喜乐；凡指着祂起誓的，必要夸口；因为说谎之人的口，必被塞住。 ###EN### But the king will rejoice in God; Everyone who swears by Him will boast; For the mouth of those who speak falsehood will be stopped.
Chapter_Header: 64
Verse_Ch: 64:1 神阿，我哀叹的时候，求你听我的声音；求你保守我的性命，不受仇敌的惊恐。 ###EN### Hear, O God, my voice in my complaint; Preserve my life from the enemy's dread.
Verse_Ch: 64:2 求你把我隐藏，使我脱离作恶之人的密谋，和作孽之人的骚乱； ###EN### Hide me from the secret counsel of evildoers, From the throng of the workers of iniquity,
Verse_Ch: 64:3 他们磨舌如刀，发出苦毒的言语，好像比准了的箭， ###EN### Who have sharpened their tongue like a sword, Who have aimed their arrow, their bitter word,
Verse_Ch: 64:4 要在暗处射完全人。他们忽然射他，并不惧怕。 ###EN### To shoot in secret places at the perfect man. They shoot suddenly at him and do not fear.
Verse_Ch: 64:5 他们彼此勉励设计恶事；他们商量暗设网罗，说，谁能看见？ ###EN### They firm up for themselves an evil matter; They talk of laying snares secretly; They say, Who will see them?
Verse_Ch: 64:6 他们图谋不义，说，我们完成了精密的计谋；他们各人的意念和心思是深的。 ###EN### They seek out injustices, saying: We have completed a carefully sought-out plan. Indeed each man's inward thought And heart are deep.
Verse_Ch: 64:7 但神要用箭射他们，他们就忽然受伤。 ###EN### But God will shoot an arrow at them; Suddenly they are wounded.
Verse_Ch: 64:8 他们必被自己的舌头所害而绊跌；凡看见他们的，必都摇头。 ###EN### They are made to stumble over each other by their own tongue; All who see them shake their heads.
Verse_Ch: 64:9 众人都要害怕，要传扬神的工作，并且思考祂的作为。 ###EN### And all men will fear And declare what has been done by God, And they will ponder His work.
Verse_Ch: 64:10 义人必因耶和华喜乐，并要投靠祂；凡心里正直的人，都要夸口。 ###EN### The righteous man will rejoice in Jehovah and take refuge in Him, And all the upright in heart will boast.
Chapter_Header: 65
Verse_Ch: 65:1 神阿，在锡安人们等候赞美你；所许的愿，也要向你偿还。 ###EN### Praise awaits You, O God, in Zion; And to You is the vow paid.
Verse_Ch: 65:2 听祷告的主阿，凡有血肉的，都要来就你。 ###EN### O You who hear prayer, To You all flesh comes.
Verse_Ch: 65:3 罪孽胜了我；至于我们的过犯，你都要遮盖。 ###EN### Iniquities prevail against me; As for our transgressions, You make propitiation for them.
Verse_Ch: 65:4 你所拣选，使他亲近你，住在你院中的，这人便为有福。我们必因你居所，你圣殿的美福得满足。 ###EN### Blessed is he whom You have chosen and bring near To dwell in Your courts. We will be satisfied with the goodness of Your house, Of Your holy temple.
Verse_Ch: 65:5 拯救我们的神阿，你必以可畏的事，按公义应允我们；你本是一切地极、和远处海上的人所倚靠的。 ###EN### By awesome deeds You answer us in righteousness, O God of our salvation, You who are the trust of all the ends of the earth And of the remotest sea;
Verse_Ch: 65:6 你既以大能束腰，就用力量立定诸山； ###EN### Who established the mountains in His strength, Girded with might;
Verse_Ch: 65:7 使诸海的响声，和其中波浪的响声，并众民的喧哗，都平静了。 ###EN### Who stilled the roaring of the seas, The roaring of their billows, And the tumult of the peoples.
Verse_Ch: 65:8 住在地极的人，因你的神迹惧怕；你使日出日落之地都欢呼。 ###EN### And they who dwell in the uttermost parts Are afraid of Your signs; You make the exitways of the morning and the evening Shout for joy.
Verse_Ch: 65:9 你眷顾并浇灌地，使地大得肥美：神的河满了水；你这样预备了地，好为人预备五谷。 ###EN### You visit the earth and water it; You enrich it greatly: The river of God is full of water. You provide men grain, for so You have prepared the earth.
Verse_Ch: 65:10 你浇透地的犁沟，润平犁脊；用甘霖使地松软；其中发芽的，蒙你赐福。 ###EN### Saturating its furrows, settling its ridges, You soften it with showers; You bless its sprouting forth.
Verse_Ch: 65:11 你以你的恩惠为年岁的冠冕，你的路径都滴下脂油； ###EN### You place a crown on a year with Your goodness, And Your wagon tracks drop fatness;
Verse_Ch: 65:12 旷野的草场也满溢，小山以欢乐束腰。 ###EN### The wilderness pastures overflow, And the hills gird themselves with exultation.
Verse_Ch: 65:13 草场以羊群为衣，山谷盖满了五谷。这一切都欢呼歌唱。 ###EN### The meadows are clothed with the flock, And the valleys cover themselves in grain; They shout for joy; indeed they sing.
Chapter_Header: 66
Verse_Ch: 66:1 全地都当向神欢呼， ###EN### Shout joyfully to God, all the earth;
Verse_Ch: 66:2 歌颂祂名的荣耀，使献给祂的赞美显为荣耀。 ###EN### Sing forth the glory of His name; Make glorious His praise.
Verse_Ch: 66:3 当对神说，你的作为何等可畏！因你的大能，仇敌要归顺你。 ###EN### Say to God, How awesome are Your deeds! Because of the greatness of Your strength, Your enemies come cringing to You.
Verse_Ch: 66:4 全地都要敬拜你，歌颂你；他们要歌颂你的名。 细拉 ###EN### All the earth will worship You And sing psalms to You; They will sing psalms to Your name.
Verse_Ch: 66:5 你们来看神所作的；祂向世人所行之事，是可畏的。 ###EN### Come and see the works of God; He is awesome in His deeds toward the sons of men.
Verse_Ch: 66:6 祂将海变成干地；众人步行过河。我们在那里因祂喜乐。 ###EN### He turned the sea into dry land; Through the river they crossed on foot. There we rejoiced in Him.
Verse_Ch: 66:7 祂用权能治理众民，直到永远；祂的眼睛鉴察列邦：悖逆的人不可自高。 细拉 ###EN### He rules by His might forever; His eyes observe the nations: Let not the rebellious exalt themselves.
Verse_Ch: 66:8 众民哪，你们当颂赞我们的神，使人得听赞美祂的声音； ###EN### Bless our God, O peoples; And make the voice of His praise heard,
Verse_Ch: 66:9 祂使我们的性命存活，也不叫我们的脚滑跌。 ###EN### Who has kept our soul in life And does not allow our feet to slip.
Verse_Ch: 66:10 神阿，你曾试验我们，熬炼我们，如熬炼银子一样。 ###EN### For You have tried us, O God; You have refined us as silver is refined.
Verse_Ch: 66:11 你使我们进入网罗，把重担放在我们身上。 ###EN### You have brought us into the net; You have put a heavy burden on our loins.
Verse_Ch: 66:12 你使人坐车轧我们的头；我们经过水火；你却领我们出到丰富之地。 ###EN### You have made men ride over our heads; We have gone through fire and water; But You have brought us forth into abundance.
Verse_Ch: 66:13 我要凭燔祭进入你的殿；我要向你还我的愿， ###EN### I will come into Your house with burnt offerings; I will pay my vows to You,
Verse_Ch: 66:14 就是在急难时我嘴唇所发的，口中所许的。 ###EN### Which my lips uttered And my mouth spoke when I was in distress.
Verse_Ch: 66:15 我要把肥畜作燔祭，连同公羊的香气献给你；我要把公牛连同山羊献上。 细拉 ###EN### I will offer to You burnt offerings of fatlings With the smoke of rams; I will offer cattle with goats.
Verse_Ch: 66:16 凡敬畏神的人，你们都来听，我要述说祂为我所行的事。 ###EN### Come, hear, all you who fear God, And I will recount what He has done for my soul.
Verse_Ch: 66:17 我曾用口呼求祂，我的舌头也颂扬祂。 ###EN### To Him I called out with my mouth, And He was extolled with my tongue.
Verse_Ch: 66:18 我若心里注重罪孽，主必不听。 ###EN### If I regarded iniquity in my heart, The Lord did not hear.
Verse_Ch: 66:19 但神实在听见了；祂垂听了我祷告的声音。 ###EN### But indeed God has heard; He has given heed to the voice of my prayer.
Verse_Ch: 66:20 神是当受颂赞的，祂并没有推却我的祷告，也没有叫祂的慈爱离开我。 ###EN### Blessed be God, Who has not turned my prayer away Nor His lovingkindness from me.
Chapter_Header: 67
Verse_Ch: 67:1 愿神怜悯我们，赐福与我们；愿祂用脸光照我们； 细拉 ###EN### God be gracious to us and bless us; May He make His face to shine upon us;
Verse_Ch: 67:2 好叫人在地上得知你的道路，在万国中得知你的救恩。 ###EN### That Your way may be known on earth, And Your salvation among all the nations.
Verse_Ch: 67:3 神阿，愿众民赞美你；愿众民都赞美你。 ###EN### Let the peoples praise You, O God; Let the peoples praise You, all of them.
Verse_Ch: 67:4 愿列邦喜乐欢呼，因为你必按公正审判众民，引导地上的列邦。 细拉 ###EN### Let the nations rejoice and shout for joy, For You will judge the peoples equitably And will guide the nations on the earth.
Verse_Ch: 67:5 神阿，愿众民赞美你；愿众民都赞美你。 ###EN### Let the peoples praise You, O God; Let the peoples praise You, all of them.
Verse_Ch: 67:6 地已经出了土产；神，就是我们的神，要赐福与我们。 ###EN### The earth has yielded its increase; God, our God, blesses us.
Verse_Ch: 67:7 神要赐福与我们；地的四极都要敬畏祂。 ###EN### God blesses us; And all the ends of the earth will fear Him.
Chapter_Header: 68
Verse_Ch: 68:1 愿神兴起；愿祂的仇敌四散；愿恨祂的人从祂面前逃跑。 ###EN### Let God arise; let His enemies be scattered; And let those who hate Him flee before Him.
Verse_Ch: 68:2 你要驱逐他们，使他们如烟被风吹散；恶人要见神的面而灭没，如蜡见火而融化。 ###EN### As smoke is driven away, You will drive them away; As wax melts before fire, The wicked will perish before God.
Verse_Ch: 68:3 惟有义人必然喜乐；他们必在神面前欢欣，并欢喜快乐。 ###EN### But the righteous will rejoice; they will exult before God And be glad with rejoicing.
Verse_Ch: 68:4 你们当向神唱诗，歌颂祂的名；要因那坐车行过荒野的人夸胜，祂的名是耶和华；要在祂面前欢乐。 ###EN### Sing to God; sing psalms to His name; Triumph in Him who rides through the deserts-For Jah is His name-and exult before Him.
Verse_Ch: 68:5 神在祂的圣所作孤儿的父，作寡妇的伸冤者。 ###EN### A Father to the orphans and a Judge for the widows Is God in His holy habitation.
Verse_Ch: 68:6 神叫孤独的有家可居住，使被囚的出来得亨通；惟有悖逆的住在干燥之地。 ###EN### God causes the solitary to dwell in a household; He brings the prisoners forth into prosperity; But the rebellious dwell in a parched land.
Verse_Ch: 68:7 神阿，你曾在你百姓前头出来，在荒野行走， 细拉 ###EN### O God, when You went forth before Your people, When You marched through the desert,
Verse_Ch: 68:8 那时地见神的面就震动，天也落雨；西乃山见了以色列神的面也震动。 ###EN### The earth trembled, the heavens also dripped, At the presence of God; Sinai there quaked At the presence of God, the God of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 68:9 神阿，你降下沛雨；你产业凋萎的时候，你使它复苏。 ###EN### You shed forth bountiful rain, O God; You confirmed Your inheritance when it languished.
Verse_Ch: 68:10 你的羊群住在其中；神阿，你凭你的恩惠为困苦人有所预备。 ###EN### Your living flock dwelt in the land; In Your goodness You provided for the poor, O God.
Verse_Ch: 68:11 主发命令；传好信息的妇女成了大群。 ###EN### The Lord gives the command; The women who bear the glad tidings are a great host.
Verse_Ch: 68:12 统兵的君王逃跑了，逃跑了！留守在家的妇女，分得了掠物。 ###EN### The kings of the armies flee. They flee! And she who abides at home Divides the spoil.
Verse_Ch: 68:13 你们虽然躺卧在羊圈之间，却像鸽子的翅膀镀了白银，翎毛镀了绿黄色的金。 ###EN### Though you lie among the sheepfolds, There are dove wings covered with silver, And its pinions, with greenish yellow gold.
Verse_Ch: 68:14 全能者在境内赶散列王的时候，势如飘雪在撒们。 ###EN### When the Almighty scattered The kings in the land, It snowed on Zalmon.
Verse_Ch: 68:15 巴珊山是大能的山，巴珊山是多峰多岭的山： ###EN### O mighty mountain, O mountain of Bashan, O many-peaked mountain, O mountain of Bashan:
Verse_Ch: 68:16 你们多峰多岭的山哪，为何嫉视神所愿居住的山？耶和华必住这山，直到永远。 ###EN### Why do you look with envy, O many-peaked mountains, At the mountain on which God desires to dwell? Indeed Jehovah will dwell there forever.
Verse_Ch: 68:17 神的车辇累万盈千；主在其中，好像在西乃，在圣所一样。 ###EN### The chariots of God are twenty thousand, Thousands upon thousands; The Lord is among them, As at Sinai, in the sanctuary.
Verse_Ch: 68:18 你已经升上高处，掳掠了那些被掳的；你在人间，甚至在悖逆的人中间，受了恩赐，叫耶和华神可以住在他们中间。 ###EN### You have ascended on high; You have led captive those taken captive; You have received gifts among men, Even the rebellious ones also, That Jehovah God may dwell among them.
Verse_Ch: 68:19 天天加给我们美福的主，就是拯救我们的神，是当受颂赞的。 细拉 ###EN### Blessed be the Lord, who day by day loads us with good; God is our salvation.
Verse_Ch: 68:20 神是为我们施行拯救的神；人能脱离死亡，是在于主耶和华。 ###EN### God is to us A God of deliverance, And with Jehovah the Lord Are the goings forth even from death.
Verse_Ch: 68:21 神要打破祂仇敌的头，就是那在自己罪过中往来之人的发顶。 ###EN### Indeed God will smash The head of His enemies, The hairy crown Of him who goes about in his guiltiness.
Verse_Ch: 68:22 主说，我要使他们从巴珊归来，使他们从深海返回； ###EN### The Lord said, I will bring them again from Bashan; I will bring them again from the depths of the sea,
Verse_Ch: 68:23 使你的脚洗在血中，使你狗的舌头，从仇敌得分。 ###EN### That you may bathe your foot in blood, That the tongue of your dogs may have their portion from the enemies.
Verse_Ch: 68:24 神阿，你是我的神，我的王；人已经看见你行走，在圣所中行走： ###EN### They have seen Your goings, O God, The goings of my God, my King, in the sanctuary:
Verse_Ch: 68:25 歌唱的行在前，作乐的随在后，都在击鼓的童女中间。 ###EN### Singers go before; players after; In the midst of virgins sounding the tambourines.
Verse_Ch: 68:26 你们从以色列源头而来的，当在各会中颂赞耶和华神。 ###EN### Bless God in the congregations, Even Jehovah, O you who are of the fountain of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 68:27 在那里，有统管他们的小便雅悯，有犹大的首领在他们的群众中，有西布伦的首领，有拿弗他利的首领。 ###EN### There are little Benjamin, who rules them, And the princes of Judah in their company, The princes of Zebulun, the princes of Naphtali.
Verse_Ch: 68:28 你的能力是你神所命定的；神阿，求你坚固你为我们所成全的事。 ###EN### Your God has commanded your strength; Strengthen, O God, that which You have done for us.
Verse_Ch: 68:29 因你在耶路撒冷的殿，列王必带贡物献给你。 ###EN### Because of Your temple at Jerusalem, Kings will bring a gift to You.
Verse_Ch: 68:30 求你叱喝芦苇中的野兽，众民牛犊中成群的公牛，把贪爱银子的踹在脚下；求你把喜好争战的众民赶散。 ###EN### Rebuke the animals of the reeds, The herd of the bulls among the calves of the peoples, Trampling on those who lust after silver; Scatter the peoples who take delight in war.
Verse_Ch: 68:31 公侯要从埃及出来朝见神；古实人要急忙向神举手祷告。 ###EN### Nobles will come out of Egypt; Cush will quickly stretch out its hands to God.
Verse_Ch: 68:32 地上的列国阿，你们要向神歌唱，要向主歌颂， 细拉 ###EN### O kingdoms of the earth, Sing to God, Sing psalms to the Lord,
Verse_Ch: 68:33 祂是那驾行在自古就有，天上之天以上的主。看哪，祂发出声音，是极大的声音。 ###EN### To Him who rides upon the ancient heaven of heavens. Behold, He utters His voice, a mighty voice.
Verse_Ch: 68:34 你们要将能力归给神；祂的威荣在以色列之上，祂的能力是在穹苍。 ###EN### Ascribe strength to God; His excellence is over Israel, And His strength is in the skies.
Verse_Ch: 68:35 神阿，你从圣所显为可畏；以色列的神，是那将力量权能赐给百姓的。神是当受颂赞的！ ###EN### You are awesome, O God, from Your sanctuaries. The God of Israel, He gives strength and power to the people. Blessed be God!
Chapter_Header: 69
Verse_Ch: 69:1 神阿，求你救我；因为众水威胁我的性命。 ###EN### Save me, O God; for the waters Threaten my life.
Verse_Ch: 69:2 我陷在深淤泥中，没有立脚之地；我到了深水中，洪水漫过我身。 ###EN### I sink in deep mire, And there is no place to stand; I have come to the depths of water, And the flood flows over me.
Verse_Ch: 69:3 我因呼求困乏，喉咙发干；我因等候我的神，眼睛失明。 ###EN### I am weary of my crying; My throat is parched; My eyes fail While I wait for my God.
Verse_Ch: 69:4 无故恨我的，比我头发还多；无理与我为仇，要把我除灭的，极为强盛；我没有抢夺的，竟要我偿还。 ###EN### More numerous than the hairs of my head Are those who hate me without cause; Mighty are those who would destroy me, Those who are wrongly my enemies. What I did not steal, I must then restore.
Verse_Ch: 69:5 神阿，我的愚昧你原知道；我的罪愆不能向你隐瞒。 ###EN### O God, You know my foolishness, And my sins of guilt are not hidden from You.
Verse_Ch: 69:6 万军的主耶和华阿，求你叫那等候你的，不要因我蒙羞；以色列的神阿，求你叫那寻求你的，不要因我受辱。 ###EN### Do not let those who wait on You be put to shame because of me, O Lord Jehovah of hosts; Do not let those who seek You be humiliated because of me, O God of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 69:7 因我为你的缘故担受了辱骂，满面羞愧。 ###EN### Because for Your sake I have borne reproach; Humiliation has covered my face.
Verse_Ch: 69:8 我的兄弟看我是外路人；我母亲的儿子看我是外邦人。 ###EN### I have become a stranger to my brothers, And a foreigner to my mother's children.
Verse_Ch: 69:9 因我为你的家，心里焦急，如同火烧；并且辱骂你之人的辱骂，都落在我身上。 ###EN### For the zeal of Your house has devoured me, And the reproaches of those who reproach You have fallen on me.
Verse_Ch: 69:10 我哭泣，以禁食刻苦我魂，这倒成了我的羞辱。 ###EN### When I wept, when my soul was in fasting, That became a reproach to me.
Verse_Ch: 69:11 我拿麻布当衣裳，就成了他们的笑谈。 ###EN### When I made sackcloth my clothing, I became a proverb to them.
Verse_Ch: 69:12 坐在城门口的谈论我，酒徒也以我为歌曲。 ###EN### Those who sit in the gate talk about me, And I am the mocking song of those who drink liquor.
Verse_Ch: 69:13 但耶和华阿，我在悦纳的时候，向你祷告；神阿，求你按你丰盛的慈爱，凭你拯救的信实，应允我。 ###EN### But as for me, my prayer is to You, O Jehovah, in an acceptable time; O God, in the abundance of Your lovingkindness answer me, In the faithfulness of Your salvation.
Verse_Ch: 69:14 求你救我出离淤泥，不让我沉陷下去；求你救我脱离那些恨我的人，救我出离深水。 ###EN### Deliver me out of the mire, and let me not sink; May I be delivered from those who hate me, And out of the depths of water.
Verse_Ch: 69:15 求你不让洪水漫过我，不让深渊吞灭我，不让坑坎在我以上合口。 ###EN### Do not let the flood of water flow over me, Nor let the deep swallow me, Nor let the pit close its mouth over me.
Verse_Ch: 69:16 耶和华阿，求你应允我，因为你的慈爱本为美好；求你按你丰盛的怜恤，回转眷顾我。 ###EN### Answer me, O Jehovah; for Your lovingkindness is good; According to the abundance of Your compassions turn to me.
Verse_Ch: 69:17 不要向你的仆人掩面，因我是在急难之中；求你速速的应允我。 ###EN### And do not hide Your face from Your servant, For I am in distress; hurry and answer me.
Verse_Ch: 69:18 求你亲近我，救赎我；求你因我的仇敌把我赎回。 ###EN### Draw near to my soul; redeem it; Ransom me because of my enemies.
Verse_Ch: 69:19 你知道我受的辱骂、欺凌、羞辱；我的敌人都在你面前。 ###EN### You know my reproach And my shame and my humiliation; All my adversaries are before You.
Verse_Ch: 69:20 辱骂伤破了我的心，我又忧愁难过；我指望有人体恤，却没有一个；我指望有人安慰，却找不着一个。 ###EN### Reproach has broken my heart, And I am sick; I looked for pity, but there was none; And for comforters, but I found none.
Verse_Ch: 69:21 他们拿苦胆给我当食物；我渴了，他们拿醋给我喝。 ###EN### But they gave me gall for my food, And for my thirst they gave me vinegar to drink.
Verse_Ch: 69:22 愿他们的筵席，在他们面前变为网罗，在他们平安的时候，变为陷阱。 ###EN### May their table become a snare before them And a trap when they are at peace.
Verse_Ch: 69:23 愿他们的眼睛昏蒙，不能看见；愿你使他们的腰常常战抖。 ###EN### May their eyes be darkened so that they cannot see; And make their loins shake continually.
Verse_Ch: 69:24 求你将你的恼恨，倒在他们身上；愿你的烈怒，追上他们。 ###EN### Pour out Your indignation upon them; And may the burning fierceness of Your anger overtake them.
Verse_Ch: 69:25 愿他们的营寨，变为荒凉；愿他们的帐棚，无人居住。 ###EN### May their camp be desolate; May there be no one to dwell in their tents.
Verse_Ch: 69:26 因为他们逼迫你所击打的人，数说你所击伤之人的伤痛。 ###EN### For they persecute him whom You have stricken, And they recount the pain of those whom You have wounded.
Verse_Ch: 69:27 求你在他们的罪孽上加罪孽，不要让他们进入你的义。 ###EN### Add iniquity to their iniquity, And do not let them come into Your righteousness.
Verse_Ch: 69:28 愿他们从生命册上被涂抹，不得与义人一同登录。 ###EN### May they be blotted out of the book of life, And may they not be written with the righteous.
Verse_Ch: 69:29 但我是困苦伤痛的；神阿，愿你的救恩将我安置在高处。 ###EN### But I am poor and pained; May Your salvation, O God, set me on high.
Verse_Ch: 69:30 我要以诗歌赞美神的名，以感谢尊祂为大； ###EN### I will praise the name of God with a song And will magnify Him with thanksgiving;
Verse_Ch: 69:31 这便叫耶和华看为美，胜似献牛，或是献有角有蹄的公牛。 ###EN### And it will be better to Jehovah than an ox Or a bull with horns and hooves.
Verse_Ch: 69:32 温柔的人看见了，就喜乐。寻求神的人，愿你们的心苏醒。 ###EN### The meek have seen it; they rejoice. You who seek God, let your heart revive.
Verse_Ch: 69:33 因为耶和华垂听了穷乏人，不藐视属祂被囚的人。 ###EN### For Jehovah listens to the needy, And He does not despise His prisoners.
Verse_Ch: 69:34 愿天和地，洋海和其中一切的动物，都赞美祂。 ###EN### Let the heavens and the earth praise Him, The seas and everything that moves in them.
Verse_Ch: 69:35 因为神要拯救锡安，建造犹大的城邑；祂的民要在那里居住，得以为业。 ###EN### For God will save Zion And build the cities of Judah; And they will abide there and possess it.
Verse_Ch: 69:36 祂仆人的后裔要承受为业，爱祂名的人也要住在其中。 ###EN### And the seed of His servants will inherit it, And those who love His name will dwell in it.
Chapter_Header: 70
Verse_Ch: 70:1 神阿，求你快快搭救我；耶和华阿，求你快快帮助我。 ###EN### O God, hasten to deliver me; O Jehovah, hasten to help me.
Verse_Ch: 70:2 愿那些寻索我命的，抱愧蒙羞；愿那些喜悦我遭难的，退后受辱。 ###EN### May those who seek my life Be put to shame and confounded; May those who take delight in my misfortune Be turned back and humiliated;
Verse_Ch: 70:3 愿那些对我说，阿哈，阿哈的，因羞愧退去。 ###EN### May those who say, Aha! Aha! Turn away because of their shame;
Verse_Ch: 70:4 愿一切寻求你的，因你欢喜快乐；愿那些爱你救恩的，常说，当尊神为大！ ###EN### May all those who seek You Be glad and rejoice in You; And may those who love Your salvation Say continually, May God be magnified!
Verse_Ch: 70:5 但我是困苦穷乏的；神阿，求你速速到我这里来。你是帮助我的，搭救我的；耶和华阿，求你不要耽延。 ###EN### But I am poor and needy; O God, hasten to me. You are my help and my Deliverer; O Jehovah, do not delay.
Chapter_Header: 71
Verse_Ch: 71:1 耶和华阿，我投靠你；求你叫我永不羞愧。 ###EN### In You, O Jehovah, do I take refuge; Never let me be put to shame.
Verse_Ch: 71:2 求你凭你的公义搭救我，救拔我；求你侧耳听我，拯救我。 ###EN### In Your righteousness deliver me and rescue me; Incline Your ear to me and save me.
Verse_Ch: 71:3 求你作我居住的磐石，使我可以常常进入其中。你已经命定要救我，因为你是我的岩石，我的山寨。 ###EN### Be to me a rock of habitation for me to come to continually. You have given command to save me, For You are my rock and my fortress.
Verse_Ch: 71:4 我的神阿，求你救我脱离恶人的手，脱离不义和残暴之人的手； ###EN### My God, rescue me from the hand of the wicked, From the hand of the unjust and cruel;
Verse_Ch: 71:5 因为主耶和华阿，你是我所盼望的，是我从年幼所倚靠的。 ###EN### For You are my hope, O Lord Jehovah, My trust from my youth.
Verse_Ch: 71:6 我从母胎中就受你扶持；使我出母腹的是你；我必常常赞美你。 ###EN### On You I have been sustained since birth; It was You who took from my mother's womb; My praise is continually of You.
Verse_Ch: 71:7 许多人以我为怪，但你是我坚固的避难所。 ###EN### I am like a wonder to many, But You are my strong refuge.
Verse_Ch: 71:8 我的口必终日满了赞美你、歌颂你荣耀的话。 ###EN### My mouth is filled with Your praise, With Your glory, all day long.
Verse_Ch: 71:9 我年老的时候，求你不要丢弃我；我力气衰弱的时候，求你不要离弃我。 ###EN### Do not cast me off in the time of old age; When my strength fails, do not forsake me.
Verse_Ch: 71:10 我的仇敌议论我，那些窥探要害我命的一同商议， ###EN### For my enemies speak concerning me, And those who watch for my soul take counsel together,
Verse_Ch: 71:11 说，神已经离弃他；我们追赶他，捉拿他罢，因为没有人搭救他。 ###EN### Saying, God has forsaken him; Pursue and lay hold of him, for there is no one to deliver him.
Verse_Ch: 71:12 神阿，求你不要远离我；我的神阿，求你速速帮助我。 ###EN### O God, do not be far away from me; My God, hasten to help me.
Verse_Ch: 71:13 愿那些与我性命为敌的，羞愧灭没；愿那些谋害我的，受辱蒙羞。 ###EN### May those who are the adversaries to my soul Be put to shame and consumed; May those who seek my misfortune Wrap themselves in reproach and humiliation.
Verse_Ch: 71:14 我却要常常盼望，并要越发赞美你。 ###EN### But I will hope continually And will add yet more to all Your praise.
Verse_Ch: 71:15 我的口终日要述说你的公义，和你的救恩，因我不知其数。 ###EN### My mouth will recount Your righteousness, Your salvation, all day long; For I do not know its full numbers.
Verse_Ch: 71:16 我要来见证主耶和华大能的作为；我要题说你独有的公义。 ###EN### I will come with the proof of the mighty acts of the Lord Jehovah; I will remind men of Your righteousness, Yours alone.
Verse_Ch: 71:17 神阿，自我年幼时，你就教训我；直到如今，我传扬你奇妙的作为。 ###EN### O God, You have taught me from my youth; And until now I have declared Your wondrous deeds.
Verse_Ch: 71:18 神阿，即使到我年老发白的时候，求你仍不离弃我，等我将你的能力指示下代，将你的大能指示后世的人。 ###EN### So even into my old age and greyheadedness, O God, do not forsake me, Until I have declared Your strength Unto the next generation, Your might unto everyone who is to come.
Verse_Ch: 71:19 神阿，你是行过大事的，你的公义甚高。神阿，谁能像你？ ###EN### And Your righteousness, O God, is so high, You who have done great things. O God, who is like You?
Verse_Ch: 71:20 你是叫我多经历重大急难的，必使我复活，使我从地的深处再上来。 ###EN### You who have shown me Many great troubles Will revive me again And bring me up again From the depths of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 71:21 你要使我越发昌大，且转来安慰我。 ###EN### You will increase my greatness And will turn and comfort me.
Verse_Ch: 71:22 我的神阿，我也要鼓瑟赞美你，赞美你的信实；以色列的圣者阿，我要弹琴歌颂你。 ###EN### I will also praise You with the harp, I will praise Your faithfulness, my God; I will sing psalms to You with the lyre, O Holy One of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 71:23 我歌颂你的时候，我的嘴唇，和你所救赎我的魂，都必欢呼。 ###EN### My lips will give a ringing shout When I sing psalms to You, And my soul, which You have redeemed.
Verse_Ch: 71:24 并且我的舌头，要终日讲论你的公义；因为那些谋害我的人，已经蒙羞受辱了。 ###EN### My tongue also will declare Your righteousness all day long; For they are put to shame, for they are confounded, They who seek my misfortune.
Chapter_Header: 72
Verse_Ch: 72:1 神阿，求你将你的判断赐给王，将你的公义赐给王的儿子。 ###EN### O God, give Your judgments to the king, And Your righteousness to the son of the king.
Verse_Ch: 72:2 祂要按公义审判你的民，按公平审判你的穷苦人。 ###EN### He will judge Your people in righteousness, And Your poor with justice.
Verse_Ch: 72:3 大山小山，都要在公义中给民结出平安的果子。 ###EN### The mountains will bear peace to the people, And the hills, in righteousness.
Verse_Ch: 72:4 祂必为民中的穷苦人伸冤，拯救穷乏之辈，压碎那欺压人的。 ###EN### He will judge the poor of the people; He will save the children of the needy And crush the oppressor.
Verse_Ch: 72:5 太阳还存，月亮还在，人要敬畏你，直到万代。 ###EN### They will fear You as long as the sun endures And as long as the moon endures Throughout the generations.
Verse_Ch: 72:6 祂必降临，像雨降在已割的草地上，如甘霖浇灌大地。 ###EN### He will drop like rain upon mown grass, Like abundant showers dripping on the earth.
Verse_Ch: 72:7 在祂的日子义人要发旺，大有平安，直到月亮不存。 ###EN### In His days the righteous will flourish, And there will be an abundance of peace Until the moon is no more.
Verse_Ch: 72:8 祂要执掌权柄，从这海直到那海，从大河直到地极。 ###EN### And He will have dominion from sea to sea And from the River unto the ends of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 72:9 住在荒野的，必在祂面前下拜，祂的仇敌必要舔土。 ###EN### The desert dwellers will bow down before Him, And His enemies will lick the dust.
Verse_Ch: 72:10 他施和海岛并沿海一带的王要进贡；示巴和西巴的王要献礼物。 ###EN### The kings of Tarshish and of the coastlands Will pay tribute; The kings of Sheba and Seba Will present gifts.
Verse_Ch: 72:11 诸王都要叩拜祂；万国都要事奉祂。 ###EN### And all the kings will bow down before Him; All the nations will serve Him.
Verse_Ch: 72:12 因为穷乏人呼求的时候，祂要搭救，没有人帮助的穷苦人，祂也要搭救。 ###EN### For He will deliver the needy man when he cries, And the poor man who has no one to help him.
