Verse_Ch: 72:13 祂要怜惜贫寒和穷乏的人，拯救穷乏人的性命。 ###EN### He will have pity on the weak and needy, And the souls of the needy He will save.
Verse_Ch: 72:14 祂要救赎他们的性命脱离欺压和强暴，他们的血在祂眼中看为宝贵。 ###EN### From oppression and violence He will redeem their soul, And their blood will be precious in His sight.
Verse_Ch: 72:15 祂要长久活着，示巴的金子要奉给祂；人要常常为祂祷告，终日颂赞祂。 ###EN### So He shall live and to Him shall be given The gold of Sheba; And prayer shall be made continually for Him; He shall be blessed all the day long.
Verse_Ch: 72:16 在地上，甚至在山顶上，五谷必然茂盛。所结的谷实，要摇曳如利巴嫩的树林；城里的人要发旺如地上的草。 ###EN### There will be an abundance of grain on the earth, Even at the tops of the mountains. Its fruit will wave like the forests of Lebanon, And those of the city will blossom like the foliage of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 72:17 祂的名要存到永远，要留传如日之久；人要因祂蒙福；万国要称祂有福。 ###EN### His name will be forever; As long as the sun endures, His name will spread; And men will be blessed in Him; All the nations will call Him blessed.
Verse_Ch: 72:18 独行奇事的耶和华神，以色列的神，是当受颂赞的； ###EN### Blessed be Jehovah God, the God of Israel, Who alone does wondrous deeds;
Verse_Ch: 72:19 祂荣耀的名也当受颂赞，直到永远；愿祂的荣耀充满全地。阿们，阿们。 ###EN### And blessed be His glorious name forever; And may His glory fill the whole earth. Amen and Amen.
Verse_Ch: 72:20 耶西的儿子大卫的祷告完毕。 ###EN### The prayers of David the son of Jesse are ended.
Chapter_Header: 73
Verse_Ch: 73:1 神实在善待以色列那些清心的人。 ###EN### Surely God is good to Israel, To those who are pure in heart.
Verse_Ch: 73:2 至于我，我的脚几乎失闪；我的脚步险些滑跌。 ###EN### But as for me, my feet were nearly turned aside; My steps had almost slipped.
Verse_Ch: 73:3 我见恶人兴旺，就嫉妒狂傲人。 ###EN### For I was envious of the arrogant, When I saw the prosperity of the wicked.
Verse_Ch: 73:4 他们死的时候没有疼痛，他们的身体也肥壮。 ###EN### For they have no pangs in their death, And their body is well nourished.
Verse_Ch: 73:5 他们没有别人所受的苦，也不像别人遭灾难。 ###EN### They do not find themselves in the hardship of men, Nor are they plagued like other men.
Verse_Ch: 73:6 所以，骄傲是他们的项链；强暴像他们遮身的衣裳。 ###EN### Therefore pride is a necklace for them, Violence covers them like a garment.
Verse_Ch: 73:7 他们的眼睛因体胖而凸出，他们心里的幻想肆意泛滥。 ###EN### Their eyes bulge out from fatness; The imaginations of their heart overflow.
Verse_Ch: 73:8 他们讥笑人，凭恶意说欺压人的话；他们说话高傲。 ###EN### They mock and wickedly speak of oppression; They speak loftily.
Verse_Ch: 73:9 他们的口亵渎诸天，他们的舌毁谤全地。 ###EN### They set their mouth against the heavens, And their tongue walks about on the earth.
Verse_Ch: 73:10 所以祂的民归回这里，充盈的水都被他们喝尽了； ###EN### Therefore his people return here, And waters of abundance are drained by them;
Verse_Ch: 73:11 他们说，神怎能晓得？至高者岂有知识么？ ###EN### And they say, How does God know? And is there knowledge with the Most High?
Verse_Ch: 73:12 看哪，这些就是恶人；他们常享安逸，积聚财宝。 ###EN### Behold, these are the wicked; And always at ease, they heap up riches.
Verse_Ch: 73:13 我实在徒然洁净了我的心，徒然洗手表明无辜； ###EN### Surely I have purified my heart in vain, And I have washed my hands in innocence.
Verse_Ch: 73:14 因为我终日遭灾难，每早晨受惩治。 ###EN### For I have been plagued all day long And chastened every morning.
Verse_Ch: 73:15 我若说，我要这样讲；看哪，我就是对你这一代的众子不忠了。 ###EN### If I had said, I will speak thus; Behold, I would have betrayed the generation of Your children.
Verse_Ch: 73:16 我思索要明白这事，眼看实系为难； ###EN### When I considered this in order to understand it, It was a troublesome task in my sight,
Verse_Ch: 73:17 等我进了神的圣所，我才看清他们的结局。 ###EN### Until I went into the sanctuary of God; Then I perceived their end.
Verse_Ch: 73:18 你实在把他们安在滑地，使他们掉在荒废之中。 ###EN### Surely You set them in slippery places; You cast them down into ruins.
Verse_Ch: 73:19 他们转眼之间，成了何等的荒凉！他们被惊恐灭尽了。 ###EN### How they are made desolate in a moment! They are utterly consumed by terrors.
Verse_Ch: 73:20 人睡醒了怎样看梦，主阿，你醒了，也必照样轻看他们的影像。 ###EN### Like a dream, when one awakes, You, O Lord, Upon arising, will despise their image.
Verse_Ch: 73:21 当时我心里酸苦，肺腑被刺， ###EN### When my heart was embittered, And inwardly I was pricked;
Verse_Ch: 73:22 我是蠢笨无知，在你面前如畜类一般。 ###EN### I was brutish and knew nothing; I was like a beast before You.
Verse_Ch: 73:23 然而我常与你同在；你紧握着我的右手。 ###EN### Nevertheless I am continually with You; You have taken hold of my right hand.
Verse_Ch: 73:24 你要以你的劝言引导我，以后必接我到荣耀里。 ###EN### You will guide me with Your counsel, And afterward You will receive me in glory.
Verse_Ch: 73:25 除你以外，在天上我有谁呢？除你以外，在地上我也没有所爱慕的。 ###EN### Whom do I have in heaven but You? And besides You there is nothing I desire on earth.
Verse_Ch: 73:26 我的肉体和我的心肠衰残，但神是我心里的磐石，又是我的业分，直到永远。 ###EN### My flesh and my heart fail, But God is the rock of my heart and my portion forever.
Verse_Ch: 73:27 看哪，远离你的，必要灭亡；凡离弃你行邪淫的，你都灭绝了。 ###EN### For behold, those who are far from You will perish; You destroy all who go about as harlots away from You.
Verse_Ch: 73:28 但我亲近神是与我有益；我以主耶和华为我的避难所，好叫我述说你一切的作为。 ###EN### But as for me, drawing near to God is good for me; I have made the Lord Jehovah my refuge, That I may declare all Your works.
Chapter_Header: 74
Verse_Ch: 74:1 神阿，你为何永远丢弃我们呢？你的怒气为何向你草场的羊如烟冒出呢？ ###EN### Why, O God, have You cast us off forever? Why does Your anger smoke against the sheep of Your pasture?
Verse_Ch: 74:2 求你记念你古时所买来的会众，就是你所赎作你产业支派的，并记念你所居住的锡安山。 ###EN### Remember Your assembly, which You have purchased of old, Which You have redeemed as the tribe of Your inheritance, And Mount Zion, where You dwell.
Verse_Ch: 74:3 求你举步到那长久荒凉之地；仇敌在圣所中将一切尽行毁灭。 ###EN### Lift up Your steps unto the perpetual ruins; The enemy has damaged everything in the sanctuary.
Verse_Ch: 74:4 你的敌人在你会所中吼叫；他们竖了自己的旗号为标帜。 ###EN### Your adversaries have roared in the midst of Your assembly place; They have set up their symbols as signs.
Verse_Ch: 74:5 他们好像人扬起斧子，砍伐林中的树。 ###EN### It looked like when men bring up axes On the thicket of the trees.
Verse_Ch: 74:6 圣所中一切的雕刻，现在他们都用斧子、锤子打坏了。 ###EN### And now they have struck down with hatchet and hammer Its carved work altogether.
Verse_Ch: 74:7 他们用火焚烧你的圣所，亵渎你名的住处，拆毁到地。 ###EN### They have set fire to Your sanctuary; They have defiled the dwelling place of Your name to the ground.
Verse_Ch: 74:8 他们心里说，我们要把这些尽行毁灭；他们就把神在地上的会所都烧毁了。 ###EN### They said in their heart, Let us oppress them completely. They have burned down all God's assembly places in the land.
Verse_Ch: 74:9 我们不见我们的标帜；不再有申言者；我们内中也没有人知道这灾祸要到几时。 ###EN### We do not see our signs; there is no longer a prophet, Nor is there anyone among us who knows how long.
Verse_Ch: 74:10 神阿，敌人辱骂要到几时呢？仇敌藐视你的名，要到永远么？ ###EN### How long, O God, will the adversary reproach? Will the enemy despise Your name forever?
Verse_Ch: 74:11 你为什么缩回你的手，缩回你的右手？求你从怀中伸出来，毁灭他们。 ###EN### Why do You withdraw Your hand, even Your right hand? Bring it forth from the midst of Your bosom; destroy them .
Verse_Ch: 74:12 但神自古以来为我的王，在全地中施行拯救。 ###EN### But God is my King of old, Accomplishing salvation in the midst of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 74:13 你曾用能力把海分开，将水上海蛇的头打破。 ###EN### You divided the sea by Your strength; You broke the heads of the sea serpents on the waters.
Verse_Ch: 74:14 你曾砸碎鳄鱼的头，把它给荒野的禽兽为食物。 ###EN### You crushed the heads of the leviathan; You gave him as food to the creatures of the desert.
Verse_Ch: 74:15 你曾开出泉源和急流；你使长流的江河干了。 ###EN### You broke open the fountain and the torrent; You dried up the ever-flowing streams.
Verse_Ch: 74:16 白昼属你，黑夜也属你；月亮和日头是你所预备的。 ###EN### The day is Yours; the night also is Yours; You prepared the moon and the sun.
Verse_Ch: 74:17 地的一切疆界，是你所立的；夏天和冬天是你所定的。 ###EN### You established all the borders of the earth: You formed the summer and the winter.
Verse_Ch: 74:18 耶和华阿，仇敌辱骂你，愚顽民藐视你的名，求你记念这事。 ###EN### Remember this: The enemy has reproached Jehovah, And a foolish people has despised Your name.
Verse_Ch: 74:19 不要将你斑鸠的性命交给野兽；不要永远忘记你穷苦人的生命。 ###EN### Do not give the soul of Your turtledove to the wild beast; Do not forget the life of Your poor forever.
Verse_Ch: 74:20 求你顾念所立的约，因为地上黑暗之处，都满了强暴的居所。 ###EN### Regard the covenant, For the dark places of the earth are full of the habitations of violence.
Verse_Ch: 74:21 不要叫受欺压的人蒙羞回去。愿困苦穷乏的人赞美你的名。 ###EN### Do not let him who is oppressed return ashamed. May the poor and needy praise Your name.
Verse_Ch: 74:22 神阿，求你起来，为自己伸诉；要记念愚顽人怎样终日辱骂你。 ###EN### Arise, O God; contend for Your own cause; Remember how the foolish man reproaches You all day long.
Verse_Ch: 74:23 不要忘记你敌人的声音；那起来敌你之人的喧哗时常上升。 ###EN### Do not forget the voice of Your adversaries; The roar of those who rise up against You goes up continually.
Chapter_Header: 75
Verse_Ch: 75:1 神阿，我们称谢你，我们称谢你，因为你的名相近，人都述说你奇妙的作为。 ###EN### We give thanks to You, O God; we give thanks, For Your name is near; men tell of Your wondrous deeds.
Verse_Ch: 75:2 你说，我选定日期，必按公正施行审判。 ###EN### When I choose the appointed time, It is I who judge with equity.
Verse_Ch: 75:3 地和其上一切的居民，都融化了；我曾立了地的柱子。 细拉 ###EN### The earth and all who dwell in it melt; I have established its pillars.
Verse_Ch: 75:4 我对狂傲人说，不要狂傲；对凶恶人说，不要举角； ###EN### I said to the boastful, Do not boast; And to the wicked, Do not lift up the horn.
Verse_Ch: 75:5 不要把你们的角高举；不要挺着颈项说狂妄话。 ###EN### Do not lift your horn on high; Do not speak arrogantly with a haughty neck.
Verse_Ch: 75:6 因为高举非从东，非从西，也非从南而来。 ###EN### For neither from the east nor from the west, And neither from the south, does exaltation come;
Verse_Ch: 75:7 惟有神断定：祂使这人降卑，使那人升高。 ###EN### For God is the Judge: He puts this one down and exalts that one.
Verse_Ch: 75:8 耶和华手里有杯，其中的酒起沫；杯内满了搀杂之物，祂倒出来；地上的恶人必都喝这酒的渣滓，而且喝尽。 ###EN### For there is a cup in the hand of Jehovah, And the wine foams; it is full of mixture, And He pours from it; indeed its dregs will all the wicked of the earth Drain off and drink up.
Verse_Ch: 75:9 至于我，我要宣扬直到永远；我要歌颂雅各的神。 ###EN### But as for me, I will declare forever, I will sing psalms to the God of Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 75:10 恶人一切的角，我要砍断；惟有义人的角，必被高举。 ###EN### And all the horns of the wicked will I cut off, But the horns of the righteous man will be exalted.
Chapter_Header: 76
Verse_Ch: 76:1 在犹大神为人所认识；在以色列祂的名为大。 ###EN### God is known in Judah; His name is great in Israel.
Verse_Ch: 76:2 在撒冷有祂的帐幕；在锡安有祂的居所。 ###EN### And in Salem is His tabernacle, And His dwelling place, in Zion.
Verse_Ch: 76:3 祂在那里折断弓上的火箭，并盾牌、刀剑、和争战的兵器。 细拉 ###EN### There He broke the flashing arrows of the bow, The shield and the sword and the battle.
Verse_Ch: 76:4 你比富有猎物的山，更有光华和荣美。 ###EN### More glorious are You, More excellent than the mountains of prey.
Verse_Ch: 76:5 心中勇敢的人，都被掠夺；他们睡了长觉，没有一个勇士能措手。 ###EN### The stouthearted are despoiled; They slept their sleep, And none of the men of strength Have found their hands.
Verse_Ch: 76:6 雅各的神阿，你的斥责一发，坐车的和骑马的都沉睡了。 ###EN### At Your rebuke, O God of Jacob, Both chariot and horse fall into deep sleep.
Verse_Ch: 76:7 惟独你是可畏的；你的怒气一发，谁能在你面前站得住呢？ ###EN### You, indeed You, are to be feared; And who may stand before You once You are angry?
Verse_Ch: 76:8 你从天上使人听见判断；地惧怕而静默， ###EN### You caused judgment to be heard from the heavens; The earth feared and was still,
Verse_Ch: 76:9 那时神起来施行审判，要救地上一切卑微的人。 细拉 ###EN### When God rose for judgment, To save all the meek of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 76:10 人的忿怒，要使你得称赞；你要以你的余怒束腰。 ###EN### For the wrath of man will praise You; You will gird Yourself with the remainder of wrath.
Verse_Ch: 76:11 你们要许愿，并向耶和华你们的神还愿；在祂四围的人，都当拿贡物献给那可畏的主。 ###EN### Make vows and pay them to Jehovah your God; Let all who are around Him bring gifts to Him who is to be feared.
Verse_Ch: 76:12 祂要挫折众领袖的骄气；祂向地上的君王，显为可畏。 ###EN### He will cut off the spirit of the princes; He is terrible to the kings of the earth.
Chapter_Header: 77
Verse_Ch: 77:1 我要向神发声呼求；我向神发声，祂必侧耳听我。 ###EN### My voice calls out to God, and I will cry out; My voice calls out to God, and He will give ear to me.
Verse_Ch: 77:2 我在急难之日寻求主；我在夜间伸手祷告，总不懈怠。我的魂不肯受安慰。 ###EN### In the day of my distress I sought the Lord; My hand was stretched out in the night, and it did not drop. My soul refused to be comforted.
Verse_Ch: 77:3 我想念神，就悲叹不安；我哀怨不平，灵便发昏。 细拉 ###EN### I remember God, and I moan; I complain, and my spirit faints.
Verse_Ch: 77:4 你叫我不能闭眼；我烦乱不安，不能说话。 ###EN### You hold open my eyelids; I am disturbed and cannot speak.
Verse_Ch: 77:5 我追想古时之日，上古之年； ###EN### I consider the days of old, The years of ancient times;
Verse_Ch: 77:6 我想起我夜间的歌曲；我的心沉思默想，我的灵也仔细省察。 ###EN### I remember my song in the night; I muse with my own heart, and my spirit carefully searches.
Verse_Ch: 77:7 难道主要永远丢弃我们，不再喜悦我们么？ ###EN### Will the Lord cast us off forever, And will He never be favorable to us again?
Verse_Ch: 77:8 难道祂的慈爱永远止息，祂的应许世世断绝么？ ###EN### Has His lovingkindness ceased forever? Has the promise come to an end for all generations?
Verse_Ch: 77:9 难道神忘记开恩，因发怒就止住祂的怜恤么？ 细拉 ###EN### Has God forgotten to be gracious? Or has He in anger shut up His compassions?
Verse_Ch: 77:10 我便说，这是我的懦弱；但我要追念至高者右手所赐的年代。 ###EN### Then I said, This is my infirmity; These are the years given me from the right hand of the Most High.
Verse_Ch: 77:11 我要回想耶和华所行的，因我要记念你古时的奇事。 ###EN### I will bring to remembrance the deeds of Jehovah, For I will remember Your wonders from of old.
Verse_Ch: 77:12 我也要默想你一切所行的，默念你的作为。 ###EN### And I will meditate on all that You have done And muse on Your doings.
Verse_Ch: 77:13 神阿，你的道路是在圣所中；有何神明大如神呢？ ###EN### O God, Your way is in the sanctuary; Who is so great a god as God?
Verse_Ch: 77:14 你是行奇事的神；你曾在众民中，使人得知你的能力。 ###EN### You are the God who does wonders; You have made known Your strength among the peoples.
Verse_Ch: 77:15 你曾用你的膀臂赎了你的民，就是雅各和约瑟的子孙。 细拉 ###EN### You redeemed Your people with Your arm, The sons of Jacob and Joseph.
Verse_Ch: 77:16 神阿，诸水见你；诸水一见，就都惊惶；深渊也都战抖。 ###EN### The waters saw You, O God; The waters saw You; they were afraid; Indeed the depths trembled.
Verse_Ch: 77:17 云中倒出水来；天空发出响声；你的箭也闪射四方。 ###EN### The clouds poured forth water; The skies sent forth a sound; Indeed Your arrows went here and there.
Verse_Ch: 77:18 你的雷声在旋风中；闪电照亮世界；大地战抖震动。 ###EN### The sound of Your thunder was in the whirlwind; Lightning illuminated the world; The earth trembled and quaked.
Verse_Ch: 77:19 你的道路在海中，你的路径在大水中；你的脚踪无人知道。 ###EN### Your way was in the sea, And Your paths in the great waters; And Your footsteps were not known.
Verse_Ch: 77:20 你曾藉摩西和亚伦的手，引导你的百姓，好像羊群一般。 ###EN### You led Your people like a flock By the hand of Moses and Aaron.
Chapter_Header: 78
Verse_Ch: 78:1 我的民哪，你们要留心听我的教训，侧耳听我口中的话。 ###EN### Give ear, O my people, to my instruction; Incline your ears to the words of my mouth.
Verse_Ch: 78:2 我要开口说比喻；我要说出古时的谜语， ###EN### I will open my mouth in a parable; I will utter riddles from of old,
Verse_Ch: 78:3 是我们所听见所知道的，也是我们的祖宗向我们所述说的。 ###EN### Which we have heard and known, And our fathers have related to us.
Verse_Ch: 78:4 我们不将这些事向他们的子孙隐瞒，要将耶和华当得的赞美，和祂的能力，并祂所作的奇事，述说给后代听。 ###EN### We will not hide them from their children, But will relate to the generation to come The praises of Jehovah and His strength And His wondrous deeds that He has done.
Verse_Ch: 78:5 因为祂在雅各中立了见证，在以色列中设了律法，是祂吩咐我们祖宗，要他们给子孙知道的； ###EN### Indeed He has established a testimony in Jacob And appointed a law in Israel, Which He commanded our fathers That they should make them known to their children;
Verse_Ch: 78:6 使将要生的后代子孙，可以晓得；他们也要起来向他们的子孙述说； ###EN### That the generation to come, The children to be born, may know them, Who should arise and relate them to their children;
Verse_Ch: 78:7 好叫他们寄望于神，不忘记神的作为，惟要遵守祂的命令； ###EN### That they might set their hope in God, And not forget the deeds of God, But observe His commandments;
Verse_Ch: 78:8 不至像他们的祖宗，是顽梗悖逆、居心不正之辈，他们的灵向着神不忠信。 ###EN### That they might not be like their fathers, A stubborn and rebellious generation, A generation that did not set their heart right, And whose spirit was not faithful to God.
Verse_Ch: 78:9 以法莲的子孙，带着兵器，拿着弓箭，临阵之日却转身退后。 ###EN### The children of Ephraim, armed archers with bows, Turned back in the day of battle.
Verse_Ch: 78:10 他们不遵守神的约，不肯遵行祂的律法； ###EN### They did not keep the covenant of God, And they refused to walk in His law.
Verse_Ch: 78:11 又忘记祂所行的，和祂向他们所显奇妙的作为。 ###EN### And they forgot His doings And His wondrous deeds that He had shown them.
Verse_Ch: 78:12 祂在埃及地，在琐安田，在他们祖宗的眼前，施行奇事。 ###EN### He did something wonderful in the sight of their fathers In the land of Egypt, in the field of Zoan.
Verse_Ch: 78:13 祂将海分开，使他们过去，又叫水立起如垒。 ###EN### He divided the sea and caused them to pass through, And He made the water stand as a heap.
Verse_Ch: 78:14 祂白日用云彩，终夜用火光，引导他们。 ###EN### And He led them with the cloud by day And all the night with a light of fire.
Verse_Ch: 78:15 祂在旷野裂开磐石，多多的给他们水喝，如从深渊而出。 ###EN### He split rocks in the wilderness And gave them abundant drink, as from the depths.
Verse_Ch: 78:16 祂使水从磐石涌出，叫水如江河流下。 ###EN### He also brought forth streams from the rock And made water run down like rivers.
Verse_Ch: 78:17 他们却仍旧得罪祂，在干旱之地悖逆至高者。 ###EN### Yet they still continued to sin against Him, To rebel against the Most High in the desert.
Verse_Ch: 78:18 他们心中试探神，随自己所欲的求食物； ###EN### And they put God to the test in their heart, By asking for food according to their desire.
Verse_Ch: 78:19 并且出言顶撞神，说，神岂能在旷野摆设筵席么？ ###EN### They also spoke against God; They said, Can God prepare a table in the wilderness?
Verse_Ch: 78:20 看哪，祂曾击打磐石，使水涌出，如同江河泛滥；祂还能赐粮食么？还能为祂的百姓预备肉么？ ###EN### Behold, He struck the rock, And water gushed out, And streams overflowed; Can He also give us bread, Or provide meat for His people?
Verse_Ch: 78:21 所以耶和华听见，就发怒。有火向雅各烧起，有怒气向以色列上腾； ###EN### Therefore Jehovah heard and was angry. And a fire was kindled against Jacob, And also anger went up against Israel;
Verse_Ch: 78:22 因为他们不相信神，不倚靠祂的救恩。 ###EN### Because they did not believe in God, And they did not trust in His salvation.
Verse_Ch: 78:23 祂却吩咐在上的穹苍，又敞开天上的门， ###EN### Yet He commanded the skies above And opened the doors of heaven;
Verse_Ch: 78:24 降吗哪像雨给他们吃，将天上的粮食赐给他们。 ###EN### And He rained down upon them manna to eat And gave them the food of heaven.
Verse_Ch: 78:25 人吃大能者的食物；祂差下粮食，使他们饱足。 ###EN### Man ate the bread of the mighty; He sent them full provision.
Verse_Ch: 78:26 祂使东风在天空刮起，又用能力引来南风。 ###EN### He made the east wind blow in the heavens And guided the south wind by His strength.
Verse_Ch: 78:27 祂降肉像雨给他们，多如尘土，又降飞鸟，多如海沙， ###EN### And He rained upon them meat like dust, And winged birds like the sand of the seas.
Verse_Ch: 78:28 落在他们的营中，在他们住处的四围。 ###EN### And He made it fall in the midst of their camp, Around their habitations.
Verse_Ch: 78:29 他们吃了，而且极其饱足；这样，祂就随了他们所欲的。 ###EN### So they ate and were well filled; Indeed what they desired He brought to them.
Verse_Ch: 78:30 他们贪而无厌，食物还在口中的时候， ###EN### They were not estranged from what they desired; Their food was still in their mouths
Verse_Ch: 78:31 神的怒气就向他们上腾，杀了他们内中的肥壮人，打倒以色列的少年人。 ###EN### When the anger of God went up against them And slew some of their fattest ones And struck down the choice men of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 78:32 虽经这一切，他们仍旧犯罪，不相信祂奇妙的作为。 ###EN### In spite of all this they still sinned And did not believe in His wondrous deeds.
Verse_Ch: 78:33 因此祂使他们的日子在虚空中耗尽，使他们的年岁在惊恐中度完。 ###EN### Therefore He consumed their days with vanity, And their years with terror.
Verse_Ch: 78:34 祂杀他们的时候，他们才求问祂，回转过来，切切的寻求神。 ###EN### When He slew them, they inquired after Him, And they returned and diligently sought God.
Verse_Ch: 78:35 他们也追念神是他们的磐石，至高的神是他们的救赎主。 ###EN### And they remembered that God was their rock, And the Most High God, their Redeemer.
Verse_Ch: 78:36 他们却用口谄媚祂，用舌向祂说谎。 ###EN### But they flattered Him with their mouth And lied to Him with their tongue.
Verse_Ch: 78:37 因他们的心向祂不坚定，在祂的约上也不忠信。 ###EN### For their heart was not steadfast toward Him, Nor were they faithful to His covenant.
Verse_Ch: 78:38 但祂有怜悯，遮盖他们的罪孽，不灭绝他们；而且屡次使自己的怒气转消，不发尽祂的忿怒。 ###EN### But He, being merciful, forgave their iniquity And did not destroy them; Indeed He turned back His anger many times And did not stir up all His wrath.
Verse_Ch: 78:39 祂想到他们不过是肉体，是一阵去而不返的风。 ###EN### And He remembered that they were flesh, A wind that goes away and does not return.
Verse_Ch: 78:40 他们在旷野悖逆祂，在荒地叫祂担忧，何其多呢！ ###EN### How often they rebelled against Him in the wilderness And grieved Him in the desert!
Verse_Ch: 78:41 他们再三试探神，惹动以色列的圣者。 ###EN### And they repeatedly put God to the test And provoked the Holy One of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 78:42 他们不追念祂的能力，和赎他们脱离敌人的日子； ###EN### They did not remember His hand, The day when He ransomed them from the adversary;
Verse_Ch: 78:43 那时祂在埃及显神迹，在琐安田显奇事， ###EN### When He set His signs in Egypt And His wonders in the field of Zoan;
Verse_Ch: 78:44 把他们的江河与溪流都变为血，使他们不能喝。 ###EN### And He turned their rivers into blood, As well as their streams, so that they could not drink.
Verse_Ch: 78:45 祂打发苍蝇成群，落在他们中间，嘬尽他们；又打发青蛙毁坏他们； ###EN### He sent among them a swarm offlies, which devoured them; And frogs, which destroyed them.
Verse_Ch: 78:46 祂把他们地里的出产交给毁蝗，把他们劳碌得来的交给群蝗。 ###EN### And He gave their increase to the consuming locust, And their labor to the swarming locust.
Verse_Ch: 78:47 祂用冰雹打坏他们的葡萄树，用严霜打坏他们的桑树； ###EN### And He killed their vines with hail, And their sycamores with ice stones.
Verse_Ch: 78:48 又把他们的牲畜交给冰雹，把他们的群畜交给闪电。 ###EN### He gave over their cattle also to the hail And their herds to the lightning bolts.
Verse_Ch: 78:49 祂打发猛烈的怒气、盛怒、恼恨和苦难，成了一群降灾祸的使者，进入他们中间。 ###EN### He sent among them the burning fierceness of His anger, Overflowing wrath and indignation and trouble, A mission of angels of evils.
Verse_Ch: 78:50 祂为自己的怒气修平了路，不使他们的魂免于死亡，乃将他们的生命交给瘟疫。 ###EN### He leveled a path for His anger; He did not spare their soul from death, But gave their life over to the pestilence.
Verse_Ch: 78:51 祂在埃及击杀一切头生的，在含的帐棚中，击杀他们力量强壮时头生的。 ###EN### And He struck all the firstborn in Egypt, The first of their vigor in the tents of Ham.
Verse_Ch: 78:52 祂却领出自己的民如羊，在旷野引他们如羊群。 ###EN### But He set forth His people like sheep And led them like a flock in the wilderness.
Verse_Ch: 78:53 祂领他们稳稳妥妥的，使他们不至害怕；海却淹没他们的仇敌。 ###EN### And He led them to safety, so that they did not fear; But the sea covered their enemies.
Verse_Ch: 78:54 祂带他们到自己圣地的境界，到祂右手所得的这山。 ###EN### And He brought them forth to His holy border, The mountain, which His right hand had acquired.
Verse_Ch: 78:55 祂在他们面前赶出外邦人，用绳子将外邦的地量给他们，拈阄分给他们为业，叫以色列支派的人在那里住在他们的帐棚里。 ###EN### And He drove out the nations before them And allotted them as an inheritance by line, And He made the tribes of Israel dwell there in their tents.
Verse_Ch: 78:56 他们仍旧试探、悖逆至高的神，不持守祂的见证； ###EN### Yet they put Him to the test and rebelled against God the Most High, And did not keep His testimonies.
Verse_Ch: 78:57 反倒退后，行诡诈，像他们的祖宗一样；他们翻转，如同诡诈的弓。 ###EN### And they turned back and dealt treacherously, as their fathers had done; They turned aside like a deceitfulbow.
Verse_Ch: 78:58 他们用邱坛惹了祂的怒气，用雕制的偶像触动祂的妒忌。 ###EN### Indeed they provoked Him to anger with their high places And made Him jealous with their graven images.
Verse_Ch: 78:59 神听见就发怒，极其厌恶以色列人。 ###EN### God heard, and He was angered; And He greatly abhorred Israel.
Verse_Ch: 78:60 于是祂离弃示罗的帐幕，就是祂在人间所搭的帐棚； ###EN### Thus He forsook the tabernacle in Shiloh, The tent in which He dwelt among men;
Verse_Ch: 78:61 又将祂的约柜交与人掳去，将祂的荣美交在敌人手中。 ###EN### And He gave over His ark into captivity, And His glory into the hand of the adversary.
Verse_Ch: 78:62 并将祂的百姓交与刀剑，向祂的产业发怒。 ###EN### He also delivered His people to the sword And was angry with His inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 78:63 他们的少年人被火烧灭，他们的处女也无喜歌。 ###EN### Fire devoured their young men, And their virgins had no marriage song.
Verse_Ch: 78:64 他们的祭司倒在刀下，他们的寡妇却不哀哭。 ###EN### Their priests fell by the sword, And their widows did not lament.
Verse_Ch: 78:65 那时主如同睡醒，像勇士因饮酒呼喊。 ###EN### Then the Lord awoke as if from sleep, Like a mighty man who shouts because of wine.
Verse_Ch: 78:66 祂打退了祂的敌人，叫他们永蒙羞辱。 ###EN### And He struck His adversaries and sent them back; He put an everlasting reproach upon them.
Verse_Ch: 78:67 并且祂弃掉约瑟的帐棚，不拣选以法莲支派， ###EN### And He rejected the tent of Joseph, And the tribe of Ephraim He did not choose.
Verse_Ch: 78:68 却拣选犹大支派，祂所爱的锡安山。 ###EN### Rather He chose the tribe of Judah, Mount Zion, which He loved.
Verse_Ch: 78:69 祂盖造祂的圣所，好像高峰，又像祂所建立永存之地。 ###EN### And He built His sanctuary like the heights, Like the earth that He has founded forever.
Verse_Ch: 78:70 又拣选祂的仆人大卫，从羊圈中选取了他； ###EN### Moreover He chose David His servant And took him from the sheepfolds;
Verse_Ch: 78:71 叫他不再跟从那些带奶的母羊，为要牧养自己的百姓雅各，和自己的产业以色列。 ###EN### From following after the ewes He brought him To shepherd Jacob His people And Israel His inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 78:72 于是，他按心中的纯全牧养他们，用手中的巧妙引导他们。 ###EN### And he shepherded them according to the integrity of his heart, And guided them by the skillfulness of his hands.
Chapter_Header: 79
Verse_Ch: 79:1 神阿，外邦人进入你的产业，污秽你的圣殿，使耶路撒冷变成了荒堆。 ###EN### O God, the nations have come into Your inheritance; They have defiled Your holy temple; They have turned Jerusalem into heaps.
Verse_Ch: 79:2 他们把你仆人的尸首，交与天空的飞鸟为食，把你圣民的肉，交与地上的野兽； ###EN### They have given the dead bodies of Your servants As food for the birds of heaven, The flesh of Your saints to the animals of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 79:3 在耶路撒冷周围流他们的血如水，无人葬埋。 ###EN### They have poured out their blood like water around Jerusalem, And there was no one to bury them.
Verse_Ch: 79:4 我们成为邻国所羞辱的，成为我们四围人所嗤笑讥刺的。 ###EN### We have become a reproach to our neighbors, A mocking and a derision to those around us.
Verse_Ch: 79:5 耶和华阿，这要到几时呢？你要动怒到永远么？你的妒忌要如火焚烧么？ ###EN### How long, O Jehovah? Will You be angry forever? Will Your jealousy burn like fire?
Verse_Ch: 79:6 愿你将你的忿怒倒在那不认识你的外邦，和那不呼求你名的国度。 ###EN### Pour out Your wrath upon the nations Who do not know You, And upon the kingdoms Who do not call upon Your name.
Verse_Ch: 79:7 因为他们侵吞了雅各，使他的住处变为荒凉。 ###EN### For they have devoured Jacob And have desolated his habitation.
Verse_Ch: 79:8 求你不要记念我们先祖的罪孽，向我们追讨；愿你的怜恤快快迎着我们，因为我们落到极卑微的地步。 ###EN### Do not remember against us the iniquities of our forefathers; May Your compassions quickly meet us, For we have been brought very low.
Verse_Ch: 79:9 拯救我们的神阿，求你因你名的荣耀，帮助我们；为你名的缘故，搭救我们，遮盖我们的罪。 ###EN### Help us, O God of our salvation, For the glory of Your name; And deliver us and expiate our sins, For Your name's sake.
Verse_Ch: 79:10 为何容外邦人说，他们的神在那里呢？愿你使我们亲眼看见，外邦人得知你伸了你仆人流血的冤。 ###EN### Why should the nations say, Where is their God? May the avenging of the blood of Your servants, which has been poured out, Be known among the nations in our sight.
Verse_Ch: 79:11 愿被囚之人的叹息，达到你面前。愿你按你的大能力，使那些命定要死的人得以存活。 ###EN### May the sighing of the prisoner come before You. According to the greatness of Your power preserve those appointed to die,
Verse_Ch: 79:12 主阿，愿你将我们邻国所羞辱你的羞辱，七倍归还到他们怀中。 ###EN### And render to our neighbors sevenfold into their bosom Their reproach, with which they have reproached You, O Lord.
Verse_Ch: 79:13 我们，就是你的民并你草场的羊，要称谢你，直到永远；我们要述说赞美你的话，直到万代。 ###EN### And we, Your people and the sheep of Your pasture, Will give You thanks forever; From generation to generation we will tell out Your praise.
Chapter_Header: 80
Verse_Ch: 80:1 领约瑟如领羊群之以色列的牧者阿，求你侧耳听；坐在二基路伯之间的阿，求你发出光来。 ###EN### O Shepherd of Israel, give ear, You who lead Joseph like a flock; You who sit between the cherubim, shine forth.
Verse_Ch: 80:2 求你在以法莲、便雅悯、玛拿西前面施展你的大能，来救我们。 ###EN### Before Ephraim and Benjamin and Manasseh Stir up Your might, And come to save us.
Verse_Ch: 80:3 神阿，求你恢复我们，使你的脸发光，我们便要得救。 ###EN### O God, restore us; And cause Your face to shine, and we will be saved.
Verse_Ch: 80:4 耶和华万军之神阿，你向你百姓的祷告发怒，要到几时呢？ ###EN### O Jehovah God of hosts, How long will You fume Against the prayer of Your people?
Verse_Ch: 80:5 你以眼泪当食物给他们吃，又多量出眼泪给他们喝。 ###EN### You have fed them with the bread of tears And have made them drink tears in large measure.
Verse_Ch: 80:6 你使邻国因我们纷争；我们的仇敌在他们中间戏笑我们。 ###EN### You have made us a cause of strife to our neighbors, And our enemies deride us among themselves.
Verse_Ch: 80:7 万军之神阿，求你恢复我们，使你的脸发光，我们便要得救。 ###EN### O God of hosts, restore us; And cause Your face to shine, and we will be saved.
Verse_Ch: 80:8 你从埃及挪出一棵葡萄树，赶出外邦人，把这树栽上。 ###EN### You brought a vine out of Egypt; You drove out nations and planted it;
Verse_Ch: 80:9 你在这树前预备了地方，它就深深扎根，爬满了地。 ###EN### You cleared the ground before it, And it took deep root and filled the land.
Verse_Ch: 80:10 它的影子遮满了山，枝子好像神的香柏树。 ###EN### The mountains were covered with its shadow, And its boughs were like the cedars of God.
Verse_Ch: 80:11 它发出枝子，直到大海，发出嫩枝，直到大河。 ###EN### It put forth its branches unto the sea, And its shoots unto the River.
Verse_Ch: 80:12 你为何拆毁这树的篱笆，任凭一切过路的人摘取？ ###EN### Why have You broken down its hedges, So that all who pass by on the way pluck it?
Verse_Ch: 80:13 林中出来的野猪把它蹧蹋，野地的走兽拿它当食物。 ###EN### The boar from the forest ravages it, And that which moves through the field feeds on it.
Verse_Ch: 80:14 万军之神阿，求你回转，从天上垂看鉴察，眷顾这葡萄树， ###EN### O God of hosts, turn, we beseech You; Look down from heaven and see, And visit this vine,
Verse_Ch: 80:15 就是你右手所栽的枝干，和你为自己所坚固的枝子。 ###EN### Even the stock which Your right hand has planted And the son whom You have strengthened for Yourself.
Verse_Ch: 80:16 这树已经被火焚烧，被刀砍伐；他们因你脸上所显的斥责灭亡了。 ###EN### It is burned with fire; it is cut down; They perish at the rebuke of Your countenance.
Verse_Ch: 80:17 愿你的手护庇你右边的人，就是你为自己所坚固的人子。 ###EN### Let Your hand be upon the man of Your right hand, Upon the son of man whom You have strengthened for Yourself;
Verse_Ch: 80:18 这样，我们便不退后离开你；求你救活我们，我们就要呼求你的名。 ###EN### Then we will not turn back from You. Revive us, and we will call upon Your name.
Verse_Ch: 80:19 耶和华万军之神阿，求你恢复我们，使你的脸发光，我们便要得救。 ###EN### O Jehovah God of hosts, restore us; Cause Your face to shine, and we will be saved.
Chapter_Header: 81
Verse_Ch: 81:1 你们当向神我们的力量欢唱，向雅各的神欢呼。 ###EN### Sing for joy to God our strength; Make a joyful noise to the God of Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 81:2 要唱起诗歌，击手鼓，弹奏美妙的琴瑟。 ###EN### Lift up a song and sound the tambourine, The pleasant lyre with the harp.
Verse_Ch: 81:3 当在月朔，在月望，在我们过节的日期吹角。 ###EN### Blow the trumpet at the new moon, At the full moon, on our feast day.
Verse_Ch: 81:4 因这是以色列的律例，是雅各之神的典章。 ###EN### For that is a statute of Israel, An ordinance of the God of Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 81:5 祂出去攻击埃及地的时候，在约瑟中间立此为证。我听见我所不明白的言语，说， ###EN### He appointed it as a testimony in Joseph When He went out over the land of Egypt. I heard a language that I did not know:
Verse_Ch: 81:6 我使你的肩得脱重担，你的手放下筐子。 ###EN### I turned your shoulder from the burden; Your hands were freed from the basket.
Verse_Ch: 81:7 你在患难中呼求，我就搭救你；我在雷的隐密处应允你；我在米利巴水那里试验你。 细拉 ###EN### You called in trouble, and I delivered you; I answered you from the secret place of thunder; I proved you at the waters of Meribah.
Verse_Ch: 81:8 我的民哪，你当听，我要警戒你：以色列阿，甚愿你肯听从我！ ###EN### Hear, O My people, and I will testify against you: O Israel, if you would listen to Me!
Verse_Ch: 81:9 在你当中不可有别的神；外邦的神，你也不可下拜。 ###EN### There shall be no strange god among you, Neither shall you worship any foreign god.
Verse_Ch: 81:10 我是耶和华你的神，是把你从埃及地领上来的；你要大大张口，我就给你充满。 ###EN### I am Jehovah your God, Who brought you up out of the land of Egypt; Open your mouth wide, and I will fill it.
Verse_Ch: 81:11 无奈我的民不听我的声音，以色列不肯服从我。 ###EN### But My people did not listen to My voice, And Israel would not consent to Me.
Verse_Ch: 81:12 我便任凭他们心里顽梗，随自己的计谋而行。 ###EN### So I gave them over to the stubbornness of their heart: They walked after their own counsels.
Verse_Ch: 81:13 甚愿我的民肯听从我，以色列肯遵行我的道路！ ###EN### Oh that My people had listened to Me, That Israel had walked in My ways!
Verse_Ch: 81:14 我便速速制伏他们的仇敌，反手攻击他们的敌人。 ###EN### I would have soon subdued their enemies And turned My hand against their adversaries.
Verse_Ch: 81:15 恨耶和华的人必来归顺，祂百姓的时日必延到永远。 ###EN### Those who hate Jehovah would have come cringing to Him, And their time would be forever.
Verse_Ch: 81:16 祂也必拿上好的麦子给他们吃；我必拿磐石所出的蜂蜜，叫你们饱足。 ###EN### And He would have fed them with the finest of wheat; Indeed with honey from the rock I would have satisfied you.
Chapter_Header: 82
Verse_Ch: 82:1 神站在神的会中；在诸神中行审判， ###EN### God stands in the congregation of God; He judges in the midst of the gods.
Verse_Ch: 82:2 说，你们审判不秉公义，徇恶人的情面，要到几时呢？ 细拉 ###EN### How long will you judge unjustly And respect the persons of the wicked?
Verse_Ch: 82:3 你们当为贫寒的人和孤儿伸冤，为困苦和贫穷的人施行公理； ###EN### Judge the poor and the orphan; Execute justice for the afflicted and the destitute;
Verse_Ch: 82:4 当救护贫寒和穷乏的人，搭救他们脱离恶人的手。 ###EN### Rescue the poor and the needy; Deliver them from the hand of the wicked.
Verse_Ch: 82:5 你们仍不知道，也不明白，在黑暗中走来走去；地的根基都摇动了。 ###EN### You do not know, nor do you understand; You go about in darkness; All the foundations of the earth are shaken.
Verse_Ch: 82:6 我曾说，你们是神，都是至高者的儿子。 ###EN### I said, You are gods, And all of you are sons of the Most High.
Verse_Ch: 82:7 然而，你们要死，与众人一样；要仆倒，像首领中的一位。 ###EN### Nevertheless you will die like men And fall like one of the princes.
Verse_Ch: 82:8 神阿，求你起来，审判这地；因为你要得万邦为业。 ###EN### Arise, O God; judge the earth; For You will inherit all the nations.
Chapter_Header: 83
Verse_Ch: 83:1 神阿，求你不要静默；神阿，求你不要闭口，也不要不作声； ###EN### O God, do not keep silent; Do not be quiet, and do not be still, O God.
Verse_Ch: 83:2 因为看哪，你的仇敌喧嚷；恨你的抬起头来。 ###EN### For, behold, Your enemies are in tumult, And those who hate You lift up their heads.
Verse_Ch: 83:3 他们同谋奸诈要害你的百姓，彼此商议要害你所隐藏的人。 ###EN### They devise crafty counsel against Your people, And conspire against Your hidden ones.
Verse_Ch: 83:4 他们说，来罢，我们将他们除灭，使他们不再成国，使以色列的名不再被人记念。 ###EN### They have said, Come and let us destroy them from being a nation, That the name of Israel may no longer be remembered.
Verse_Ch: 83:5 他们同心商议，彼此结盟，要抵挡你； ###EN### For they have conspired together with one heart; It is against You that they have made an alliance:
Verse_Ch: 83:6 就是以东帐棚的人和以实玛利人，摩押人和夏甲人， ###EN### The tents of Edom and the Ishmaelites, Moab and the Hagarites,
Verse_Ch: 83:7 迦巴勒、亚扪和亚玛力，非利士同推罗的居民； ###EN### Gebal and Ammon and Amalek, Philistia along with the inhabitants of Tyre;
Verse_Ch: 83:8 亚述也与他们联合；他们作了罗得子孙的帮手。 细拉 ###EN### Assyria is also joined with them; They have been a help to the children of Lot.
Verse_Ch: 83:9 求你待他们如待米甸，如在基顺河待西西拉和耶宾一样： ###EN### Do with them as with Midian, As with Sisera and Jabin, at the brook Kishon:
Verse_Ch: 83:10 他们在隐多珥灭亡，成了地上的粪土。 ###EN### They were destroyed at Endor; They became dung for the earth.
Verse_Ch: 83:11 求你叫他们的贵胄像俄立和西伊伯，叫他们的首领都像西巴和撒慕拿； ###EN### Make their nobles like Oreb and Zeeb, And all their princes like Zebah and Zalmunna,
Verse_Ch: 83:12 这些人曾说，我们要得神的住处，作为自己的产业。 ###EN### Who said, Let us possess for ourselves The habitations of God.
Verse_Ch: 83:13 我的神阿，求你叫他们像随风滚转的草，像风前的碎秸。 ###EN### O my God, make them like a tumbleweed, Like stubble before the wind.
Verse_Ch: 83:14 火怎样焚烧树林，火焰怎样烧着山岭， ###EN### Like fire that burns a forest And like a flame that sets mountains on fire,
Verse_Ch: 83:15 求你也照样用你的狂风追赶他们，用你的暴雨恐吓他们。 ###EN### So pursue them with Your tempest, And terrify them with Your storm.
Verse_Ch: 83:16 耶和华阿，愿你使他们满面羞愧，好叫他们寻求你的名。 ###EN### Fill their faces with shame, That they may seek Your name, O Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 83:17 愿他们永远羞愧惊惶，愿他们抱愧灭亡； ###EN### May they be ashamed and dismayed forever, And may they be confounded and perish;
Verse_Ch: 83:18 使他们知道惟独你名为耶和华的，是管理全地的至高者。 ###EN### That they may know that You alone, whose name is Jehovah, Are the Most High over all the earth.
Chapter_Header: 84
Verse_Ch: 84:1 万军之耶和华阿，你的居所何等可爱！ ###EN### How lovely are Your tabernacles, O Jehovah of hosts!
Verse_Ch: 84:2 我的魂羡慕，甚至渴想耶和华的院宇；我的心肠，我的肉体，向活神呼吁。 ###EN### My soul longs, indeed even faints, For the courts of Jehovah; My heart and my flesh cry out To the living God.
Verse_Ch: 84:3 万军之耶和华，我的王我的神阿，在你的两座坛那里，连麻雀也找着房屋；燕子也为自己找着菢雏之窝。 ###EN### At Your two altars even the sparrow has found a home; And the swallow, a nest for herself, Where she may lay her young, O Jehovah of hosts, my King and my God.
Verse_Ch: 84:4 住在你殿中的，便为有福；他们仍要赞美你。 细拉 ###EN### Blessed are those who dwell in Your house; They will yet be praising You.
Verse_Ch: 84:5 因你有力量，心中想往锡安大道的，这人便为有福。 ###EN### Blessed is the man whose strength is in You, In whose heart are the highways to Zion.
Verse_Ch: 84:6 他们经过流泪谷，叫这谷变为泉源之地；并有秋雨之福，盖满了这谷。 ###EN### Passing through the valley of Baca, They make it a spring; Indeed the early rain covers it with blessings.
Verse_Ch: 84:7 他们行走，力上加力，各人到锡安朝见神。 ###EN### They go from strength to strength; Each appears before God in Zion.
Verse_Ch: 84:8 耶和华万军之神阿，求你听我的祷告；雅各的神阿，求你侧耳听。 细拉 ###EN### O Jehovah God of hosts, hear my prayer; Give ear, O God of Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 84:9 神阿，求你垂顾我们的盾牌；求你观看你受膏者的面。 ###EN### Behold our shield, O God; And look upon the face of Your anointed.
Verse_Ch: 84:10 在你的院宇住一日，胜似在别处住千日；我宁愿站在我神殿的门槛，也不愿住在恶人的帐棚里。 ###EN### For a day in Your courts is better than a thousand; I would rather stand at the threshold of the house of my God Than dwell in the tents of the wicked.
Verse_Ch: 84:11 因为耶和华神是日头，是盾牌；耶和华赐下恩典和荣耀；祂未尝留下一样好处，不给那些行动正直的人。 ###EN### For Jehovah God is a sun and a shield; Jehovah gives grace and glory; He does not withhold anything good From those who walk uprightly.
Verse_Ch: 84:12 万军之耶和华阿，信靠你的人，便为有福。 ###EN### O Jehovah of hosts, blessed is the man Who trusts in You.
Chapter_Header: 85
Verse_Ch: 85:1 耶和华阿，你喜悦了你的地，使雅各从被掳归回。 ###EN### You have been pleased, O Jehovah, with Your land; You have turned the captivity of Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 85:2 你赦免了你百姓的罪孽，遮盖了他们一切的罪。 细拉 ###EN### You have forgiven the iniquity of Your people; You have covered all their sin.
Verse_Ch: 85:3 你收去了所发的忿怒，使你猛烈的怒气转消。 ###EN### You have taken away all Your wrath; You have turned from the fierceness of Your anger.
Verse_Ch: 85:4 拯救我们的神阿，求你恢复我们，止住你向我们所发的恼怒。 ###EN### Restore us, O God of our salvation, And cause Your indignation toward us to cease.
Verse_Ch: 85:5 你要向我们发怒到永远么？你要将你的怒气延留到万代么？ ###EN### Will You be angry with us forever? Will You extend Your anger from generation to generation?
Verse_Ch: 85:6 你不再将我们救活，使你的百姓因你喜乐么？ ###EN### Will You not again revive us, That Your people may rejoice in You?
Verse_Ch: 85:7 耶和华阿，求你向我们显示你的慈爱，又将你的救恩赐给我们。 ###EN### Show us, O Jehovah, Your lovingkindness, And grant us Your salvation.
Verse_Ch: 85:8 我要听神耶和华所说的话，因为祂必向祂的百姓，祂的虔诚人，说平安的话；他们却不可再转向愚妄。 ###EN### I will hear what God Jehovah will speak, For He will speak peace To His people and to His faithful ones; But let them not turn again unto folly.
Verse_Ch: 85:9 祂的救恩，诚然与敬畏祂的人相近，叫荣耀住在我们的地上。 ###EN### Surely His salvation is near to those who fear Him, That glory may dwell in our land.
Verse_Ch: 85:10 慈爱和真实，彼此相遇；公义和平安，彼此相亲。 ###EN### Lovingkindness and truth have met together; Righteousness and peace have kissed each other.
Verse_Ch: 85:11 真实从地生出，公义从天俯视。 ###EN### Truth has sprung forth from the earth, And righteousness has looked down from heaven.
Verse_Ch: 85:12 耶和华必赐下好处，我们的地要多出土产。 ###EN### Indeed Jehovah will give what is good, And our land will give its increase.
Verse_Ch: 85:13 公义要行在祂面前，叫祂的脚踪成为可走的路。 ###EN### Righteousness will go before Him And make His footsteps a way to walk in.
Chapter_Header: 86
Verse_Ch: 86:1 耶和华阿，求你侧耳应允我，因我是困苦穷乏的。 ###EN### Incline Your ear, O Jehovah; answer me; For I am poor and needy.
Verse_Ch: 86:2 求你保存我的性命；因我是忠信的。你是我的神，求你拯救这信靠你的仆人。 ###EN### Keep my soul; for I am faithful; Save Your servant who trusts in You, O You who are my God.
Verse_Ch: 86:3 主阿，求你恩待我，因我终日呼求你。 ###EN### Be gracious to me, O Lord; For to You do I call out all day long.
Verse_Ch: 86:4 主阿，求你使仆人的魂喜乐；因为我的魂仰望你。 ###EN### Cause the soul of Your servant to rejoice, For unto You, O Lord, do I lift up my soul.
Verse_Ch: 86:5 主阿，你本为良善，乐意饶恕人，对一切呼求你的人，有丰盛的慈爱。 ###EN### For You, O Lord, are good and ready to forgive And abundant in lovingkindness to all who call upon You.
Verse_Ch: 86:6 耶和华阿，求你侧耳听我的祷告，垂听我恳求的声音。 ###EN### Give ear, O Jehovah, to my prayer, And give heed to the voice of my supplications.
Verse_Ch: 86:7 我在患难之日要呼求你，因为你必应允我。 ###EN### In the day of my distress I call upon You, For You answer me.
Verse_Ch: 86:8 主阿，诸神之中没有可比你的；你的作为也无可比。 ###EN### There is none like You among the gods, O Lord; Nor are there any works like Yours.
Verse_Ch: 86:9 主阿，你所造的万邦，都要来到你面前下拜；他们也要荣耀你的名。 ###EN### All the nations which You have made will come And worship before You, O Lord; And they will glorify Your name.
Verse_Ch: 86:10 因你为大，且行奇妙的事；惟独你是神。 ###EN### For You are great, and You do wondrous deeds; You alone are God.
Verse_Ch: 86:11 耶和华阿，求你将你的道路指教我；我要行在你的真理中。求你使我专心敬畏你的名。 ###EN### Teach me, O Jehovah, Your way; I will walk in Your truth. Make my heart single in fearing Your name.
Verse_Ch: 86:12 主我的神阿，我要全心赞美你；我要荣耀你的名，直到永远。 ###EN### I will praise You, O Lord my God, with all my heart; And I will glorify Your name forever.
Verse_Ch: 86:13 因为你向我发的慈爱是大的，你救了我的魂，免入极深的阴间。 ###EN### For Your lovingkindness is great toward me, And You have delivered my soul from the lowest Sheol.
Verse_Ch: 86:14 神阿，骄傲的人起来攻击我，又有一伙强横的人寻索我的命；他们不将你摆在面前。 ###EN### O God, the proud have risen up against me, And a company of violent men seek my life; And they do not set You before them.
Verse_Ch: 86:15 但主阿，你是有怜恤有恩典的神，不轻易发怒，并有丰盛的慈爱和真实。 ###EN### But You, O Lord, are a compassionate and gracious God, Long-suffering and abundant in lovingkindness and truth.
Verse_Ch: 86:16 求你转向我，恩待我；将你的力量赐给你仆人，救你婢女的儿子。 ###EN### Turn to me and be gracious to me; Give Your strength to Your servant, And save the son of Your female servant.
Verse_Ch: 86:17 求你向我显出善待我的凭据，叫恨我的人看见便羞愧；因为你耶和华帮助了我，安慰了我。 ###EN### Show me a token of goodness, That those who hate me may see it and be ashamed; For You, O Jehovah, have helped me and comforted me.
Chapter_Header: 87
Verse_Ch: 87:1 耶和华所立的根基在圣山上。 ###EN### His foundation is in the holy mountains.
Verse_Ch: 87:2 祂爱锡安的门，胜于爱雅各一切的住处。 ###EN### Jehovah loves the gates of Zion More than all the dwellings of Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 87:3 神的城阿，有荣耀的事是指着你说的。 细拉 ###EN### Glorious things are spoken of you, O city of God.
Verse_Ch: 87:4 我要题起拉哈伯和巴比伦人，他们是认识我的人；看哪，还有非利士和推罗并古实人，他们说，这一个生在那里。 ###EN### I will make mention of Rahab and Babylon as those who know Me; Behold, Philistia and Tyre along with Cush: This one was born there, they say .
Verse_Ch: 87:5 但论到锡安必说，这一个那一个都生在其中；而且至高者必亲自坚立这城。 ###EN### But of Zion it will be said, This one and that one were born in her, And the Most High Himself will establish her.
Verse_Ch: 87:6 当耶和华记录众民的时候，祂要数点出，这一个生在那里。 细拉 ###EN### Jehovah will count When He records the peoples: This One was born there.
Verse_Ch: 87:7 歌唱的同跳舞的都要说，我的泉源都在你里面。 ###EN### Then singing as well as dancing, they will say, All my springs are in you.
Chapter_Header: 88
Verse_Ch: 88:1 耶和华拯救我的神阿，我昼夜在你面前呼求。 ###EN### O Jehovah, the God of my salvation, I have cried out by day and in the night before You.
Verse_Ch: 88:2 愿我的祷告达到你面前；求你侧耳听我的呼求。 ###EN### May my prayer come before You; Incline Your ear to my cry.
Verse_Ch: 88:3 因为我的魂里饱受患难，我的性命临近阴间。 ###EN### For my soul is full of troubles, And my life draws near to Sheol.
Verse_Ch: 88:4 我算在下坑的人之中，如同没有帮助的人一样。 ###EN### I am accounted among those who go down into the pit; I am like a man without any help,
Verse_Ch: 88:5 我被丢弃在死人之中，好像被杀的人躺在坟墓里；他们是你不再记念的，与你的手隔绝了。 ###EN### Abandoned among the dead, Like the slain that lie in the grave, Whom You remember no more, And they are cut off from Your hand.
Verse_Ch: 88:6 你把我放在极深的坑里，在黑暗的地方，在深处。 ###EN### You have put me in the lowest pit, In the dark places, in the depths.
Verse_Ch: 88:7 你的忿怒重压着我，你用你一切的波浪使我受苦。 细拉 ###EN### Your wrath lies heavily upon me, And You have afflicted me with all Your waves.
Verse_Ch: 88:8 你使我的知友远离我，使我为他们所憎恶。我被拘困，不得出来。 ###EN### You have put my acquaintances far from me; You have made me an abomination to them. I am shut in and cannot go out.
Verse_Ch: 88:9 我的眼睛因困苦而干瘪；耶和华阿，我天天呼求你，向你展开双手祷告。 ###EN### My eye wastes away at the affliction; I have called out to You, O Jehovah, every day; I have spread out my hands to You.
Verse_Ch: 88:10 你岂要行奇事给死人看么？难道阴魂还能起来赞美你么？ 细拉 ###EN### Will You perform wonders for the dead? Will the deceased rise up and praise You?
Verse_Ch: 88:11 岂能在坟墓里述说你的慈爱么？岂能在灭亡中述说你的信实么？ ###EN### Will Your lovingkindness be declared in the grave, Or Your faithfulness in Abaddon?
Verse_Ch: 88:12 你的奇事岂能在幽暗里被知道么？你的公义岂能在忘记之地被知道么？ ###EN### Will Your wonders be made known in the darkness, Or Your righteousness in the land of forgetfulness?
Verse_Ch: 88:13 耶和华阿，我却呼求你；早晨我的祷告要达到你面前。 ###EN### But I, O Jehovah, have cried out to You; And in the morning my prayer comes before You.
Verse_Ch: 88:14 耶和华阿，你为何丢弃我的魂？为何掩面不顾我？ ###EN### Why, O Jehovah, have You rejected my soul? Why do You hide Your face from me?
Verse_Ch: 88:15 我自幼受苦，几乎死亡；我忍受你的惊恐，慌张不安。 ###EN### I have been afflicted and about to die since my youth; I bear Your terrors; I am overwhelmed.
Verse_Ch: 88:16 你的烈怒漫过我身；你的惊吓把我剪除。 ###EN### Your fierce wrath has gone over me; Your terrors have cut me off.
Verse_Ch: 88:17 这些终日如水环绕我，一齐来围困我。 ###EN### They surrounded me like water all day long; They altogether encompassed me.
Verse_Ch: 88:18 你使我的爱友良朋远离我；我的知友都在黑暗里。 ###EN### You have put far from me Lover and friend; My acquaintances are in darkness.
Chapter_Header: 89
Verse_Ch: 89:1 我要歌唱耶和华的慈爱，直到永远；我要用口将你的信实传与万代。 ###EN### I will sing of the lovingkindness of Jehovah forever; From generation to generation I will make known Your faithfulness with my mouth.
Verse_Ch: 89:2 因我曾说，你的慈爱必建立到永远；你必将你的信实，坚立在诸天之上。 ###EN### For I have said, Lovingkindness will be built up forever; In the heavens themselves You will establish Your faithfulness.
Verse_Ch: 89:3 我与我所拣选的人立了约；我向我的仆人大卫起了誓： ###EN### I have made a covenant with My chosen one; I have sworn to David My servant:
Verse_Ch: 89:4 我要坚立你的后裔，直到永远；我要建立你的宝座，直到万代。 细拉 ###EN### I will establish your seed forever, And I will build up your throne from generation to generation.
Verse_Ch: 89:5 耶和华阿，诸天要称赞你的奇事；在圣者的会中，要称赞你的信实。 ###EN### And the heavens will praise Your wonders, O Jehovah, Indeed Your faithfulness in the congregation of the holy ones.
Verse_Ch: 89:6 在天空谁能比耶和华呢？大能者的众子中，有谁像耶和华呢？ ###EN### For who in the skies can be compared to Jehovah? Who among the sons of the mighty is like Jehovah,
Verse_Ch: 89:7 祂在圣者的议会中，是大可畏的神，比一切在祂四围的更可畏惧。 ###EN### Like God, greatly feared in the council of the holy ones And awesome beyond all around Him?
Verse_Ch: 89:8 耶和华万军之神阿，谁能像你这大能的耶和华呢？你的信实是在你的四围。 ###EN### O Jehovah God of hosts, who is like You, the mighty Jah? Your faithfulness also surrounds You.
Verse_Ch: 89:9 你管辖海的狂涛：波浪翻腾，你使它平静。 ###EN### You rule the swelling of the sea: When its waves rise up, You still them.
Verse_Ch: 89:10 你把拉哈伯打碎，如同被杀的人；你用有能的膀臂打散了你的仇敌。 ###EN### You crushed Rahab like one slain; You scattered Your enemies with the arm of Your strength.
Verse_Ch: 89:11 诸天属你，地也属你；世界和其中所充满的，都是你建立的。 ###EN### The heavens are Yours; the earth also is Yours; The world and its fullness You have founded.
Verse_Ch: 89:12 南北都是你创造的；他泊和黑门都因你的名欢呼。 ###EN### You created the north and the south; Tabor and Hermon shout for joy at Your name.
Verse_Ch: 89:13 你有大能的膀臂；你的手有力，你的右手也高举。 ###EN### You have an arm with might; Your hand is strong; Your right hand is high.
Verse_Ch: 89:14 公义和公平，是你宝座的根基；慈爱和真实，行在你面前。 ###EN### Righteousness and justice are the foundation of Your throne; Lovingkindness and truth go before Your face.
Verse_Ch: 89:15 知道向你欢呼的，那民是有福的；耶和华阿，他们在你的面光中行走。 ###EN### Blessed are the people who know the joyful shout; They walk, O Jehovah, in the light of Your countenance.
Verse_Ch: 89:16 他们因你的名终日欢腾，因你的公义得以高举。 ###EN### In Your name they exult all day long, And in Your righteousness they are exalted.
Verse_Ch: 89:17 你是他们力量的荣耀；因着你的恩惠，我们的角必被高举。 ###EN### For You are the glory of their strength, And in Your favor our horn is exalted.
Verse_Ch: 89:18 我们的盾牌属耶和华，我们的王属以色列的圣者。 ###EN### For our shield belongs to Jehovah, And our king, to the Holy One of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 89:19 当时你在异象中论到你的圣者，说，我已把救助之力，加给那有能者；我已高举那从民中所拣选的。 ###EN### Then You spoke in vision Of Your Holy One, and You said, I have given help to One who is mighty; I have exalted One chosen from My people.
Verse_Ch: 89:20 我寻得我的仆人大卫，用我的圣膏油膏了祂。 ###EN### I have found David My Servant; With My holy oil I have anointed Him,
Verse_Ch: 89:21 我的手必坚定的与祂同在；我的膀臂也必坚固祂。 ###EN### With whom My hand will be established; My arm will also strengthen Him.
Verse_Ch: 89:22 仇敌必不勒索祂，凶恶之子也不苦害祂。 ###EN### The enemy will not exact anything from Him, Nor will the son of wickedness afflict Him.
Verse_Ch: 89:23 我要在祂面前打碎祂的敌人，击败那些恨祂的人。 ###EN### And I will crush His adversaries before Him, And I will strike those who hate Him.
Verse_Ch: 89:24 我的信实和我的慈爱，要与祂同在；因我的名，祂的角必被高举。 ###EN### And My faithfulness and My lovingkindness will be with Him, And in My name His horn will be exalted.
Verse_Ch: 89:25 我要使祂的左手伸到海上，右手伸到河上。 ###EN### And I will set His hand on the sea And His right hand on the rivers.
Verse_Ch: 89:26 祂要称呼我说，你是我的父，是我的神，是拯救我的磐石。 ###EN### He will call upon Me, saying, You are My Father, My God and the rock of My salvation.
Verse_Ch: 89:27 我也要立祂为长子，为地上最高的君王。 ###EN### I will also make Him the Firstborn, The highest of the kings of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 89:28 我要向祂守住我的慈爱，直到永远；我与祂立的约，必要坚定。 ###EN### I will keep My lovingkindness for Him forever, And My covenant will stand firm with Him.
Verse_Ch: 89:29 我也要使祂的后裔存到永远，使祂的宝座如天之久。 ###EN### And I will establish His seed forever, And His throne as the days of heaven.
Verse_Ch: 89:30 倘若祂的子孙离弃我的律法，不遵行我的典章， ###EN### If His children forsake My law And do not walk in My ordinances,
Verse_Ch: 89:31 渎犯我的律例，不遵守我的诫命， ###EN### If they profane My statutes And do not keep My commandments,
Verse_Ch: 89:32 我就要用杖责罚他们的过犯，用鞭责罚他们的罪孽。 ###EN### I will punish their transgression with a rod And their iniquity with stripes.
Verse_Ch: 89:33 只是我必不将我的慈爱，全然从祂挪去，也必不背弃我的信实。 ###EN### But My lovingkindness I will not utterly take away from Him, Nor will I be false to My own faithfulness.
Verse_Ch: 89:34 我必不违犯我的约，也不改变我嘴唇所出的。 ###EN### I will not profane My covenant, Nor will I change what has gone forth from My lips.
Verse_Ch: 89:35 我一次指着自己的圣别起誓；我必不向大卫说谎。 ###EN### Once I have sworn by My holiness; I will not lie to David.
Verse_Ch: 89:36 祂的后裔要存到永远，祂的宝座在我面前，如日之恒一般； ###EN### His seed shall endure forever, And His throne, like the sun before Me;
Verse_Ch: 89:37 又如月亮永远坚立；这天上的见证是确实的。 细拉 ###EN### It shall be established forever like the moon; And the witness in the skies is firm.
Verse_Ch: 89:38 但你已丢掉弃绝他；你已恼怒你的受膏者。 ###EN### But You have cast off and rejected; You have been angry with Your anointed.
Verse_Ch: 89:39 你厌恶了与你仆人所立的约，将他的冠冕抛掷于地，玷污了。 ###EN### You have abhorred the covenant of Your servant; You have profaned his crown by casting it to the ground.
Verse_Ch: 89:40 你拆毁了他一切的围墙；你使他的保障变为荒场。 ###EN### You have broken down all his walls; You have brought his strongholds to ruin.
Verse_Ch: 89:41 凡过路的人都抢夺他；他成了邻国所羞辱的。 ###EN### All who pass by on the way plunder him; He has become a reproach to his neighbors.
Verse_Ch: 89:42 你高举了他敌人的右手；你叫他一切的仇敌喜乐。 ###EN### You have exalted the right hand of his adversaries; You have caused all his enemies to rejoice.
Verse_Ch: 89:43 你叫他的刀剑卷刃，叫他在争战之中站立不住。 ###EN### Indeed You have turned back the edge of his sword And have not made him stand in the battle.
Verse_Ch: 89:44 你使他的光辉止息，将他的宝座推倒于地。 ###EN### You have made his brightness cease And have cast down his throne to the ground.
Verse_Ch: 89:45 你减少他青年的日子；你使他披上羞愧。 细拉 ###EN### You have shortened the days of his youth; You have covered him with shame.
Verse_Ch: 89:46 耶和华阿，这要到几时呢？你要将自己隐藏到永远么？你的忿怒如火焚烧，要到几时呢？ ###EN### How long, O Jehovah? Will You hide Yourself forever? How long will Your wrath burn like fire?
Verse_Ch: 89:47 求你记念我的时候是何等的短少－你所创造的一切世人，你要使他们归于何等的虚空！ ###EN### Remember how short my time is-For what vanity You have created all the sons of men!
Verse_Ch: 89:48 什么人能常活而不见死？他能救自己的魂脱离阴间的权势么？ 细拉 ###EN### What man will live and not see death? Will he deliver his soul from the power of Sheol?
Verse_Ch: 89:49 主阿，你先前所施行的慈爱，就是你凭自己的信实向大卫起誓的，在那里呢？ ###EN### Where are Your former acts of lovingkindness, O Lord, Which You swore to David in Your faithfulness?
Verse_Ch: 89:50 主阿，求你记念仆人们所受的羞辱，记念我怎样将一切强盛之民的羞辱承当在我怀里； ###EN### Remember, O Lord, the reproach of Your servants, How I bear in my bosom the reproach of all the mighty peoples,
Verse_Ch: 89:51 耶和华阿，你的仇敌，用这羞辱羞辱了你的仆人，羞辱了你受膏者的脚踪。 ###EN### With which Your enemies have reproached, O Jehovah, With which they have reproached the footsteps of Your anointed.
Verse_Ch: 89:52 耶和华是当受颂赞的，直到永远。阿们，阿们。 ###EN### Blessed be Jehovah forever. Amen and Amen.
Chapter_Header: 90
Verse_Ch: 90:1 主阿，你世世代代作我们的居所。 ###EN### O Lord, You have been our dwelling place In all generations.
Verse_Ch: 90:2 诸山未曾生出，地与世界你未曾造成，从亘古到永远，你是神。 ###EN### Before the mountains were brought forth, And before You gave birth to the earth and the world, Indeed from eternity to eternity, You are God.
Verse_Ch: 90:3 你使人归回尘土，说，你们世人要归回。 ###EN### You return man to dust And say, Return, you sons of men.
Verse_Ch: 90:4 在你看来，千年如刚过的昨日，又如夜间的一更。 ###EN### For a thousand years in Your sight Are like yesterday when it passes by And like a watch in the night.
Verse_Ch: 90:5 你仿佛用暴雨将他们冲去；他们如睡一觉；早晨，他们如重新生长的草； ###EN### You sweep them away as with a rain flood; they are as in a sleep: In the morning they are like grass that comes up anew.
Verse_Ch: 90:6 早晨发旺，重新生长，晚上割下枯干。 ###EN### In the morning it flourishes and comes up anew; In the evening it is cut down, and it dries up.
Verse_Ch: 90:7 我们因你的怒气而消灭，因你的忿怒而惊惶。 ###EN### For we have been consumed by Your anger, And by Your wrath we have been troubled.
Verse_Ch: 90:8 你将我们的罪孽摆在你面前，将我们隐藏的罪摆在你面光之中。 ###EN### You have set our iniquities before You, Our secret sins in the light of Your countenance.
Verse_Ch: 90:9 我们经过的日子，都在你盛怒之中；我们度尽的年岁，好像一声叹息。 ###EN### For all our days have passed away in Your overflowing wrath; We bring our years to an end like a sigh.
Verse_Ch: 90:10 我们一生的年日是七十岁，若是强壮可到八十岁；但其中所矜夸的，不过是劳苦愁烦，转眼成空，我们便如飞而去。 ###EN### The days of our years are seventy years, Or, if because of strength, eighty years; But their pride is labor and sorrow, For it is soon gone, and we fly away.
Verse_Ch: 90:11 谁晓得你怒气的威势？谁按着你该受的敬畏晓得你的盛怒？ ###EN### Who knows the power of Your anger, And Your overflowing wrath according to the fear that is due You?
Verse_Ch: 90:12 求你指教我们怎样数算自己的日子，好叫我们得着智慧的心。 ###EN### Teach us then to number our days That we may gain a heart of wisdom.
Verse_Ch: 90:13 耶和华阿，我们要等到几时呢？求你转回，为你的仆人后悔。 ###EN### Return, O Jehovah! How long? And repent concerning Your servants.
Verse_Ch: 90:14 求你使我们在早晨饱得你的慈爱，好叫我们一生欢呼喜乐。 ###EN### Satisfy us in the morning with Your lovingkindness That we may give a ringing shout and rejoice all our days.
Verse_Ch: 90:15 求你照着你使我们受苦的日子，照着我们遭难的年岁，叫我们喜乐。 ###EN### Cause us to rejoice according to the days that You have afflicted us, According to the years that we have seen evil.
Verse_Ch: 90:16 愿你的作为向你仆人显现，愿你的威荣向他们子孙显明。 ###EN### Let Your work appear to Your servants, And Your splendor, to their children.
Verse_Ch: 90:17 愿主我们神的恩惠，归于我们身上；愿你坚立我们手所作的工，归于我们身上；我们手所作的工，愿你坚立。 ###EN### And let the favor of the Lord our God be upon us, And establish the work of our hands upon us; Indeed the work of our hands, establish it.
Chapter_Header: 91
Verse_Ch: 91:1 住在至高者隐密处的，必住在全能者的荫下。 ###EN### He who dwells in the secret place of the Most High Will abide in the shadow of the Almighty.
Verse_Ch: 91:2 我要论到耶和华说，祂是我的避难所，是我的山寨，是我的神，是我所信靠的！ ###EN### I say of Jehovah, My refuge and My fortress, My God in whom I trust!
Verse_Ch: 91:3 因为祂必救你脱离捕鸟人的网罗，脱离毒害的瘟疫。 ###EN### For He will deliver You From the snare of the fowler, From the deadly pestilence.
Verse_Ch: 91:4 祂必用自己的翎毛遮蔽你，你要投靠在祂的翅膀底下；祂的真实，是大小的盾牌。 ###EN### With His pinions He will cover You, And under His wings You will take refuge; His truth is a shield and a buckler.
Verse_Ch: 91:5 你必不怕黑夜的惊骇，或是白日的飞箭； ###EN### You will not be afraid of the terror by night, Or of the arrow that flies by day,
Verse_Ch: 91:6 也不怕黑暗中流行的瘟疫，或是午间损毁人的毒病。 ###EN### Or of the pestilence that walks in darkness, Or of the destruction that lays waste at noon.
Verse_Ch: 91:7 虽有千人仆倒在你旁边，万人仆倒在你右边，灾害却不得临近你。 ###EN### A thousand will fall at Your side, And ten thousand at Your right hand; But it will not come near to You.
Verse_Ch: 91:8 不过你要亲眼观看，见恶人遭报。 ###EN### You will only look on with Your eyes And see the recompense of the wicked.
Verse_Ch: 91:9 因你已将至高者，耶和华我的避难所，当你的居所； ###EN### For You have made Jehovah, who is my refuge, Even the Most High, Your habitation,
Verse_Ch: 91:10 祸患必不临到你，灾害也不挨近你的帐棚。 ###EN### No evil will befall You, Nor will any plague come near Your tent.
Verse_Ch: 91:11 因祂要为你吩咐祂的使者，在你所行的一切道路上保护你。 ###EN### For He will give His angels charge concerning You To keep You in all Your ways.
Verse_Ch: 91:12 他们要用手托着你，免得你的脚碰在石头上。 ###EN### They will bear You up in their hands, Lest You dash Your foot against a stone.
Verse_Ch: 91:13 你要踹在狮子和虺蛇的身上，践踏少壮狮子和大蛇。 ###EN### You will tread upon the lion and the cobra; You will trample the young lion and the serpent.
Verse_Ch: 91:14 神说，因为祂专一爱我，我要搭救祂；因为祂认识我的名，我要把祂安置在高处。 ###EN### Because He has set His love upon Me, I will rescue Him; I will set Him on high, because He has known My name.
Verse_Ch: 91:15 祂要呼求我，我就应允祂。祂在急难中，我要与祂同在；我要搭救祂，使祂尊贵。 ###EN### He will call upon Me, and I will answer Him. I will be with Him in distress; I will deliver Him and honor Him.
Verse_Ch: 91:16 我要使祂足享长寿，将我的救恩显明给祂。 ###EN### With an extension of His days I will satisfy Him, And I will show Him My salvation.
Chapter_Header: 92
Verse_Ch: 92:1 称谢耶和华，歌颂你至高者的名， ###EN### It is good to give thanks to Jehovah And to sing psalms to Your name, O Most High;
Verse_Ch: 92:2 早晨传扬你的慈爱，夜间传扬你的信实， ###EN### To declare Your lovingkindness in the morning And Your faithfulness in the nights,
Verse_Ch: 92:3 弹奏十弦的乐器和瑟，用琴弹出幽雅的声音；这本为美事。 ###EN### Upon an instrument of ten strings and upon a harp, Upon the higgaion of the lyre.
Verse_Ch: 92:4 因为耶和华阿，你借着你所作的使我喜乐；因你手的工作，我要欢呼。 ###EN### For You have made me rejoice, O Jehovah, because of what You have done; Because of the works of Your hands I will shout for joy.
Verse_Ch: 92:5 耶和华阿，你的工作何其大！你的意念极其深！ ###EN### How great are Your works, O Jehovah! So very deep are Your thoughts!
Verse_Ch: 92:6 无知人不晓得，愚顽人也不明白。 ###EN### A senseless man does not know them, Nor does a fool understand them.
Verse_Ch: 92:7 恶人茂盛如草，一切作孽之人发旺的时候，正是他们要灭亡，直到永远。 ###EN### When the wicked sprout like grass, And all the workers of iniquity blossom, It is so that they may be destroyed forever.
Verse_Ch: 92:8 耶和华阿，惟有你为至高，直到永远。 ###EN### But You are on high forever, O Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 92:9 耶和华，看哪，你的仇敌；看哪，你的仇敌都要灭亡；一切作孽的都要离散。 ###EN### For behold, Your enemies, O Jehovah; For behold, Your enemies will perish; All the workers of iniquity will be scattered.
Verse_Ch: 92:10 你却高举了我的角，如野牛的角；我是被新油膏了的。 ###EN### But You have exalted my horn like that of a wild ox; I am anointed with fresh oil.
Verse_Ch: 92:11 我眼睛看见我的仇敌遭报；我耳朵听见那些起来攻击我的作恶之人受罚。 ###EN### And my eye has seen its desire for my enemies; My ears have heard their desire for the evildoers who rise up against me.
Verse_Ch: 92:12 义人要发旺如棕树，生长如利巴嫩的香柏树。 ###EN### The righteous man will flourish like the palm tree; He will grow like a cedar in Lebanon.
Verse_Ch: 92:13 他们栽植于耶和华的殿中，发旺在我们神的院里。 ###EN### Planted in the house of Jehovah, They will flourish in the courts of our God.
Verse_Ch: 92:14 他们年老的时候，仍要结果子；要满了汁浆而常发青； ###EN### They will still bring forth fruit in old age; They will be full of sap and green;
Verse_Ch: 92:15 好显明耶和华是正直的；祂是我的磐石，在祂毫无不义。 ###EN### To declare that Jehovah is upright; He is my rock, and there is no unrighteousness in Him.
Chapter_Header: 93
Verse_Ch: 93:1 耶和华作王；祂以威严为衣穿上。耶和华以能力为衣，以能力束腰。世界就坚立，必不动摇。 ###EN### Jehovah reigns; He is clothed with majesty. Jehovah is clothed, He has girded Himself, with strength. Indeed the world has been established; it will not be moved.
Verse_Ch: 93:2 你的宝座自古就立定；你从亘古就有。 ###EN### Your throne is established from of old; You are from eternity.
Verse_Ch: 93:3 耶和华阿，大水扬起了；大水扬起了声音，扬起了波浪的响声。 ###EN### The floods have lifted up, O Jehovah; The floods have lifted up their voice; The floods lift up their roaring.
Verse_Ch: 93:4 耶和华在高处大有能力，胜过众水的声音，胜过洋海的大浪！ ###EN### More than the voices of many waters, Than the mighty breakers of the sea, Jehovah on high is mighty!
Verse_Ch: 93:5 耶和华阿，你的法度极为确定；你的殿称为圣别，是合宜的，直到永远。 ###EN### Your testimonies are very sure; Holiness befits Your house, O Jehovah, forevermore.
Chapter_Header: 94
Verse_Ch: 94:1 耶和华阿，你是伸冤的神；伸冤的神阿，求你发出光来！ ###EN### O God of vengeance, O Jehovah, O God of vengeance, shine forth!
Verse_Ch: 94:2 审判全地的主阿，求你挺身而立，使骄傲人受应得的报应。 ###EN### Lift Yourself up, O Judge of the earth; Render the reward upon the proud.
Verse_Ch: 94:3 耶和华阿，恶人欢跃要到几时呢？要到几时呢？ ###EN### How long, O Jehovah, will the wicked, How long will the wicked exult?
Verse_Ch: 94:4 他们絮絮叨叨，说狂妄的话；一切作孽的人都夸耀自己。 ###EN### They burst out; they speak arrogantly; All the workers of iniquity boast.
Verse_Ch: 94:5 耶和华阿，他们强压你的百姓，苦害你的产业。 ###EN### They crush Your people, O Jehovah, And afflict Your inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 94:6 他们杀死寡妇和寄居的，又杀害孤儿。 ###EN### They slay the widow and the stranger, And they murder orphans.
Verse_Ch: 94:7 他们说，耶和华必看不见，雅各的神必不思念。 ###EN### And they say, Jehovah does not see, And the God of Jacob does not consider.
Verse_Ch: 94:8 你们民间的无知人当思想；你们愚顽人，到几时才有智慧呢？ ###EN### Consider, you senseless ones among the people; And you foolish ones, when will you become wise?
Verse_Ch: 94:9 设置耳朵的，难道自己听不见么？造作眼睛的，难道自己看不见么？ ###EN### He who planted the ear, does He not hear? And He who formed the eye, does He not see?
Verse_Ch: 94:10 管教列邦的，就是教导人知识的，难道自己不责备人么？ ###EN### He who disciplines the nations, He who teaches man knowledge, does He not reprove?
Verse_Ch: 94:11 耶和华知道人的意念是虚妄的。 ###EN### Jehovah knows the thoughts of man, That they are vanity.
Verse_Ch: 94:12 耶和华阿，你所管教，用律法所教训的人，是有福的； ###EN### Blessed is the man Whom You discipline, O Jehovah, And teach out of Your law;
Verse_Ch: 94:13 你使他在遭难的日子，得享安息，等到为恶人预备的坑挖好。 ###EN### That You may give him rest from the days of evil Until the pit is dug for the wicked.
Verse_Ch: 94:14 因为耶和华必不丢弃祂的百姓，也不离弃祂的产业。 ###EN### For Jehovah will not abandon His people, Nor will He forsake His inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 94:15 审判要归向公义，心里正直的必都随从。 ###EN### For judgment will return unto righteousness, And all the upright in heart will follow it.
Verse_Ch: 94:16 谁肯为我起来攻击作恶的？谁肯为我站起抵挡作孽的？ ###EN### Who will rise up for me against the evildoers? Who will stand up for me against the workers of iniquity?
Verse_Ch: 94:17 若不是耶和华帮助我，我的魂早已住在寂静之中了。 ###EN### Unless Jehovah had been my help, My soul would have soon dwelt in silence.
Verse_Ch: 94:18 我正说我失了脚，耶和华阿，那时你的慈爱扶持了我。 ###EN### When I said, My foot has slipped, Your lovingkindness, O Jehovah, upheld me.
Verse_Ch: 94:19 我里面思虑繁多，那时你的安慰使我的魂欢乐。 ###EN### When my disquieting thoughts within me are many, Your comfortings delight my soul.
Verse_Ch: 94:20 那借着律例制造祸患，在位上行毁坏的，岂能与你相交么？ ###EN### Shall the seat of destruction be united with You, Which devises trouble through its statutes?
Verse_Ch: 94:21 他们结党攻击义人的性命，将无辜的人定为死罪。 ###EN### They band together against the soul of the righteous man And condemn innocent blood.
Verse_Ch: 94:22 但耶和华向来作我的高台，我的神作了我投靠的磐石。 ###EN### But Jehovah has been my high tower, And my God the rock of my refuge;
Verse_Ch: 94:23 祂叫他们的罪孽归到他们身上；祂要因他们的恶灭绝他们；耶和华我们的神要把他们灭绝。 ###EN### And He will return their iniquity upon them And destroy them in their own evil; Jehovah our God will destroy them.
Chapter_Header: 95
Verse_Ch: 95:1 来阿，我们要向耶和华欢唱，向拯救我们的磐石欢呼。 ###EN### Come, let us sing for joy to Jehovah; Let us make a joyful noise to the rock of our salvation.
Verse_Ch: 95:2 我们要到祂面前来称谢祂，用诗歌向祂欢呼。 ###EN### Let us come before His presence with thanksgiving; Let us make a joyful noise to Him with psalms.
Verse_Ch: 95:3 因耶和华是大神，是大君王，超乎万神之上。 ###EN### For Jehovah is a great God And a great King above all gods.
Verse_Ch: 95:4 地的深处在祂手中，山的高峰也属祂。 ###EN### In His hand are the depths of the earth, The heights of the mountains are His also.
Verse_Ch: 95:5 海洋属祂，是祂造的；旱地也是祂手造成的。 ###EN### The sea is His, and He made it; And His hands formed the dry land.
Verse_Ch: 95:6 来阿，我们要屈身敬拜，在造我们的耶和华面前跪下。 ###EN### Come, let us worship and bow down; Let us kneel before Jehovah our Maker.
Verse_Ch: 95:7 因为祂是我们的神，我们是祂草场上的民，是祂手下的羊。你们今日若听见祂的声音， ###EN### For He is our God, And we are the people of His pasture And the flock of His hand. Today, if you hear His voice,
Verse_Ch: 95:8 就不可硬着心，像在米利巴，像在旷野玛撒的日子一样； ###EN### Do not harden your heart as at Meribah, As in the day of Massah in the wilderness;
Verse_Ch: 95:9 那时你们的祖宗虽然看见我的作为，还是试探我，试验我。 ###EN### When your fathers tested Me; They tried Me, even though they had seen My work.
Verse_Ch: 95:10 四十年之久，我厌烦那一代的人，说，他们是心里迷糊的百姓，竟不晓得我的法则； ###EN### For forty years I loathed that generation, And I said, They are a people who go astray in heart; And they do not know My ways;
Verse_Ch: 95:11 所以我在怒中起誓，说，他们绝不可进入我的安息！ ###EN### Therefore I swore in My anger: They shall by no means enter into My rest!
Chapter_Header: 96
Verse_Ch: 96:1 你们要向耶和华唱新歌；全地都要向耶和华歌唱。 ###EN### Sing to Jehovah a new song; Sing to Jehovah, all the earth.
Verse_Ch: 96:2 要向耶和华歌唱，颂赞祂的名，天天传扬祂的救恩。 ###EN### Sing to Jehovah, bless His name; Proclaim His salvation from day to day.
Verse_Ch: 96:3 要在列邦中述说祂的荣耀，在万民中述说祂的奇事。 ###EN### Declare His glory among the nations, His wondrous deeds among all the peoples.
Verse_Ch: 96:4 因耶和华为大，当受极大的赞美；祂在万神之上当受敬畏。 ###EN### For Jehovah is great and much to be praised; He is to be feared above all gods.
Verse_Ch: 96:5 众民的神都属虚无，惟独耶和华造作诸天。 ###EN### For all the gods of the peoples are idols, But Jehovah made the heavens.
Verse_Ch: 96:6 有尊荣和威严在祂面前，有能力与华美在祂圣所。 ###EN### Majesty and splendor are before Him; Strength and beauty are in His sanctuary.
Verse_Ch: 96:7 众民中的各族阿，你们要将荣耀能力归给耶和华，都归给耶和华； ###EN### Ascribe to Jehovah, O families of the peoples, Ascribe to Jehovah, glory and strength;
Verse_Ch: 96:8 要将耶和华的名所当得的荣耀归给祂，拿供物来进入祂的院宇。 ###EN### Ascribe to Jehovah the glory of His name; Bring an offering, and come into His courts.
Verse_Ch: 96:9 当以圣别的妆饰敬拜耶和华；全地要在祂面前战抖。 ###EN### Worship Jehovah in holy splendor; Tremble before Him, all the earth.
Verse_Ch: 96:10 要在列邦中说，耶和华作王；世界就坚立，必不动摇；祂要按公正审判众民。 ###EN### Say among the nations, Jehovah reigns; Indeed the world has been established; it will not be moved; He will judge the peoples with equity.
Verse_Ch: 96:11 愿天喜乐，愿地欢腾；愿海和其中所充满的澎湃； ###EN### Let the heavens rejoice and the earth be glad; Let the sea and its fullness roar.
Verse_Ch: 96:12 愿田和其中所有的都欢乐；那时，林中的树木都要在耶和华面前欢唱， ###EN### Let the field and all that is in it exult; Then all the trees of the forest will sing for joy
Verse_Ch: 96:13 因为祂来了；祂来要审判这地；祂要按公义审判世界，按祂的真实判断众民。 ###EN### Before Jehovah, for He is coming; For He is coming to judge the earth; He will judge the world with righteousness, And the peoples with His truth.
Chapter_Header: 97
Verse_Ch: 97:1 耶和华作王！愿地欢腾，愿众海岛喜乐。 ###EN### Jehovah reigns! Let the earth be glad; Let the many islands rejoice.
Verse_Ch: 97:2 密云和幽暗，在祂的四围；公义和公平，是祂宝座的根基。 ###EN### Clouds and deep darkness surround Him; Righteousness and justice are the foundation of His throne.
Verse_Ch: 97:3 有火在祂前头行，烧灭祂四围的敌人。 ###EN### A fire goes before Him And burns up His adversaries all around.
Verse_Ch: 97:4 祂的闪电光照世界；地看见便震动。 ###EN### His lightning illumines the world; The earth sees and trembles.
Verse_Ch: 97:5 诸山见耶和华的面，就是全地之主的面，便镕化如蜡。 ###EN### The mountains melt like wax at the presence of Jehovah, At the presence of the Lord of the whole earth.
Verse_Ch: 97:6 诸天传扬祂的公义，万民看见祂的荣耀。 ###EN### The heavens declare His righteousness, And all the peoples see His glory.
Verse_Ch: 97:7 愿一切事奉雕制的偶像，靠虚无之神像自夸的，都蒙羞愧；万神哪，你们都当拜祂。 ###EN### Let all who serve a graven image be ashamed, Who make their boast in idols; Worship Him, all you gods.
Verse_Ch: 97:8 耶和华阿，因你的判断，锡安听见就喜乐，犹大的女子也欢腾。 ###EN### Zion hears and rejoices, And the daughters of Judah are glad, Because of Your judgments, O Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 97:9 因为耶和华阿，你是管理全地的至高者；你被尊崇，远超万神之上。 ###EN### For You, O Jehovah, are most high over all the earth; You are exalted far above all gods.
Verse_Ch: 97:10 你们爱耶和华的，当恨恶邪恶！祂保护虔诚人的性命，搭救他们脱离恶人的手。 ###EN### O you who love Jehovah, hate evil! He preserves the souls of His faithful ones; He delivers them from the hand of the wicked.
Verse_Ch: 97:11 撒播亮光是为义人，撒播喜乐是为心里正直的人。 ###EN### Light is sown for the righteous man, And rejoicing for the upright in heart.
Verse_Ch: 97:12 义人哪，你们当因耶和华喜乐，赞美祂可记念的圣名。 ###EN### Rejoice in Jehovah, O righteous ones; And praise His holy memorial.
Chapter_Header: 98
Verse_Ch: 98:1 你们要向耶和华唱新歌，因为祂行了奇妙的事。祂的右手和圣臂，为祂行了拯救。 ###EN### Sing to Jehovah a new song, For He has done wonderful things. His right hand and His holy arm Have accomplished salvation for Him.
Verse_Ch: 98:2 耶和华使人知道祂的救恩，在列邦人眼前显出祂的公义。 ###EN### Jehovah has made His salvation known; In the sight of the nations He has revealed His righteousness.
Verse_Ch: 98:3 祂记念祂向以色列家所施的慈爱与信实；地的四极，都看见我们神的救恩。 ###EN### He remembered His lovingkindness and His faithfulness Toward the house of Israel; All the ends of the earth have seen The salvation of our God.
Verse_Ch: 98:4 全地都要向耶和华欢呼；要发出大声，欢呼歌颂。 ###EN### Make a joyful noise to Jehovah, all the earth; Break forth, and sing for joy, and sing psalms.
Verse_Ch: 98:5 要用琴歌颂耶和华，用琴和诗歌的声音歌颂祂。 ###EN### Sing psalms to Jehovah with the lyre, With the lyre and the sound of melody.
Verse_Ch: 98:6 要用号和角声，在君王耶和华面前欢呼。 ###EN### With trumpets and the sound of the horn Make a joyful noise before the King, Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 98:7 愿海和其中所充满的澎湃，世界和住在其间的也要发声。 ###EN### Let the sea and its fullness roar, The world and those who inhabit it.
Verse_Ch: 98:8 愿江河拍手；愿诸山在耶和华面前一同欢呼， ###EN### Let the rivers clap their hands; Let the mountains sing for joy together
Verse_Ch: 98:9 因为祂来，要审判地；祂要按公义审判世界，按公正判断众民。 ###EN### Before Jehovah, for He is coming To judge the earth. He will judge the world with righteousness And the peoples with equity.
Chapter_Header: 99
Verse_Ch: 99:1 耶和华作王；众民当战抖。祂坐在二基路伯之间；地当动摇。 ###EN### Jehovah reigns; let the peoples tremble. He sits between the cherubim; let the earth shake.
Verse_Ch: 99:2 耶和华在锡安为大；祂被尊崇，超乎万民之上。 ###EN### Jehovah is great in Zion, And He is exalted over all the peoples.
Verse_Ch: 99:3 他们当赞美你大而可畏的名，这名是圣别的； ###EN### Let them praise Your great and awesome name-It is holy -
Verse_Ch: 99:4 又当赞美王的能力，祂喜爱公平。你坚立公正，在雅各中施行公理和公义。 ###EN### And the strength of the King, who loves justice. You have established equity; You have executed Justice and righteousness in Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 99:5 你们当尊崇耶和华我们的神，在祂脚凳前下拜；祂是圣别的。 ###EN### Exalt Jehovah our God, And worship at His footstool; Holy is He.
Verse_Ch: 99:6 在祂的祭司中有摩西和亚伦，在呼求祂名的人中有撒母耳，他们呼求耶和华，祂就应允他们。 ###EN### Moses and Aaron among His priests, And Samuel among those who called on His name-They called out to Jehovah, And He answered them.
Verse_Ch: 99:7 祂在云柱中对他们说话；他们遵守祂的法度，和祂所赐给他们的律例。 ###EN### In the pillar of cloud He spoke to them; They kept His testimonies and the statute that He gave them.
Verse_Ch: 99:8 耶和华我们的神阿，你应允了他们；你是赦免他们的神，却也是按他们所行施行报应的一位。 ###EN### O Jehovah our God, You answered them; You were a forgiving God to them, Yet One avenging their deeds.
Verse_Ch: 99:9 你们要尊崇耶和华我们的神，在祂的圣山下拜；因为耶和华我们的神是圣别的。 ###EN### Exalt Jehovah our God, And worship on His holy mountain; For holy is Jehovah our God.
Chapter_Header: 100
Verse_Ch: 100:1 全地当向耶和华欢呼。 ###EN### Make a joyful noise to Jehovah, all the earth.
Verse_Ch: 100:2 你们当欢喜的事奉耶和华；当欢唱着到祂面前来。 ###EN### Serve Jehovah with rejoicing; Come before His presence with joyful singing.
Verse_Ch: 100:3 你们当晓得耶和华是神；我们是祂造的，也是属祂的；我们是祂的民，也是祂草场的羊。 ###EN### Know that it is Jehovah who is God; It is He who has made us and not we ourselves. We are His people and the sheep of His pasture.
Verse_Ch: 100:4 当称谢着进入祂的门，赞美着进入祂的院；当感谢祂，颂赞祂的名。 ###EN### Enter His gates with thanksgiving, His courts with praise; Give thanks to Him; bless His name.
Verse_Ch: 100:5 因为耶和华本为善；祂的慈爱存到永远，祂的信实直到万代。 ###EN### For Jehovah is good; His lovingkindness is forever, And His faithfulness is to all generations.
Chapter_Header: 101
Verse_Ch: 101:1 我要歌唱慈爱和公平；耶和华阿，我要向你歌颂。 ###EN### I will sing of lovingkindness and justice; To You, O Jehovah, I will sing psalms.
Verse_Ch: 101:2 我要谨慎遵行完全的道路。你几时到我这里来呢？我要存完全的心，行在我家中。 ###EN### I will give careful heed to the way of the perfect. When will You come to me? I will walk in the perfectness of my heart Within my house.
Verse_Ch: 101:3 卑下的事，我都不摆在我眼前；偏离正路之人所作的事，我甚恨恶，不容沾在我身上。 ###EN### I will not set anything base Before my eyes; I hate what those who turn aside do; It will not cling to me.
Verse_Ch: 101:4 弯曲的心必远离我；一切的恶事，我不认识。 ###EN### A perverse heart will depart from me; No evil will I know.
Verse_Ch: 101:5 在暗中谗谤他邻居的，我必灭绝；眼目高傲，心里骄纵的，我必不容忍。 ###EN### He who secretly slanders his neighbor, Him I will destroy; He who is of a haughty look and a proud heart, Him I will not tolerate.
Verse_Ch: 101:6 我眼要看这地忠信的人，叫他们与我同住；行在完全道路上的，他要伺候我。 ###EN### My eyes are on the faithful of the land, That they may abide with me; He who walks in the way of the perfect, He will minister to me.
Verse_Ch: 101:7 行诡诈的，必不得住在我家里；说谎话的，必不得在我眼前坚立。 ###EN### He who practices deceit Will not dwell within my house; He who speaks lies will not be maintained In my sight.
Verse_Ch: 101:8 我每日早晨，要灭绝这地所有的恶人，好把一切作孽的，从耶和华的城里剪除。 ###EN### Morning by morning I will destroy All the wicked of the land, In order to cut off from the city of Jehovah All the workers of iniquity.
Chapter_Header: 102
Verse_Ch: 102:1 耶和华阿，求你听我的祷告；愿我的呼求达到你那里。 ###EN### O Jehovah, hear my prayer; And let my cry come unto You.
Verse_Ch: 102:2 我在急难的日子，求你不要向我掩面；求你向我侧耳；我呼求的日子，求你快快应允我。 ###EN### Do not hide Your face from me On the day of my distress; Incline Your ear to me; On the day when I call out, answer me quickly.
Verse_Ch: 102:3 因为我的年日如烟消逝，我的骨头如柴烧焦。 ###EN### For my days are consumed in smoke, And my bones burn like a hearth.
Verse_Ch: 102:4 我的心被击打，如草枯干，甚至我忘记吃饭。 ###EN### My heart is stricken like grass and dried up; Indeed I have even forgotten to eat my bread.
Verse_Ch: 102:5 因我唉哼的声音，我的骨头紧贴着肉。 ###EN### Because of the voice of my groaning My bones cling to my flesh.
Verse_Ch: 102:6 我如同旷野的鹈鹕；我好像荒场的鸱鸮。 ###EN### I am like a pelican of the wilderness; I have become like an owl of the desolate places.
Verse_Ch: 102:7 我儆醒不睡，就像房顶上孤单的麻雀。 ###EN### I watch, and I am like A lone sparrow on a housetop.
Verse_Ch: 102:8 我的仇敌终日辱骂我；向我猖狂的人，指着我赌咒。 ###EN### All day long my enemies reproach me; Those who deride me use me as a curse.
Verse_Ch: 102:9 我吃过炉灰，如同吃饭，用眼泪与我所喝的搀和。 ###EN### For I have eaten ashes like bread, And have mixed my drink with weeping,
Verse_Ch: 102:10 这都因你的恼恨和忿怒；因你把我拾起，又把我抛去。 ###EN### Because of Your indignation and Your wrath; For You have taken me up and cast me away.
Verse_Ch: 102:11 我的年日如日影偏斜；我也如草枯干。 ###EN### My days are like a shadow that declines, And I am dried up like grass.
Verse_Ch: 102:12 耶和华阿，你却永远长存；你可记念的名，也存到万代。 ###EN### But You, O Jehovah, abide forever; And Your memorial is from generation to generation.
Verse_Ch: 102:13 你必起来怜恤锡安，因现在是恩待她的时候；所定的日期已经到了。 ###EN### You will arise and have compassion on Zion, For it is time to be gracious to her; the appointed time has come.
Verse_Ch: 102:14 你的仆人原来喜悦她的石头，恩待她的尘土。 ###EN### For Your servants take pleasure in her stones, And show favor to her soil.
Verse_Ch: 102:15 列国要敬畏耶和华的名，地上诸王都要敬畏你的荣耀； ###EN### And the nations will fear the name of Jehovah, And all the kings of the earth, Your glory;
Verse_Ch: 102:16 因为耶和华建造了锡安，在祂荣耀里显现了。 ###EN### For Jehovah has built up Zion; He has appeared in His glory.
Verse_Ch: 102:17 祂垂顾穷乏人的祷告，并不藐视。 ###EN### He has regarded the prayer of the destitute, And has not despised their prayer.
Verse_Ch: 102:18 这必为后代的人记下，将来受造的民要赞美耶和华。 ###EN### This will be written for a generation to come, And a people to be created will praise Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 102:19 因为祂已从至高的圣所俯视；耶和华从天向地观看， ###EN### For He has looked down from the height of His sanctuary; From heaven Jehovah beheld the earth,
Verse_Ch: 102:20 要垂听被囚之人的叹息，释放那些命定要死的人； ###EN### To hear the groaning of the prisoner, To release those appointed to die;
Verse_Ch: 102:21 使人在锡安传述耶和华的名，在耶路撒冷传述赞美祂的话； ###EN### That the name of Jehovah may be declared in Zion, And His praise, in Jerusalem,
Verse_Ch: 102:22 就是在众民和列国一同聚集，事奉耶和华的时候。 ###EN### When the peoples are gathered together, And the kingdoms, to serve Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 102:23 祂使我的力量中途衰弱，使我的年日短少。 ###EN### He has weakened my strength in the way; He has shortened my days.
Verse_Ch: 102:24 我说，我的神阿，不要在我中年把我提去；你的年数世世无穷。 ###EN### I said, My God, Do not take me away in the middle of my days; Your years are throughout all generations.
Verse_Ch: 102:25 你起初立了地的根基，诸天也是你手的工作。 ###EN### Of old You laid the foundation of the earth, And the heavens are the work of Your hands.
Verse_Ch: 102:26 天地都要灭没，你却长存；天地都要像衣服渐渐旧了；你要将天地如衣裳更换，天地就改变了。 ###EN### They will perish, but You endure; Indeed all of them will wear out like a garment; Like clothing You will change them, And they will be changed.
Verse_Ch: 102:27 惟有你仍是一样，你的年数也没有穷尽。 ###EN### But You are the same, And Your years are without end.
Verse_Ch: 102:28 你仆人的子孙要长久安居，他们的后裔要坚立在你面前。 ###EN### The children of Your servants will continue, And their seed will be established before You.
Chapter_Header: 103
Verse_Ch: 103:1 我的魂哪，你要颂赞耶和华；在我里面的一切，都要颂赞祂的圣名。 ###EN### Bless Jehovah, O my soul; And all that is within me, bless His holy name.
Verse_Ch: 103:2 我的魂哪，你要颂赞耶和华，不可忘记祂的一切恩惠： ###EN### Bless Jehovah, O my soul; And do not forget all His benefits:
Verse_Ch: 103:3 祂赦免你的一切罪孽，医治你的一切疾病； ###EN### He pardons all your iniquities; He heals all your diseases;
Verse_Ch: 103:4 祂救赎你的命不见朽坏，以慈爱和怜恤为你的冠冕； ###EN### He redeems your life from the pit; He crowns you with lovingkindness and compassions;
Verse_Ch: 103:5 祂用美物使你所愿的得以满足，以致你如鹰反老还童。 ###EN### He satisfies the prime of your life with good, So that your youth is renewed like the eagle.
Verse_Ch: 103:6 耶和华施行公义，为一切受欺压的伸冤。 ###EN### Jehovah executes righteous acts, And judgments for all who are oppressed.
Verse_Ch: 103:7 祂使摩西知道祂的法则，叫以色列人晓得祂的作为。 ###EN### He made His ways known to Moses; His acts, to the children of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 103:8 耶和华有怜恤，有恩典，不轻易发怒，且有丰盛的慈爱。 ###EN### Jehovah is compassionate and gracious, Long-suffering and abundant in lovingkindness.
Verse_Ch: 103:9 祂不长久责备，也不永远怀怒。 ###EN### He will not always contend with us, Nor will He keep His anger forever.
Verse_Ch: 103:10 祂没有按我们的罪过对待我们，也没有照我们的罪孽报应我们。 ###EN### He has not dealt with us according to our sins, Nor has He recompensed us according to our iniquities.
Verse_Ch: 103:11 天离地何等的高，祂的慈爱向敬畏祂的人，也是何等的大。 ###EN### For as high as the heavens are above the earth, So great is His lovingkindness upon those who fear Him.
Verse_Ch: 103:12 东离西有多远，祂叫我们的过犯，离我们也有多远。 ###EN### As far as the east is from the west, So far has He removed our transgressions from us.
Verse_Ch: 103:13 父亲怎样怜恤他的儿女，耶和华也怎样怜恤敬畏祂的人。 ###EN### As compassionate as a father is toward his children, So compassionate is Jehovah toward those who fear Him.
Verse_Ch: 103:14 因为祂知道我们的本体，记念我们不过是尘土。 ###EN### For He knows our frame; He remembers that we are dust.
Verse_Ch: 103:15 至于世人，他的年日如草一样；他发旺如野地的花： ###EN### Man-his days are like grass; He flourishes like a field flower:
Verse_Ch: 103:16 经风一吹，便归无有；原处也不再认识它。 ###EN### For the wind passes over it, and it is no more; And its own place knows of it no longer.
Verse_Ch: 103:17 但耶和华的慈爱，临及敬畏祂的人，从亘古到永远；祂的公义，也归于子子孙孙； ###EN### But Jehovah's lovingkindness is from eternity Unto eternity upon those who fear Him, And His righteousness is to the children's children;
Verse_Ch: 103:18 就是那些遵守祂的约，记念祂的训辞而遵行的人。 ###EN### To those who keep His covenant And remember His precepts so as to do them.
Verse_Ch: 103:19 耶和华在天上立定宝座，祂的国统管万有。 ###EN### Jehovah has established His throne in the heavens, And His kingdom rules over all.
Verse_Ch: 103:20 你们作祂天使，就是听从祂的命令，大有能力执行祂话语的，都要颂赞耶和华。 ###EN### Bless Jehovah, you His angels, Who are mighty in strength to perform His word, By obeying the voice of His word.
Verse_Ch: 103:21 你们作祂众军，作祂仆役，行祂所喜悦的，都要颂赞耶和华。 ###EN### Bless Jehovah, all you His hosts, You His ministers who execute His will.
Verse_Ch: 103:22 你们一切被祂造的，在祂所治理的各处，都要颂赞耶和华。我的魂哪，你要颂赞耶和华。 ###EN### Bless Jehovah, all you His works, In all places of His dominion. Bless Jehovah, O my soul.
Chapter_Header: 104
Verse_Ch: 104:1 我的魂哪，你要颂赞耶和华。耶和华我的神阿，你为至大。你以尊荣威严为衣服， ###EN### Bless Jehovah, O my soul. O Jehovah my God, You are very great. You are clothed with majesty and splendor,
Verse_Ch: 104:2 披上亮光，如披外袍；铺张诸天，如铺幕幔。 ###EN### Wrapped with light as with a garment; You stretch out the heavens like a tent curtain.
Verse_Ch: 104:3 耶和华在诸水中立楼阁的栋梁，用云彩为车辇，借着风的翅膀而行。 ###EN### He lays the beams of His upper chambers in the waters; He makes the clouds His chariot; He walks upon the wings of the wind.
Verse_Ch: 104:4 祂以风为使者，以火焰为仆役； ###EN### He makes winds His messengers, Flames of fire His ministers.
Verse_Ch: 104:5 将地立在根基上，使地永永远远不动摇。 ###EN### He established the earth upon its foundations, So that it cannot be moved forever and ever.
Verse_Ch: 104:6 你用深渊如衣裳覆盖地面；诸水立于山岭之上。 ###EN### You covered it with the deep as with a garment; The waters stood above the mountains.
