Verse_Ch: 104:7 你的斥责一发，水便奔逃；你的雷声一发，水便奔流， ###EN### At Your rebuke they fled; At the voice of Your thunder they rushed away -
Verse_Ch: 104:8 (诸山升上，诸谷沉下，)归你为诸水所建立之处。 ###EN### The mountains rose, the valleys sank-To the place that You established for them.
Verse_Ch: 104:9 你定了界限，使水不能过去，不再转回覆盖地面。 ###EN### You set a border that they may not pass over, That they may not turn back to cover the earth.
Verse_Ch: 104:10 耶和华使泉源涌在山谷，流在山间； ###EN### He makes the springs gush forth in the valleys; They run among the mountains;
Verse_Ch: 104:11 使野地的走兽有水喝；野驴得解其渴。 ###EN### They give drink to every beast of the field; The wild asses quench their thirst.
Verse_Ch: 104:12 天上的飞鸟在水旁住宿，在枝叶间鸣叫。 ###EN### The birds of heaven dwell alongside them; They utter their voice among the branches.
Verse_Ch: 104:13 祂从楼阁中浇灌山岭。因祂作为的果效，地就丰足。 ###EN### He waters the mountains from His upper chambers. The earth is satisfied with the fruit of Your works.
Verse_Ch: 104:14 祂使草生长，给牲畜吃；使菜蔬生长，供给人用，使人从地里出产食物： ###EN### He causes the grass to grow for the cattle, And herbage for man's use, That he may bring forth food from the earth:
Verse_Ch: 104:15 有酒使人心喜悦，有油使人容光焕发，有粮给人加添心力。 ###EN### Even wine that cheers man's heart, Oil that makes his face shine, And bread that sustains man's heart.
Verse_Ch: 104:16 耶和华的树木，就是祂所栽种，利巴嫩的香柏树，都满了汁浆， ###EN### The trees of Jehovah are full of sap, The cedars of Lebanon, which He planted,
Verse_Ch: 104:17 雀鸟在其上搭窝；至于鹳，松树是它的房屋。 ###EN### Where the birds build their nests; As for the stork, the cypresses are her house.
Verse_Ch: 104:18 高山为野山羊的住所；岩石为石獾的藏处。 ###EN### The high mountains are for the wild goats; The cliffs are a refuge to the rockbadgers.
Verse_Ch: 104:19 耶和华造月亮为定节令；日头自知何时沉落。 ###EN### He made the moon to mark seasons; The sun knows the time of its going down.
Verse_Ch: 104:20 你安设黑暗，便有了夜晚；夜间林中的百兽就四处爬动。 ###EN### You make darkness, and it is night, In which all the beasts of the forest creep about.
Verse_Ch: 104:21 少壮狮子吼叫，要抓食，向神寻求食物。 ###EN### The young lions roar after their prey, Even to seek their food from God.
Verse_Ch: 104:22 日头一出，兽便退隐，卧在洞里。 ###EN### The sun rises: they retreat And lie down in their dens.
Verse_Ch: 104:23 人出去作工，劳碌直到晚上。 ###EN### Man goes forth to his work And to his labor until evening.
Verse_Ch: 104:24 耶和华阿，你所造的何其多！这些都是你用智慧造成的；遍地满了你的造物。 ###EN### How many are Your works, O Jehovah! In wisdom You have made all of them; The earth is full of Your creatures.
Verse_Ch: 104:25 那边有海，又大又广；其中有爬物无数，大小活物都有。 ###EN### Yonder is the sea, great and extensively wide; There the creeping things are, even without number, The small animals with the great.
Verse_Ch: 104:26 那里有船航行；有你所造的鳄鱼，在其中嬉戏。 ###EN### There the ships go; Leviathan is there, whom You have formed To play in it.
Verse_Ch: 104:27 这一切都仰望你按时给它们食物。 ###EN### They all wait for You, That You may give them food at the proper time.
Verse_Ch: 104:28 你给它们，它们便拾取；你张开手，它们就饱得美食。 ###EN### You give to them; they gather. You open Your hand; they are satisfied with good.
Verse_Ch: 104:29 你掩面，它们便惊惶；你收回它们的气，它们就死亡，归于尘土。 ###EN### You hide Your face; they are troubled. You take away their breath; they perish, And return to their dust.
Verse_Ch: 104:30 你发出你的灵，它们便受造，你也使地面更换一新。 ###EN### You send forth Your Spirit; they are created, And You renew the surface of the ground.
Verse_Ch: 104:31 愿耶和华的荣耀存到永远！愿耶和华因自己所造的喜乐； ###EN### May the glory of Jehovah endure forever! May Jehovah rejoice in His works,
Verse_Ch: 104:32 祂看地，地便震动；祂摸山，山就冒烟！ ###EN### He who looks on the earth, and it trembles; He who touches the mountains, and they smoke!
Verse_Ch: 104:33 我要一生向耶和华唱诗；我还活的时候，要向我神歌颂。 ###EN### I will sing to Jehovah while I live; I will sing psalms to my God while I yet have being.
Verse_Ch: 104:34 愿祂以我的默念为甘甜；我要因耶和华喜乐。 ###EN### May my musing be sweet to Him; I will rejoice in Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 104:35 愿罪人从地上灭绝，愿恶人归于无有。我的魂哪，你要颂赞耶和华。阿利路亚。 ###EN### May the sinners be consumed from off the earth, And may the wicked be no more. Bless Jehovah, O my soul. Hallelujah.
Chapter_Header: 105
Verse_Ch: 105:1 你们要称谢耶和华，呼求祂的名，在万民中传扬祂的作为。 ###EN### Give thanks to Jehovah; call upon His name; Make known His deeds among the peoples.
Verse_Ch: 105:2 要向祂唱诗、歌颂，谈论祂一切奇妙的作为。 ###EN### Sing to Him; sing psalms to Him; Muse upon all His wondrous deeds.
Verse_Ch: 105:3 要因祂的圣名夸耀；寻求耶和华的人，心中应当喜乐。 ###EN### Glory in His holy name; Let the heart of those who seek Jehovah rejoice.
Verse_Ch: 105:4 要寻求耶和华与祂的能力，时常寻求祂的面。 ###EN### Seek Jehovah and His strength; Seek His face continually.
Verse_Ch: 105:5 祂仆人亚伯拉罕的后裔，祂所拣选雅各的子孙哪，你们要记念祂所行奇妙的作为，和祂的奇事，并祂口中的判语。 ###EN### Remember His wondrous deeds, which He has done, His signs and the judgments of His mouth,
Verse_Ch: 105:6  ###EN### O seed of Abraham His servant, O children of Jacob, His chosen ones.
Verse_Ch: 105:7 祂是耶和华我们的神，全地都有祂的判断。 ###EN### He is Jehovah our God; His judgments are in all the earth.
Verse_Ch: 105:8 祂记念祂的约，直到永远；记念祂所吩咐的话，直到千代， ###EN### He has remembered His covenant forever, The word that He commanded to a thousand generations,
Verse_Ch: 105:9 就是祂与亚伯拉罕所立的约，向以撒所起的誓。 ###EN### The covenant that He made with Abraham, And His oath unto Isaac.
Verse_Ch: 105:10 祂又将这约向雅各定为律例，向以色列定为永远的约， ###EN### And He confirmed it unto Jacob as a statute, Unto Israel as an eternal covenant,
Verse_Ch: 105:11 说，我必将迦南地赐给你，作你们产业的分。 ###EN### Saying, To you I will give the land of Canaan, The portion of your inheritance;
Verse_Ch: 105:12 当时他们人数有限，非常稀少，并且在那地为寄居的。 ###EN### When they were men few in number, Indeed very few and strangers in the land.
Verse_Ch: 105:13 他们从这邦游到那邦，从这国行到那国。 ###EN### And they went about from nation to nation, From one kingdom to another people.
Verse_Ch: 105:14 祂不容什么人欺压他们，为他们的缘故责备君王， ###EN### He allowed no man to oppress them; Indeed He rebuked kings for their sake.
Verse_Ch: 105:15 说，不可触犯我所膏的人，也不可加害我的申言者。 ###EN### Saying, Do not touch My anointed ones, And do My prophets no harm.
Verse_Ch: 105:16 祂命饥荒降在那地上，将所倚靠的粮食，全行断绝。 ###EN### And He called a famine upon the land; He broke the whole staff of bread.
Verse_Ch: 105:17 祂在他们以先打发一个人去；约瑟被卖为奴仆。 ###EN### He sent a man before them; Joseph was sold as a servant.
Verse_Ch: 105:18 人用脚镣伤他的脚，他被铁链捆拘。 ###EN### They afflicted his feet with fetters; He himself was placed in irons.
Verse_Ch: 105:19 耶和华的话试炼他，直等到他所说的应验了。 ###EN### Until the time when his word came to pass, The word of Jehovah tried him.
Verse_Ch: 105:20 王打发人把他解开，治理众民的，把他释放了； ###EN### The king sent men and freed him, Even the ruler of the peoples, and let him go.
Verse_Ch: 105:21 立他作王家之主，掌管王一切所有的， ###EN### He made him lord of his house And ruler over all his possessions,
Verse_Ch: 105:22 使他随意捆绑王的臣宰，将智慧教导王的长老。 ###EN### To imprison his princes at will, And to teach his elders wisdom.
Verse_Ch: 105:23 于是以色列到了埃及，雅各在含地寄居。 ###EN### Then Israel came into Egypt, And Jacob sojourned in the land of Ham.
Verse_Ch: 105:24 耶和华使祂的百姓极其繁多，使他们比敌人强盛； ###EN### And He made His people very fruitful, And caused them to be mightier than their adversaries.
Verse_Ch: 105:25 使敌人的心转去恨祂的百姓，并用诡计待祂的仆人。 ###EN### He turned their heart to hate His people, To deal craftily with His servants.
Verse_Ch: 105:26 祂打发祂的仆人摩西，和祂所拣选的亚伦。 ###EN### He sent Moses His servant, And Aaron, whom He had chosen.
Verse_Ch: 105:27 他们在敌人中间施行祂的神迹，在含地施行祂的奇事。 ###EN### They set His signs among them, And wonders in the land of Ham.
Verse_Ch: 105:28 祂打发黑暗，使那地黑暗；他们没有违背祂的话。 ###EN### He sent darkness and made it dark; And they did not rebel against His words.
Verse_Ch: 105:29 祂叫埃及的水变为血，叫他们的鱼死了。 ###EN### He turned their waters into blood, And killed their fish.
Verse_Ch: 105:30 在他们的地上，甚至在他们君王的内室，青蛙多多滋生。 ###EN### Their land teemed with frogs, Even in the chambers of their kings.
Verse_Ch: 105:31 祂说一声，苍蝇就成群而来，并且他们四境之内都有了虱子。 ###EN### He spoke, and a swarm of flies came; There were gnats within all their borders.
Verse_Ch: 105:32 祂给他们降下冰雹为雨，在他们的地上降下火焰。 ###EN### He gave them hail for rain, And flaming fire in their land.
Verse_Ch: 105:33 祂也击打他们的葡萄树和无花果树，打坏他们境内的树木。 ###EN### He struck their vines and their fig trees, And He broke the trees of their borders.
Verse_Ch: 105:34 祂说一声，群蝗和舔蝗就来，不计其数， ###EN### He spoke, and the swarming locusts came, And the licking locusts, even without number.
Verse_Ch: 105:35 吃尽了他们地上各样的菜蔬，和土地的出产。 ###EN### And they ate every herb in their land, And they ate the fruit of their ground.
Verse_Ch: 105:36 祂又击杀他们那地一切的长子，就是他们强壮时头生的。 ###EN### He struck all the firstborn in their land, The first of all their vigor.
Verse_Ch: 105:37 祂领自己的百姓带银子金子出来，祂支派中没有一个软弱的。 ###EN### And He brought them out with silver and gold, And there was none among His tribes who stumbled.
Verse_Ch: 105:38 他们出来的时候，埃及人便欢喜；因为埃及人惧怕他们。 ###EN### Egypt rejoiced at their going forth, For a dread of them had fallen upon them.
Verse_Ch: 105:39 祂铺张云彩当遮盖，夜间使火光照。 ###EN### He spread a cloud for a covering, And a fire to give light by night.
Verse_Ch: 105:40 他们一求，祂就使鹌鹑飞来，并用天上的粮食，叫他们饱足。 ###EN### They asked, and He brought quails; And He satisfied them with the bread of heaven.
Verse_Ch: 105:41 祂打开磐石，水就涌出；在干旱之处，水流成河。 ###EN### He opened the rock, and water gushed forth; It ran in the dry places like a river.
Verse_Ch: 105:42 这都因祂记念祂的圣言，和祂的仆人亚伯拉罕。 ###EN### For He remembered His holy word And Abraham His servant.
Verse_Ch: 105:43 祂带领百姓欢乐而出，带领选民欢呼前往。 ###EN### And He brought forth His people with gladness, His chosen ones with a ringing shout.
Verse_Ch: 105:44 祂将列国的地赐给他们，他们便承受众民劳碌得来的， ###EN### And He gave them the lands of the nations, And they took possession of the labor of the peoples,
Verse_Ch: 105:45 好使他们谨守祂的律例，遵守祂的律法。阿利路亚。 ###EN### So that they might keep His statutes And observe His laws. Hallelujah.
Chapter_Header: 106
Verse_Ch: 106:1 阿利路亚。你们要称谢耶和华，因祂本为善，祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### Hallelujah. Give thanks to Jehovah, for He is good, For His lovingkindness is forever.
Verse_Ch: 106:2 谁能述说耶和华大能的作为？谁能宣告一切赞美祂的话？ ###EN### Who can utter the mighty acts of Jehovah, Or declare all His praise?
Verse_Ch: 106:3 那些维护公理，常行公义的人，是有福的。 ###EN### Blessed are those who maintain justice, Who execute righteousness at all times.
Verse_Ch: 106:4 耶和华阿，你用恩惠待你的百姓，求你也用这恩惠记念我；求你用你的救恩眷顾我， ###EN### Remember me, O Jehovah, with Your favor toward Your people; Visit me with Your salvation,
Verse_Ch: 106:5 使我得见你的选民享美福，因你国民的喜乐而喜乐，与你的产业一同夸耀。 ###EN### That I may see the prosperity of Your chosen ones, That I may rejoice in the joy of Your nation, That I may glory with Your inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 106:6 我们与我们的祖宗一同犯罪；我们作了孽，行了恶。 ###EN### We have sinned with our fathers; We committed iniquity; we have acted wickedly.
Verse_Ch: 106:7 我们的祖宗在埃及不明白你的奇事；他们不记念你丰盛的慈爱，反倒在红海边行了悖逆。 ###EN### Our fathers in Egypt Did not understand Your wonders; They did not remember the multitude of Your acts of lovingkindness, But rebelled by the sea, at the Red Sea.
Verse_Ch: 106:8 然而祂因自己的名拯救他们，为要使人知道祂的大能。 ###EN### But He saved them for His name's sake, That He might make His power known.
Verse_Ch: 106:9 祂斥责红海，海便干了；祂带领他们经过深处，如同经过旷野。 ###EN### Thus He rebuked the Red Sea, and it dried up; And He led them through the depths as through the wilderness.
Verse_Ch: 106:10 祂拯救他们脱离恨他们之人的手，救赎他们脱离仇敌的手。 ###EN### And He saved them from the hand of him who hated them, And redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.
Verse_Ch: 106:11 水淹没他们的敌人，没有一个存留。 ###EN### The water then covered their adversaries; Not one of them was left.
Verse_Ch: 106:12 那时他们才信了祂的话，歌唱赞美祂。 ###EN### Then they believed His words; They sang His praise.
Verse_Ch: 106:13 他们很快就忘了祂的作为，不等候祂的指教， ###EN### Soon they forgot His works; They did not wait for His counsel,
Verse_Ch: 106:14 反倒在旷野大起贪欲，在荒地试探神。 ###EN### But lusted exceedingly in the wilderness, And tempted God in the desert.
Verse_Ch: 106:15 祂将他们所求的赐给他们，却使他们的魂衰弱。 ###EN### And He gave them their request, But He sent leanness into their soul.
Verse_Ch: 106:16 他们又在营中嫉妒摩西，和耶和华的圣者亚伦。 ###EN### And they were jealous of Moses in the camp And of Aaron, the holy one of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 106:17 于是地裂开，吞下大坍，并掩盖亚比兰一党的人。 ###EN### The earth opened, and it swallowed up Dathan And covered the company of Abiram.
Verse_Ch: 106:18 有火在他们的党中着起，有火焰烧毁了恶人。 ###EN### And a fire burned among their company; A flame engulfed the wicked.
Verse_Ch: 106:19 他们在何烈山造了牛犊，叩拜铸成的像。 ###EN### They made a calf in Horeb, And worshipped a molten image.
Verse_Ch: 106:20 如此将他们的荣耀，换为吃草之牛的像。 ###EN### Thus they exchanged their glory For the image of an ox that eats grass.
Verse_Ch: 106:21 他们竟忘了神他们的救主；祂曾在埃及行大事， ###EN### They forgot God their Savior, Who had done great things in Egypt,
Verse_Ch: 106:22 在含地行奇事，在红海边行可畏的事。 ###EN### Wondrous deeds in the land of Ham, Awesome things by the Red Sea.
Verse_Ch: 106:23 所以祂说要灭绝他们；若非有祂所拣选的摩西站在祂面前，堵住破口，使祂的忿怒转消，不灭绝他们，他们早已灭亡了。 ###EN### Therefore He said that He would destroy them, And would have, had not Moses His chosen one Stood in the breach before Him To turn away His wrath from destroying them.
Verse_Ch: 106:24 他们又藐视那可喜爱之地，不信祂的话； ###EN### Then they despised the pleasant land; They did not believe in His word;
Verse_Ch: 106:25 反倒在自己帐棚内发怨言，不听耶和华的声音。 ###EN### Rather they murmured in their tents; They did not listen to the voice of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 106:26 所以祂对他们举手起誓，必叫他们倒在旷野， ###EN### Therefore He lifted up His hand and swore to them That He would make them fall in the wilderness,
Verse_Ch: 106:27 叫他们的后裔倒在列国之中，分散在各地。 ###EN### And that He would make their seed fall among the nations, And that He would disperse them among the lands.
Verse_Ch: 106:28 他们又与巴力毗珥连合，且吃了祭死神的物。 ###EN### Then they joined themselves to Baal-peor, And ate sacrifices offered to the dead.
Verse_Ch: 106:29 这样，他们以所行的惹耶和华发怒，便有瘟疫爆发在他们中间。 ###EN### Thus they provoked Him to anger by their actions, And the plague broke out among them.
Verse_Ch: 106:30 那时非尼哈站起来干豫，瘟疫才止息。 ###EN### Then Phinehas stood up and intervened, And the plague was stayed;
Verse_Ch: 106:31 那就算为他的义，世世代代直到永远。 ###EN### And it has been accounted to him as righteousness From generation to generation unto eternity.
Verse_Ch: 106:32 他们在米利巴水又叫耶和华发怒，甚至摩西也因他们受了亏损； ###EN### Then they angered Him at the waters of Meribah, So that it went ill with Moses on account of them;
Verse_Ch: 106:33 是因他们违背祂的灵；摩西用嘴说了急躁的话。 ###EN### For they rebelled against His Spirit, And he spoke rashly with his lips.
Verse_Ch: 106:34 他们不照耶和华所吩咐的，灭绝外邦民， ###EN### They did not destroy the peoples, As Jehovah had commanded them;
Verse_Ch: 106:35 反与他们混杂相合，学习他们的行为， ###EN### But they mingled themselves with the nations And learned their practices.
Verse_Ch: 106:36 事奉他们的偶像；这就成了自己的网罗。 ###EN### And they served their idols, Which became a snare to them.
Verse_Ch: 106:37 他们又把自己的儿女献给鬼魔为祭物， ###EN### They also sacrificed their sons And their daughters to demons,
Verse_Ch: 106:38 流无辜人的血，就是自己儿女的血，把他们献给迦南的偶像为祭物；那地就被血污秽了。 ###EN### And poured out innocent blood, The blood of their sons and daughters, whom they sacrificed to the idols of Canaan; And the land was polluted with bloodshed.
Verse_Ch: 106:39 这样，他们被自己所作的污秽了，在行为上犯了邪淫。 ###EN### Thus they were defiled by their practices, And went about as harlots by their actions.
Verse_Ch: 106:40 耶和华向祂的百姓发怒，憎恶祂的产业。 ###EN### And the anger of Jehovah was kindled against His people, And He abhorred His inheritance.
Verse_Ch: 106:41 祂将他们交在外邦人的手里：恨他们的人就辖制他们， ###EN### And He gave them over into the hand of the nations: And those who hated them ruled over them,
Verse_Ch: 106:42 他们的仇敌也欺压他们，他们就伏在那些人手下。 ###EN### And their enemies oppressed them, And they were subdued under their hand.
Verse_Ch: 106:43 祂屡次搭救他们，他们却设谋悖逆，就因自己的罪孽降为卑下。 ###EN### Many times He delivered them, But they were rebellious in their counsel, And they were brought low in their iniquity.
Verse_Ch: 106:44 然而祂听见他们呼求的时候，就看顾他们的急难； ###EN### Yet He regarded their distress When He heard their cry,
Verse_Ch: 106:45 为他们的缘故记念祂的约，照祂丰盛的慈爱后悔； ###EN### And for their sake He remembered His covenant, And repented according to the multitude of His acts of lovingkindness;
Verse_Ch: 106:46 祂也使他们在一切掳掠他们的人面前蒙怜恤。 ###EN### And He caused them to find compassion With all their captors.
Verse_Ch: 106:47 耶和华我们的神阿，求你拯救我们，从外邦中招聚我们，我们好称谢你的圣名，以赞美你为夸耀。 ###EN### Save us, O Jehovah our God; And gather us out of the nations, That we may give thanks to Your holy name, That we may glory in Your praise.
Verse_Ch: 106:48 耶和华以色列的神，从亘古直到永远，是当受颂赞的。愿众民都说，阿们。阿利路亚。 ###EN### Blessed be Jehovah the God of Israel, From eternity to eternity. And let all the people say, Amen. Hallelujah.
Chapter_Header: 107
Verse_Ch: 107:1 你们要称谢耶和华，因祂本为善，祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### Give thanks to Jehovah, for He is good, For His lovingkindness is forever.
Verse_Ch: 107:2 愿耶和华的赎民说这话，他们是祂从敌人手中所救赎的， ###EN### Let the redeemed of Jehovah say so, Whom He redeemed from the hand of the adversary,
Verse_Ch: 107:3 从各地，从东从西，从北从南，所招聚来的。 ###EN### And gathered out of the lands, From the east and from the west, From the north and from the south.
Verse_Ch: 107:4 他们在旷野，在荒野的路上飘流，寻不见可住的城邑； ###EN### They wandered in the wilderness, on the desert way; They found no city of habitation.
Verse_Ch: 107:5 又饥又渴，里面的魂发昏。 ###EN### Hungry and thirsty, Their soul fainted within them.
Verse_Ch: 107:6 于是他们在患难中哀求耶和华，祂就从他们的祸患中搭救他们； ###EN### Then they cried out to Jehovah in their trouble, And He delivered them from their distresses.
Verse_Ch: 107:7 又领他们行走直路，使他们走到可居住的城邑。 ###EN### And He led them on a straight way That they might come to a city of habitation.
Verse_Ch: 107:8 但愿人因耶和华的慈爱，和祂向世人所行的奇事，都称谢祂。 ###EN### Let them give thanks to Jehovah for His lovingkindness And for His wondrous deeds to the children of men.
Verse_Ch: 107:9 因祂使干渴的人得以满足，使饥饿的人得饱美物。 ###EN### For He satisfies the thirsty soul, And the famished soul He fills with good.
Verse_Ch: 107:10 那些坐在黑暗中死荫里的人，被困苦和铁链捆锁， ###EN### Some inhabited darkness and the shadow of death, And were bound in affliction and irons,
Verse_Ch: 107:11 是因他们违背神的话语，藐视至高者的指教； ###EN### Because they rebelled against the words of God And spurned the counsel of the Most High;
Verse_Ch: 107:12 所以祂用劳苦制伏他们的心；他们跌倒，无人扶助。 ###EN### Therefore He brought down their heart with labor; They stumbled, and there was no one to help them.
Verse_Ch: 107:13 于是他们在患难中哀求耶和华，祂就从他们的祸患中拯救他们。 ###EN### Then they cried out to Jehovah in their trouble, And He saved them from their distresses.
Verse_Ch: 107:14 祂从黑暗和死荫里，领他们出来，折断他们的绑索。 ###EN### He brought them out of darkness and the shadow of death, And He broke apart their bonds.
Verse_Ch: 107:15 但愿人因耶和华的慈爱，和祂向世人所行的奇事，都称谢祂。 ###EN### Let them give thanks to Jehovah for His lovingkindness And for His wondrous deeds to the children of men.
Verse_Ch: 107:16 因为祂打破了铜门，砍断了铁闩。 ###EN### For He breaks down the doors of bronze And cuts down the bars of iron.
Verse_Ch: 107:17 愚妄人因自己过犯的行径，和自己的罪孽受苦。 ###EN### Some were fools, because of their way of transgression; And because of their iniquities, they were afflicted.
Verse_Ch: 107:18 他们的魂厌恶各样的食物，就临近死门。 ###EN### Their soul loathed all food, And they drew near to the gates of death.
Verse_Ch: 107:19 于是他们在患难中哀求耶和华，祂就从他们的祸患中拯救他们。 ###EN### Then they cried out to Jehovah in their trouble, And He saved them out of their distresses.
Verse_Ch: 107:20 祂发出话语医治他们，救他们不见朽坏。 ###EN### He sent forth His word and healed them, And He delivered them from the pits of destruction .
Verse_Ch: 107:21 但愿人因耶和华的慈爱，和祂向世人所行的奇事，都称谢祂。 ###EN### Let them give thanks to Jehovah for His lovingkindness And for His wondrous deeds to the children of men.
Verse_Ch: 107:22 愿他们献上感谢祭，用乐歌述说祂的作为。 ###EN### And let them offer sacrifices of thanksgiving And declare His doings in joyful song.
Verse_Ch: 107:23 那些坐船下到海中，在大水上经理事务的人， ###EN### Those who go down to the sea in ships, Conducting business on the mighty waters,
Verse_Ch: 107:24 他们看见耶和华的作为，并祂在深水中的奇事。 ###EN### These see Jehovah's doings And His wondrous deeds in the deep.
Verse_Ch: 107:25 因祂一吩咐，就兴起狂风，扬起海中的波浪。 ###EN### For He commanded and raised up a storm wind, And it lifted up the waves of the sea.
Verse_Ch: 107:26 他们上到天空，下到深渊；他们的心因灾难便融化。 ###EN### They mounted up to the heavens; they went down to the depths; Their soul melted in the calamity.
Verse_Ch: 107:27 他们摇摇晃晃，东倒西歪，好像醉酒的人；他们的智慧无法可施。 ###EN### They reeled and staggered like a drunken man, And were at their wits' end.
Verse_Ch: 107:28 于是他们在患难中哀求耶和华，祂就领他们从祸患中出来。 ###EN### Then they cried out to Jehovah in their trouble, And He brought them out of their distresses.
Verse_Ch: 107:29 祂使狂风止息，海浪就平静。 ###EN### He made the storm be still, And the waves of the sea were calm;
Verse_Ch: 107:30 风息浪静，他们便欢喜，祂就引他们到所愿去的港口。 ###EN### And they rejoiced that they were quiet, And He brought them to the haven they desired.
Verse_Ch: 107:31 但愿人因耶和华的慈爱，和祂向世人所行的奇事，都称谢祂。 ###EN### Let them give thanks to Jehovah for His lovingkindness And for His wondrous deeds to the children of men.
Verse_Ch: 107:32 愿他们在百姓的大会中尊崇祂，在长老的会集中赞美祂。 ###EN### And let them exalt Him in the congregation of the people And praise Him in the assembly of the elders.
Verse_Ch: 107:33 祂使江河变为旷野，叫水泉变为干渴之地； ###EN### He turns rivers into a wilderness, And springs of water into thirsty ground;
Verse_Ch: 107:34 使多结果实的地变为咸地，这都因其间居民的邪恶。 ###EN### Fruitful land into a salt flat, Because of the wickedness of those who dwell in it.
Verse_Ch: 107:35 祂使旷野变为水潭，叫旱地变为水泉。 ###EN### He turns a wilderness into a pool of water, And a dry land into springs of water.
Verse_Ch: 107:36 祂使饥饿的人住在那里，好兴建可住的城邑， ###EN### And He makes the hungry dwell there, That they may prepare a city of habitation
Verse_Ch: 107:37 又种田地，栽葡萄园，得着丰盛的出产。 ###EN### And sow fields and plant vineyards And get a fruitful yield.
Verse_Ch: 107:38 祂又赐福给他们，叫他们大大增多；也不叫他们的牲畜减少。 ###EN### He also blesses them, and they are multiplied greatly; And He does not let their cattle decrease.
Verse_Ch: 107:39 当他们因暴虐、患难、愁苦，人数减少，并且卑屈， ###EN### When they are diminished and bowed down Through oppression, trouble, and sorrow,
Verse_Ch: 107:40 祂使贵胄蒙羞被辱，使他们在荒废无路之地飘流。 ###EN### He pours contempt on princes, And makes them wander in a pathless waste.
Verse_Ch: 107:41 祂却将穷乏人安置在高处，脱离苦难，使他的家族繁衍，如同羊群。 ###EN### But He raises the needy man high above affliction And makes his families like flocks.
Verse_Ch: 107:42 正直人看见就喜乐；一切作孽之人都塞口无言。 ###EN### The upright see it and rejoice; And all iniquity stops its mouth.
Verse_Ch: 107:43 谁有智慧？愿他留意这些事，并思想耶和华的慈爱。 ###EN### Who is wise? Then let him observe these things And consider the lovingkindness of Jehovah.
Chapter_Header: 108
Verse_Ch: 108:1 神阿，我心坚定；我要以我的荣耀唱诗歌颂。 ###EN### My heart is fixed, O God; I will sing, indeed I will sing psalms, Even with my glory.
Verse_Ch: 108:2 琴瑟阿，你们当醒起！我要极早醒起。 ###EN### Awake, O harp and lyre! I will awaken the dawn.
Verse_Ch: 108:3 耶和华阿，我要在众民中称谢你；我要在列邦中歌颂你。 ###EN### I will give thanks to You among the peoples, O Jehovah; And I will sing psalms to You among the nations.
Verse_Ch: 108:4 因为你的慈爱大过诸天，你的信实达到穹苍。 ###EN### For Your lovingkindness is higher than the heavens, And Your faithfulness reaches to the sky.
Verse_Ch: 108:5 神阿，愿你被高举，过于诸天；愿你的荣耀遍及全地。 ###EN### Be exalted above the heavens, O God; And let Your glory be above all the earth.
Verse_Ch: 108:6 求你用右手拯救我们，应允我们，好叫你所亲爱的人得救。 ###EN### That Your beloved ones may be delivered, Save with Your right hand, and answer us.
Verse_Ch: 108:7 神已经在祂的圣别中说，我要欢乐；我要分开示剑，丈量疏割谷。 ###EN### God has spoken in His holiness: I will exult; I will divide Shechem And measure out the Valley of Succoth.
Verse_Ch: 108:8 基列是我的；玛拿西是我的；以法莲是我的头盔；犹大是我的杖； ###EN### Gilead is Mine; Manasseh is Mine; And Ephraim is the helmet for My head; Judah is My scepter.
Verse_Ch: 108:9 摩押是我的沐浴盆；我要向以东抛鞋；我必向非利士夸胜欢呼。 ###EN### Moab is My washbowl; Upon Edom I will cast My sandal; Over Philistia I will shout.
Verse_Ch: 108:10 谁能领我进坚固城？谁能引我到以东地？ ###EN### Who will bring me into the fortified city? Who will lead me to Edom?
Verse_Ch: 108:11 神阿，你不是丢弃了我们么？神阿，你不和我们的军兵一同出战么？ ###EN### Will not You, O God, who rejected us And who did not go forth, O God, with our armies?
Verse_Ch: 108:12 求你帮助我们脱离敌人，因为人的拯救是枉然的。 ###EN### Give us help from the adversary, For salvation by man is vain.
Verse_Ch: 108:13 我们因神才得奋勇行事，践踏我们敌人的就是祂。 ###EN### In God we will do valiantly, And it is He who will tread down our adversaries.
Chapter_Header: 109
Verse_Ch: 109:1 我所赞美的神阿，求你不要闭口不言； ###EN### O God of my praise, do not be silent;
Verse_Ch: 109:2 因为恶人的嘴和诡诈人的口，已经张开攻击我；他们用撒谎的舌头对我说话。 ###EN### For the mouth of the wicked man and the mouth of deceit are opened against me; They speak to me with a lying tongue.
Verse_Ch: 109:3 他们围绕我，说怨恨的话，又无故的攻打我。 ###EN### And with words of hatred they have surrounded me And have fought against me without cause.
Verse_Ch: 109:4 他们与我为敌以报我爱，但我专心祷告。 ###EN### In return for my love they have become my adversaries, But I am all prayer.
Verse_Ch: 109:5 他们向我以恶报善，以恨报爱。 ###EN### And they have set against me evil in return for good And hatred in return for my love.
Verse_Ch: 109:6 愿你派一个恶人辖制他，派一个对头站在他右边。 ###EN### Appoint a wicked man over him, And let an adversary stand at his right hand.
Verse_Ch: 109:7 他受审判的时候，愿他被定为恶；愿他的祷告，反成为罪。 ###EN### When he is judged, let him come forth wicked; And let his prayer be counted as sin.
Verse_Ch: 109:8 愿他的年日短少；愿别人得他的职分。 ###EN### May his days be few; May another take his office.
Verse_Ch: 109:9 愿他的儿女为孤儿，他的妻子为寡妇。 ###EN### May his children be orphans, And his wife a widow.
Verse_Ch: 109:10 愿他的儿女飘流讨饭，从他们荒凉之处出来求食。 ###EN### And may his children wander all about and beg, And may they seek food far from their desolated ruins.
Verse_Ch: 109:11 愿债主设下网罗夺取他一切所有的，愿外人抢走他劳碌得来的。 ###EN### May the creditor seize all that he has, And may strangers plunder the fruit of his labor.
Verse_Ch: 109:12 愿无人向他延施怜悯；愿无人恩待他的孤儿。 ###EN### May there be no one to extend him mercy, Nor anyone to be kind to his orphans.
Verse_Ch: 109:13 愿他的后人断绝；愿他的名字在下代就被涂抹。 ###EN### May his posterity be cut off; In the generation following may his name be blotted out.
Verse_Ch: 109:14 愿他祖宗的罪孽被耶和华记念，愿他母亲的罪过不被涂抹。 ###EN### May his father's iniquity be remembered before Jehovah, And may his mother's sin not be blotted out.
Verse_Ch: 109:15 愿这些罪常在耶和华面前，以致祂将他们的名号从地上剪除； ###EN### May they be before Jehovah continually, So that He may cut off the memory of them from the earth;
Verse_Ch: 109:16 因为他未曾想过要施慈爱，却逼迫困苦、穷乏、和伤心的人，要把他们治死。 ###EN### Because he did not remember to show lovingkindness, But persecuted the poor and needy and brokenhearted, To put them to death.
Verse_Ch: 109:17 他爱咒骂，咒骂就临到他；他不喜爱祝福，祝福就远离他。 ###EN### Indeed he loved cursing, so it came on him; And he took no delight in blessing, so it was far from him.
Verse_Ch: 109:18 他拿咒骂当衣服穿上，这咒骂就如水进入他里面，像油进入他的骨头。 ###EN### And he clothed himself with cursing like his garment, So it came into his inward parts like water And into his bones like oil.
Verse_Ch: 109:19 愿这咒骂当他遮身的衣服，当他常束的腰带。 ###EN### Let it be to him like the cloak that he wraps around himself, And as a belt with which he constantly girds himself.
Verse_Ch: 109:20 这就是我的对头，和说恶言攻击我的人，从耶和华那里所受的报应。 ###EN### This is the reward from Jehovah for my adversaries And for those who speak evil against my soul.
Verse_Ch: 109:21 主耶和华阿，求你为你名的缘故恩待我；因你的慈爱美好，求你搭救我； ###EN### But You, O Jehovah Lord, deal with me, For Your name's sake; Because Your lovingkindness is good, deliver me.
Verse_Ch: 109:22 因为我困苦穷乏，内心受伤。 ###EN### For I am poor and needy, And my heart is wounded within me.
Verse_Ch: 109:23 我如日影渐渐偏斜而去；我如蝗虫被抖掉。 ###EN### I am gone like a shadow that declines; I am shaken off like the locust.
Verse_Ch: 109:24 我因禁食，膝骨软弱，我身上的肉也消瘦无油。 ###EN### My knees wobble through fasting, And my flesh has become lean, without fatness.
Verse_Ch: 109:25 我也成了他们所羞辱的：他们看见我，便摇头。 ###EN### I have also become a reproach to them: When they see me, they shake their heads.
Verse_Ch: 109:26 耶和华我的神阿，求你帮助我；求你照你的慈爱拯救我； ###EN### Help me, O Jehovah my God; Save me according to Your lovingkindness;
Verse_Ch: 109:27 他们就知道这是你的手，是你耶和华行了这事。 ###EN### And they will know that this is Your hand, That it is You, O Jehovah, who have done it.
Verse_Ch: 109:28 任凭他们咒骂，惟愿你赐福；他们几时起来，就必蒙羞，你的仆人却要欢喜。 ###EN### Let them curse, but You bless; When they arise, they will be put to shame, And Your servant will rejoice.
Verse_Ch: 109:29 愿我的对头披戴羞辱，愿他们以自己的羞愧为外袍遮身。 ###EN### May my adversaries be clothed with humiliation, And may they wrap themselves with their own shame as with a mantle.
Verse_Ch: 109:30 我要用口极力称谢耶和华，我要在众人中间赞美祂； ###EN### I will give much thanks to Jehovah with my mouth, And in the midst of the multitude I will praise Him;
Verse_Ch: 109:31 因为祂站在穷乏人的右边，要救他脱离那些审判他魂的人。 ###EN### For He stands at the right hand of the needy To save him from those who judge his soul.
Chapter_Header: 110
Verse_Ch: 110:1 耶和华对我主说，你坐在我的右边，等我使你的仇敌作你的脚凳。 ###EN### Jehovah declares to my Lord, Sit at My right hand Until I make Your enemies Your footstool.
Verse_Ch: 110:2 耶和华必从锡安伸出你能力的杖来：你要在你的仇敌中间掌权。 ###EN### Jehovah will send forth The scepter of Your strength from Zion: Rule in the midst of Your enemies.
Verse_Ch: 110:3 当你争战的日子，你的民要以奉献为彩饰，甘心献上自己。你的少年人对你必如清晨的甘露。 ###EN### Your people will offer themselves willingly In the day of Your warfare, In the splendor of their consecration. Your young men will be to You Like the dew from the womb of the dawn.
Verse_Ch: 110:4 耶和华起了誓，必不后悔；祂说，你是照着麦基洗德的等次，永远为祭司。 ###EN### Jehovah has sworn, And He will not change: You are a Priest forever According to the order of Melchizedek.
Verse_Ch: 110:5 主在你右边；祂发怒的日子，必打伤列王。 ###EN### The Lord is at Your right hand; He will shatter kings in the day of His anger.
Verse_Ch: 110:6 祂要在列邦中施行审判，使那处满了尸首；祂要在大地上打伤仇敌的头。 ###EN### He will execute judgment among the nations; He will fill the place with corpses; He will shatter the head Over a great land.
Verse_Ch: 110:7 祂要喝路旁的河水；因此祂必抬起头来。 ###EN### He will drink from the brook by the way; Therefore He will lift up His head.
Chapter_Header: 111
Verse_Ch: 111:1 阿利路亚！我要在正直人的聚集中，并在大会中，全心称谢耶和华。 ###EN### Hallelujah! I will give thanks to Jehovah with all my heart In the council of the upright and in the assembly.
Verse_Ch: 111:2 耶和华的作为本为大，凡喜爱祂作为的都必究察。 ###EN### Great are the works of Jehovah, And sought out by all who delight in them.
Verse_Ch: 111:3 祂所行的是尊荣和威严，祂的公义存到永远。 ###EN### His work is majesty and splendor, And His righteousness endures forever.
Verse_Ch: 111:4 祂行了奇事，使人记念；耶和华有恩典，有怜恤。 ###EN### He has caused His wondrous deeds to be remembered; Jehovah is gracious and compassionate.
Verse_Ch: 111:5 祂赐粮食给敬畏祂的人；祂永远记念祂的约。 ###EN### He gives food to those who fear Him; He remembers His covenant forever.
Verse_Ch: 111:6 祂向百姓显出祂作为的大能，把列国赐给他们为业。 ###EN### He has shown His people the power of His works By giving them the heritage of the nations.
Verse_Ch: 111:7 祂手所作的，是真实公平；祂的训辞都是确实的： ###EN### The works of His hands are truth and justice; All His precepts are sure:
Verse_Ch: 111:8 是永永远远坚定的，是按真实正直施行的。 ###EN### They are maintained forever and ever, They are executed in truth and uprightness.
Verse_Ch: 111:9 祂向百姓施行救赎；祂命定祂的约，直到永远；祂的名圣别可畏。 ###EN### He has sent redemption to His people; He has commanded His covenant forever; Holy and awesome is His name.
Verse_Ch: 111:10 敬畏耶和华是智慧的开端；凡实行祂训辞的，便为明智；赞美祂的话存到永远。 ###EN### The fear of Jehovah is the beginning of wisdom; All who practice His precepts have a good understanding. His praise endures forever.
Chapter_Header: 112
Verse_Ch: 112:1 阿利路亚！敬畏耶和华，甚喜爱祂命令的，这人便为有福。 ###EN### Hallelujah! Blessed is the man who fears Jehovah, Who delights greatly in His commandments.
Verse_Ch: 112:2 他的后裔在地上必强盛；正直人的后代必蒙福。 ###EN### His seed will be mighty on the earth; The generation of the upright will be blessed.
Verse_Ch: 112:3 他家中有赀财和财富，他的义存到永远。 ###EN### Wealth and riches are in his house, And his righteousness endures forever.
Verse_Ch: 112:4 正直人在黑暗中，有光向他出现；他有恩惠，有怜恤，有公义。 ###EN### Light in the darkness arises to the upright; They are gracious and compassionate and righteous.
Verse_Ch: 112:5 施恩与人，借贷与人的，这人必得亨通；他被审判的时候，要诉明自己的冤。 ###EN### It is well with the man who is gracious and lends; He will maintain his cause in judgment.
Verse_Ch: 112:6 因为他永不动摇；义人必被记念，直到永远。 ###EN### For he will never be moved; The righteous man will be remembered forever.
Verse_Ch: 112:7 他必不怕凶恶的信息；他心坚定，信靠耶和华。 ###EN### He will not be afraid of evil tidings; His heart is steadfast, trusting in Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 112:8 他的心得了扶持，总不惧怕，直到他看见敌人遭报。 ###EN### His heart is sustained, he is not afraid, Until he sees what should happen to his adversaries.
Verse_Ch: 112:9 他分施赒济贫穷；他的义存到永远。他的角必被高举，而有尊荣。 ###EN### He has scattered abroad; he has given to the needy; His righteousness endures forever; His horn will be exalted with honor.
Verse_Ch: 112:10 恶人看见便恼恨，必咬牙而融化；恶人的心愿要归灭绝。 ###EN### The wicked man will see it and be angry; He will gnash his teeth and melt away; The desire of the wicked will perish.
Chapter_Header: 113
Verse_Ch: 113:1 阿利路亚！耶和华的仆人哪，你们要赞美，赞美耶和华的名。 ###EN### Hallelujah! Praise, you servants of Jehovah, Praise the name of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 113:2 耶和华的名，是当受颂赞的，从今时直到永远。 ###EN### Let the name of Jehovah be blessed, From now and to eternity.
Verse_Ch: 113:3 从日出之地到日落之处，耶和华的名是应当赞美的。 ###EN### From the rising of the sun to its setting The name of Jehovah is to be praised.
Verse_Ch: 113:4 耶和华超乎万国之上，祂的荣耀高过诸天。 ###EN### Jehovah is high above all the nations, And His glory is above the heavens.
Verse_Ch: 113:5 谁像耶和华我们的神呢？祂坐在至高之处， ###EN### Who is like Jehovah our God, Who has set His throne on high,
Verse_Ch: 113:6 降卑自己，观看天上地上的事。 ###EN### Who humbles Himself to behold The heavens and the earth?
Verse_Ch: 113:7 祂从灰尘里抬举贫寒人，从粪堆中提拔穷乏人； ###EN### He raises the poor from the dust; From the ash heap He lifts the needy;
Verse_Ch: 113:8 使他们与尊贵人同坐，就是与祂百姓中的尊贵人同坐。 ###EN### That He may seat them with princes, With the princes of His people.
Verse_Ch: 113:9 祂使不能生育的妇人安居家中，作多子的快乐母亲。阿利路亚！ ###EN### He causes the barren woman to keep house As a joyful mother of children. Hallelujah.
Chapter_Header: 114
Verse_Ch: 114:1 以色列出了埃及，雅各家离开说异语之民； ###EN### When Israel went forth from Egypt, The house of Jacob from among a people of unintelligible speech,
Verse_Ch: 114:2 那时犹大成为祂的圣所，以色列成为祂所治理的国。 ###EN### Judah became His sanctuary, Israel, His dominion.
Verse_Ch: 114:3 沧海看见就奔逃，约但河也倒流。 ###EN### The sea saw and fled; The Jordan turned back.
Verse_Ch: 114:4 大山踊跃如公羊，小山踊跃如羊羔。 ###EN### The mountains skipped like rams, The hills, like lambs.
Verse_Ch: 114:5 沧海阿，你为何奔逃？约但河阿，你为何倒流？ ###EN### What troubles you, O sea, that you flee? O Jordan, that you turn back?
Verse_Ch: 114:6 大山哪，你为何踊跃如公羊？小山哪，你为何踊跃如羊羔？ ###EN### O mountains, that you skip like rams? O hills, like lambs?
Verse_Ch: 114:7 大地阿，你见了主的面，就是雅各神的面，便震动； ###EN### Tremble at the presence of the Lord, O earth, At the presence of the God of Jacob,
Verse_Ch: 114:8 祂叫磐石变为水池，叫坚石变为水泉。 ###EN### Who turns the rock into a pool of water, The flint into a fountain of water.
Chapter_Header: 115
Verse_Ch: 115:1 耶和华阿，荣耀不要归与我们，不要归与我们，要因你的慈爱和真实，归与你的名。 ###EN### Not to us, O Jehovah, not to us, But to Your name give glory, For the sake of Your lovingkindness and Your truth.
Verse_Ch: 115:2 为何容外邦人说，他们的神在那里呢？ ###EN### Why should the nations say, Where then is their God?
Verse_Ch: 115:3 然而我们的神在天上；祂随自己的喜悦行事。 ###EN### But our God is in the heavens; He does whatever He pleases.
Verse_Ch: 115:4 他们的偶像不过是金的银的，是人手所造的； ###EN### Their idols are mere silver and gold, The work of human hands.
Verse_Ch: 115:5 有口却不能言，有眼却不能看， ###EN### They have mouths, but they do not speak; They have eyes, but they do not see.
Verse_Ch: 115:6 有耳却不能听，有鼻却不能闻， ###EN### They have ears, but they do not hear; They have noses, but they do not smell.
Verse_Ch: 115:7 有手却不能摸，有脚却不能走，喉咙也不能出声。 ###EN### They have hands, but they do not feel; They have feet, but they do not walk; They make no sound in their throat.
Verse_Ch: 115:8 造它们的，并一切倚靠它们的，都要和它们一样。 ###EN### Those who make them, All who trust in them, Are like them.
Verse_Ch: 115:9 以色列阿，当信靠耶和华；祂是他们的帮助，和他们的盾牌。 ###EN### O Israel, trust in Jehovah. He is their help and their shield.
Verse_Ch: 115:10 亚伦家阿，当信靠耶和华；祂是他们的帮助，和他们的盾牌。 ###EN### O house of Aaron, trust in Jehovah. He is their help and their shield.
Verse_Ch: 115:11 你们敬畏耶和华的，当信靠耶和华；祂是他们的帮助，和他们的盾牌。 ###EN### O you who fear Jehovah, trust in Jehovah. He is their help and their shield.
Verse_Ch: 115:12 耶和华向来记念我们；祂还要赐福给我们，要赐福给以色列家，赐福给亚伦家； ###EN### Jehovah has been mindful of us; He will bless us; He will bless the house of Israel; He will bless the house of Aaron;
Verse_Ch: 115:13 凡敬畏耶和华的，无论大小，祂必赐福给他们。 ###EN### He will bless those who fear Jehovah, Both small and great.
Verse_Ch: 115:14 愿耶和华叫你们和你们的子孙，日见加增。 ###EN### May Jehovah give you increase, Both you and your children.
Verse_Ch: 115:15 愿你们蒙造天地之耶和华的福。 ###EN### May you be blessed of Jehovah, Maker of heaven and earth.
Verse_Ch: 115:16 天是耶和华的天；地，祂却给了世人。 ###EN### The heavens are the heavens of Jehovah, But He has given the earth to the children of men.
Verse_Ch: 115:17 死人不能赞美耶和华；下到寂静中的，也都不能。 ###EN### The dead do not praise Jehovah, Nor do any that go down into silence.
Verse_Ch: 115:18 但我们要颂赞耶和华，从今时直到永远。阿利路亚。 ###EN### But we will bless Jehovah From now and to eternity. Hallelujah.
Chapter_Header: 116
Verse_Ch: 116:1 我爱耶和华，因为祂听了我的声音，我的恳求； ###EN### I love Jehovah because He hears My voice, my supplications,
Verse_Ch: 116:2 祂既向我侧耳，我一生要呼求祂。 ###EN### Because He inclines His ear to me; Therefore I will call upon Him all my days.
Verse_Ch: 116:3 死亡的绳索围绕我，阴间的痛苦临到我；我遭遇患难愁苦。 ###EN### The bonds of death encompassed me, And the distresses of Sheol fell upon me; I fell upon trouble and sorrow.
Verse_Ch: 116:4 然而我呼求耶和华的名。耶和华阿，求你救我的性命。 ###EN### But I called upon the name of Jehovah. O Jehovah, I pray, deliver my soul.
Verse_Ch: 116:5 耶和华有恩典，有公义；我们的神有怜恤。 ###EN### Jehovah is gracious and righteous, Indeed our God is compassionate.
Verse_Ch: 116:6 耶和华保护愚蒙人：我落到卑微的地步，祂救了我。 ###EN### Jehovah preserves the simple: I was brought low, and He saved me.
Verse_Ch: 116:7 我的魂哪，你要仍归安息，因为耶和华厚待了你。 ###EN### Return to your rest, O my soul; For Jehovah has dealt bountifully with you.
Verse_Ch: 116:8 主阿，你救我的性命免了死亡，救我的眼免了流泪，救我的脚免了跌倒。 ###EN### For You have delivered my soul from death, My eyes from tears, My feet from stumbling.
Verse_Ch: 116:9 我要在耶和华面前，行在活人之地。 ###EN### I will walk before Jehovah In the land of the living.
Verse_Ch: 116:10 我信，所以我说话；我受了极大的困苦。 ###EN### I believed, therefore I spoke; I was afflicted greatly.
Verse_Ch: 116:11 我曾急促的说，人都是说谎的。 ###EN### I said in my haste, All men are liars.
Verse_Ch: 116:12 我拿什么回报耶和华对我的一切厚待？ ###EN### What shall I return to Jehovah For all His benefits toward me?
Verse_Ch: 116:13 我要举起救恩的杯，呼求耶和华的名。 ###EN### I will take up the cup of salvation And call upon the name of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 116:14 哦，我要在祂众民面前，向耶和华还我的愿。 ###EN### I will pay my vows to Jehovah, Oh, in the presence of all His people.
Verse_Ch: 116:15 在耶和华眼中看虔诚人的死，极为宝贵。 ###EN### Precious in the sight of Jehovah Is the death of His faithful ones.
Verse_Ch: 116:16 耶和华阿，我真是你的仆人；我是你的仆人，是你婢女的儿子；你已经解开我的绑索。 ###EN### Oh, Jehovah! Surely I am Your servant; I am Your servant, the son of Your female servant; You have loosed my bonds.
Verse_Ch: 116:17 我要将感谢祭献给你，又要呼求耶和华的名。 ###EN### To You I will offer a sacrifice of thanksgiving, And I will call upon the name of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 116:18 哦，我要在祂众民面前，向耶和华还我的愿； ###EN### I will pay my vows to Jehovah, Oh, in the presence of all His people,
Verse_Ch: 116:19 我要在耶和华殿的院内，耶路撒冷阿，就是在你中间，还我的愿。阿利路亚。 ###EN### In the courts of the house of Jehovah, In the midst of you, O Jerusalem. Hallelujah.
Chapter_Header: 117
Verse_Ch: 117:1 万国阿，你们都当赞美耶和华；万民哪，你们都当称颂祂。 ###EN### Praise Jehovah, all you nations; Laud Him, all you peoples.
Verse_Ch: 117:2 因为祂向我们大施慈爱；耶和华的信实，存到永远。阿利路亚。 ###EN### For His lovingkindness is great toward us, And the faithfulness of Jehovah is forever. Hallelujah.
Chapter_Header: 118
Verse_Ch: 118:1 你们要称谢耶和华，因祂本为善，祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### Give thanks to Jehovah, for He is good, For His lovingkindness is forever.
Verse_Ch: 118:2 愿以色列说，祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### Let Israel say, His lovingkindness is forever.
Verse_Ch: 118:3 愿亚伦家说，祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### Let the house of Aaron say, His lovingkindness is forever.
Verse_Ch: 118:4 愿敬畏耶和华的说，祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### Let those who fear Jehovah say, His lovingkindness is forever.
Verse_Ch: 118:5 我在急难中呼求耶和华，耶和华就应允我，把我安置在宽阔之处。 ###EN### Out of my distress I called upon Jehovah; Jehovah answered me and set me in a place broad and free.
Verse_Ch: 118:6 有耶和华帮助我，我必不惧怕；人能把我怎么样呢？ ###EN### Jehovah is for me; I will not be afraid. What can man do to me?
Verse_Ch: 118:7 有耶和华帮助我，作我的帮助者，我必看见那恨我的人遭报。 ###EN### Jehovah is for me as my Helper, And I will see what should happen to those who hate me.
Verse_Ch: 118:8 投靠耶和华，胜过倚靠人。 ###EN### It is better to take refuge in Jehovah Than to trust in man.
Verse_Ch: 118:9 投靠耶和华，胜过倚靠尊贵人。 ###EN### It is better to take refuge in Jehovah Than to trust in princes.
Verse_Ch: 118:10 万民围绕我；我在耶和华的名里，必剿灭他们！ ###EN### All nations surrounded me; In the name of Jehovah I indeed cut them down!
Verse_Ch: 118:11 他们围绕我，确实围绕我；我在耶和华的名里，必剿灭他们！ ###EN### They surrounded me; yes, they surrounded me; In the name of Jehovah I indeed cut them down!
Verse_Ch: 118:12 他们如同蜜蜂围绕我，必像烧荆棘的火被扑灭；我在耶和华的名里，必剿灭他们！ ###EN### They surrounded me like bees; They were extinguished like a fire of thorns; In the name of Jehovah I indeed cut them down!
Verse_Ch: 118:13 人推撞我，要叫我跌倒，但耶和华帮助了我。 ###EN### I was pushed hard that I might fall; But Jehovah helped me.
Verse_Ch: 118:14 耶和华是我的力量，是我的诗歌，祂也成了我的拯救。 ###EN### Jehovah is my strength and my song, And He has become my salvation.
Verse_Ch: 118:15 在义人的帐棚里，有欢呼得拯救的声音。耶和华的右手施展大能； ###EN### The voice of rejoicing and salvation Is in the tents of the righteous. The right hand of Jehovah does valiantly;
Verse_Ch: 118:16 耶和华的右手高举；耶和华的右手施展大能。 ###EN### The right hand of Jehovah is exalted; The right hand of Jehovah does valiantly.
Verse_Ch: 118:17 我必不至于死，仍要存活，并要述说耶和华的作为。 ###EN### I will not die, but live, And declare the works of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 118:18 耶和华虽严严的惩治我，却没有将我交于死亡。 ###EN### Jehovah has severely chastened me, But He has not given me over to death.
Verse_Ch: 118:19 你们要给我敞开义门：我要进去，称谢耶和华。 ###EN### Open to me the gates of righteousness: I will enter in through them; I will give thanks to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 118:20 这是耶和华的门；义人要从这门进去。 ###EN### This is the gate of Jehovah; The righteous shall enter in through it.
Verse_Ch: 118:21 我要称谢你，因为你已经应允我，并且成了我的拯救。 ###EN### I will give thanks to You, for You have answered me And have become my salvation.
Verse_Ch: 118:22 匠人所弃的石头，已成了房角的头块石头。 ###EN### The stone which the builders rejected Has become the head of the corner.
Verse_Ch: 118:23 这是耶和华所作的，在我们眼中看为希奇。 ###EN### This is from Jehovah; It is wonderful in our sight.
Verse_Ch: 118:24 这是耶和华所定的日子；我们在其中要欢腾喜乐。 ###EN### This is the day that Jehovah has made; Let us exult and rejoice in it.
Verse_Ch: 118:25 耶和华阿，求你拯救！耶和华阿，求你使我们亨通！ ###EN### O Jehovah, do save, we pray! O Jehovah, do send prosperity, we pray!
Verse_Ch: 118:26 在耶和华名里来的，是当受颂赞的；我们从耶和华的殿中，为你们祝福。 ###EN### Blessed is He who comes in the name of Jehovah; We bless you from the house of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 118:27 耶和华是神，祂光照了我们；当用绳索把节期的祭牲拴住，牵到坛角那里。 ###EN### Jehovah is God, And He has given us light; Bind the sacrifice of the feast with cords To the horns of the altar.
Verse_Ch: 118:28 你是我的神，我要称谢你；你是我的神，我要尊崇你。 ###EN### You are my God, and I give thanks to You. You are my God; I will exalt You.
Verse_Ch: 118:29 你们要称谢耶和华，因祂本为善；祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### Give thanks to Jehovah, for He is good, For His lovingkindness is forever.
Chapter_Header: 119
Verse_Ch: 119:1 行径完全，遵行耶和华律法的，这样的人是有福的。 ###EN### Blessed are those whose way is perfect, Who walk in the law of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 119:2 遵守祂的法度，全心寻求祂的，这样的人是有福的。 ###EN### Blessed are those who keep His testimonies, Who seek Him with all their heart.
Verse_Ch: 119:3 他们不作不义的事，惟遵行祂的道路。 ###EN### Surely they do no wrong; They walk in His ways.
Verse_Ch: 119:4 耶和华阿，你曾将你的训辞吩咐我们，要我们殷勤遵守。 ###EN### You have commanded that Your precepts Be diligently kept.
Verse_Ch: 119:5 但愿我的行径坚定，得以遵守你的律例！ ###EN### Oh that my ways may be established So as to keep Your statutes!
Verse_Ch: 119:6 我看重你的一切诫命，就不至于羞愧。 ###EN### Then I will not be put to shame, When I regard all Your commandments.
Verse_Ch: 119:7 我学了你公义的典章，就以正直的心称谢你。 ###EN### I will give thanks to You with uprightness of heart When I learn Your righteous ordinances.
Verse_Ch: 119:8 我必守你的律例；求你总不要丢弃我。 ###EN### I will keep Your statutes; Do not utterly forsake me.
Verse_Ch: 119:9 少年人用什么使他的行径纯洁呢？是要遵行你的话。 ###EN### With what should a young man keep his way pure? By guarding it according to Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:10 我全心寻求了你，求你不要叫我偏离你的诫命。 ###EN### With all my heart I have sought You; Do not let me wander from Your commandments.
Verse_Ch: 119:11 我将你的话珍藏在心里，免得我得罪你。 ###EN### In my heart I have treasured up Your word That I might not sin against You.
Verse_Ch: 119:12 耶和华阿，你是当受颂赞的；求你将你的律例教训我。 ###EN### Blessed are You, O Jehovah; Teach me Your statutes.
Verse_Ch: 119:13 我用嘴唇述说你口中的一切典章。 ###EN### With my lips I have declared All the ordinances of Your mouth.
Verse_Ch: 119:14 我喜悦你法度的道路，如同喜悦一切的财物。 ###EN### I have rejoiced in the way of Your testimonies As much as in all riches.
Verse_Ch: 119:15 我要默想你的训辞，看重你的道路。 ###EN### I will muse upon Your precepts And regard Your ways.
Verse_Ch: 119:16 我要在你的律例中自乐；我不忘记你的话。 ###EN### I will take delight in Your statutes; I will not forget Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:17 求你厚待你的仆人，使我存活，并且遵守你的话。 ###EN### Deal bountifully with Your servant that I may live And keep Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:18 求你开我的眼睛，使我看出你律法中的奇妙。 ###EN### Open my eyes that I may behold Wondrous things out of Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:19 我是在地上寄居的；求你不要向我隐瞒你的诫命。 ###EN### I am a sojourner in the earth; Do not hide Your commandments from me.
Verse_Ch: 119:20 我时刻羡慕你的典章，甚至心碎。 ###EN### My soul is crushed with longing For Your ordinances at all times.
Verse_Ch: 119:21 偏离你诫命，受咒诅的骄傲人，你已经责备他们。 ###EN### You have rebuked the proud, the cursed, Who wander from Your commandments.
Verse_Ch: 119:22 求你除掉我所受的羞辱和藐视，因我遵守你的法度。 ###EN### Roll away from me reproach and contempt, For I have kept Your testimonies.
Verse_Ch: 119:23 虽有首领坐着妄论我，你仆人却默想你的律例。 ###EN### Princes as well have sat and spoken against me, But Your servant mused upon Your statutes.
Verse_Ch: 119:24 你的法度是我所喜乐的，是我的谋士。 ###EN### Also Your testimonies are my delight; They are my counselors.
Verse_Ch: 119:25 我的性命几乎归于尘土；求你照你的话将我救活。 ###EN### My soul clings to the dust; Enliven me according to Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:26 我述说我的行径，你应允了我；求你将你的律例教训我。 ###EN### I have recounted my ways, and You have answered me; Teach me Your statutes.
Verse_Ch: 119:27 求你使我明白你训辞的道路，我就默想你的奇事。 ###EN### Cause me to understand the way of Your precepts, And I will muse upon Your wondrous deeds.
Verse_Ch: 119:28 我的心因愁苦而融化；求你照你的话使我坚立。 ###EN### My soul melts because of grief; Strengthen me according to Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:29 求你使我离开虚谎的道路，开恩将你的律法赐给我。 ###EN### Remove from me the way of falsehood, And graciously grant me Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:30 我拣选了忠信的道路，将你的典章摆在我面前。 ###EN### I have chosen the way of faithfulness; Your ordinances I have set before me.
Verse_Ch: 119:31 我紧紧跟随你的法度；耶和华阿，求你不要叫我羞愧。 ###EN### I cling to Your testimonies; O Jehovah, do not put me to shame.
Verse_Ch: 119:32 你既开广我的心，我就奔跑你诫命的道路。 ###EN### I run the way of Your commandments, For You enlarge my heart.
Verse_Ch: 119:33 耶和华阿，求你将你律例的道路指教我，我必遵守到底。 ###EN### Teach me, O Jehovah, the way of Your statutes; And I will keep it to the end.
Verse_Ch: 119:34 求你赐我悟性，我便遵守你的律法；且要全心谨守。 ###EN### Give me understanding, and I will observe Your law; Indeed I will keep it with all my heart.
Verse_Ch: 119:35 求你使我行在你诫命的道路上，因为我喜悦这道路。 ###EN### Cause me to go on the path of Your commandments, For in it I delight.
Verse_Ch: 119:36 求你使我的心趋向你的法度，不趋向不义之财。 ###EN### Incline my heart to Your testimonies And not to unjust gain.
Verse_Ch: 119:37 求你叫我转眼不看虚假，叫我在你的道路中活着。 ###EN### Turn my eyes from beholding vanity, And enliven me in Your ways.
Verse_Ch: 119:38 求你坚定你对仆人的话，这话是叫人敬畏你。 ###EN### Confirm to Your servant Your word, Which is for fearing You.
Verse_Ch: 119:39 求你使我所怕的羞辱远离我；因你的典章本为美。 ###EN### Turn away my reproach, which I fear; For Your ordinances are good.
Verse_Ch: 119:40 看哪，我羡慕你的训辞；求你使我在你的公义中活着。 ###EN### Behold, I have longed after Your precepts; Enliven me in Your righteousness.
Verse_Ch: 119:41 耶和华阿，愿你照你的话，使你的慈爱，就是你的救恩，临到我身上。 ###EN### May Your lovingkindness also come to me, O Jehovah, Your salvation according to Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:42 我就有话回答那羞辱我的，因我信靠你的话。 ###EN### Thus I will have an answer for him who reproaches me, For I trust in Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:43 求你叫真理的话，总不离开我口，因我仰望了你的典章。 ###EN### And do not take the word of truth utterly from my mouth, For I have hoped in Your ordinances.
Verse_Ch: 119:44 我要常守你的律法，直到永永远远。 ###EN### Thus I will keep Your law continually, Forever and ever.
Verse_Ch: 119:45 我要行在宽阔之地，因我寻求了你的训辞。 ###EN### And I will walk at liberty, For I have sought Your precepts.
Verse_Ch: 119:46 我也要在君王面前，论说你的法度，并不以为耻。 ###EN### I will also speak of Your testimonies before kings And not be ashamed.
Verse_Ch: 119:47 我要在你的诫命中自乐，这些诫命是我所爱的。 ###EN### And I will take delight in Your commandments, Which I love.
Verse_Ch: 119:48 我要向你的诫命举手，这些诫命是我所爱的；我也要默想你的律例。 ###EN### And I will lift up my hand to Your commandments, which I love; And I will muse upon Your statutes.
Verse_Ch: 119:49 求你记念向你仆人所说的话，你曾使我在这话中有盼望。 ###EN### Remember the word to Your servant In which You have made me hope.
Verse_Ch: 119:50 这是我在患难中的安慰，因为你的话将我救活。 ###EN### This is my comfort in my affliction, For Your word has enlivened me.
Verse_Ch: 119:51 骄傲的人极力讥诮我；我却没有偏离你的律法。 ###EN### The proud have derided me greatly; I have not swerved from Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:52 耶和华阿，我记念你从古以来的典章，就得了安慰。 ###EN### I have remembered Your ordinances from long ago, O Jehovah, and have comforted myself.
Verse_Ch: 119:53 我因恶人离弃你的律法，就怒气发作，犹如火烧。 ###EN### Raging indignation seizes me because of the wicked, Who forsake Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:54 在我寄居的住所，你的律例成了我的诗歌。 ###EN### Your statutes have become my songs of praise In the house of my pilgrimage.
Verse_Ch: 119:55 耶和华阿，我夜间记念你的名，遵守你的律法。 ###EN### I have remembered Your name In the night, O Jehovah, And have kept Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:56 我所以如此，是因我守了你的训辞。 ###EN### This has been mine, That I have kept Your precepts.
Verse_Ch: 119:57 耶和华是我的业分；我曾说，我要遵守你的言语。 ###EN### Jehovah is my portion; I have promised to keep Your words.
Verse_Ch: 119:58 我全心求过你的恩；愿你照你的话恩待我。 ###EN### I entreated Your favor with my whole heart; Be gracious to me according to Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:59 我筹算自己的道路，就转步归向你的法度。 ###EN### I considered my ways And turned my feet toward Your testimonies.
Verse_Ch: 119:60 我急忙遵守你的诫命，并不迟延。 ###EN### I hurried and did not delay To keep Your commandments.
Verse_Ch: 119:61 恶人的绳索缠绕我，我却没有忘记你的律法。 ###EN### The cords of the wicked surround me, But I have not forgotten Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:62 我因你公义的典章，半夜起来称谢你。 ###EN### At midnight I rise up to give thanks to You Because of Your righteous ordinances.
Verse_Ch: 119:63 凡敬畏你，守你训辞的人，我都与他作伴。 ###EN### I am a companion to all who fear You And to those who keep Your precepts.
Verse_Ch: 119:64 耶和华阿，你的慈爱遍满大地；求你将你的律例教训我。 ###EN### Your lovingkindness, O Jehovah, fills the earth; Teach me Your statutes.
Verse_Ch: 119:65 耶和华阿，你向来是照你的话善待仆人。 ###EN### You have dealt well with Your servant, O Jehovah, according to Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:66 求你将明辨和知识教训我，因我相信你的诫命。 ###EN### Teach me proper discernment and knowledge, For I believe in Your commandments.
Verse_Ch: 119:67 我受苦以先，走迷了路；现在却遵守你的话。 ###EN### Before I was afflicted, I went astray; But now I keep Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:68 你本为善，所行的也善；求你将你的律例教训我。 ###EN### You are good and One who does good; Teach me Your statutes.
Verse_Ch: 119:69 骄傲人编造谎言攻击我；我却要全心守你的训辞。 ###EN### The proud have plastered lies against me; With my whole heart I will keep Your precepts.
Verse_Ch: 119:70 他们的心迟钝，如蒙脂油；我却以你的律法为乐。 ###EN### Their heart is heavy as with fat; But I delight in Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:71 我受苦是与我有益，为要使我学习你的律例。 ###EN### It is good for me that I have been afflicted, That I might learn Your statutes.
Verse_Ch: 119:72 你口中的律法与我有益，胜过千万的金银。 ###EN### The law of Your mouth is better to me Than thousands of pieces of gold and silver.
Verse_Ch: 119:73 你的手造作我、建立我；求你赐我悟性，可以学习你的诫命。 ###EN### Your hands have made me and fashioned me; Give me understanding that I may learn Your commandments.
Verse_Ch: 119:74 敬畏你的人看见我就喜乐，因我仰望你的话。 ###EN### Those who fear You will see me and rejoice, For I have hoped in Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:75 耶和华阿，我知道你的判语是公义的；你使我受苦，是以信实待我。 ###EN### I know, O Jehovah, that Your judgments are righteous And that in faithfulness You afflicted me.
Verse_Ch: 119:76 求你照着你对仆人所说的话，以慈爱安慰我。 ###EN### Let Your lovingkindness, I beseech You, be my comfort, According to Your word to Your servant.
Verse_Ch: 119:77 愿你的怜恤临到我，使我存活；因你的律法是我的喜乐。 ###EN### Let Your compassions come to me, and I will live; For Your law is my delight.
Verse_Ch: 119:78 愿骄傲人蒙羞，因为他们以谎言屈枉我；但我要默想你的训辞。 ###EN### Let the proud be put to shame, for they have subverted my cause with a lie; But I will muse upon Your precepts.
Verse_Ch: 119:79 愿敬畏你的人归向我，他们就知道你的法度。 ###EN### Let those who fear You turn to me, And they will know Your testimonies.
Verse_Ch: 119:80 愿我的心在你的律例上完全，使我不至蒙羞。 ###EN### May my heart be perfect in Your statutes, That I may not be put to shame.
Verse_Ch: 119:81 我的魂因渴想你的救恩以致衰竭；我仰望你的话语。 ###EN### My soul faints while longing for Your salvation; I hope in Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:82 我的眼因盼望你的话语以致昏蒙，我说，你几时才安慰我？ ###EN### My eyes faint while longing for Your word, As I say, When will You comfort me?
Verse_Ch: 119:83 我好像烟薰的皮袋，但我不忘记你的律例。 ###EN### For I have become like a wineskin in the smoke; But I do not forget Your statutes.
Verse_Ch: 119:84 你仆人的日子有多少？你几时才向逼迫我的人施行公理呢？ ###EN### How many are the days of Your servant? When will You execute justice upon my persecutors?
Verse_Ch: 119:85 不依从你律法的骄傲人，为我掘了坑。 ###EN### The proud have dug pits for me, Those who are not according to Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:86 你的诫命尽都信实；他们诡诈的逼迫我；求你帮助我。 ###EN### All Your commandments are faithful; They persecute me falsely; help me.
Verse_Ch: 119:87 他们几乎把我从地上灭绝；但我没有离弃你的训辞。 ###EN### They have almost consumed me upon the earth; But I have not forsaken Your precepts.
Verse_Ch: 119:88 求你照你的慈爱将我救活，我就遵守你口中的法度。 ###EN### Enliven me according to Your lovingkindness, And I will keep the testimony of Your mouth.
Verse_Ch: 119:89 耶和华阿，你的话立定在天，直到永远。 ###EN### Forever, O Jehovah, Does Your word stand firm in heaven.
Verse_Ch: 119:90 你的信实存到万代；你坚定了地，地就长存。 ###EN### Your faithfulness is from generation to generation; You established the earth, and it abides.
Verse_Ch: 119:91 万物照你的判语存到今日，因为它们都是你的仆役。 ###EN### They abide to this day according to Your ordinances, For all things are Your servants.
Verse_Ch: 119:92 我若不是以你的律法为乐，早就在患难中灭绝了。 ###EN### Unless Your law had been my delight, I would have perished in my affliction.
Verse_Ch: 119:93 我永不忘记你的训辞，因你用这训辞将我救活。 ###EN### I will never forget Your precepts, For by them You have enlivened me.
Verse_Ch: 119:94 我是属你的；求你救我，因我寻求了你的训辞。 ###EN### I am Yours; save me, For I have sought Your precepts.
Verse_Ch: 119:95 恶人等待我，要灭绝我，我却要揣摩你的法度。 ###EN### The wicked have waited for me in order to destroy me, But I consider Your testimonies.
Verse_Ch: 119:96 我看一切圆满的事都有尽头，惟有你的诫命极其宽广。 ###EN### I have seen an end to all perfection, But Your commandment is all-expansive.
Verse_Ch: 119:97 我何等爱你的律法，终日不住的默想。 ###EN### Oh, how I love Your law! All day long it is my musing.
Verse_Ch: 119:98 你的诫命使我比仇敌有智慧，因这些诫命常与我同在。 ###EN### Your commandments make me wiser than my enemies, For they are always with me.
Verse_Ch: 119:99 我比我所有的师傅更通达，因我默想你的法度。 ###EN### I have more insight than all my teachers, For Your testimonies are my musing.
Verse_Ch: 119:100 我比年老的更明白，因我守了你的训辞。 ###EN### I understand more than the aged, For I have kept Your precepts.
Verse_Ch: 119:101 我禁止我的脚走一切的邪路，为要遵守你的话。 ###EN### I have withheld my feet from every evil way, That I might keep Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:102 我没有偏离你的典章，因为你教训了我。 ###EN### I have not turned aside from Your ordinances, For You have taught me.
Verse_Ch: 119:103 你的言语在我上膛何等甘美！在我口中比蜜更甜！ ###EN### How sweet are Your words to my taste! Sweeter than honey to my mouth!
Verse_Ch: 119:104 我借着你的训辞，得以明白；所以我恨一切虚假的行径。 ###EN### Through Your precepts I gain understanding; Therefore I hate every false way.
Verse_Ch: 119:105 你的话是我脚前的灯，是我路上的光。 ###EN### Your word is a lamp to my feet And a light to my path.
Verse_Ch: 119:106 我曾起誓遵守你公义的典章，我必坚守这誓言。 ###EN### I have sworn and will confirm it, That I will keep Your righteous ordinances.
Verse_Ch: 119:107 我甚是受苦；耶和华阿，求你照你的话将我救活。 ###EN### I have been greatly afflicted; O Jehovah, enliven me according to Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:108 耶和华阿，求你悦纳我口中的甘心祭，且将你的典章教训我。 ###EN### Accept, I pray, the freewill offerings of my mouth, O Jehovah; And teach me Your ordinances.
Verse_Ch: 119:109 我的性命常在危险之中，我却不忘记你的律法。 ###EN### My soul is continually in my hand, But I do not forget Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:110 恶人为我设下网罗，我却没有偏离你的训辞而迷失。 ###EN### The wicked have laid a trap for me, But I do not stray from Your precepts.
Verse_Ch: 119:111 你的法度是我永远的产业，因为这是我心中的欢乐。 ###EN### Your testimonies are my heritage forever, For they are the gladness of my heart.
Verse_Ch: 119:112 我的心倾向你的律例，要永远遵行，一直到底。 ###EN### I have inclined my heart to perform Your statutes Forever, to the end.
Verse_Ch: 119:113 心怀二意的人，为我所恨；但你的律法，为我所爱。 ###EN### I hate those who are double-minded, But I love Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:114 你是我藏身之处，又是我的盾牌；我仰望你的话语。 ###EN### You are my hiding place and my shield; In Your word do I hope.
Verse_Ch: 119:115 你们作恶的人离开我罢，我好遵守我神的诫命。 ###EN### Depart from me, you evildoers, That I may keep the commandments of my God.
Verse_Ch: 119:116 求你照你的话扶持我，使我存活，也不叫我因所盼望的蒙羞。 ###EN### Uphold me according to Your word that I may live, And do not let me be ashamed of my hope.
Verse_Ch: 119:117 求你扶持我，使我得救，我必时常看重你的律例。 ###EN### Hold me up that I may be safe, And I will regard Your statutes continually.
Verse_Ch: 119:118 凡偏离你律例的人，你都轻弃他们，因为他们的诡诈必归虚空。 ###EN### You spurn all those who stray from Your statutes, For their deceitfulness is vain.
Verse_Ch: 119:119 凡地上的恶人，你除掉他们好像除掉渣滓；因此我爱你的法度。 ###EN### You do away with all the wicked ones of the earth like dross; Therefore I love Your testimonies.
Verse_Ch: 119:120 我因惧怕你，肉就发抖，我也怕你的判语。 ###EN### My flesh trembles for fear of You, And I am afraid of Your judgments.
Verse_Ch: 119:121 我行过公理和公义；求你不要把我撇给欺压我的人。 ###EN### I have performed justice and righteousness; Do not leave me to my oppressors.
Verse_Ch: 119:122 求你为仆人作保，使我得好处；不容骄傲人欺压我。 ###EN### Guarantee Your servant's well-being; Do not let the proud oppress me.
Verse_Ch: 119:123 我的眼因盼望你的救恩和你公义的话，以致昏蒙。 ###EN### My eyes faint while longing for Your salvation And for Your righteous word.
Verse_Ch: 119:124 求你照你的慈爱待仆人，将你的律例教训我。 ###EN### Deal with Your servant according to Your lovingkindness, And teach me Your statutes.
Verse_Ch: 119:125 我是你的仆人；求你赐我悟性，使我得知你的法度。 ###EN### I am Your servant; give me understanding, That I may know Your testimonies.
Verse_Ch: 119:126 这是耶和华行事的时候，因为人干犯了你的律法。 ###EN### It is time for Jehovah to act, For they have broken Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:127 所以我爱你的诫命，胜过金子，且胜过精金； ###EN### Therefore I love Your commandments More than gold, indeed, more than fine gold;
Verse_Ch: 119:128 因此你一切的训辞，在万事上，我都以为正直；我恨恶一切虚假的行径。 ###EN### Therefore I esteem all Your precepts concerning all things to be right, And I hate every false way.
Verse_Ch: 119:129 你的法度奇妙；所以我全魂谨守。 ###EN### Your testimonies are wonderful; Therefore my soul keeps them.
Verse_Ch: 119:130 你的言语一解开，就发出亮光，使愚蒙人通达。 ###EN### The opening of Your words gives light, Imparting understanding to the simple.
Verse_Ch: 119:131 我张口喘气，因我切慕你的诫命。 ###EN### I opened my mouth wide and panted, For I longed for Your commandments.
Verse_Ch: 119:132 求你照着你待那些爱你名之人的常例，转向我，恩待我。 ###EN### Turn to me, and be gracious to me, As is Your custom with those who love Your name.
Verse_Ch: 119:133 求你用你的话使我脚步稳当，不许什么罪孽辖制我。 ###EN### Establish my footsteps in Your word, And do not let any iniquity have dominion over me.
Verse_Ch: 119:134 求你救赎我脱离人的欺压，使我遵守你的训辞。 ###EN### Redeem me from man's oppression, That I may keep Your precepts.
Verse_Ch: 119:135 求你用脸光照仆人，又将你的律例教训我。 ###EN### Cause Your face to shine on Your servant, And teach me Your statutes.
Verse_Ch: 119:136 我的眼泪像河水流下，因为他们不守你的律法。 ###EN### My eyes shed streams of water, Because men do not keep Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:137 耶和华阿，你是公义的；你的判语也是正直的。 ###EN### You are righteous, O Jehovah; And Your judgments are upright.
Verse_Ch: 119:138 你凭公义和至大的信实，命定了你的法度。 ###EN### You have commanded Your testimonies in righteousness And great faithfulness.
Verse_Ch: 119:139 我心里焦急，如同火烧，因我的敌人忘记了你的言语。 ###EN### My zeal has consumed me, For my adversaries have forgotten Your words.
Verse_Ch: 119:140 你的话极其精炼，为你的仆人所爱。 ###EN### Your word is very pure, And Your servant loves it.
Verse_Ch: 119:141 我微小被人藐视，却不忘记你的训辞。 ###EN### I am small and despised, But I do not forget Your precepts.
Verse_Ch: 119:142 你的公义是永远的公义，你的律法尽是真理。 ###EN### Your righteousness is an eternal righteousness, And Your law is truth.
Verse_Ch: 119:143 我遭遇患难窘迫，你的诫命却是我的喜乐。 ###EN### Distress and anguish have come upon me, But Your commandments are my delight.
Verse_Ch: 119:144 你的法度永远是公义的；求你赐我悟性，我就活了。 ###EN### Your testimonies are righteous forever; Give me understanding, and I will live.
Verse_Ch: 119:145 耶和华阿，我全心呼求你，求你应允我。我必遵守你的律例。 ###EN### I called with my whole heart; answer me, O Jehovah. I will keep Your statutes.
Verse_Ch: 119:146 我向你呼求，求你救我；我要遵守你的法度。 ###EN### I called upon You; save me, And I will observe Your testimonies.
Verse_Ch: 119:147 我趁天未亮呼求；我仰望了你的言语。 ###EN### I anticipated the dawn and cried out; I hoped in Your words.
Verse_Ch: 119:148 我趁夜更未换，将眼睁开，为要默想你的话语。 ###EN### My eyes anticipated the night watches, That I might muse upon Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:149 求你照你的慈爱，听我的声音；耶和华阿，求你照你的典章将我救活。 ###EN### Hear my voice according to Your lovingkindness; O Jehovah, according to Your ordinances enliven me.
Verse_Ch: 119:150 意逼迫我的人临近了；他们远离你的律法。 ###EN### Those who persecute me with evil intent draw near; They are far from Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:151 耶和华阿，你与我相近；你一切的诫命尽是真理。 ###EN### You are near, O Jehovah; And all Your commandments are truth.
Verse_Ch: 119:152 我从你的法度，久已知道那是你永远立定的。 ###EN### Of old I have known from Your testimonies That You have founded them forever.
Verse_Ch: 119:153 求你看顾我的苦难，搭救我；因我没有忘记你的律法。 ###EN### Look at my affliction, and deliver me; For I have not forgotten Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:154 求你为我辨屈，救赎我；求你照你的话将我救活。 ###EN### Plead my case, and redeem me; Enliven me according to Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:155 救恩远离恶人，因为他们不寻求你的律例。 ###EN### Salvation is far from the wicked, For they do not seek Your statutes.
Verse_Ch: 119:156 耶和华阿，你的怜恤本为大；求你照你的典章将我救活。 ###EN### Great are Your compassions, O Jehovah; Enliven me according to Your ordinances.
Verse_Ch: 119:157 逼迫我的和敌挡我的很多，但我没有偏离你的法度。 ###EN### Many are my persecutors and my adversaries, But I have not swerved from Your testimonies.
Verse_Ch: 119:158 我看见奸诈的人就厌恶，因为他们不遵守你的话。 ###EN### I saw the treacherous and loathed them, Because they did not keep Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:159 你看我怎样爱你的训辞；耶和华阿，求你照你的慈爱将我救活。 ###EN### See how I have loved Your precepts; O Jehovah, enliven me according to Your lovingkindness.
Verse_Ch: 119:160 你话语的总和是真理，你一切公义的典章永远长存。 ###EN### The sum of Your word is truth, And all Your righteous ordinances are forever.
Verse_Ch: 119:161 首领无故的逼迫我，但我的心畏惧你的言语。 ###EN### Princes have persecuted me without cause, But my heart stands in awe of Your words.
Verse_Ch: 119:162 我因你的话欢喜，好像人得了许多掳物。 ###EN### I rejoice at Your word, Like one who finds great spoil.
Verse_Ch: 119:163 虚谎是我所恨恶所憎嫌的，惟你的律法是我所爱的。 ###EN### I hate and abhor falsehood, But I love Your law.
Verse_Ch: 119:164 我因你公义的典章，一天七次赞美你。 ###EN### Seven times a day I praise You For Your righteous ordinances.
Verse_Ch: 119:165 爱你律法的人有大平安，什么都不能使他们绊跌。 ###EN### There is great peace for those who love Your law, And there is no occasion of stumbling for them.
Verse_Ch: 119:166 耶和华阿，我仰望了你的救恩，遵行了你的诫命。 ###EN### I have hoped for Your salvation, O Jehovah; And I have done Your commandments.
Verse_Ch: 119:167 我的魂守了你的法度，这些法度我甚喜爱。 ###EN### My soul has kept Your testimonies, And I love them very much.
Verse_Ch: 119:168 我遵守了你的训辞和法度，因我一切的行径都在你面前。 ###EN### I have kept Your precepts and Your testimonies, For all my ways are before You.
Verse_Ch: 119:169 耶和华阿，愿我的呼吁达到你面前；求你照你的话赐我悟性。 ###EN### Let my cry come before You, O Jehovah; Give me understanding according to Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:170 愿我的恳求达到你面前；求你照你的话搭救我。 ###EN### Let my supplication come before You; Deliver me according to Your word.
Verse_Ch: 119:171 愿我的嘴唇倾吐赞美的话，因为你将你的律例教训我。 ###EN### Let my lips pour forth praise, For You teach me Your statutes.
Verse_Ch: 119:172 愿我的舌头歌唱你的话，因你一切的诫命尽是公义。 ###EN### Let my tongue sing of Your word, For all Your commandments are righteousness.
Verse_Ch: 119:173 愿你用手帮助我，因我拣选了你的训辞。 ###EN### Let Your hand be ready to help me, For I have chosen Your precepts.
Verse_Ch: 119:174 耶和华阿，我切慕你的救恩，你的律法也是我的喜乐。 ###EN### I have longed for Your salvation, O Jehovah, And Your law is my delight.
Verse_Ch: 119:175 愿我的性命存活，可以赞美你；愿你的典章帮助我。 ###EN### Let my soul live, and it will praise You; And let Your ordinances help me.
Verse_Ch: 119:176 我如亡羊走迷了路；求你寻找仆人，因我没有忘记你的诫命。 ###EN### I have gone astray like a lost sheep; seek Your servant, For I have not forgotten Your commandments.
Chapter_Header: 120
Verse_Ch: 120:1 我在急难中呼求耶和华，祂就应允我。 ###EN### In my distress I called out to Jehovah, And He answered me.
Verse_Ch: 120:2 耶和华阿，求你救我脱离说谎的嘴唇，脱离诡诈的舌头。 ###EN### O Jehovah, deliver my soul from lying lips, From a tongue of deceit.
Verse_Ch: 120:3 诡诈的舌头阿，要给你什么呢？要拿什么加给你呢？ ###EN### What should be given to you, And what further shall be done to you, O tongue of deceit?
Verse_Ch: 120:4 就是勇士的利箭，连同罗腾木的炭火！ ###EN### The sharp arrows of a mighty man, With the burning coals of the broom tree!
Verse_Ch: 120:5 我有祸了，因我寄居在米设，住在基达帐棚之中。 ###EN### Woe is me, for I sojourn in Meshech, I dwell among the tents of Kedar.
Verse_Ch: 120:6 我与那恨恶和平的人，许久同住。 ###EN### Long has my soul had its dwelling With him who hates peace.
Verse_Ch: 120:7 我愿和平；但我发言，他们就要争战。 ###EN### I am for peace; but when I speak, They are for war.
Chapter_Header: 121
Verse_Ch: 121:1 我要向山举目。我的帮助从何而来？ ###EN### I will lift up my eyes to the hills. From where will my help come?
Verse_Ch: 121:2 我的帮助从造天地的耶和华而来。 ###EN### My help comes from Jehovah, Who made heaven and earth.
Verse_Ch: 121:3 祂必不叫你的脚滑跌；保护你的必不打盹。 ###EN### He will not let your foot slip; He who keeps you will not slumber.
Verse_Ch: 121:4 看哪，保护以色列的，也不打盹，也不睡觉。 ###EN### Behold, Israel's Keeper Will neither slumber nor sleep.
Verse_Ch: 121:5 保护你的是耶和华；耶和华在你右边荫庇你。 ###EN### Jehovah is your Keeper; Jehovah is your shade at your right hand.
Verse_Ch: 121:6 白日太阳必不伤你，夜间月亮必不害你。 ###EN### The sun will not strike you by day, Nor the moon by night.
Verse_Ch: 121:7 耶和华要保护你，免受一切的灾害；祂要保护你的性命。 ###EN### Jehovah will keep you from all evil; He will keep your soul.
Verse_Ch: 121:8 你出你入，耶和华要保护你，从今时直到永远。 ###EN### Jehovah will keep your going out and your coming in From now and to eternity.
Chapter_Header: 122
Verse_Ch: 122:1 人对我说，我们往耶和华的殿去，我就欢喜。 ###EN### I rejoiced when they said to me, Let us go to the house of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 122:2 耶路撒冷阿，我们的脚，站在你的门内。 ###EN### Our feet are standing Within your gates, O Jerusalem.
Verse_Ch: 122:3 耶路撒冷被建造，如同连络整齐的一座城； ###EN### Jerusalem has been built as a city That has been compacted together;
Verse_Ch: 122:4 众支派，就是耶和华的支派，上那里去，作以色列的见证，称谢耶和华的名。 ###EN### To which the tribes go up, The tribes of Jehovah-A custom for Israel-To give thanks to the name of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 122:5 因为在那里设立了审判的宝座，就是大卫家的宝座。 ###EN### For there thrones are set for judgment, Thrones of the house of David.
Verse_Ch: 122:6 你们要为耶路撒冷求平安。耶路撒冷阿，爱你的人必然兴旺。 ###EN### Pray for the peace of Jerusalem. Those who love you will prosper.
Verse_Ch: 122:7 愿你城中平安，愿你宫内兴旺。 ###EN### Peace be within your bulwarks, And prosperity within your citadels.
Verse_Ch: 122:8 因我弟兄和同伴的缘故，我要说，愿平安在你中间。 ###EN### For my brothers' and companions' sake I will now say, Peace be within you.
Verse_Ch: 122:9 因耶和华我们神殿的缘故，我要为你求好处。 ###EN### For the sake of the house of Jehovah our God I will seek your good.
Chapter_Header: 123
Verse_Ch: 123:1 坐在天上的主阿，我向你举目。 ###EN### To You do I lift up my eyes, You who sit enthroned in heaven.
Verse_Ch: 123:2 看哪，仆人的眼睛怎样望主人的手，使女的眼睛怎样望主母的手，我们的眼睛也照样望耶和华我们的神，直到祂恩待我们。 ###EN### Behold, as the eyes of the servants Look to the hand of their masters, As the eyes of a servant girl Look to the hand of her mistress, So our eyes look to Jehovah our God, Until He is gracious to us.
Verse_Ch: 123:3 耶和华阿，求你恩待我们，恩待我们；因为我们饱受藐视，到了极点。 ###EN### Be gracious to us, O Jehovah, be gracious to us; For we are greatly filled with contempt.
Verse_Ch: 123:4 我们的魂饱受那些安逸人的讥诮，和骄傲人的藐视，到了极点。 ###EN### Our soul is greatly filled With the scorn of those who are at ease, With the contempt of the proud.
Chapter_Header: 124
Verse_Ch: 124:1 以色列人要说，若不是耶和华在我们这边， ###EN### If it had not been Jehovah who was on our side, Oh, let Israel say,
Verse_Ch: 124:2 若不是耶和华在我们这边，当人起来攻击我们， ###EN### If it had not been Jehovah who was on our side When men rose up against us;
Verse_Ch: 124:3 向我们发怒的时候，早就把我们活活的吞了； ###EN### Then they would have swallowed us up alive When their anger burned against us;
Verse_Ch: 124:4 那时，大水必漫过我们，河水必淹没我们； ###EN### Then the waters would have washed us away; The stream would have passed over our soul;
Verse_Ch: 124:5 那时，狂傲的水必淹没我们。 ###EN### Then the proud waters Would have passed over our soul.
Verse_Ch: 124:6 耶和华是当受颂赞的，祂没有把我们交给敌人，作他们爪牙下的猎物。 ###EN### Blessed be Jehovah, who has not given us As prey to their teeth.
Verse_Ch: 124:7 我们好像雀鸟从捕鸟人的网罗里逃脱；网罗破裂，我们逃脱了。 ###EN### Our soul has escaped like a bird, Out of the snare of the fowlers; The snare is broken, And we have escaped.
Verse_Ch: 124:8 我们得帮助，是在于造天地之耶和华的名。 ###EN### Our help is in the name of Jehovah, Who made heaven and earth.
Chapter_Header: 125
Verse_Ch: 125:1 信靠耶和华的人，好像锡安山，永远存在，总不动摇。 ###EN### Those who trust in Jehovah are like Mount Zion, Which cannot be moved but abides forever.
Verse_Ch: 125:2 众山怎样围绕耶路撒冷，耶和华也照样围绕祂的百姓，从今时直到永远。 ###EN### Jerusalem-mountains surround her; And Jehovah surrounds His people From now and to eternity.
Verse_Ch: 125:3 恶人的杖必不落在义人的业分上，免得义人伸手作罪孽。 ###EN### For the scepter of wickedness will not rest Upon the allotment of the righteous, That the righteous would not put forth Their hands to iniquity.
Verse_Ch: 125:4 耶和华阿，求你善待那些为善，和心里正直的人。 ###EN### Do good, O Jehovah, to the good And to those upright in their hearts.
Verse_Ch: 125:5 至于那些偏行弯曲道路的人，耶和华必将他们和作孽的人一同带去受刑。愿平安归于以色列。 ###EN### But as for those who turn aside to their crooked ways, Jehovah will lead them off with the workers of iniquity. Peace be upon Israel.
Chapter_Header: 126
Verse_Ch: 126:1 当耶和华使那些被掳的人归回锡安的时候，我们好像作梦的人。 ###EN### When Jehovah turned again the captivity of Zion, We were like those who dream.
Verse_Ch: 126:2 那时我们满口喜笑，满舌欢呼。那时列国中有人说，耶和华为他们行了大事。 ###EN### At that time our mouth was filled with laughter And our tongue with a ringing shout. At that time they said among the nations, Jehovah has done great things for them.
Verse_Ch: 126:3 耶和华为我们行了大事，我们就欢喜。 ###EN### Jehovah has done great things for us; We are joyful.
Verse_Ch: 126:4 耶和华阿，求你使我们被掳的人归回，好像南地的河水复流。 ###EN### Turn again, O Jehovah, our captivity Like the streams in the south.
Verse_Ch: 126:5 流泪撒种的，必欢呼收割。 ###EN### Those who sow in tears Will reap with a ringing shout.
Verse_Ch: 126:6 那带种子流着泪出去撒播的，必要欢呼着带禾捆回来。 ###EN### He who goes forth and weeps, Bearing seed for scattering, Will no doubt come in with a ringing shout, Bearing his sheaves with him.
Chapter_Header: 127
Verse_Ch: 127:1 若不是耶和华建造房屋，建造的人就枉然劳力；若不是耶和华看守城池，看守的人就枉然儆醒。 ###EN### Unless Jehovah builds the house, Those who build it labor in vain. Unless Jehovah keeps the city, The guard watches in vain.
Verse_Ch: 127:2 你们清晨早起，夜晚歇卧，吃劳碌得来的饭，本是枉然；耶和华在祂所亲爱的人睡觉时，必仍然赐给他们食物。 ###EN### It is vain for you to rise up early, To lie down late, To eat the bread of toil; All the same, He gives to His beloved while they sleep.
Verse_Ch: 127:3 看哪，儿女是耶和华所赐的产业；腹中的果子是祂所给的赏赐。 ###EN### Behold, children are the heritage of Jehovah, The fruit of the womb a reward.
Verse_Ch: 127:4 少年时所生的儿女，好像勇士手中的箭。 ###EN### Like arrows in the hand of a mighty man, So are the children of one's youth.
Verse_Ch: 127:5 箭袋充满了箭的人，便为有福。他们在城门口和仇敌说话的时候，必不至于羞愧。 ###EN### Blessed is the man Who fills his quiver with them. He will not be put to shame When he speaks with enemies in the gate.
Chapter_Header: 128
Verse_Ch: 128:1 凡敬畏耶和华、遵行祂道路的人，便为有福。 ###EN### Blessed is everyone who fears Jehovah, Who walks in His ways.
Verse_Ch: 128:2 你要吃亲手劳碌得来的；你要蒙福，并且顺利。 ###EN### You will indeed eat the labor of your hands; You will be blessed, and it will go well with you.
Verse_Ch: 128:3 你妻子在你的内室，好像多结果子的葡萄树。你儿女围绕你的桌子，好像橄榄栽子。 ###EN### Your wife will be like a fruitful vine In the innermost parts of your house. Your children will be like olive shoots Round about your table.
Verse_Ch: 128:4 敬畏耶和华的人，必要这样蒙福。 ###EN### Thus will the man be blessed Who fears Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 128:5 愿耶和华从锡安赐福给你；愿你一生的日子，看见耶路撒冷的美福。 ###EN### Jehovah bless you from Zion; And may you see the prosperity of Jerusalem All the days of your life.
Verse_Ch: 128:6 愿你看见你儿女的儿女。愿平安归于以色列。 ###EN### May you also see the children of your children. Peace be upon Israel.
Chapter_Header: 129
Verse_Ch: 129:1 以色列当说，从我幼年以来，敌人屡次苦害我， ###EN### Many times have they afflicted me since my youth, Oh, let Israel say,
Verse_Ch: 129:2 从我幼年以来，敌人屡次苦害我，却没有胜过我。 ###EN### Many times have they afflicted me since my youth, Yet they did not prevail against me.
Verse_Ch: 129:3 他们好像扶犁的，在我背上扶犁而耕；耕的犁沟甚长。 ###EN### The plowers plowed on my back; They made their furrows long.
Verse_Ch: 129:4 耶和华是公义的；祂砍断了恶人的绳索。 ###EN### Jehovah is righteous; He has cut the cords of the wicked.
Verse_Ch: 129:5 愿恨恶锡安的，都蒙羞退后。 ###EN### May all who hate Zion Be put to shame and turned back.
Verse_Ch: 129:6 愿他们像房顶上的草，未长成而枯萎； ###EN### May they be like grass on the housetops, Which withers before it grows up,
Verse_Ch: 129:7 收割的不够一把，捆禾的也不够满怀。 ###EN### With which the reaper does not fill his hand, Or he who binds sheaves, his bosom.
Verse_Ch: 129:8 过路的也不说，愿耶和华所赐的福，归于你们；我们在耶和华的名里，给你们祝福。 ###EN### Nor may those who pass by say, The blessing of Jehovah be upon you! We bless you in the name of Jehovah.
Chapter_Header: 130
Verse_Ch: 130:1 耶和华阿，我从深处向你呼求。 ###EN### Out of the depths I have called upon You, O Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 130:2 主阿，求你听我的声音；愿你侧耳听我恳求的声音。 ###EN### O Lord, hear my voice; Let Your ears be attentive To the voice of my supplications.
Verse_Ch: 130:3 耶和华阿，你若察看罪孽，主阿，谁能站得住呢？ ###EN### If You, O Jehovah, marked iniquities, Who, O Lord, would stand?
Verse_Ch: 130:4 但在你有赦免之恩，要叫人敬畏你。 ###EN### But with You there is forgiveness, That You would be feared.
Verse_Ch: 130:5 我等候耶和华；我的魂等候，我也仰望祂的话。 ###EN### I wait for Jehovah; my soul waits, And in His word I hope.
Verse_Ch: 130:6 我的魂等候主，胜于守夜的等候天亮，胜于守夜的等候天亮。 ###EN### My soul waits for the Lord More than watchmen for the morning, Yes, watchmen for the morning.
Verse_Ch: 130:7 以色列阿，你当仰望耶和华；因耶和华有慈爱，在祂那里有丰盛的救赎； ###EN### Hope in Jehovah, O Israel; For with Jehovah there is lovingkindness, And with Him abundantly there is redemption;
Verse_Ch: 130:8 祂必救赎以色列脱离一切的罪孽。 ###EN### And it is He who will redeem Israel From all its iniquities.
Chapter_Header: 131
Verse_Ch: 131:1 耶和华阿，我的心不狂傲，我的眼不高大；过于重大和希奇的事，我也不去行。 ###EN### O Jehovah, my heart is not proud, Nor are my eyes haughty; Nor do I go about in things too great Or too wondrous for me.
Verse_Ch: 131:2 我使我的魂平稳安静，好像断过奶的孩子在他母亲怀中；我的魂在我里面真像断过奶的孩子。 ###EN### Surely I have calmed And quieted my soul, Like a weaned child with its mother; Like a weaned child is my soul within me.
Verse_Ch: 131:3 以色列阿，你当仰望耶和华，从今时直到永远。 ###EN### Hope in Jehovah, O Israel, From now and to eternity.
Chapter_Header: 132
Verse_Ch: 132:1 耶和华阿，求你记念大卫，记念他所受的一切苦难。 ###EN### Remember, O Jehovah, for David's sake All his afflictions;
Verse_Ch: 132:2 他怎样向耶和华起誓，向雅各的大能者许愿，说， ###EN### How he swore to Jehovah And vowed to the Mighty One of Jacob:
Verse_Ch: 132:3 我必不进我的帐幕，也不上我的床榻； ###EN### I shall not go into the tent of my house; I shall not go up onto the couch of my bed;
Verse_Ch: 132:4 我不容我的眼睛睡觉，也不容我的眼皮打盹； ###EN### I shall not give sleep to my eyes, Slumber to my eyelids;
Verse_Ch: 132:5 直等我为耶和华寻得所在，为雅各的大能者寻得居所。 ###EN### Until I find a place for Jehovah, A tabernacle for the Mighty One of Jacob.
Verse_Ch: 132:6 看哪，我们听说约柜在以法他，我们在基列耶琳就寻见了。 ###EN### Behold, we heard of it in Ephrathah; We found it in the fields of Jaar.
Verse_Ch: 132:7 我们要进祂的居所，在祂脚凳前下拜。 ###EN### We will go into His tabernacle; We will worship at His footstool.
Verse_Ch: 132:8 耶和华阿，求你兴起，和你有能力的约柜同入你安息之所。 ###EN### Arise, O Jehovah, unto Your resting place, You and the Ark of Your strength.
Verse_Ch: 132:9 愿你的祭司披上公义，愿你的虔诚人欢呼。 ###EN### Let Your priests be clothed with righteousness, And let Your faithful ones give a ringing shout.
Verse_Ch: 132:10 求你因你仆人大卫的缘故，不厌弃你的受膏者。 ###EN### For the sake of David Your servant, Do not turn away the face of Your Anointed One.
Verse_Ch: 132:11 耶和华向大卫凭真实起了誓，必不反覆，说，我要从你本身所生的，立一位坐在你的宝座上。 ###EN### Jehovah has sworn unto David in truth; He will not turn from it: Of the fruit of your body I will set One upon your throne.
Verse_Ch: 132:12 你的众子若守我的约，和我所教训他们的法度，他们的子孙也必永远坐在你的宝座上。 ###EN### If your children keep My covenant And My testimonies that I will teach them, Their children also will sit Upon your throne forever.
Verse_Ch: 132:13 因为耶和华拣选了锡安，愿意当作自己的居所， ###EN### For Jehovah has chosen Zion; He has desired it for His habitation.
Verse_Ch: 132:14 说，这是我永远安息之所；我要住在这里，因为是我所愿意的。 ###EN### This is My resting place forever; Here will I dwell, for I have desired it.
Verse_Ch: 132:15 我要丰厚的赐福与其中的粮，使其中的穷人饱得食物。 ###EN### I will abundantly bless its provision; I will satisfy its poor with bread.
Verse_Ch: 132:16 我要使其中的祭司披上救恩，其中的虔诚人大声欢呼。 ###EN### And its priests I will clothe with salvation, And its faithful ones will shout with a ringing shout.
Verse_Ch: 132:17 我要叫大卫的角在那里长出；我为我的受膏者预备明灯。 ###EN### There I will cause a horn of David to shoot forth; I have prepared a lamp for My anointed one.
Verse_Ch: 132:18 我要使他的仇敌披上羞耻，但他的冠冕要在他头上发光。 ###EN### I will clothe his enemies with shame, But on him his crown will shine.
Chapter_Header: 133
Verse_Ch: 133:1 看哪，弟兄和睦同居，是何等的善，何等的美！ ###EN### Behold, how good and how pleasant it is For brothers to dwell in unity!
Verse_Ch: 133:2 这好比那上好的油，浇在亚伦的头上，流到胡须，又流到他的衣襟； ###EN### It is like the fine oil upon the head That ran down upon the beard, Upon Aaron's beard, That ran down upon the hem of his garments;
Verse_Ch: 133:3 又好比黑门的甘露，降在锡安山；因为在那里有耶和华所命定的福，就是永远的生命。 ###EN### Like the dew of Hermon That came down upon the mountains of Zion. For there Jehovah commanded the blessing: Life forever.
Chapter_Header: 134
Verse_Ch: 134:1 耶和华的众仆人，夜间站在耶和华殿中的，你们当颂赞耶和华。 ###EN### Bless Jehovah now, All you servants of Jehovah Who stand by night in the house of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 134:2 你们当在圣所举手，颂赞耶和华。 ###EN### Lift up your hands in the sanctuary, And bless Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 134:3 愿造天地的耶和华，从锡安赐福给你们。 ###EN### May Jehovah, who made heaven and earth, Bless you from Zion.
Chapter_Header: 135
Verse_Ch: 135:1 阿利路亚！你们要赞美耶和华的名；耶和华的仆人，站在耶和华殿中，站在我们神殿院中的，你们要赞美祂。 ###EN### Hallelujah! Praise the name of Jehovah; Praise Him, you servants of Jehovah,
Verse_Ch: 135:2  ###EN### Who stand in the house of Jehovah, In the courts of the house of our God.
Verse_Ch: 135:3 你们要赞美耶和华，耶和华本为善；要歌颂祂的名，因为这名是可喜悦的。 ###EN### Praise Jehovah, for Jehovah is good; Sing psalms to His name, for it is pleasant.
Verse_Ch: 135:4 耶和华拣选了雅各归祂自己，拣选了以色列作祂自己的珍宝。 ###EN### For Jehovah has chosen Jacob for Himself, Israel for His personal treasure.
Verse_Ch: 135:5 因为我知道耶和华为大，也知道我们的主超乎万神之上。 ###EN### For I know that Jehovah is great And that our Lord is above all gods.
Verse_Ch: 135:6 耶和华在天上，在地上，在海中，在一切的深处，都随自己的喜悦而行。 ###EN### Whatever Jehovah pleases He does In heaven and on earth, In the seas and all the depths.
Verse_Ch: 135:7 祂使云雾从地极上腾，造电随雨而闪，从祂府库中带出风来。 ###EN### He causes the vapors to ascend from the ends of the earth; He makes lightning for the rain; He brings forth wind from His treasuries.
Verse_Ch: 135:8 祂将埃及头生的，连人带牲畜，都击杀了。 ###EN### He struck the firstborn of Egypt, Both of man and of beast.
Verse_Ch: 135:9 埃及阿，祂施行神迹奇事在你当中，在法老和他一切臣仆身上。 ###EN### He sent signs and wonders into your midst, O Egypt, Upon Pharaoh and all his servants.
Verse_Ch: 135:10 祂击打许多国，又杀戮大能的王， ###EN### He struck many nations And slew mighty kings:
Verse_Ch: 135:11 就是亚摩利人的王西宏、和巴珊王噩、并迦南一切的国王， ###EN### Sihon the king of the Amorites And Og the king of Bashan And all the kingdoms of Canaan.
Verse_Ch: 135:12 将他们的地赐给祂的百姓以色列为业。 ###EN### And He gave their land as an inheritance, An inheritance to Israel His people.
Verse_Ch: 135:13 耶和华阿，你的名存到永远；耶和华阿，你可记念的名存到万代。 ###EN### O Jehovah, Your name is forever; O Jehovah, Your memorial is from generation to generation.
Verse_Ch: 135:14 耶和华要为祂的百姓伸冤，祂要怜恤祂的仆人。 ###EN### For Jehovah will execute judgment for His people, And He will have compassion concerning His servants.
