Verse_Ch: 135:15 列国的偶像是银的金的，是人手所造的； ###EN### The idols of the nations are mere silver and gold, The work of human hands.
Verse_Ch: 135:16 有口却不能言，有眼却不能看， ###EN### They have mouths, but they do not speak; They have eyes, but they do not see.
Verse_Ch: 135:17 有耳却不能听，口中也没有气息。 ###EN### They have ears, but they do not give ear; And there is no breath in their mouths.
Verse_Ch: 135:18 造它们的，并一切倚靠它们的，都要和它们一样。 ###EN### Those who make them, All who trust in them, Will be like them.
Verse_Ch: 135:19 以色列家阿，你们要颂赞耶和华。亚伦家阿，你们要颂赞耶和华。 ###EN### O house of Israel, bless Jehovah. O house of Aaron, bless Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 135:20 利未家阿，你们要颂赞耶和华。你们敬畏耶和华的，要颂赞耶和华。 ###EN### O house of Levi, bless Jehovah. O you who fear Jehovah, bless Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 135:21 住在耶路撒冷的耶和华，当从锡安受颂赞。阿利路亚。 ###EN### Blessed be Jehovah from Zion, Who dwells in Jerusalem. Hallelujah.
Chapter_Header: 136
Verse_Ch: 136:1 你们要称谢耶和华，因祂本为善；祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### Give thanks to Jehovah, for He is good; For His lovingkindness is forever.
Verse_Ch: 136:2 你们要称谢万神之神，因祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### Give thanks to the God of gods, For His lovingkindness is forever.
Verse_Ch: 136:3 你们要称谢万主之主，因祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### Give thanks to the Lord of lords, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:4 要称谢那独行大奇事的，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### To Him who alone does great wonders, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:5 要称谢那用聪明造天的，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### To Him who by understanding made the heavens, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:6 要称谢那铺地在水以上的，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### To Him who spread forth the earth over the waters, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:7 要称谢那造大光的，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### To Him who made the great lights, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:8 祂造日头管白昼，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### The sun for ruling the day, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:9 祂造月亮星宿管黑夜，因祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### The moon and the stars for ruling the night, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:10 要称谢那击杀埃及人头生的，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### To Him who struck Egypt in their firstborn, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:11 祂领以色列人从他们中间出来，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### And brought forth Israel from their midst, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:12 祂用大能的手和伸出来的膀臂，领他们出来，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### With a mighty hand and an outstretched arm, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:13 要称谢那使红海分开的，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### To Him who divided the Red Sea apart, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:14 祂领以色列人从其中经过，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### And brought Israel over through the midst of it, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:15 祂把法老和他的军兵推翻在红海里，因祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### And shook off Pharaoh and his force into the Red Sea, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:16 要称谢那引导自己的民行走旷野的，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### To Him who marched His people through the wilderness, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:17 要称谢那击杀大君王的，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### To Him who struck great kings, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:18 祂杀戮威严的君王，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### And slew majestic kings, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:19 就是杀戮亚摩利人的王西宏，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### Sihon the king of the Amorites, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:20 又杀巴珊王噩，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### And Og the king of Bashan, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:21 祂将他们的地赐给祂的百姓为业，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### And gave their land as an inheritance, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:22 就是赐给祂的仆人以色列为业，因祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### An inheritance to Israel His servant, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:23 祂记念我们在卑微的地步，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### Who remembered us in our low estate, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:24 祂救拔我们脱离敌人，因祂的慈爱永远长存； ###EN### And rescued us from our adversaries, For His lovingkindness is forever;
Verse_Ch: 136:25 祂赐粮食给凡有血肉的，因祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### Who gives food to all flesh, For His lovingkindness is forever.
Verse_Ch: 136:26 你们要称谢天上的神，因祂的慈爱永远长存。 ###EN### Give thanks to the God of heaven, For His lovingkindness is forever.
Chapter_Header: 137
Verse_Ch: 137:1 我们曾在巴比伦的河边坐下，一追想锡安就哭了。 ###EN### By the rivers of Babylon, There we sat down; indeed, we wept When we remembered Zion.
Verse_Ch: 137:2 我们把琴挂在那里的柳树上， ###EN### On the willows in the midst of it We hung up our lyres,
Verse_Ch: 137:3 因为在那里，掳掠我们的要我们唱歌，苦待我们的要我们作乐，说，给我们唱一首锡安歌罢。 ###EN### For there our captors required of us songs, And those who tormented us required of us mirth, saying, Sing for us One of the songs of Zion.
Verse_Ch: 137:4 我们怎能在外邦地唱耶和华的歌呢？ ###EN### How can we sing the song of Jehovah In a foreign land?
Verse_Ch: 137:5 耶路撒冷阿，我若忘记你，情愿我的右手忘记技巧。 ###EN### If I forget you, O Jerusalem, Let my right hand forget its skill.
Verse_Ch: 137:6 我若不记念你，若不看耶路撒冷过于我所最喜乐的，情愿我的舌头贴于上膛。 ###EN### Let my tongue cling to the roof of my mouth, If I do not remember you, If I do not prefer Jerusalem Above my chief joy.
Verse_Ch: 137:7 耶和华阿，求你记念以东人在耶路撒冷遭难的日子所行的，他们说，拆毁！拆毁！直拆到根基！ ###EN### Remember, O Jehovah, Against the children of Edom, The day of Jerusalem, Who said, Lay it bare! Lay it bare, Down to its foundation!
Verse_Ch: 137:8 将要被灭的巴比伦城阿，照你待我们的行为报复你的，那人便为有福。 ###EN### O daughter of Babylon, who are to be devastated, Happy will he be who repays you The recompense of what you have rendered to us.
Verse_Ch: 137:9 拿你的婴孩摔在磐石上的，那人便为有福。 ###EN### Happy will he be who seizes your little ones And dashes them against the rock.
Chapter_Header: 138
Verse_Ch: 138:1 我要全心称谢你，在诸神面前歌颂你。 ###EN### I will give You thanks with all my heart; Before the gods I will sing psalms to You.
Verse_Ch: 138:2 我要向你的圣殿下拜，为你的慈爱和真实称谢你的名；因你使你的话显为大，超过你一切的名声。 ###EN### I will bow toward Your holy temple And give thanks to Your name For Your lovingkindness and Your truth, For You have magnified Your word above all Your name.
Verse_Ch: 138:3 我呼求的日子，你就应允我，鼓励我，使我魂里有能力。 ###EN### On the day that I called out, You answered me; You encouraged me with strength in my soul.
Verse_Ch: 138:4 耶和华阿，地上的君王都要称谢你，因他们听见了你口中的言语。 ###EN### All the kings of the earth will give thanks to You, O Jehovah; For they have heard the words of Your mouth.
Verse_Ch: 138:5 他们要歌颂耶和华的作为，因耶和华大有荣耀。 ###EN### And they will sing of the ways of Jehovah, For great is the glory of Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 138:6 耶和华虽高，仍看顾低微的人；祂却从远处认出骄傲的人。 ###EN### For though Jehovah is high, He regards the lowly; And the haughty He knows from afar.
Verse_Ch: 138:7 我虽行在患难中，你必使我存活；我的仇敌发怒，你必伸手抵挡他们，你的右手也必救我。 ###EN### Though I walk in the midst of trouble, You will preserve me; Against the wrath of my enemies You will stretch out Your hand, And Your right hand will save me.
Verse_Ch: 138:8 耶和华必成全关乎我的事；耶和华阿，你的慈爱永远长存；求你不要撇弃你亲手所造的。 ###EN### Jehovah will complete that which concerns me. O Jehovah, Your lovingkindness is forever; Do not forsake the works of Your own hands.
Chapter_Header: 139
Verse_Ch: 139:1 耶和华阿，你已经鉴察我，认识我。 ###EN### O Jehovah, You have searched me and known me.
Verse_Ch: 139:2 我坐下，我起来，你都晓得；你从远处知道我的意念。 ###EN### You know when I sit down and when I rise up; You understand my thoughts from afar.
Verse_Ch: 139:3 我行路，我躺卧，你都细察，你也深知我一切所行的。 ###EN### You thoroughly search my path and my lying down, And You are acquainted with all my ways.
Verse_Ch: 139:4 我的话还未到舌头上，耶和华阿，你已完全知晓。 ###EN### For a word is not yet on my tongue, And already You, O Jehovah, know it completely.
Verse_Ch: 139:5 你在我前后环绕我，按手在我身上。 ###EN### You have closed in on me behind and before And have laid Your hand on me.
Verse_Ch: 139:6 这样的知识太奇妙，是我不能测的；至高，是我不能及的。 ###EN### O knowledge too wonderful for me! It is so high; I cannot attain to it.
Verse_Ch: 139:7 我往那里去躲避你的灵？我往那里逃躲避你的面？ ###EN### Where shall I go, away from Your Spirit, And where shall I flee from Your presence?
Verse_Ch: 139:8 我若升到天上，你在那里；我若在阴间下榻，你也在那里。 ###EN### If I ascend into heaven, You are there; If I make my bed in Sheol, there You are.
Verse_Ch: 139:9 我若展开清晨的翅膀，飞到海极居住， ###EN### If I take the wings of the dawn And settle at the limits of the sea,
Verse_Ch: 139:10 就是在那里，你的手也必引导我，你的右手必紧握着我。 ###EN### There also Your hand will lead me, And Your right hand will take hold of me.
Verse_Ch: 139:11 我若说，黑暗必定遮蔽我，我周围的亮光必成为黑夜； ###EN### And if I say, Surely darkness will cover me, And the light around me will be night;
Verse_Ch: 139:12 黑暗对你也不是黑暗，黑夜必如白昼发亮；黑暗和光明在你看都是一样。 ###EN### Even the darkness is not dark to You, And night shines like day; The darkness is like the light.
Verse_Ch: 139:13 我的肺腑是你所造的；我在母腹中，你已把我联络起来。 ###EN### For it was You who formed my inward parts; You wove me together in my mother's womb.
Verse_Ch: 139:14 我要赞美你，因我受造奇妙可畏；你的作为奇妙，这是我魂深知道的。 ###EN### I will praise You, for I am awesomely and wonderfully made; Your works are wonderful, And my soul knows it well.
Verse_Ch: 139:15 我在隐密中受造，在地的深处巧妙的形成，那时，我的形体并不向你隐藏。 ###EN### My frame was not hidden from You When I was made in secret, Skillfully fashioned in the depths of the earth.
Verse_Ch: 139:16 我未成形的体质，你的眼早已看见了；你所定的日子，我尚未度过一日，都写在你的册上了。 ###EN### Your eyes saw my unformed substance; And in Your book all of them were written: The days that were ordained for me, When not one of them was yet.
Verse_Ch: 139:17 神阿，你的意念对我何等宝贵！其数何等众多！ ###EN### And how precious are Your thoughts to me, O God! How great is the sum of them!
Verse_Ch: 139:18 我若数点，比海沙更多。我睡醒的时候，仍与你同在。 ###EN### If I should count them, they would be more than the sand. When I awake, I am still with You.
Verse_Ch: 139:19 神阿，愿你杀戮恶人－所以你们好流人血的，离开我去罢－ ###EN### Oh that You, O God, would slay the wicked-Depart from me therefore, you men of bloodshed -
Verse_Ch: 139:20 就是那些恶意说话顶撞你的人，他们是你的仇敌，妄称你的名。 ###EN### Those who speak of You with evil intent, Who as Your enemies take Your name in vain.
Verse_Ch: 139:21 耶和华阿，恨恶你的，我岂不恨恶他们么？起来攻击你的，我岂不厌恶他们么？ ###EN### Do I not hate those who hate You, O Jehovah? And do I not loathe those who rise up against You?
Verse_Ch: 139:22 我切切的恨恶他们；他们成了我的仇敌。 ###EN### I hate them with a perfect hatred; They have become my own enemies.
Verse_Ch: 139:23 神阿，求你鉴察我，知道我的心；试炼我，知道我的思虑； ###EN### Search me, O God, and know my heart; Try me, and know my anxious thoughts;
Verse_Ch: 139:24 看在我里面有什么害人的行径没有，引导我走永远的道路。 ###EN### And see if there is some harmful way in me, And lead me on the eternal way.
Chapter_Header: 140
Verse_Ch: 140:1 耶和华阿，求你搭救我脱离恶人，保守我脱离强暴的人； ###EN### Deliver me, O Jehovah, from evil men; From violent men preserve me;
Verse_Ch: 140:2 他们心中图谋恶事，不断挑启争端。 ###EN### Who devise evil schemes in their hearts And continually stir up wars.
Verse_Ch: 140:3 他们使舌头尖利如蛇；嘴里有虺蛇的毒气。 细拉 ###EN### They have sharpened their tongues like that of a serpent; The poison of adders is under their lips.
Verse_Ch: 140:4 耶和华阿，求你保护我脱离恶人的手，保守我脱离强暴的人；他们图谋推我跌倒。 ###EN### Keep me, O Jehovah, from the hands of the wicked; From violent men preserve me; Who devise schemes to thrust me down.
Verse_Ch: 140:5 骄傲人为我暗设网罗和绳索；他们在路旁铺下网，为我设下圈套。 细拉 ###EN### The proud have hidden a trap for me and cords; They have spread a net by the wayside; They have set snares for me.
Verse_Ch: 140:6 我曾对耶和华说，你是我的神；耶和华阿，求你侧耳听我恳求的声音。 ###EN### I said to Jehovah, You are my God; Give ear, O Jehovah, to the voice of my supplications.
Verse_Ch: 140:7 主耶和华，我救恩的力量阿，在争战的日子，你遮护了我的头。 ###EN### O Jehovah Lord, strength of my salvation, You have covered my head in the day of battle.
Verse_Ch: 140:8 耶和华阿，求你不要遂恶人的心愿；不要成就他们的计谋，免得他们自高。 细拉 ###EN### O Jehovah, do not grant the desires of the wicked man; Do not let his evil scheme advance, Lest he be exalted.
Verse_Ch: 140:9 至于那些昂首围困我的人，愿他们嘴唇的毒害把自己淹没了。 ###EN### As for the head of those who surround me, May the mischief of their own lips cover them.
Verse_Ch: 140:10 愿火炭落在他们身上；愿他们被丢在火中，抛在深坑里，不能再起来。 ###EN### May burning coals drop down upon them; May they be thrown down into the fire, Into deep pits, never to rise again.
Verse_Ch: 140:11 愿说谗言的人，在地上坚立不住；愿祸患猎取强暴的人，将他打倒。 ###EN### Let no slanderer be established in the land; Let evil hunt down the violent man speedily.
Verse_Ch: 140:12 我知道耶和华必为困苦人伸冤，必为穷乏人辨屈。 ###EN### I know that Jehovah will maintain the cause of the afflicted And justice for the needy.
Verse_Ch: 140:13 义人必要称谢你的名；正直人必住在你面前。 ###EN### Surely the righteous will give thanks to Your name; The upright will dwell in Your presence.
Chapter_Header: 141
Verse_Ch: 141:1 耶和华阿，我曾呼求你；求你快快临到我这里。我呼求你的时候，愿你侧耳听我的声音。 ###EN### O Jehovah, I have called upon You; hasten to me. Give ear to my voice when I call out to You.
Verse_Ch: 141:2 愿我的祷告如香陈列在你面前，愿我举手祈求，如献晚祭。 ###EN### Let my prayer be set before You as incense, The lifting up of my hands as the evening offering.
Verse_Ch: 141:3 耶和华阿，求你在我的口边设立守卫；求你把守我嘴唇的门户。 ###EN### Set a watch, O Jehovah, before my mouth; Keep the door of my lips.
Verse_Ch: 141:4 求你不叫我的心偏向恶事，以致我和行罪孽的人一同行恶；也不叫我吃他们的美食。 ###EN### Do not let my heart turn to anything evil, To practice deeds of wickedness With men who commit iniquity; And let me not eat of their delicacies.
Verse_Ch: 141:5 愿义人凭慈爱击打我，责备我；这算为我头上的膏油，愿我的头不躲闪，因我仍要祷告，抵制人的恶行。 ###EN### Let the righteous strike me in kindness and reprove me; Let not my head refuse oil upon the head, For still my prayer is against their evil deeds.
Verse_Ch: 141:6 他们的审判官被扔在岩下；他们要听我的话，因为这话令人愉悦。 ###EN### Their judges are thrown down by the sides of the rock, And they hear my words, that they are pleasant.
Verse_Ch: 141:7 我们的骨头散在阴间门口，好像人耕田刨地掘起的土块。 ###EN### As when one plows and breaks up the earth, Our bones are scattered at the mouth of Sheol.
Verse_Ch: 141:8 主耶和华阿，我的眼目仰望你；我投奔于你，求你不要将我的性命倾倒出来。 ###EN### For my eyes are upon You, O Jehovah Lord; In You I take refuge; do not pour out my soul.
Verse_Ch: 141:9 求你保护我脱离他们为我设的网罗，和作孽之人的圈套。 ###EN### Keep me from the trap they have set for me And from the snares of the workers of iniquity.
Verse_Ch: 141:10 愿恶人落在自己的网里，我却得以安然经过。 ###EN### May the wicked fall into their own nets While I alone pass by.
Chapter_Header: 142
Verse_Ch: 142:1 我发声哀求耶和华，发声恳求耶和华。 ###EN### With my voice I cry to Jehovah; With my voice I make my supplication to Jehovah.
Verse_Ch: 142:2 我在祂面前倾吐我的苦情，在祂面前诉说我的患难。 ###EN### I pour out my complaint before Him; I declare my trouble before Him.
Verse_Ch: 142:3 我的灵在我里面发昏的时候，你知道我的路径。在我所行的道路上，人为我暗设网罗。 ###EN### When my spirit fainted within me, You knew my path. On the way on which I walked They have hidden a trap for me.
Verse_Ch: 142:4 求你向我右边观看，因为没有人认识我；我无处逃避，也没有人眷顾我。 ###EN### Look on my right hand and see, For there is no one who regards me; Refuge has failed me; No one cares for me.
Verse_Ch: 142:5 耶和华阿，我曾向你哀求；我说，你是我的避难所，是我在活人之地的业分。 ###EN### I cried to You, O Jehovah; I said, You are my refuge, My portion in the land of the living.
Verse_Ch: 142:6 求你垂听我的呼求，因我落到极卑微的地步；求你救我脱离逼迫我的人，因为他们比我强大。 ###EN### Give heed to my cry, For I have been brought very low; Deliver me from those who persecute me, For they are stronger than I.
Verse_Ch: 142:7 求你领我出离被囚之地，我好称谢你的名。义人必环绕我，因为你必厚待我。 ###EN### Bring my soul out of prison, That I may give thanks to Your name. The righteous will surround me, For You will deal bountifully with me.
Chapter_Header: 143
Verse_Ch: 143:1 耶和华阿，求你听我的祷告，侧耳听我的恳求，凭你的信实和公义应允我； ###EN### O Jehovah, hear my prayer; Give ear to my supplications; Answer me in Your faithfulness and in Your righteousness;
Verse_Ch: 143:2 求你不要传唤你的仆人去受审，因为在你面前，凡活着的人没有一个是义的。 ###EN### And do not enter into judgment with Your servant, For no one alive is righteous in Your sight.
Verse_Ch: 143:3 原来仇敌逼迫我，将我的命压倒在地，使我住在幽暗之处，像死了许久的人一样。 ###EN### For the enemy has persecuted my soul; He has crushed my life down to the ground; He has caused me to dwell in dark places, like those who have been long dead.
Verse_Ch: 143:4 所以，我的灵在我里面发昏；我的心在我里面惊惧。 ###EN### Therefore my spirit faints within me; My heart is appalled in the midst of me.
Verse_Ch: 143:5 我追想古时之日，默念你的一切作为，默想你手的工作。 ###EN### I remember the days of old; I meditate upon all that You have done; I muse upon the work of Your hands.
Verse_Ch: 143:6 我向你伸开双手祷告，我的魂渴想你，如干旱之地盼雨一样。 细拉 ###EN### I spread out my hands to You; My soul thirsts for You like a parched land.
Verse_Ch: 143:7 耶和华阿，求你速速应允我；我的灵耗尽。不要向我掩面，免得我像那些下坑的人一样。 ###EN### Hurry and answer me, O Jehovah; My spirit fails. Do not hide Your face from me, Lest I become like those who go down into the pit.
Verse_Ch: 143:8 求你使我清晨得听你的慈爱，因我信靠你。求你使我知道当行的道路，因我的魂仰望你。 ###EN### Cause me to hear Your lovingkindness in the morning, For in You I trust. Make known to me the way on which I should walk, For to You I lift up my soul.
Verse_Ch: 143:9 耶和华阿，求你救我脱离我的仇敌；我逃往你那里避难。 ###EN### Deliver me from my enemies, O Jehovah; I have fled to You for a refuge.
Verse_Ch: 143:10 求你指教我遵行你的旨意，因你是我的神；愿你至善的灵引我到平坦之地。 ###EN### Teach me to do Your will, For You are my God; Let Your good Spirit lead me In a plain country.
Verse_Ch: 143:11 耶和华阿，求你为你的名将我救活；凭你的公义，将我从患难中领出来； ###EN### For Your name's sake, O Jehovah, preserve me alive; In Your righteousness bring my soul out of trouble.
Verse_Ch: 143:12 凭你的慈爱剪除我的仇敌，灭绝一切欺压我的人，因我是你的仆人。 ###EN### And in Your lovingkindness cut off my enemies And destroy all those who oppress my soul, For I am Your servant.
Chapter_Header: 144
Verse_Ch: 144:1 耶和华我的磐石，是当受颂赞的；祂教导我的手争战，教导我的指头打仗。 ###EN### Blessed be Jehovah my rock, Who teaches my hands for war And my fingers for battle:
Verse_Ch: 144:2 祂是我慈爱的主，我的山寨，我的高台，我的搭救者，我的盾牌，是我所投靠的；祂使我的百姓服在我以下。 ###EN### My Lord of lovingkindness and my fortress, My high retreat and my Deliverer, My shield and He in whom I take refuge, Who subdues my people under me.
Verse_Ch: 144:3 耶和华阿，人算什么，你竟认识他？世人算什么，你竟顾念他？ ###EN### O Jehovah, what is man, that You take knowledge of him, And the son of man, that You think of him?
Verse_Ch: 144:4 人好像一口气；他的年日如同影儿过去。 ###EN### Man is like a breath; His days are like a passing shadow.
Verse_Ch: 144:5 耶和华阿，求你使天下垂，亲自降临；摸山，山就冒烟。 ###EN### O Jehovah, bow Your heavens down and descend; Touch the mountains, and they will smoke.
Verse_Ch: 144:6 求你发出闪电，使仇敌四散；射出你的箭，使他们溃乱。 ###EN### Flash forth lightning, and scatter them; Send forth Your arrows, and discomfit them.
Verse_Ch: 144:7 求你从高处伸手救拔我，拯救我出离大水，脱离外邦人的手； ###EN### Stretch forth Your hand from on high; Rescue me and deliver me From the great waters, From the hand of foreigners;
Verse_Ch: 144:8 他们的口说虚谎的话，他们的右手是起假誓的右手。 ###EN### Whose mouth speaks deceit, And whose right hand is a right hand of falsehood.
Verse_Ch: 144:9 神阿，我要向你唱新歌；用十弦瑟向你歌颂； ###EN### O God, I will sing a new song to You; Upon a harp of ten strings I will sing psalms to You,
Verse_Ch: 144:10 你是那使君王得救的，你是那救仆人大卫脱离害命之刀的。 ###EN### Who gives salvation to kings, Who rescues David His servant from the hurtful sword.
Verse_Ch: 144:11 求你救拔我，拯救我脱离外邦人的手；他们的口说虚谎的话；他们的右手是起假誓的右手。 ###EN### Rescue me and deliver me from the hand of foreigners, Whose mouth speaks deceit, And whose right hand is a right hand of falsehood.
Verse_Ch: 144:12 愿我们的儿子，从幼年好像树木长大；愿我们的女儿，如同房角的柱石，是按宫殿的样式凿成的； ###EN### May our sons be like plants Grown up in their youth; May our daughters be like corner pillars Hewn out in fashion for a palace;
Verse_Ch: 144:13 愿我们的仓盈满，能出各样的粮食；愿我们的羊，在田间孳生千万。 ###EN### May our barns be full, Furnishing produce of all kinds; May our sheep bring forth thousands And ten thousands in our fields;
Verse_Ch: 144:14 愿我们的牛驮着满驮；愿无人闯进来抢夺，也无人出去争战，我们的街市上也无哭号的声音。 ###EN### May our oxen be fully laden; May there be no breaking in to rob or going forth to fight, Or outcry in our streets.
Verse_Ch: 144:15 有这样光景的百姓，便为有福；有耶和华为他们的神，这百姓便为有福。 ###EN### Blessed are the people who are so; Blessed are the people whose God is Jehovah.
Chapter_Header: 145
Verse_Ch: 145:1 我的神我的王阿，我要尊崇你；我要永永远远颂赞你的名。 ###EN### I will extol You, O my God and King; And I will bless Your name forever and ever.
Verse_Ch: 145:2 我要天天颂赞你，我要永永远远赞美你的名。 ###EN### Every day I will bless You, And I will praise Your name forever and ever.
Verse_Ch: 145:3 耶和华本为大，该受大赞美；其大无法测度。 ###EN### Great is Jehovah, and much to be praised; And His greatness is unsearchable.
Verse_Ch: 145:4 这一代要对另一代称颂你的作为，他们要传扬你的大能。 ###EN### One generation will laud Your works to another, And they will declare Your mighty acts.
Verse_Ch: 145:5 我要默想你威严的尊荣，和你奇妙的作为。 ###EN### Upon the glorious splendor of Your majesty And upon Your wondrous works I will muse.
Verse_Ch: 145:6 人要讲说你可畏之事的能力，我也要述说你的伟大。 ###EN### And men will speak of the might of Your awesome deeds, And I will declare Your greatness.
Verse_Ch: 145:7 他们要记念且说出你至大的美善，并要欢唱你的公义。 ###EN### They will utter the memory of Your great goodness And will sing for joy of Your righteousness.
Verse_Ch: 145:8 耶和华有恩典，有怜恤，不轻易发怒，大有慈爱。 ###EN### Jehovah is gracious and compassionate, Long-suffering and great in lovingkindness.
Verse_Ch: 145:9 耶和华善待万有，祂的怜恤覆庇祂一切所造的。 ###EN### Jehovah is good to all, And His compassions are upon all His works.
Verse_Ch: 145:10 耶和华阿，你一切所造的，都要赞美你；你的虔诚人也要颂赞你。 ###EN### All Your works will praise You, O Jehovah; And Your faithful ones will bless You.
Verse_Ch: 145:11 他们要讲说你国的荣耀，谈论你的大能， ###EN### They will speak of the glory of Your kingdom And tell of Your power,
Verse_Ch: 145:12 好叫世人知道你大能的作为，并你国度的威荣。 ###EN### To make known to the sons of men Your mighty acts And the glorious splendor of Your kingdom.
Verse_Ch: 145:13 你的国是永远的国，你的管治权存到万代。 ###EN### Your kingdom is an eternal kingdom, And Your dominion is throughout all generations.
Verse_Ch: 145:14 耶和华扶持一切跌倒的人，扶起一切被压下的人。 ###EN### Jehovah upholds all who are falling And raises up all who are bowed down.
Verse_Ch: 145:15 众人的眼目都仰望你，你按时给他们食物。 ###EN### The eyes of everyone wait for You, And You give them their food in due season.
Verse_Ch: 145:16 你张开手，使一切有生命的物都随愿饱足。 ###EN### You open up Your hand And satisfy the desire of every living thing.
Verse_Ch: 145:17 耶和华在祂一切所行的，无不公义；在祂一切所作的，都有慈爱。 ###EN### Jehovah is righteous in all His ways, And faithfully kind in all His doings.
Verse_Ch: 145:18 凡呼求耶和华的，就是真实呼求祂的，耶和华便与他们相近。 ###EN### Jehovah is near to all who call upon Him, To all who call upon Him in truth.
Verse_Ch: 145:19 敬畏祂的，祂必成就他们的心愿，也必听他们的呼求，拯救他们。 ###EN### He will fulfill the desire of those who fear Him, And He will hear their cry and save them.
Verse_Ch: 145:20 耶和华保护一切爱祂的人，却要灭绝一切的恶人。 ###EN### Jehovah preserves all who love Him, But He will destroy all the wicked.
Verse_Ch: 145:21 我的口要说出赞美耶和华的话，凡有血肉的都要永永远远颂赞祂的圣名。 ###EN### My mouth will speak the praise of Jehovah, And all flesh will bless His holy name forever and ever.
Chapter_Header: 146
Verse_Ch: 146:1 阿利路亚！我的魂哪，你要赞美耶和华！ ###EN### Hallelujah! Praise Jehovah, O my soul!
Verse_Ch: 146:2 我一生要赞美耶和华；我还活着的时候，要歌颂我的神。 ###EN### I will praise Jehovah while I live; I will sing psalms to my God while I yet have being.
Verse_Ch: 146:3 你们不要倚靠尊贵人，不要倚靠世人，他一点不能拯救。 ###EN### Do not trust in princes, In a son of man, with whom there is no salvation.
Verse_Ch: 146:4 他的气一断，就归回尘土；他所打算的，当日就销灭了。 ###EN### His breath goes forth; he returns to his earth; On that day his plans perish.
Verse_Ch: 146:5 以雅各的神为帮助，仰望耶和华他神的，这人便为有福。 ###EN### Blessed is the man whose help is the God of Jacob, Whose hope is in Jehovah his God,
Verse_Ch: 146:6 耶和华造天、地、海、和其中的万物；祂守信实，直到永远； ###EN### Who made heaven and earth And the sea, and all that is in them; Who keeps faith forever;
Verse_Ch: 146:7 祂为受欺压的伸冤，赐食物给饥饿的。耶和华释放被囚的； ###EN### Who executes judgment for the oppressed; Who gives food to the famished. Jehovah frees the prisoners;
Verse_Ch: 146:8 耶和华开了瞎子的眼睛；耶和华扶起被压下的人；耶和华喜爱义人； ###EN### Jehovah opens the eyes of the blind; Jehovah raises up those who are bowed down; Jehovah loves the righteous;
Verse_Ch: 146:9 耶和华保护寄居的，扶持孤儿和寡妇，却使恶人的道路弯曲。 ###EN### Jehovah preserves the sojourners; He upholds the orphan and the widow; But He subverts the way of the wicked.
Verse_Ch: 146:10 耶和华要作王，直到永远，锡安哪，你的神要作王，直到万代！阿利路亚！ ###EN### Jehovah will reign forever, Your God, O Zion, forever and ever. Hallelujah!
Chapter_Header: 147
Verse_Ch: 147:1 阿利路亚！歌颂我们的神，这本为美善；赞美的话是合宜的。 ###EN### Hallelujah! For it is good to sing psalms to our God; For it is pleasant; praise is fitting.
Verse_Ch: 147:2 耶和华建造耶路撒冷，聚集以色列被赶散的人。 ###EN### Jehovah builds up Jerusalem; He gathers the outcasts of Israel.
Verse_Ch: 147:3 祂医好伤心的人，缠裹他们的伤处。 ###EN### He heals the brokenhearted And binds up their wounds.
Verse_Ch: 147:4 祂数点星宿的数目，一一给它们起名。 ###EN### He counts the number of the stars; He calls them all by their names.
Verse_Ch: 147:5 我们的主为大，大有能力；祂的聪明无穷无尽。 ###EN### Great is our Lord, and mighty in power; His understanding is infinite.
Verse_Ch: 147:6 耶和华扶持卑微的人，将恶人贬降于地。 ###EN### Jehovah uplifts the lowly; He brings the wicked down to the ground.
Verse_Ch: 147:7 你们要以感谢向耶和华歌唱，用琴向我们的神歌颂； ###EN### Sing unto Jehovah with thanksgiving; Sing psalms to our God with the lyre;
Verse_Ch: 147:8 祂用云遮天，为地备雨，使草生长在山上， ###EN### Who covers the heavens with clouds, Who prepares rain for the earth, Who causes grass to grow on the mountains,
Verse_Ch: 147:9 赐食物给走兽和啼叫的小乌鸦。 ###EN### Who gives to the beast its food, And to the young ravens who cry.
Verse_Ch: 147:10 祂不喜悦马的力大，不喜爱人的腿快。 ###EN### He takes no delight in the strength of horses; Nor pleasure in the legs of man.
Verse_Ch: 147:11 耶和华喜爱敬畏祂和盼望祂慈爱的人。 ###EN### Jehovah takes pleasure in those who fear Him, In those who hope in His lovingkindness.
Verse_Ch: 147:12 耶路撒冷阿，你要颂赞耶和华；锡安哪，你要称颂你的神； ###EN### Laud Jehovah, O Jerusalem; Praise your God, O Zion;
Verse_Ch: 147:13 因为祂坚固了你城门的门闩，赐福给你中间的儿女。 ###EN### For He has strengthened the bars of your gates; He has blessed your children within you.
Verse_Ch: 147:14 祂使你境内平安；用上好的麦子使你饱足。 ###EN### He makes peace in your borders; He satisfies you with the finest wheat.
Verse_Ch: 147:15 祂向地发出命令；祂的话速速传开。 ###EN### He sends forth His command to the earth; His word runs very swiftly.
Verse_Ch: 147:16 祂降雪如羊毛，撒霜如炉灰。 ###EN### He gives snow like wool; He scatters frost like ashes;
Verse_Ch: 147:17 祂掷下冰雹如碎渣；祂发出寒冷，谁能受得住呢？ ###EN### He casts His hail like crumbs-Who can stand before His cold?
Verse_Ch: 147:18 祂一发出祂的话，这些就都融化；祂使风刮起，水便流动。 ###EN### He sends forth His word and melts them; He causes His wind to blow; the waters flow.
Verse_Ch: 147:19 祂将祂的话指示雅各，将祂的律例和典章指示以色列。 ###EN### He declares His word to Jacob, His statutes and His ordinances to Israel.
Verse_Ch: 147:20 别国祂都没有这样对待过；至于祂的典章，他们向来都不知道。阿利路亚！ ###EN### He has not dealt so with any other nation; And as for His ordinances, they have not known them. Hallelujah!
Chapter_Header: 148
Verse_Ch: 148:1 阿利路亚！你们要从天上赞美耶和华，要在高处赞美祂。 ###EN### Hallelujah! Praise Jehovah from the heavens; Praise Him in the heights.
Verse_Ch: 148:2 祂的众使者都要赞美祂；祂的众军都要赞美祂。 ###EN### Praise Him, all His angels; Praise Him, all His hosts.
Verse_Ch: 148:3 日头月亮，你们要赞美祂；放光的众星，你们都要赞美祂。 ###EN### Praise Him, sun and moon; Praise Him, all stars of light.
Verse_Ch: 148:4 诸天的天，和诸天之上的水，你们都要赞美祂。 ###EN### Praise Him, you heaven of heavens, And you waters that are above the heavens.
Verse_Ch: 148:5 愿这些都赞美耶和华的名；因祂一吩咐，这些便都造成。 ###EN### Let them praise the name of Jehovah; For He commanded, and they were created.
Verse_Ch: 148:6 祂将这些立定，直到永永远远；祂颁布了命令，就不能废去。 ###EN### And He established them forever and ever; He gave the decree which shall not pass away.
Verse_Ch: 148:7 你们要从地上赞美耶和华，大鱼和一切深渊， ###EN### Praise Jehovah from the earth, You sea monsters and all the depths;
Verse_Ch: 148:8 火与冰雹，雪和烟雾，执行祂话的狂风， ###EN### Fire and hail, snow and smoke; Stormy wind that executes His word;
Verse_Ch: 148:9 大山和一切小山，结果子的树木和一切香柏树， ###EN### Mountains and all hills; Fruit trees and all cedars;
Verse_Ch: 148:10 野兽和一切牲畜，爬物和飞鸟， ###EN### Animals wild and tame; Creeping things and birds of flight;
Verse_Ch: 148:11 地上的君王和万民，首领和地上一切审判官， ###EN### Kings of the earth and all peoples; Princes and all judges of the earth;
Verse_Ch: 148:12 少年人以及处女，老年人并孩童，都当赞美耶和华。 ###EN### Choice young men as well as virgins; Old men with young men.
Verse_Ch: 148:13 愿这些都赞美耶和华的名，因为独有祂的名被尊崇；祂的荣美超乎天地之上。 ###EN### Let them praise the name of Jehovah, For His name alone is exalted; His glory is above the earth and the heavens.
Verse_Ch: 148:14 祂已将祂百姓的角举起，使祂一切圣民以色列人，就是与祂相近的百姓，都赞美祂。阿利路亚！ ###EN### And He has raised up a horn for His people, The praise of all His faithful ones, The children of Israel, a people near to Him. Hallelujah!
Chapter_Header: 149
Verse_Ch: 149:1 阿利路亚！你们要向耶和华唱新歌，在圣民的会中唱出对祂的赞美。 ###EN### Hallelujah! Sing a new song to Jehovah; Sing His praise in the congregation of His faithful ones.
Verse_Ch: 149:2 愿以色列因造他的主喜乐；愿锡安的民因他们的王欢腾。 ###EN### Let Israel rejoice in his Maker; Let the children of Zion exult in their King.
Verse_Ch: 149:3 愿他们跳舞赞美祂的名，击鼓弹琴歌颂祂。 ###EN### Let them praise His name with dancing; Let them sing psalms to Him with the tambourine and the lyre.
Verse_Ch: 149:4 因为耶和华喜爱祂的百姓；祂用救恩给低微的人作妆饰。 ###EN### For Jehovah takes pleasure in His people; He adorns the lowly with salvation.
Verse_Ch: 149:5 愿圣民在荣耀中欢乐；愿他们在床上欢呼。 ###EN### Let the faithful ones exult in glory; Let them give a ringing shout upon their beds.
Verse_Ch: 149:6 愿他们口中称赞神为高，愿他们手里有两刃的刀， ###EN### Let the high praises of God be in their throats, And a two-edged sword in their hand,
Verse_Ch: 149:7 为要报复列邦，刑罚众民； ###EN### To execute vengeance on the nations And punishment among the peoples;
Verse_Ch: 149:8 要用链子捆他们的君王，用铁镣锁他们的尊贵人； ###EN### To bind their kings with fetters And their nobles with chains of iron;
Verse_Ch: 149:9 要在他们身上施行所记录的审判。祂的圣民都有这尊荣。阿利路亚！ ###EN### To execute upon them the judgment written. This honor is for all His faithful ones. Hallelujah!
Chapter_Header: 150
Verse_Ch: 150:1 阿利路亚！你们要在神的圣所赞美祂，在祂显能力的穹苍赞美祂。 ###EN### Hallelujah! Praise God in His sanctuary; Praise Him in the firmament of His power.
Verse_Ch: 150:2 要因祂大能的作为赞美祂，按着祂的宏伟至大赞美祂。 ###EN### Praise Him for His mighty acts; Praise Him according to His vast greatness.
Verse_Ch: 150:3 要用角声赞美祂，鼓瑟弹琴赞美祂； ###EN### Praise Him with the blast of the trumpet; Praise Him with the harp and lyre;
Verse_Ch: 150:4 击鼓跳舞赞美祂，用丝弦的乐器和箫的声音赞美祂； ###EN### Praise Him with the tambourine and with dancing; Praise Him with the stringed instrument and the pipe.
Verse_Ch: 150:5 用大响的钹赞美祂，用高声的钹赞美祂。 ###EN### Praise Him with the loud cymbals; Praise Him with the loud clanging cymbals.
Verse_Ch: 150:6 凡有气息的，都要赞美耶和华。阿利路亚！ ###EN### Let everything that has breath praise Jehovah. Hallelujah!
